Disease: dmaa (Asthma)

Description: 
sookshm shvaas nliyom mem koii rog utpnn ho jaane ke kaarण jb kisii vykti ko sms lene mem preshaanii hone lgtii hai tb yh sthiti dmaa rog khlaatii hai, is rog mem vykti ko khmsii kii smsyaa bhii hotii hai।

Symptoms: 
- jb dmaa rog se piid़it rogii ko dauraa pd़taa hai to use sookhii yaa aithndaar khmsii hotii hai।
- jb rog bhut adhik bdh़ jaataa hai to dauraa aane kii sthiti utpnn ho jaatii hai jisse rogii ko sms lene mem bhut adhik dikkt aatii hai tthaa vykti chhtptaane lgtaa hai।
- dmaa rog se piid़it rogii ko kph skht, bdboodaar tthaa doriidaar nikltaa hai।
- piid़it rogii ko sms lenem mem bhut adhik kthinaaii hotii hai।
- yh rog strii-purush donom ko ho sktaa hai।
- raat ke smy mem lgbhg 2 bje ke baad daure adhik pd़te haim।
- rogii ko rog ke shuruaatii smy mem khmsii, srsraaht aur sms ukhd़ne ke daure pd़ne lgte haim।
- sms lete smy adhik jor lgaane pr rogii kaa chehraa laal ho jaataa hai।
- sms lete smy hlkii-hlkii siitii bjne kii aavaaj bhii sunaaii pd़tii hai।
- sms lene tthaa sms ko baahr chhod़ne mem kaaphii jor lgaanaa pd़taa hai।

Reasons: 
- aushdhiyom kaa adhik pryog krne ke kaarण kफ़ sookh jaane se dmaa ho jaataa hai।
- khaan-paan ke glt triike se yh rog ho sktaa hai।
- maansik tnaav, krodh tthaa adhik bhy ke kaarण bhii dmaa hone kaa ek kaarण hai।
- khoon mem kisii prkaar se dosh utpnn ho jaane ke kaarण bhii dmaa ho sktaa hai।
- nshiile pdaarthom kaa adhik sevn krnaa bhii is rog kaa kaarण hai।
- khmsii, jukaam tthaa njlaa rog adhik smy tk rhne se dmaa ho sktaa hai।
- bhookh se adhik bhojn khaane se dmaa ho sktaa hai।
- mirch-msaale, tle-bhune khaady pdaarthom tthaa grishth bhojn krne se yh rog ho sktaa hai।
- phephd़om mem kmjorii, hृdy mem kmjorii, gurdom mem kmjorii, mtom mem kmjorii, snaayumणdl mem kmjorii tthaa naakd़aa rog ho jaane ke kaarण dmaa ho jaataa hai।
- mnushy kii shvaas nlikaa mem dhool tthaa thmd lg jaane ke kaarण bhii dmaa ho sktaa hai।
- dhool ke kण, khopd़ii ke khurणd, kuchh paudhom ke pushprj, aणde tthaa aise hii any pdaarthom kaa bhojn mem adhik sevn krne ke kaarण yh rog ho sktaa hai।
- mnushy ke shriir kii paachn nliyom mem jln utpnn krne vaale pdaarthom kaa sevn krne se bhii dmaa ho sktaa hai।
- ml-mootr ke veg ko baar-baar rokne se yh rog ho sktaa hai।
- grd, dhum, gmdgii, bdboo, gmde bistr, puraanii kitaabem aur kpड़om kii jhaaड़, khetom kii jhaaड़, skht srdii, brsaat, jukaam, phloo, aadi sookshm kणom kaa sms dvaaraa phephड़om mem jaane se dmaa ho sktaa hai।
- vaataavrण mem prdooshण se hone vaalii elrjii
- iske alaavaa kii logom mem kuchh nishchit dvaaom (espiriin aur betaa- blॉkrs) ke sevn se bhii dmaa ke risk phaiktrs bdh़ skte haim।
- atydhik bhaavnaatmk abhivyktiym (jaise chiikhne-chillaane yaa phir jordaar triike se hmsnaa bhii) bhii kuchh logom mem dmaa kii smsyaa ko bdh़aakr daure kii sthiti utpnn kr sktii haim।
- asthmaa yaa elrjii kaa paarivaarik itihaas (aanivmshik dmaa)
- jnm ke smy km vjn aur smy se phle bchchom kaa jnm, jnm ke phle aur / yaa jnm ke baad tmbaakoo ke dhuem ke smprk
- bhiid़, vaayuprdooshण, dhool (ghr yaa baahr kii) yaa pepr kii dst, rsoii kaa dhum, nmii, siiln, mausm privrtn, srdii-jukaam, dhoomrpaan, phaastphoods, tnaav v chimtaa, paaltoo jaanvr ke smprk mem rhnaa aur peड़-paudhom aur phoolom ke praagkणom (paudhe ke phoolom mem paaye jaane vaale sookshm kणom ko praagkण khte haim) aadi ko shaamil kiyaa jaataa hai।

Treatments:
- rogii ko grm bistr pr sonaa chaahie। 
- dhoomrpaan nhiim krnaa chaahie। 
- bhojn mem mirch-msaaledaar chiijom kaa sevn nhiim krnaa chaahie। 
- dhool tthaa dhume bhre vaataavrण se bchnaa chaahie। 
- maansik preshaanii, tnaav, krodh tthaa ld़aaii-jhgdom se bchnaa chaahie। 
- shraab, tmbaakoo tthaa any nshiile pdaarthom kaa sevn nhiim krnaa chaahie। 

Home Remedies:
- lhsun dmaa ke ilaaj mem kaaphii kaargr saabit hotaa hai। 30 milii doodh mem lhsun kii pmch kliym ubaalem aur is mishrण kaa hr roj sevn krne se dme mem shuruaatii avsthaa mem kaaphii phaaydaa miltaa hai।
- adrk kii grm chaay mem lhsun kii do pisii kliym milaakr piine se bhii asthmaa niymtrit rhtaa hai। sbere aur shaam is chaay kaa sevn krne se mriij ko phaaydaa hotaa hai।
- adrk kaa ek chmmch taajaa rs, ek kp maithii ke kaaढ़e aur svaadaanusaar shhd is mishrण mem milaaem। dme ke mriijom ke lie yh mishrण laajvaab saabit hotaa hai।
- dmaa rogii paanii mem ajvaain milaakr ise ubaalem aur paanii se uthtii bhaap lem, yh ghreloo upaay kaaphii phaaydemmd hotaa hai।
- 4-5 laumg lem aur 125 milii paanii mem 5 mint tk ubaalem। is mishrण ko chhaankr ismem ek chmmch shuddh shhd milaaem~ aur grm-grm pii lem। hr roj do se tiin baar yh kaaढ़aa bnaakr piine se mriij ko nishchit roop se laabh hotaa hai।
- 180 mimii paanii mem mutthiibhr shjn kii pttiym milaakr kriib 5 mint tk ubaalem। mishrण ko thmdaa hone dem, usmem chutkiibhr nmk, kaaliimirch aur niiboo rs bhii milaayaa jaa sktaa hai। is soop kaa niymit roop se istemaal dmaa upchaar mem kaargr maanaa gyaa hai।
- maithii kaa kaaढ़aa taiyaar krne ke lie ek chmmch maithiidaanaa aur ek kp paanii ubaalem। hr roj sbere-shaam is mishrण kaa sevn krne se nishchit laabh miltaa hai।
- ek pkaa kelaa chhilkaa lekr chaakoo se lmbaaii mem chiiraa lgaakr usmem ek chhotaa chmmch do graam kpड़aa chhaan kii huii kaalii mirch bhr dem। phir use bgair chhiile hii, kele ke vृksh ke ptte mem achchhii trh lpet kr dore se bmdh kr 2-3 ghmte rkh dem। baad mem kele ke ptte shit use aag mem is prkaar bhoone kii upr kaa pttaa jle। thmdaa hone pr kele kaa chhilkaa nikaalkr kelaa khaa lem।


Disease: mdhumeh (Diabetes)

Description: 
mdhumeh yaa daaybitiij haal ke saalom mem hone vaalaa sbse khtrnaak jiivnshailii rog maanaa jaataa hai। hr saal kii hjaar log isse prbhaavit hote haim। aaiyem jaanem mdhumeh ke baarem mem jise log aam bolchaal kii bhaashaa me shugr (Sugar ki Bimari) bhii khte haim।

Symptoms: 
- atydhik pyaas lgnaa aur baar baar peshaab aanaa (Excessive Thirst): yh mdhumeh hone ke pukhtaa lkshण haim
- jkhmom kaa jldii nhii bhrnaa aur baar baar smkrmण se prbhaavit honaa (Slow Healing Sores and Recurrent Infections)
- thkaan mhsoos honaa (Feeling Lazy): koshikaaom mem glookoज़ nhii phumchne ke kaarण shriir ko oorjaa aapoorti poorii trh se nhii ho paatii hai aur mdhumeh kaa rogii hmeshaa thkaan mhsoos krtaa hai
- dhumdhlaa dikhnaa (Blurred Vision): rkt mem atirikt shugr kii upsthiti ke kaarण m~khom kii koshikaaom mem rkt aapoorti pr asr pड़taa hai aur dhiire dhiire m~khe prbhaavit hone lgtii haim
- pairo aur haathom mem jhnjhnaaht honaa (Tingling in Hands & Feet): rkt mem atirikt shugr kaa kaarण hmaare tmtrikaa prणaalii ko nuksaan phumchaa sktaa hai
- msooड़om mem soojn (Swollen Gums): mdhumeh ke kaarण msooड़om mem smkrmण kaa khtraa bढ़ jaataa hai
- rkt mem atirikt shugr kii upsthiti ke kaarण gurde rkt ko saaफ़ krne ke lie adhik kaam krne lgte haim aur mootr ke dvaaraa atirikt shugr ko shriir se baahr niklte haim। is kaarण baar baar peshaab aataa hai aur atydhik pyaas lgtii hai
- vjn km honaa (Weight Loss): hmaare shriir mem jb koshikaaom ko glookoज़ nhii miltaa to shriir, shriir mem upsthit vsaa tthaa mmspeshio se uskii aapoorti krtaa hai jiske kaarण shriir mem jmaa vsaa aur mmspeshio mem kmii aatii hai aur vjn bhut jldii km hone lgtaa hai

Treatments:
mdhumeh yaa daaybitiij se bchaav kaa sbse bढ़iyaa upaay hai iskii jaankaarii rkhnaa aur svsth jiivnshailii apnaanaa। daaybitiij se bchne ke kuchh khaan upaay nimn haim:
- prtidin ek ghmtaa vyaayaam jroor krem।
- apne ghr mem prtidin mdhumeh kaa test krem। rkt mem shugr kii maatraa kaa dhyaan rkhem।
- insulin imjekshn (Insulin Injetion) ko taiyaar krnaa aur svym lgaanaa aanaa chaahie।
- ek insulin pmp (Insulin Pump) saath rkhnaa।
- kaarbohaaidret (Carbohydrate) kii gintii ko dhyaan mem rkhnaa।
- rktchaap (Blood Pressure) km hone pr mtvpoorण jaankaarii kaa dhyaan rkhnaa


Disease: vaayrl bukhaar (Viral Fever)

Description: 
vaayrs ke smkrmण se hone vaale bukhaar ko vaayrl phiivr (Viral Fever) khte haim। vaayrl bukhaar ke vaayrs gle mem suptaavsthaa mem nishkriy rhte haim। thmde vaataavrण ke smprk mem aane, phrij kaa thmdaa paanii, shiitl pey piine aadi se ye vaayrs skriy hokr hmaare prtirkshaa tmtr ko prbhaavit kr dete haim।

Symptoms: 
- m~khem laal honaa
- is bukhaar mem shriir kaa taap 101 digrii se 103 digrii yaa aur jyaadaa bhii ho jaataa hai
- khmsii aur jukaam honaa
- jod़om mem drd aur soojn honaa
- thkaan aur gle mem drd honaa
- naak bhnaa honaa
- bdn drd honaa
- bhookh n lgnaa
- letne ke baad uthne mem kmjorii mhsoos krnaa
- sirdrd honaa

Reasons: 
vaayrl bukhaar shriir ke kmज़or prtirkshaa tmtr (Immune System) kii vjh se hotaa hai। agr shriir kii prtirkshण kshmtaa yaa imyoon sistm mjboot ho to yh biimaarii jldii nhiim hotii। 

Treatments:
vaayrl bukhaar kaa upaay (Treatment of Viral Fever)
- bukhaar agr 102 digrii tk hai aur koii aur khtrnaak lkshण nhiim haim to mriij kii dekhbhaal ghr pr hii kr skte haim।
- mriij ke shriir pr saamaany paanii kii pttiym rkhem। pttiym tb tk rkhem, jb tk shriir kaa taapmaan km n ho jaae। pttii rkhne ke baad vh grm ho jaatii hai islie use sirph 1 mint tk hii rkhem।
- agr maathe ke saath - saath shriir bhii grm hai to nॉrml paanii mem kpd़aa bhigokr nichod़em aur usse poore shriir ko pomchhem।
- mriij ko hr chhh ghmte mem pairaasitaamॉl (Paracetamol) kii ek golii de skte haim। doosrii koii golii dॉktr se poochhe binaa n dem।
- bchchom ko hr chaar ghmte mem 10 milii prti kilo vjn ke anusaar dvaa de skte haim।
- do din tk bukhaar thiik n ho to mriij ko dॉktr ke paas jroor le jaaem।
- saaph - sphaaii kaa pooraa khyaal rkhem। mriij ko vaayrl hai, to usse thod़ii doorii bnaae rkhem aur rogii ke dvaaraa istemaal kii gii chiijem istemaal n krem।
- mriij ko pooraa aaraam krne dem, khaaskr tej bukhaar mem। aaraam bhii bukhaar mem ilaaj kaa kaam krtaa hai।
- mriij chhiimkne se phle naak aur mumh pr rumaal rkhem। isse vaayrl hone pr doosrom mem phailegaa nhiim।
- vaayrl phiivr mem emtiibॉytik dvaaom kii koii bhoomikaa nhiim hotii। vaayrl phiivr 5 se 7 dinom mem thiik ho jaataa hai। 
- is rog kaa ilaaj lkshणom ke aadhaar pr kiyaa jaataa hai, rogii ko pryaapt maatraa mem glookoj aur ilektrolaait lenaa chaahie।


Disease: khsraa (Measles)

Description: 
khsraa (Measles), ek atymt smkraamk biimaarii hai। khsraa miijls vaayrs (Measles Virus) se phailtaa hai। isse grsit rogii kaa phle glaa khraab hotaa hai aur uske baad bukhaar aataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- mkhom mem laalii, soojn, chipchipaapn, khujlii, paanii niklnaa।
- khmsii aur jukaam honaa
- gle mem drd rhtaa hai।
- chaar din kaa bukhaar, bukhaar 40°C(104°F) tk phumch sktaa hai।
- tiinom sii -khmsii (Cough), bhtii huii naak (Coryza) aur m~kh kaa aanaa (Conjunctivitis)।
- bchchaa baar-baar rotaa hai।
- shriir mem tootn, thkaan, chiड़chiड़aapn hotaa hai।

Reasons: 
abhii tk jञaat kaarणom ke anusaar mnushy ke dvaaraa hii khsraa ek se doosre mnusy tk phailtaa hai। rogii ke kpड़e, bistr, rumaal aadi istemaal krne se vaayrl phailne kaa khtraa bढ़ jaataa hai।
khsraa ke jokhim (Risk Factors of Measles or Khasra)
khsraa mem naak se paanii bhii aa sktaa hai। ydi biimaarii kaa uchit upchaar n ho, to phephd़e mem bhii iskaa smkrmण ho sktaa hai। bd़om mem yh smkrmण vaayrl nimoniyaa mem bdl sktaa hai। yh dshaa rogii ke lie khtrnaak saabit ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
khsraa se bchaav kaa sbse behtriin triikaa hai iske rogii ke smprk mem naa aanaa। lekin agr khsraa (Khasra) ho bhii jaae to nimn upaay dvaaraa isse bchaav mumkin hai:
- prbhaavit bchche/rogii ko ekaant mem rkhem visheshkr daane sookhne v ppड़ii htne pr।
- roj taaje paanii se, binaa saabun aaraam se nhlaaem, daanom ko jyaadaa n rgड़em।
- dhiile, sootii, sphed kpड़e phnaaem tthaa unhem roj bdlem।
- bukhaar kii tejii mem sir pr deshii ghii kii maalish v paanii mem sootii motaa kpड़aa bhigokr rkhem।
- mukh v dmt saaph rkhne ke liye gungune paanii mem thoड़ii sii laal dvaa (poteshiym prmaignet) daalkr kullaa kraaem।
- dmtom ko mguliyom se jor dekr n saaph kraaem।
- bistr kii sootii chaadr ko prtidin bdlem।
- khaane mem saamaany, hlkaa, pchne vaalaa khaanaa dem।
- nmkiin vstuem km maatraa mem dem, jisse khujlii n ho।
- vitaamin yukt pdaarth jaise paalk, gaajr aadi jyaadaa dem।
- mkhom mem sote smy gulaab jl daalem। subh uthne pr borik paaudr gungune paanii mem daalkr dhiime-dhiime rooii bhigokr mkhom ko dhoyem।
- ghr se baahr n le jaayem, bhut jroorii ho to sootii mote kpड़e se dhk kr hii le jaaem।
- dhyaan rkhe kii rogii kaa kmraa bhut thmdaa, grm yaa siiln vaalaa n ho।
- khsre kaa mdeshaa hone pr yh aavshyk hai ki kisii yogy daaktr se ilaaj kraayaa jaae। isse bchne kaa ekmaatr upaay bchchom kaa tiikaakrण hai।


Disease: bdhज़mii (Gastric Problem)

Description: 
paachnkriyaa ke dauraan pet mem gais kaa bnnaa ek saamaany prkriyaa hai। shriir kii any prkriyaaom kii trh pet mem gais kaa bnnaa aur baahr nikl jaanaa bhii ek saamaany prkriyaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- khttii dkaarem aanaa,
- khaanaa yaa khttaa paanii (esid) mumh mem aa jaanaa,
- gle se khrkhraaht mhsoos honaa aur sms phoolne kii bhii shikaayt honaa,
- chhaatii ke nichle bhaag mem drd kaa mhsoos honaa aur ultii krne kaa mn krnaa,
- svbhaav mem  chiड़chiड़aapn aa jaanaa,

Reasons: 
- aniymit jiivnshailii
- jyaadaa tnaav
- jyaadaa tlaa- bhunaa bhojn
- smokimg, drimkimg
- raajmaa, kaale chne, sphed chne, lobiyaa, sookhe hre mtr, pॉpkॉrn, sookhii mkkii jaise anaaj pet mem gais paidaa kr skte haim।

Treatments:
bdhjmii yaa gaistrik kii smsyaa se nijaat paane kaa sbse achchhaa triikaa hai khaanpaan kaa dhyaan rkhnaa। dॉktrom ke anusaar gaistrik se nijaat paane ke aasaan upaay nimn haim:
- gais kii biimaarii mem upchaar ke saath apnii jiivnshailii mem bdlaav laakr isse chhutkaaraa paayaa jaa sktaa hai।
- gaistrik rogiyom ko bchaav ke liye kuchh saavdhaaniym brtnii chaahie taaki rog jyaadaa n bढ़ paaye।
- din bhr mem mukhy aahaar 2 baar ke sthaan pr 3-4 baar thoड़ii maatraa mem krem।
- tnaav n lem aur jldbaajii se bchem, gusse pr kaaboo rkhem।
- vyaayaam aur grm paanii piine se bhii gaistrik ke rogiyom ko aaraam miltaa hai।   

Home Remedies:
gais ko chikitsiiy bhaashaa mem apch ke roop mem jaanaa jaataa hai। gais ke lkshण soojn, dkaar, jln aur mtlii ho skte hai। gais aur apch hmaare pet mem paachk rs ke sraav se hone vaalii smsyaaem haim। pet mem maujood esid pet ke mdr jln paidaa krnaa shuroo kr detaa hai। ismem vykti ko bechainii, siine aur pet mem jln mhsoos hotii hai।
gais kii smsyaa jyaadaa tailiiy yaa msaaledaar khaanaa khaane se hotii hai, saath hii ydi pet khaalii hai tb bhii gais kii smsyaa ho sktii hai। bhut jyaadaa chaay yaa kॉफ़ii piine vaalom ko bhii gais kii smsyaa ho sktii hai। gais kii smsyaa ydi bढ़ jaae to smsyaa gmbhiir ho sktii hai islie smy rhte is pr kaaboo krnaa aavshyk hotaa hai। aaie aapko btaate haim kuchh ghreloo upaay jinhem apnaakr aap gais kii smsyaa se chhutkaaraa paa skte haim।


Disease: gthiyaa (Gout)

Description: 
gthiyaa (Gout) yaa vaatrkt ek saamaany rog hai jismem rogii ke ek yaa kii jod़om mem drd, akd़n yaa soojn aa jaatii hai। is rog mem jod़om mem gmthem bn jaatii haim aur chubhn jaisii tej piid़aa hotii hai। yh rog rkt mem yoorik esid kaa str bdh़ne se hotaa hai,jiskaa prmukh kaarण yoorik esid apchyn (Metabolism) se hai।

Symptoms: 
- kbhii-kbhii pairom, sir, tkhne, ghutnom, jmgh aur jod़om mem drd ke saath-saath soojn aanaa
- kbhii-kbhii bukhaar kii shikaayt
- kisii mg kaa shoony ho jaanaa
- khaayaa bhojn n pchnaa
- joड़om ko chhoone tthaa hilaane mem ashniiy drd honaa
- shriir mem khoon kii kmii hojaanaa aadi gthiyaa ke mukhy lkshण haim
- shriir mem bhaariipn

Reasons: 
gthiyaa rog ko jiivnshailii se juड़aa rog maanaa jaataa hai। adhikmsh maamlom mem iske mukhy kaarण nimn hote haim: 
jiivnshailii (Causes of Gout)
- 12% rogiyom mem gthiyaa (Gathiya) kaa mukhy kaarण aahaar ko maanaa gyaa hai। shraab , phruktoj-yukt pey, mms, mchhlii ke sevn se gthiyaa kaa jokhim bdh़taa hai।
- chyaapchy mem aaii khraabii
- motaapaa
kii rog bhii aise hote haim jinkii vjh se gthiyaa rog ho jaataa hai। yh rog nimn haim: 
- gurde kii biimaarii
- metaabolik simdrom
- pॉliisaaythiimiyaa
- led pॉyjnimg
- vृkkvaat
- hiimolitik eniimiyaa
- soraaysis aur mg prtisthaapn (Organ Replacement)
- mootrvrdhk dvaaiym (haaidroklorthaaydaaid) kaa sevn krne se bhii gthiyaa ho sktaa hai। 
- naaysin, espirin, saaiklosporin aur tekrolims aadi dvaaiym bhii gthiyaa rog kaa kaarण bn sktii haim। 

Treatments:
- baar-baar pd़ne vaale daurom (Attack) ko rokne ke lie dॉktr kii slaah se yoorik esid km krne kii dvaaiym le skte haim।
- saath mem drd aur soojn km krne ke lie nॉn-stiirॉydl emtiiinphlemetrii dvaaiym (NSAIDs), kolchisiin aur stirॉyds bhii le skte haim। yh dvaaiym praayh 1-2 hphte tk diye jaate haim।
- gthiyaa ke rogiyom ko protiinyukt aahaar se prhej krnaa chaahie। shriir mem protiin kii kmii ko door krne ke lie chokryukt aate kii rotii tthaa chhilke vaalii moomg kii daal khaaem। 
- uble anaaj, chaavl, baajraa, jau, gehoom, chpaatii aadi bhojn mem smmilit krem।
- ublii huii hrii sbjiym, mkurit anaaj, saaboodaanaa, giriidaar phl, shhd tthaa sbhii prkaar ke phl (khtte phl evm kele ko chhod़kr) pryaapt maatraa mem lem।
- niymit thlem, vyaayaam (kshmtaanusaar) evm maalish krem। kbj n hone dem। hphte mem ek din upvaas rkhnaa chaahie। isse drd mem raaht miltii hai।

Home Remedies:
umr bdh़ne pr ak‍sr logom ko gthiyaa kii shikaayt hone lgtii hai। iske piichhe sbse bd़aa kaarण bॉdii mem yoorik esid kii adhiktaa honaa hotaa hai। jb bॉdii mem yoorik esid j‍yaadaa ho jaataa hai to vh shriir ke joड़om mem chhote- chhote kris‍tl ke roop mem jmaa hone lgtaa hai isii kaarण joड़om mem drd aur aimthn hotii hai। gthiyaa ko kii s‍thaanom pr aamvt bhii khaa jaataa hai।


Disease: piilaa bukhaar (Yellow Fever)

Description: 
piitjvr yaa piilaa bukhaar (Yellow fever) tejii se hone vaalaa ek smkraamk bukhaar haim, jo achaank shuroo hotaa hai। is rog kaa kaark ek sookshm vishaaणu (Flavivirus) hotaa hai, jiskaa smvhn ediis iijiptiaaii (Aedes Aegypti) jaati ke mchchhrom dvaaraa hotaa hai।

- kmjorii mhsoos honaa

- thmd ke saath bukhaar aanaa,
- piiliyaa ho jaanaa,
- shriir mem piiड़aa honaa
- sir drd honaa,

Reasons: 
piilaa bukhaar ke lkshण
- anidraa, kaale dst, rktstraav, pittyukt mootr, rktchaap kii kmii aur naad़ii kii shithiltaa,
- kmjorii mhsoos honaa
- kॉphii ke rmg kii mitlii aanaa,
- ghaatk avsthaa mem mootr aanaa bmd ho jaanaa।
- thmd ke saath bukhaar aanaa,
- piiliyaa ho jaanaa,
- shriir mem piiड़aa honaa
- sir drd honaa,

Treatments:
piitjvr kaa ek bhii lkshण nज़r aane pr turmt dॉktr ko dikhaae। agr rogii ko tej bukhaar ho aur uskaa shriir bhii piilaa pड़ rhaa ho to binaa smy gmvaaem dॉktr se slaah lenii chaahie।

Home Remedies:
ylo phiivr yaa piit jvr smkrmण se hone vaalii khtrnaak biimaarii hai, lekin iske lie bhut se ilaaj maujood haim jo is pr kaaboo paa skte haim। piit jvr yaa piilaa bukhaar maadaa mchchhr ke kaatne se hotaa hai। piile bukhaar mem rogii kaa liivr daimej hone yaa piiliyaa hone kaa khtraa rhtaa hai। saath hii rogii ko ultiym bhii ho sktii haim। piile bukhaar se nijaat ke lie bhut se ghreloo nuskhe bhii haim, jisse praakृtik triike se iskaa upchaar kiyaa jaa ske।
1. tulsii aur kaalii mirch (Basil and Black Pepper)
kaalii mirch piile bukhaar ke ilaaj mem bhut kaargr saabit ho rhii hai। aadhaa liitr distild paanii mem kuchh tulsii ke ptte daalkr ublne dem। is paanii mem aadhaa chmmch kaalii mirch kaa paaudr milaaem। is paanii ko rmg bdlne tk ublne dem। yh paanii n kevl piile bukhaar ko km krtaa hai blki aapko turmt oorjaa bhii detaa hai। is paanii mem tiin chmmch shhd bhii milaayaa jaa sktaa hai। ise din mem do baar piiem।
2. pyaaj़ (Onion)
ek kchchaa pyaaj lem aur do hissom mem kaat lem। ise ovn mem daalkr lgbhg 15 mint ke lie 400 digrii pr semk lem। aisaa krne se pyaaj kaa rs aasaanii se nikl jaataa hai। is rs mem kuchh boomde shhd kii milaaem। is mitrण ko piile bukhaar se nijaat ke lie istemaal krem।
3. lhsun (Garlic)
baar baar ultii hone se dihaaidreshn ho jaataa hai jisse shriir aamtaur pr kmjor ho jaataa hai aur isse shriir kii imyoonitii bhii ghttii hai। lhsun apne vaayrl virodhii, emtii baiktiiriyl aur emtii ऑksiidemt guणom ke lie jaanaa jaataa hai। lhsun prtirkshaa prणaalii ko mjboot bnaane ke saath saath vaayrl aur baiktiiriyl smkrmण se shriir kii rkshaa krne mem skriy bhoomikaa nibhaataa hai। chhh se ds lhsun kii klii lekr unhem kuchl lem। is lhsun ko aap yoom bhii khaa skte haim yaa phir shhd milaakr subh subh khaaem। 
4. naariyl paanii (Coconut Water)
piile bukhaar mem dihaaidreshn se bchne ke lie naariyl paanii behd laabhkaarii hai। yh shriir ko haaidret krke any poshk ttvom kii poorti krtaa hai। ek din mem km se km tiin se chaar baar naariyl piiem।
5. gnne kaa rs (Sugarcane Juice)
dihaaidreshn piile bukhaar kaa sbse khtrnaak lkshण hai। aise mem gnne kaa rs kmjor shriir ko sphoorti detaa hai। gnne ke rs se nirjlit shriir ke lie aavshyk vitaamin aur khnij kii aapoorti kii jaa sktii hai। gnne kaa rs shriir kii mmspeshiyom mem glookoj kii aapoorti krtaa hai। shriir mem aavshyk protiin kii kmii ko pooraa krne ke lie din mem tiin baar gnne ke rs kaa istemaal kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।yh bhii piile bukhaar se piid़it mriij kii uchch shriir ke taapmaan ko km kr detaa hai।
6. jau kaa paanii (Barley Water or Jau ka pani)
jau ek smpoorण anaaj hai jismem svsth jiivn shailii ke lie sbhii aavshyk poshk ttv hai maujood haim। jau mem vitaamin bii 1, bii 2, bii 5, 9 aur vitaamin ii hotaa hai। yh piile bukhaar se piiड़it mriij kii soojn aur shriir ke uchch taapmaan ko km krtaa hai। ek din mem tiin baar jau kaa paanii piine se piile bukhaar mem aaraam miltaa hai।
7. niimboo aur nmk (Lemon and Salt)
piile bukhaar se piiड़it vykti ko dihaaidreshn kii smsyaa ho jaatii hai। aise mem vykti aur jyaadaa thkaa huaa lgtaa hai। ek gilaas paanii mem niimboo ke rs kii kuchh boomde milaakr piine se bhii piile bukhaar mem kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai। is niimboo vaale paanii mem ek chutkii nmk bhii milaaem। yh paanii dihaaidreshn kii kmii ko pooraa krtaa hai aur rogii ko oorjaa detaa hai।


Disease: phaaileriyaa (Elephantiasis)

Description: 
phaaileriyaa rog, jise haathii pmv yaa phiil pmv bhii khte haim, (Elephantiasis) mem aksr haath yaa pair bhut jyaadaa sooj jaate haim। iske alaavaa phaaileriyaa rog se piid़it vykti ke kbhii haath, kbhii mdkosh, kbhii stn aadi yaa kbhii any mg bhii sooj skte haim। aam bolchaal kii bhaashaa mem haathiipmv (HathipaonHathipaon) bhii khaa jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- ek yaa j़yaadaa haath v pairom mem (j़yaadaatr pairom mem) soojn
- kॅpkॅpii ke saath bukhaar aanaa
- gle mem soojn aanaa
- guptmg evm jॉgho ke biich gilthii honaa tthaa drd rhnaa
- purooshom ke mdkosh mem soojn (haaidrosil) honaa
- pairom v haathom kii lsikaa vaahikaaem laal ho jaatii haim

Reasons: 
- jin kshetrom mem phaaileriyaa aam baat hotii hai un kshetrom mem jyaadaa smy tk rhne se smkrmण kaa khtraa bdh़ jaataa hai। ​

Treatments:
phaaileriyaa se bchaav (Treatment of Elephantiasis)
- mchchhrom se bchaav phaaileriyaa (Hathipaon) ko rokne kaa ek prmukh upaay hai। kyooleks mchchhr jiske kaarण phaaileriyaa kaa smkrmण phailtaa hai aam taur pr shaam aur subh ke vkt kaattaa hai। 
- kisii aise kshetr mem jhm phaaileriyaa phailaa huaa hai vhm khud ko mchchhr ke kaatne se bchaanaa chaahie। 
- aise kpड़e phnem jinse pm~v aur bmh poorii trh se dhk jaaem।
- aavshyktaa pd़e to permethrin yukt (permethrin ek aam simthetik raasaaynik kiitnaashk hotaa hai) kpd़om kaa upyog krem। baajaar mem permethrin yukt kpड़e milte haim।
- mchchhrom ko maarne ke lie kiit spre kaa chhiड़kaav krem।
- ilaaj biimaarii kii praarmbhik avsthaa mem hii shuroo ho jaanaa chaahie।

Home Remedies:
eliiphemtitis yaani shliipd jvr ek prjiivii ke kaarण phailtii hai jo ki mchchhr ke kaatne se shriir ke mdr prvesh krtaa hai। is biimaarii se mriij ke pair haathii ke pairom kii trh phool jaate haim। is rog ke hone se n kevl shaariirik viklmgtaa ho sktii hai blki mriijom kii maansik aur aarthik sthiti bhii bigड़ sktii hai। 
eliiphemtitis ko lsiikaa phaaileriyaa bhii khaa jaataa hai kyomki phaaileriyaa shriir kii lsikaa prणaalii ko prbhaavit krtaa hai। yh rog mnushyom ke haath- pairom ke saath hii jnnmgom ko bhii prbhaavit krtaa hai। phaaileriyaa ke upchaar ke lie yhm hm aapko kuchh ghreloo aur aayurvedik nuskhe btaa rhe haim, jinke istemaal se aap nishchy hii laabh uthaa paaemge।
1. laumg (Laung or Clove)- laumg phaaileriyaa ke upchaar ke lie bhut prbhaavii ghreloo nuskhaa hai। laumg mem maujood emjaaim prjiivii ke pnpte hii use khtm kr dete haim aur bhut hii prbhaavii triike se prjiivii ko rkt se nsht kr dete haim। rogii laumg se taiyaar chaay kaa sevn kr skte haim।
2. kaale akhrot kaa tel (Black walnut oil)- kaale akhrot ke tel ko ek kp grm paanii mem tiin se chaar boomde daalkr piem। is mitrण ko din mem do baar piyaa jaa sktaa hai। akhrot ke mdr maujood guणom se khoon mem maujood kiiड़om kii smkhyaa km hone lgtii hai aur dhiire dhiire ekdm khtm ho jaatii hai। jld priणaam ke lie km se km chhh hphte prtidin is upaay ko krem।
3. bhojn (Food)- phaaileriyaa ke ilaaj ke lie apne roj ke khaane mem kuchh aahaar jaise lhsun, anaanaas, miithe aaloo, shkrkmdii, gaajr aur khubaanii aadi shaamil krem। inmem vitaamin e hotaa hai aur baiktriiriyaa ko maarne ke lie vishesh guण bhii hote haim। 
4. mvlaa (Amla)- mvlaa mem vitaamin sii prchur maatraa mem hotaa hai। ismem enthelmimthimk (Anthelmintic) bhii hotaa hai jo ki ghaav ko jldii bhrne mem behd laabhprd hai। mvlaa ko roj khaane se imphekshn door rhtaa hai।
5. ashvgmdhaa (Ashwagandha)- ashvgmdhaa shilaajiit kaa mukhy hissaa hai, jiske aayurved mem bhut se upyog haim। ashvgmdhaa ko phaaileriyaa ke ilaaj ke lie bhii istemaal kiyaa jaataa hai।
6. braahmii (Brahmi)- braahmii puraane smy se hii bhut sii biimaariyom ke ilaaj ke lie istemaal kii jaatii hai। phaaileriyaa ke ilaaj ke lie braahmii ko piiskr uskaa lep lgaayaa jaataa hai। rojaanaa aisaa krne se rogii soojn km ho jaatii hai।
7. adrk (Ginger)- phaaileriyaa se nijaat ke lie sookhe adrk kaa paaudr yaa somth kaa roj grm paanii se sevn krem। iske sevn se shriir mem maujood prjiivii nsht hote haim aur mriij ko jldii thiik hone mem mdd miltii hai। 
8. shmkhpushpii (Shankhpushpi)- phaaileriyaa ke upchaar ke lie shmkhpushpii kii jड़ ko grm paanii ke saath piiskr pest taiyaar krem। is pest ko prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। isse soojn km hone mem mdd milegii।
9. kulthii (Kulthi)- kulthii yaa hॉrs graam (Horse Gram) mem chiimtiyom dvaaraa nikaalii gii mittii aur mde kii sphedii milaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। is lep ko prtidin prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem, soojn se aaraam milegaa।
10. agr (Agarwood)- agr ko paanii ke saath milaakr lep taiyaar krem। is lep ko prtidin 20 mint ke lie din mem do baar prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। isse ghaav jldii bhrte haim aur soojn km hotii hai। ghaav mem maujood baiktiiriyaa bhii mr jaate haim।
11. rॉk saalt (Rock Salt)- shmkhpushpii aur saumth ke paaudr mem rॉk saalt milaakr, ek ek chutkii roj do baar grm paanii ke saath lem।


Disease: apch (Indigestion)

Description:

Home Remedies:
indaaijeshn yaa apch kii smsyaa ko chikitsiiy bhaashaa mem daaysepsiyaa (Dyspepsia) khaa jaataa hai। apch kii smsyaa pet mem bhojn ko pchaane vaale rsom ke strvit n hone se hotii hai। yh smsyaa khaaskr bhut tej msaale vaalaa khaanaa yaa bhut tailiiy khaanaa khaane se hotii hai। ydi aap bhookh se jyaadaa khaa lete haim tb bhii aapko apch kii smsyaa ho sktii hai। 
apch ke dauraan vykti ko bhut jyaadaa gais, ultii, pet mem drd, siine yaa pet mem jln aadi smsyaaem ho sktii haim। apch se raaht ke lie kuchh ghreloo upaay laabhkaarii saabit hote haim। aaie jaante haim aise hii prbhaavii ghreloo nuskhom ke baare mem-
1. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)
seb ke sirke mem yoom to esidik guण hote haim lekin yh esid se raaht dene mem bhii prbhaavii hai। apch se raaht ke lie ek chmmch kchche aur anphiltrd seb ke sirke ko ek kp paanii mem milaaem। iske baad ismem ek chmmch kchchaa shhd milaaem। is pey ko din mem do se tiin baar piiem। apch se raaht milegii।
2. saumph (Saunf)
apch se bchaav ke lie saumph bhii behd guणkaarii hai। bhut msaaledaar aur vsaa vaale khaane se hone vaalii apch ko behd jldii thiik kr detii hai। apch se bchaav ke lie saumph ke daanom ko tve pr hlkaa saa grm krem aur uskaa paaudr bnaa lem। paanii ke saath is paaudr ko din mem do baar lem। saumph ke daanom se taiyaar chaay yaa saumph ko yoom hii mumh mem daalkr chbaane se bhii apch se raaht miltii hai। saath hii yh maauth phreshnr kii trh kaam bhii krtii hai।
3. adrk (Ginger)
adrk mem maujood paachn rs aur emjaaim khaane ko pchaane mem behd laabhkaarii haim। apch se raaht ke lie adrk ke chhote chhaate tukड़om pr nmk daalkr unhem yoom hii chbaayaa jaa sktaa hai। iske alaavaa do chmmch adrk ke rs mem niimboo kaa rs, thoड़aa saa kaalaa aur thoड़aa saa sphed nmk milaakr binaa paanii ke piine se behd raaht miltii hai। 
iske alaavaa adrk ke rs aur shhd ko gungune paanii ke saath bhii liyaa jaa sktaa hai। adrk kii chaay bhii behd laabhkaarii hotii hai। itnaa hii nhiim khaanaa bnaane mem adrk kaa pryog msaale ke taur pr krne se bhii adrk behd laabh detaa hai।
4. bekimg sodaa (Baking Soda)
apch se bchne ke lie bekimg sodaa sbse aasaan ghreloo upaay hai। aadhe gilaas paanii mem thodaa़ saa bekimg sodaa milaakr is paanii ko piiem। isse turmt raaht miltii hai।
5. ajvaayn (Ajwain)
ajvaayn pet ko duroost rkhne aur khaane ko pchaane ke saath hii pet drd se bhii raaht detii hai। saumth aur ajvaayn ko milaakr paaudr bnaaem। ek chmmch paaudr mem kaalii mirch milaaem aur grm paanii ke saath piiem। is pey ko din mem ek yaa do baar pii skte haim। ajvaayn ke daanom ko mumh mem rkhkr chbaane se bhii aaraam miltaa hai।
6. hrbl chaay (Herbal Tea)
pudiinaa yaa kaimomaail kii hrbl yaa griin tii bhii paachn shkti ko duroost rkhtii hai। khaanaa khaane ke baad ek kp hrbl tii piine se khaanaa jldii pchtaa hai aur pet mem vsaa bhii jmaa nhiim hotii। aise mem aapkaa vjn bhii thiik rhtaa hai। lekin khaane ke baad saamaany chaay yaa kॉphii se bchnaa chaahie। 
7. nmkiin chhaachh (Salted Buttermilk)
khaane ke saath nmkiin chhaachh kaa istemaal bhii aapkii paachn shkti ko bढ़aataa hai। raat ke smy dhii kii jgh chhaachh mem kaalaa nmk aur bhunaa huaa jiiraa daalkr piiem। pet mem jln se bhii raaht milegii। itnaa hii nhiim subh naashte mem aur dophr ke khaane mem bhii chhaachh kaa istemaal srvottm hai। grmiyom ke dinom mem yh pet ke saath hii poore shriir ke lie bhii phaaydemmd hai।


Disease: ghutnom kaa drd (Knee Pain)

Description: 
ghutnaa shriir kaa sbse bd़aa tthaa jtil jod़ hai। yh ek saaynoviyl jod़ (Sinovial Joint) kaa udaahrण haim। is jod़ mem mukhyt chaar hddiyom, lgbhg 15 mmspeshiyom ke alaavaa ek aur mhttvpoorण chiiज़ hotii hai jise kaartiilej (Cartilage) khte haim।

Symptoms: 
- ghutne kaa drd baaem, daaem yaa donom ghutnom mem ho sktaa hai।
- ghutne mem soojn ho jaatii hai aur chlte smy ghutne mem drd hotaa hai।
