- rogii ko baithne ke pshchaat uthkr khd़e hone mem kaaphii tkliiph hotii hai।
- smy gujrne ke saath-saath yh tiivr tthaa bhymkr drd kaa roop le letaa hai।
- hvaa chlne, thmd lgne, thmdii chiijem khaane, jaad़aa, grmii, brsaat aadi ke mausm mem yh rog bdh़ jaataa hai।

Reasons: 
- arthraaitis- riiyoometaaid, aastiyoarthraaitis aur gaaut shit athvaa smbmdhit ootk vikaar
- brsaaitis- ghutne pr baar-baar dbaav se soojn (jaise lmbe smy ke lie ghutne ke bl baithnaa, ghutne kaa adhik upyog krnaa athvaa ghutne mem chot)
- tentiinaaitis- aapke ghutne mem saamne kii or drd jo siidh़iyom athvaa chdh़aav pr chdh़te aur utrte smy bdh़ jaataa hai। yh dhaavkom, skॉyr aur saaikil chlaane vaalom ko hotaa hai।
- bekrs sist- ghutne ke piichhe paanii se bhraa soojn jiske saath arthraaitis jaise any kaarणom se soojn bhii ho sktii hai। ydi sist pht jaatii hai to aapke ghutne ke piichhe kaa drd niiche aapkii pimdlii tk jaa sktaa hai।
- ghisaa huaa kaartilej ghutne ke joड़ ke mdr kii or athvaa baahr kii or drd paidaa kr sktaa hai। 
- ghisaa huaa ligaamemt (e sii el tiyr)- ghutne mem drd aur asthaayitv utpnn kr sktaa hai।
- niikaip (Knee Cap) kaa visthaapn। 
- jhtkaa lgnaa athvaa moch- achaank athvaa apraakृtik dhmg se muड़ jaane ke kaarण ligaamemt mem maamoolii chot। 
- joड़ mem smkrmण (imphekshn)। 
- ghutne kii chot- aapke ghutne mem rkt sraav ho sktaa hai jisse drd adhik hotaa hai |
- shroणi vikaar (Pelvic Disorder)- yh drd utpnn kr sktaa hai jo ghutne mem mhsoos hotaa hai। udaahrण ke lie iliyotibiyl baimd simdrom ek aisii chot hai jo aapke shroणi se aapke ghutne ke baahr tk jaatii hai।
- motaapaa, jiske kaarण ghutnom pr adhik bojh pड़taa hai, jisse ghutne kaa kaartilej ghis jaataa hai। hddii ke sirom pr pड़ne vaalaa adhik dbaav is drd ko aur adhik bढ़aa detaa hai।

Treatments:
​​ghutnom ke drd se nijaat paane kaa sbse behtr upaay isse bchnaa maanaa jaataa hai। dॉktrom ke anusaar svsth jiivnshailii aur vjn ko niymtrण mem rkhkr is biimaarii se aasaanii se bchaa jaa sktaa hai। ghutnom ke drd se bchaav ke kuchh any upaay nimn haim:
- apnaa vjn niymtrit rkhem। 
- svimimg krnaa sbse phaaydemmd hai। 
- daud़ne se jyaadaa chlnaa achchhaa rhtaa hai। 
- jmgh kii mmspeshiyom se smbmdhit vyaayaam krem।
- phl v sbjiyom kaa bhrpoor sevn krem। inmem emtiiऑksiidemt bhrpoor maatraa mem hote haim। 
- ghutnom ko mod़kr nhiim baithnaa chaahie।  pet ko saaph rkhem tthaa kbj n hone dem। 
- ghutnom ke niiche athvaa biich mem ek tkiyaa rkhkr soem।
- din mem km se km 2 baar brph lgaaem।
- dॉktr se smy-smy pr jmch kraate rhem। 

Home Remedies:
ghutnom ke drd kii sbse bड़ii vjh hai ovrvet honaa। agr aapke shriir kaa vjn jyaadaa hai to jaahir hai aapkaa bhaar shne mem aapke ghutnom ko tkliiph hogii। iske alaavaa phijikl ektivitii km hone, kailshiym kii kmii hone yaa arthraaitis (arthritis) hone se bhii ghutnom mem drd rhtaa hai। mmspeshiyom mem tnaav rhne yaa kisii chot kii vjh se bhii ghutnom kaa drd aapko preshaan kr sktaa hai। 
aaie jaanem kuchh ghreloo upaay, jinhem apnaakr aap ghutnom ke drd se raaht paa skte haim।
1. thmdaa sek (Cold fomentation)
ghutnom ke drd se raaht ke lie thmdaa sek diyaa jaa sktaa hai। yh sbse aasaan aur prbhaavii triikom mem se ek hai। ghutnom ko thmdaa sek dene se yh rkt vaahikaaom ko kstaa hai jisse rkt prvaah km hotaa hai aur soojn bhii ghttii hai। 
kaise krem-
ek ptlii tauliyaa mem brph ke tukड़e lpet lem। 10 se 20 mint ke lie drd prbhaavit ghutne ke hisse ko sekem। aapkaa drd dhiire dhiire door ho jaaegaa। is upaay ko rojaanaa do yaa tiin baar kr skte haim।
2. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)
seb kaa sirkaa bhii ghutne ke drd ko km krne mem shaayk hai। ye ghutne ke joड़ ke bhiitr khnij ikththaa krtaa hai aur haanikaark vishaakt pdaarthom ko nsht krtaa hai।
kaise krem- 
do kp फ़iltrd paanii mem do chmmch seb kaa sirkaa milaaem। dinbhr mem yh ghol piiem। poorii trh thiik hone tk rojaanaa is tॉnik kaa sevn krem।
baaltii mem grm paanii daalkr usmem do kp seb kaa sirkaa milaakr 30 mint ke lie paanii mem prbhaavit ghutne bhigaakr baith jaaem। isse ghutnom ke drd mem kaaphii raaht milegii।
ek chmmch seb kaa sirkaa aur jaitoon ke tel ko braabr bhaagom mem milaakr ghutnom kii maalish krem, phaaydaa hogaa।
3. laal mirch (Red Chilli)
laal mirch ke istemaal se ghutnom ke drd mem bhii raaht miltii hai, ismem maujood kepsaaisin drd nivaark kii trh kaam krtaa hai।
kaise krem- 
ek se deढ़ kp tel mem do bड़e chmmch laal mirch paaudr daalkr ek pest taiyaar krem। km se km ek sptaah tk hr din do baar yh pest ghutnom pr lgaaem। ghutnom ke drd se raaht milegii।
ek kp seb ke sirke mem ek chauthaaii yaa aadhaa chmmch laal mirch paaudr daalkr mitrण taiyaar krem। is mitrण ko ghutnom pr lgaane se drd aur soojn km ho jaatii hai। jb tk ghutnom drd se raaht n ho tb tk hr din is pest ko 20 mint ke lie ghutnom pr lgaa skte haim। 
4. adrk (Ginger)
ghutne kaa drd mmspeshiyom mem tnaav kii vjh se ho yaa gthiyaa ke kaarण, adrk donom hii sthiti mem behd laabhprd hai। ismem emtii़phlemebl guण hote haim jo ghutne kii soojn aur drd ko km kr dete haim।
kaise krem-
ek kp paanii mem thoड़aa saa adrk kaa tukड़aa lekr 10 mint ubaal lem। iske baad isko thmdaa krke ismem thoड़aa saa niimboo kaa rs aur shhd milaaem। is ghol ko roj piiem। aap chaahem to adrk ke tel se ghutnom kii maalish bhii kr skte haim। 
5. hldii (Haldi)
hldii ghutne ke drd ko door krne ke lie ek prbhaavii aur praakृtik upchaar hai। hldii mem maujood kurkyoomin emtiiऑksiidemt kii trh kaam krtaa hai aur drd km krne mem mdd krtaa hai।
kaise krem-
ek kp paanii mem adrk aur hldii ko thoड़aa thoड़aa milaakr 10 mint ke lie ise ubaal lem। iske baad isko gungunaa hone ke baad shhd milaaem। din mem do baar ise piiem।
ek gilaas doodh mem hldii daalkr ubaalem aur usmem shhd milaakr piiem। isse bhii ghutnom kaa drd thiik hotaa hai।
not: 
* hldii rkt ko ptlaa krtii hai, aise mem khoon ptlaa (Blood Thinning) krne kii dvaa lene vaalom ke lie yh thiik nhiim।
* shhd ko bhut grm paanii yaa doodh mem nhiim milaanaa chaahie।
6. niimboo (Lemon)
niimboo bhii gthiyaa kii vjh se ghutne ke drd ke lie ek ghreloo laabhkaarii upaay hai। niimboo mem paayaa jaane vaalaa saaitrik esid (citric acid) gthiyaa mem yoorik esid kristl ko ghulaataa hai।
kaise krem-
ek niimboo chhote-chhote tukड़om mem kaatem। in tukड़om ko sootii kpड़e mem daalkr grm til ke tel mem dubaaem। iske baad pmch se 10 mint ke lie prbhaavit ghutne pr kpड़aa rkhem। ek din mem do baar aisaa krne se drd poorii trh chlaa jaataa hai।
ek gilaas paanii mem niimboo nichaaड़kr piine se bhii laabh hotaa hai।


Disease: kushthrog (Leprosy)

Description: 
kushthrog (Leprosy) maaikobaikteriym leprii (Mycobacterium Leprae) aur maaikobaikteriym leprometॉsis (Mycobacterium Lepromatosis) jiivaaणuom ke kaarण hone vaalii ek diirghkaalik biimaarii (Chronic Disease) hai। yh mukhy roop se maanv tvchaa (Skin), ooprii shvsn pth kii shleshmikaa (Mucous Membrane of Upper respiratory Track) , pridhiiy tmtrikaaom (Peripheral Nerves), mkhom aur shriir ke kuchh any kshetrom ko prbhaavit krtii hai। ydi kushthrog (Kushth Rog) kaa uchit smy pr upchaar n kiyaa jaaye to yh rog bढ़ sktaa hai, jisse tvchaa, nsom, haath-pairom aur mkhom mem sthaayii kshti ho sktii hai।

Symptoms: 
- chehre pr, nitmbom pr, shriir ke an‍y his‍som kii doosrii or bhut saare, nrm evm jinkii pribhaashaa n btaaii jaae aise laal v s‍prshkshm yaa s‍prshhiin dhb‍be ho jaanaa।
- t‍vchaa ke rmg tthaa gthn mem privrtn dikhaaii denaa ।
- t‍vchaa pr ek rmghiin daag jo thod़aa yaa poorii trh s‍prshhiin ho yaa us daag pr kisii chubhn kaa anubhv nhiim honaa।
- smaanyt t‍vchaa pr paaye jaane vaale piile yaa taamr rmg ke dhb‍be jo sun‍n hom yaa
- haath aur pairom kaa sun‍n ho jaanaa।

Reasons: 
- maaikobaikteriym leprii (Mycobacterium leprae) aur maaikobaikteriym leprometॉsis (Mycobacterium lepromatosis) jiivaaणu

Treatments:
- srkaarii asptaal dvaaraa rihaaishii ilaakom mem maujood svaasth kemdrom mem ni:shulk ilaaj uplbdh hai। 
- agr shriir pr ek se pmch dhbbe ho to chhh maah tk dvaaii lenii chaahie। 
- 6 se 12 dhbbe ho to 12 maah yaa isse adhik smt tk dvaaii lene se yh rog poorii trh se thiik ho jaataa hai। 

Home Remedies:
lepresii (Leprosy) yaani kushth rog se vykti n kevl shaariirik blki maansik roop se bhii prbhaavit hotaa hai। kushth rogiyom ke prti doosre logom ke asaamaany rvaiye se yh rogii niraash ho jaate haim। kushth rog shriir ke kisii bhii hisse mem ho sktaa hai। jis hisse pr bhii kushth rog kaa prbhaav hotaa hai vhm kii tvchaa dekhne mem smkrii sii njr aatii hai aur vh hissaa saamaany trh se kaam nhiim krtaa।
kii baar kushth rog se prbhaavit tvchaa sooj jaatii hai aur us sthaan pr laal chktte bhii pड़ skte haim। iske alaavaa prbhaavit hisse pr phphole jaisii tvchaa bhii ubhr sktii hai। kul milaakr kushth rogii behd preshaanii mhsoos krte haim। kushth rog ke upchaar ke lie kuchh ghreloo nuskhe haim, jinhem apnaakr kaaphii hd tk kushth rog ko thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai-
hldii (Turmeric)
hldii mem haaidekotaayl hotaa hai। hldii ko pttii pr lgaakr prbhaavii sthaan pr bmdhaa jaa sktaa hai। hldii se tvchaa kii soojn, rmjktaa aadi km ho jaatii hai kyomki yh mrhm kaa kaam krtii hai।
niim (Neem)
niim kii pttiyom kii piiskr lep ke roop mem pryog krem। niim mem baiktiiriyaa se chhutkaaraa paane ke lie uttm emtiiseptik ejemt hotaa hai। pttiyom ke lep ko ek din mem km se km do baar prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। behtr priणaam ke lie niim ke pest mem kaalii mirch kaa paaudr milaaem। iske alaavaa niim ke pttom ko paanii mem ubaalkr us paanii se nhaane se bhii aaraam miltaa hai।
eromaatherepii (Aromatherapy)
kushth rog ke ilaaj ke lie eromaatherepii bhii lii jaa sktii hai। is therepii mem vibhinn guणkaarii telom kaa istemaal hotaa hai jo ki shriir ke lie tॉnik kii trh kaam krtaa hai aur emtseptik ejemt ke roop mem bhii shriir ko phaaydaa phumchaate haim।
mmdookprणii yaa gotoo kolaa (Gotu kola or Centella Asiatica)
mmdookprणii yaa gotoo kolaa ko pryog bhut kii tvchaa smbmdhii bimaariyom se nijaat ke lie pryog kiyaa jaataa hai। shriir ke ghaav, jln aadi ke upchaar ke lie bhii gotoo kolaa kaa istemaal hotaa hai। gotoo kolaa ko sir drd aur bukhaar ke lie bhii istemaal kiyaa jaataa hai। gotoo kolaa ke pttom ko paanii mem tb tk ubaalem jb tk paanii aadhaa n ho jaae। iske baad is paanii ko chhaankr iskaa tiin chauthaaii hissaa rojaanaa din mem tiin baar piiem। kushth rog mem laabh hogaa।
raaijoms (Risomes)
raaijoms mem emtiiphmgl guण hote haim। raaijoms kaa svaad kड़vaa aur tej hotaa hai aur bhut tej mhk bhii hotii hai। kchchii raaijoms ko kushth rog ke upchaar ke lie istemaal krem।
baabchii (Babchi)
kushth rog ke ilaaj ke lie baabchii sbse asrkaark jd़ii-bootii maanii jaatii hai। baabchii ke biijom kaa paaudr bnaakr kushth rog ke ilaaj ke lie istemaal kiyaa jaataa hai। iske alaavaa baabchii ke pttom kaa pest bnaakr bhii prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se kushth rog mem aaraam miltaa hai। isse soojn km hotii hai aur vykti kaa rog thiik hone kii prkriyaa bhii tej hotii hai।
vhiit graas (Wheat Grass)
vhiit graas kushth rog ke ilaaj ke lie ek chmtkaarii prॉdkt hai। iske istemaal se ek raat mem hii rog mem aaraam mhsoos kiyaa jaa sktaa hai tthaa tiin mhiine ke lgaataar istemaal se lgbhg kushth ko thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। vhiit graas ko pest bnaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
kaalmograa kaa tel (Kalmogra Oil)
yh tel bhii kushth rog ke ilaaj mem behd laabhkaarii hai। kaalmograa ke tel mem niimboo kii kuchh boomde milaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr maalish krne se behd laabh hotaa hai। iske tel mem emtiibaiktiiriyl guण hote haim, jo ki ghaav ko tejii se bhrte haim aur baiktiiriyaa ko khtm krte haim।


Disease: agnaashyshoth (Pancreatitis)

Description: 
agnyaashyshoth (Pancreatitis) agnyaashy (Pancreas) mem soojn honaa hai। agnyaashy pet ke piichhe udr guhaa mem sthit ek mg hai, agnyaashy saamaany roop se chhotii mt mem paachn emjaaimom ko chhoड़taa hai। agr yh paachk emjaaim chhotii mt mem phum~chne se phle hii skriy ho jaate hai to yh agnyaashy ko nuksaan phum~chaa skte haim।

Symptoms: 
- aamtaur pr, hrdy kii gti aur sm~som kii dr donom bdh़ jaate haim।
- pet (udr) ke ooprii hisse mem tej drd honaa
- bukhaar aur dst
- mtlii aur ultii

Reasons: 
agnaashyshoth ke kaarण (Pancreatitis Causes)
- agnaashyshoth aksr pet kii smsyaaom ke kaarण hotaa hai। iske kuchh ahm kaarण nimn haim: 
- shraab kaa adhik sevn (sbse aam kaarण)
- pitt nlikaaom mem baadhaaem
- srjrii 
- kuchh vishesh dvaaiym~ lenaa
- ajञaat kaarण (lgbhg 15 % maamlom)
- oomchaa rkt mem traaiglisraaid ke str (hypertriglyceridemia)
- smkrmण (baiktiiriyl, vaayrl, phphoomd, yaa prjiivii)
- echaaiivii smkrmण
- agnyaashy kii jnmjaat asaamaanytaa
- iiaarsiipii kii uljhn (imdoskopik prtigaamii Cholangiopancreatography)
- aanuvmshiktaa
- estrojen
- slphonaamaaids
- tetraasaaiklin
- thiyaajaaids
- agnaashy ke kaimsr
haaiprlipidemiyaa (rkt vsaa kaa uchch str)
ati kailshiym rkttaa (rkt mem kailshiym ke uchch saamgrii)

Treatments:
- agnaashyshoth kaa upchaar agnaashyshoth (Pancreatitis) kii gmbhiirtaa pr nirbhr krtaa hai।
- saaph-sphaaii se rhem। 
- gmde paanii ke smprk mem aane se bchnaa hogaa।
- agnaashyshoth ke hone kaa aabhs hone pr turmt dॉktr ko dikhaae। 


Disease: maaigren (Migraine)

Description: 
maaigren sr mem hone vaale sbse tej drdom mem se ek hai। iskii vjh se sr aur kaan ke piichhe ke hisse mem ashniiy drd kaa anubhv hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- agr aapkaa vjn, bgair koshish kiye huye, pichhle 2 mhiinom mem, 5 kilograam se adhik ght gyaa hai
- agr sir mem drd hotaa hai aur baar-baar peshaab aataa hai to smjh lem ki aap maaiigren se piidi़t haim।
- aisaa bhii paayaa gyaa hai ki jb maaiigren kaa drd hotaa hai to v‍ykti ko chॉklet khaane kii prbl ichchhaa hotii hai, use lgtaa hai ki chॉklet khaakr uske sir kaa drd thiik ho jaaegaa।
- din bhr bevjh jm‍haaii aanaa bhii maaiigren kaa lkshण hai।
- photophobiyaa (prkaash ke prti atirikt smvednshiiltaa),
- phonophobiyaa (dhvni ke prti atirikt smvednshiiltaa),
- maaigren sirdrd se piid़it ek tihaaii logom ko ऑraa (Aura) ke maadhym se iskaa poorvaabhaas ho jaataa hai, ऑraa kisii bhii vs‍tu yaa v‍ykti ke aaspaas usii aakaar mem roshnii kaa dikhnaa, maaiigren kaa sbse phlaa lkshण hotaa hai। aisaa ahsaas drd ke dauraan 5 mint se 1 ghmte tk rhtaa hai।
- maaigren se grs‍t haim logom mem saains ke lkshण bhii njr aate haim। bhymkr sirdrd ke saath mkhom se paanii niklegaa yaa naak jaam hogii।
- maaiigren kaa drd hone pr niimd shii se nhiim aatii hai। thkaan mhsoos hotii hai pr niimd nhiim aatii।
- maaiigren ke dauraan piiड़it kii bhaavnaaem bhut tejii se bdltii haim। vh kbhii j‍yaadaa ugr aur kbhii j‍yaadaa shmt ho jaate hai।
- maaiigren mem drd ke dauraan mkhom mem bhii bhyaank drd hotaa hai। plkem jhpkaane mem bhii bhyaank jln hotii hai।
- srdrd ke saath mitlii, ultii aanaa,
- sir mem ek saaid hii drd shuroo hotaa hai।
- sir mem drd itnaa j‍yaadaa bdh़ jaataa hai ki grdn bhii dukhne lgtii hai।

Reasons: 
maaigren aksr tnaav ke kaarण hotaa hai। lekin kii any vjhem bhii hai jinkii vjh se maaigren ho sktaa hai jaise: 
maaigren hone ke  smbhaavit kaarण (Causes and Reason of Migraine Pain)
- tnaav ke kaarण maaigren kaa drd sbse jyaadaa hotaa hai।
- jo log din - raat kaam mem lge rhte hai yaa pdh़te rhte hai, unhem maaigren kii smsyaa sbse jyaadaa hotii hai।
- tej dhoop yaa thmdii hvaa mem bhii maaigren kaa drd uthtaa hai।
- maaigren kaa drd, taapmaan bdh़ne, adhik nmii vaale sthaanom pr jyaadaa jldii hotaa hai।
- haal hii mem hue kii adhyynom mem ptaa chlaa hai ki jo log kaiphiin kii jyaadaa maatraa lete hai unhem bhii maaigren kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
- lmbe smy tk tej myoojik sunne se bhii maaigren kaa ataik pd़ jaataa hai jisse uthne vaalaa drd 72 ghmte tk hotaa hai।
- riektiv haaipoglaaisiimiyaa (Reactive Hypoglycemia) se bhii maaigren kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
- ek din mem nau ghmte se jyaadaa niimd lene pr bhii maaigren kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
- ghmtom tk khaalii pet rhne ke kaarण gais kii smsyaa aur sir mem drd hone lgtaa hai।

Treatments:
- maaigren kaa sirdrd km krne ke lie ek sbse srl upchaar hai apne sir pr aais paik rkhem। aais paik mstishk mem rkt ke prvaah ko niymtrit krne mem mdd krtaa hai aur drd ko km kr detaa hai। prbhaavit kshetr, knptii aur grdn pr prbhaavii raaht ke lie aais paik ko dhiire-dhiire rgd़em।
- maaigren (Migraine) mem agr sir, grdn aur kmdhom kii maalish kii jaae to yh is drd se raaht dilaane mem bhut mddgaar saabit hotaa hai। iske lie hlkii khushboo vaale tel kaa pryog kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
- ek tauliye ko grm paanii mem dubaakr,us grm tauliye se drd vaale hissom kii maalish krem।
- kuchh logom ko thmde paanii se kii gii isii trh kii maalish se bhii aaraam miltaa hai। iske lie aap brph ke tukd़om kaa upyog bhii kr skte haim।
- maaigren yaa klstr sirdrd ataik ke dauraan log aksr seks krne se bchte haim lekin haaliyaa adhyyn mem jrmnii ke shodhkrtaaom ne paayaa ki maaigren se piid़it 60 phiisdii aur klstr sirdrd (sir ke ek trph drd) se piid़it 37 phiisdii logom ne sviikaar kiyaa ki drd se raaht paane mem seks ne unkii mdd kii hai। yh adhyyn 'siphaaljiyaa' naamk ptrikaa mem prkaashit huaa hai.

Home Remedies:
maaigren bhii ek trh kaa sir drd hai jo ki sir ke kisii ek hisse mem bhut tejii se hotaa hai। vykti ko sir drd hone pr kii baar ultii krne jaisaa bhii mhsoos hotaa hai। is trh ke sir drd mem mkhe laal ho jaatii haim kii baar sooj bhii jaatii haim। lekin chimtaa kii baat nhiim hai kyomki maaigren ke lie bhut se ghreloo nuskhe maujood haim jo ki maaigren se drd se raaht dene mem kaargr haim। aaie jaante haim ese hii ghreloo utpaadom aur unke prbhaavom ke baare mem-
1- laivemdr ऑyl (Lavender Oil)
laivemdr ऑyl saamaany sir drd aur maaigren drd ke lie ek upyogii ghreloo upaay hai। laivemdr tel kii khushboo maaigren mem behd prbhaavii hotii hai। grm paanii mem kuchh boomde laivemdr ऑyl kii daalkr use soomghne se behd aaraam miltaa hai। laivemdr ऑyl kaa pryog kbhii bhii maukhik roop se nhiim krnaa chaahie।
2-  peprmimt tel (Peppermint Oil)
pudiinaa sir ke tnaav ko km krne mem maahir aushdhi hai। iske tel kii tej mhk shriir mem rkt prvaah ko niymtrit krtii hai। maaigren yaa saamaany sir drd bhii aksr rkt prvaah ke km hone se hotaa hai aise mem peprmimt ऑyl rkt prvaah ko km krke sir drd ko thiik krtaa hai। is tel kii hlkii maatraa daayrekt maathe pr lgaa skte haim। jyaadaa n lgaaem anythaa jln bhii mhsoos ho sktii hai।
3-  tulsii kaa tel (Basil or Tulsi)
tulsii ke praakृtik guणom ko sbhii jaante haim lkin aapko btaa dem ki tulsii maaigren mem bhii behd prbhaavii hai। tulsii kaa tel kaa istemaal maaigren ke drd mem kaaphii aaraam detaa hai। tulsii kaa tel mmspeshiyom ko aaraam detaa hai jisse sir kaa tnaav km hotaa hai aur drd se raaht miltii hai।
4- phiks aahaar (Dedicated Diet)
sir drd ko km krne aur maaigren ke drd se raaht ke lie apne aahaar mem kuchh krne homge। maaigren ke drd se prbhaavit logom ko saadhaarण mkkhn kii jgh piint btr yaani moomgphlii se bnaa mkkhn istemaal krnaa chaahie। evokaido, kelaa aur khtte phl aadi kaa istemaal krnaa chaahie।
5-  sir kii maalish (Oil Massage)
sir ke drd ko km krne ke lie maalish bhii ek bhut prbhaavii triikaa hai। eksprts kii maanem to sir ke piichhe ke hisse kii maalish krne se maaigren se bhut raaht miltii hai। iske saath hii haath pairom kii maalish bhii kii jaanii chaahie। maalish krne se bhii rkt smchaar tej hotaa hai।
6- adrk (Ginger)
adrk sirdrd dauraan jii michlaane aur ultii kii anubhooti hone vaale lkshणom se raaht detaa hai।iske saath hii adrk se soojn aur drd bhii km hote haim। adrk mem maujood emtii phlemebl guण pershaanii paidaa krne vaale lkshणom ko rokte haim। adrk ke chhote se tukड़e ko dhokr, chhiilkr use paanii mem ubaalkr, thmdjञ kr lem। is paanii mem shhd aur niimboo kii kuchh boomdem milaakr piine se behd laabh miltaa hai।
7- kॉफ़ii (Coffee)
kii logom ko tej maaigren ke drd mem kॉphii piine se bhii turmt raaht ho jaatii hai। kॉphii mem maujood kaiphiin maaigren tiृgr kii trh kaam krtaa hai aur edenosaain ke prbhaav ko km kr detaa hai। haalmki bhut jyaadaa kaiphiinyukt pdaarth bhii seht ke lie nuksaandaayk hote haim lekin ek kp kॉphii aapke svaasthy ko laabh phumchaatii hai।
8- dhniyaa (Coriander or Dhania)
dhniyaa khaane ko pchaane aur svaadisht bnaane ke lie behriin msaale ke roop mem jaanaa jaataa hai, lekin praachiin kaal se dhniye kaa pryog maaigren aur sir drd kii dvaa ke roop mem bhii kiyaa jaataa hai। maaigren mem dhniyaa ke biijom se taiyaar kii gii chaay beh laabhkaarii hotii hai। dhniyaa ke kuchh biijom ko grm paanii mem 10 mint ubaalem, uske baad ismem svaadaanusaar chiinii milaakr piem। dhniyaa vaalii chaay maaigren ke drd ke saath-saath saamaany sir drd mem bhii laabhkaarii hai।


Disease: nimoniyaa (Pneumonia)

Description: 
kisii ek biimaarii se hmaare desh mem itnii mautem nhiim hotiim jitnii nimoniyaa (Pneumonia ) se hotii haim। nimoniyaa se bchaav aur iskaa ilaaj behd sugm hai lekin aksr logom ke paas iske juड़ii jaankaarii nhiim hotii। jaanie nimoniyaa ke vishy mem sbhii baatem।

Symptoms: 
- chhote yaa nvjaat bchchom mem koii vishesh lkshण dikhaaii nhiim detaa hai।
- bchche dekhne se biimaar lgem to unhem nimoniyaa ho sktaa hai।
- srdii,  haaii phiivr,  kph,  kmpkpii,  shriir mem drd,  sir drd,  mmspeshiyom mem drd।

Reasons: 
nimoniyaa ke kaarण (Pneumonia Causes)
- baiktiiriyaa
- vaayrs
- phmgs
- iske atirikt kuchh rsaaynom aur phephd़e mem lgii chot ke kaarण bhii nimoniyaa hotaa hai।

Treatments:
- rogii ko ek svchchh kmre mem rkhem। is baat kaa dhyaan rkhe ki rogii ke kmre mem soory kaa prkaash avshy aaye।
- shriir, khaaskr chhaatii aur pairom, ko grm rkhne ke lie kmre ko grm rkhem tthaa rogii ko achchhii trh se dhkem।
- siine mem drd aur bechainii se raaht paane ke lie, ek chmmch lhsun kaa rs le skte haim ।
- tulsii bhii nimoniyaa mem bhut upyogii hai। tulsii ke kuchh taaje pttom kaa rs lekr usmem kaalii mirch piis kr milaa lem aur yh rs hr chhh ghmte ke mtraal pr dem ।
- adhikmshth: nimoniyaa (Pneumonia) kaa ilaaj, dॉktr kii dekh rekh mem, binaa asptaal mem daakhil hue ho sktaa hai।
- aamtaur pr, maukhik emtiibaayotik dvaaom, aaraam, trl pey pdaarth, aur ghr pr dekhbhaal poorण svaasthy laabh ke lie pryaapt haim। 

Home Remedies:
bhaart vrsh mem nimoniyaa (Pneumonia), kisii any biimaarii ke mukaable, mृtyu kaa sbse bड़aa kaarण hai। 
nimoniyaa moolth phephड़o (Lungs) mem smkrmण hone se hotaa hai। 
phle se biimaar logom kii prtirkshaa prणaalii (Immune System) phle se hii kmjor hotii hai islie svsth logom ke mukaable unhem nimoniyaa hone kii smbhaavnaa adhik hotii hai।  
nimoniyaa ke ghreloo upchaar  (Home Remedies For Pneumonia)
- hldii, kaalii mirch, methii aur adrk jaise prtidin upyog mem aane vaale khaady prdaarth phephd़om ke lie phaaydemmd hote haim। 
- til ke biij bhii nimoniyaa ke upchaar mem shaayk hote haim। 300 miliiliitr paanii mem 15 graam til ke biij, ek chutkii saadhaarण nmk, ek chmmch
- alsii aur ek chmmch shhd milkr prtidin upyog krne se phephd़om se kph baahr nikltaa hai। 
- taajaa adrk kaa rs lene yaa adrk ko choosne se bhii nimoniyaa mem aaraam miltaa hai।        
- thoड़e se gungune paanii ke saath shhd lenaa bhii laabhdaayk rhtaa hai।  
- grm taarpiin tel kaa aur kpoor ke mishrण se chhaatii pr maalish krne se nimoniyaa se raaht miltii hai। 
- rogii kaa kmraa svchchh, aur grm honaa chaahie। kmre mem soory kii raushnii avshy aanii chaahiye।  
- rogii ke shriir ko grm rkhem, visheshkr chhaatii aur pairom ko।  
- tulsii bhii nimoniyaa mem bhut upyogii hai। tulsii ke kuchh taaje pttom kaa rs, ek chutkii kaalii mirch mem milkr rkh lem aur hr chh ghmte ke baad dem।  


Disease: enoreksiyaa (Anorexia)

Description: 
bhookh n lgne ko medikl bhaashaa mem enoreksiyaa (Anorexia) yaa aruchi rog khte haim। enoreksiyaa (Anorexia) yaa aruchi rog mem rogii ko bhookh nhiim lgtii, ydi jbrdstii bhojn kiyaa bhii jaay to vh aruchikr lgtaa hai। is rog se piiड़it vykti 1 yaa 2 graas se jyaadaa nhiim khaa paataa aur use binaa kuchh khaaye -piye hii khttii dkaarem aane lgtii haim।

Symptoms: 
- km khaane pr bhii pet bhraa prtiit honaa
- kisii kaary ko krne kii ichchhaa nhiim honaa
- khaanaa khaane kii ichchhaa n honaa
- khoon kii kmii honaa
- chehraa kmtihiin evm kaalaa pड़ jaanaa
- jyaadaa pyaas lgnaa
- thodii saa kaam krne pr thkaan honaa
- maansik ashmti se grst honaa
- mum~h mem grmii evm mum~h se bdboo aanaa
- shriir ke vjn mem din-b-din kmii hote jaanaa
- sookhii dkaarem aanaa
- hृdy ke smiip lgaataar jln honaa

Reasons: 
enoreksiyaa ke shaariirik kaarणom (Physical Reason of Hunger Disorder): 
- paachn tmtr mem gd़bd़ii hone ke kaarण jiibh mem kisii bhii prkaar kaa svaad n honaa
- bukhaar honaa, vishm jvr (mleriyaa) ke baad
- jigr tthaa aamaashy kii khraabii
- pet saaph n rhnaa yaanii kbj honaa
- aniymit dhmg se aahaar krnaa
- der tk jaagnaa, subh der se uthnaa
- bhojn kaa svaadisht n honaa
- bhookh km krne vaale aahaar kaa sevn
- chaay-kॉphii kaa adhik sevn krnaa, aadi

Treatments:
- gehoom ke chokr mem semdhaa nmk aur ajvaayn milaakr rotii bnaakr khaane se bhookh tej hotii hai।
- ek seb yaa seb ke rs ke prtidin sevn se khoon saaph hotaa hai aur bhookh bhii lgtii hai।
- ek gilaas paanii mem jiiraa, hiimg, pudiinaa, kaaliimirch aur nmk daalkr piine se aruchi door hotii hai।
- prtidin methii mem chhaumkii gii daal yaa sbज़ii ke sevn se bhookh bढ़tii hai।
- niimboo ko kaatkr ismem semdhaa nmk daalkr bhojn se phle choosne se kbj door hokr paachnkriyaa tej ho jaatii hai।

Home Remedies:
bhojn mem aruchi ko enoreksiyaa (Anorexia Nervosa) bhii khte haim। kii logom ko apne vjn aur phitnes kii itnii chimtaa ho jaatii hai ki vo haarsh daaytimg krne lgte haim aur phir shuru ho jaatii hai enoreksiyaa kii biimaarii। ismem shriir kaa vjn kaaphii km ho jaataa hai। shriir mem hddii aur mmspeshiyom pr kii jmii vsaa lgaataar bhookhe rhne se jlne lgtii hai aur shriir mem sirph hddii kaa dh़mchaa hii shesh rh jaataa hai।
enoreksiyaa kii biimaarii khaaskr mॉdlimg aur phaishn imdstrii mem kaam kr rhii km umr kii ld़kiyom mem jyaadaa hotaa hai, kyomki unhem smaart aur phit dikhne ke lie 'jiiro phiigr' jaisii kaayaa bnaanii pd़tii hai। lekin baad mem yhii jiiro phiigr unke lie jaanlevaa bn jaatii hai।
enoreksiyaa biimaarii ke baad n aapko bhookh lgtii hai aur n hii kisii chiij mem ruchi। is biimaarii ke baad aap khud ko bhaavnaatmk, mnovaijञaanik, saamaajik aur shaariirik rup se itnaa asurkshit mhsoos krne lgte haim ki aapmem khudkushii krne tk kii bhaavnaa prbl ho jaatii hai।
enoreksiyaa kaa ydi shii smy pr ilaaj nhiim ho to iske kaaphii gmbhiir priणaam hote haim, msln- haart kii biimaarii, shriir mem ilektrolaaits kaa asmtuln, jaanlevaa eniimiyaa, kidnii khraab hone se jaan tk jaa sktii hai। aksr kii logom ko ptaa hii nhiim chltaa hai ki unhem enoreksiyaa kii biimaarii hai। agr yh ptaa chl jaae to kii ghreloo upchaar aur mnauvaijञaanik upchaar se iskaa ilaaj smbhv hai। khaaskr ghreloo upchaar se mriijom mem khaane ke  prti ruchi to paidaa kii hii jaatii hai।
enoreksiyaa ke ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies for Anorexia)
lhsun  (Garlic)
lhsun bhookh jgaane kii sbse kaargr ghreloo upaay hai। ise khaane ke baad ek khaas trh ke emjaaim kaa sraav hotaa hai jo bhookh jgaataa hai aur paachn kriyaa ko mjboot krtaa hai। roj subh kchche lhsun ke tiin aur chaar daane ek kp paanii ke saath khaa lem। agr kchchaa lhsun khaane mem kd़vaa lgtaa hai to use ubaal kr usmem nmk aur niimboo ke rs milaa kr bhii khaa skte haim।
adrk (Ginger)
bhookh jgaane ke lie aap aadhaa chmmch kte hue adrk kaalaa nmk ke saath khaanaa khaane se aadhaa ghmte phle khaaem, kaaphii kaam kregaa। ise istemaal krem। aap khaane ko naa nhiim kr skte haim ise lene ke baad। aap adrk ke chaay kaa bhii sevn kr sktii haim।
smtraa (Orange)
smtrom mem bhii bhookh jgaane kii kshmtaa hotii hai। smtraa n sirph aapke paachn tmtr ko thiik krtaa hai blki isse kbj bhii door hotaa hai। ise jb mn kre chaar-chhh phmk chhiilkr khaate rhem। ise kaale nmk, niimboo ke rs ke saath bhii khaa sktii haim yaa phir joos bhii pii skte haim।
mimt (Mint)
mimt bhookh lgaane kii kudrtii dvaa hai। enoreksiyaa ke ilaaj mem ise aajmaayaa jaa sktaa hai। iske svaad aur khaas sugmdh ke kaarण bhookh kii ichchhaa jgtii hai। ise khaane se dipreshn aur tnaav bhii km hogii। do chmmch mimt ke ptte se nikaale joos roj subh piiem yaa phir mimt se bnii chaay bhii pii sktii haim।
lemn baam (Lemon Balm)
yh nrv tॉnik kii trh kaam krtaa hai aur isse bhookh bhii lgtii hai। ise khaane se tnaav km hotaa hai aur niimd bhii achchhii aatii hai। ek chmmch lemn baam kii sookhii pttiyom ko ek kp grm paanii mem daalem aur ise thod़ii der dh़mk dem। thmdhaa hone pr ise chaay kii trh piiem। kaaphii kaam kregaa।
hrbl chaay (Herbal Tea)
hrbl chaay yaa griin tii aur kii trh ke jd़ii-bootiyom ko milaa kr bnii chaay piine se bhookh jgtii hai। tnaav aur dipreshn km hotii hai। enoreksiyaa mem hrbl tii piine kii slaah dii jaatii hai।
msaaj (Massage)
msaaj therepii sirph tnaav aur dipreshn hii nhiim door krtii hai blki isse bhookh bhii lgtii hai। medikl jrnl mem enoreksiyaa ke ilaaj mem msaaj therepii ko bhii mediisin ke rup mem shaamil kiyaa gyaa hai। kisii spaa mem jaakr hrbl msaaj tremd msaajr se lem, kaaphii phaaydaa kregaa।
yog (Yoga)
enoreksiyaa biimaarii se paidaa huii bhaavnaatmk asurkshaa ko door bhgaataa hai yog। yog mem aise kii aasn haim khaaskr- kpotaasn(kbootr ke smaan), shlbhaasn। ise krne se aap bhut jld thiik ho sktii haim।
ekyoopmkchr aur ekyoopreshr (Acupuncture and Acupressure)
ekyoopmkchr aur ekyoopreshr  donom kii mdd se enoreksiyaa se ld़ii jaa sktii hai। ise aajmaane se aapko achchhaa anubhv hogaa aur rilaiks mhsoos kremge। kisii khaas nrv pr ekyoopmkchr yaa ekyoopreshr krne se bhookh bhii lgne lgtii hai।
dhyaan (Meditation)
mn kii ashmti enoreksiyaa kaa khaas lkshण hai। ise bhgaane ke lie subh-shaam dhyaan krem। mn aur aatmaa ko shmti milegii aur mn mem skaaraatmk vichaar aaemge।
aur bhii haim kii tips (Some more tips)
niymit rup mem grup therepii mem shaamil ho।
apnaa ek daait plaan bnaaem aur is pr aml krem, isse bhaage nhiim।
subh nishchit rup se naashtaa krem, ise apnii aadt mem shaamil krem।
hrii sbjiyom aur hre saag ke soop bnaa kr piiem।
bhookh jgaane ke lie msaaledaar bhojn khaanaa shuru krem।


Disease: drd (Pain)

Description: 
drd yaa piid़aa (About Pain in Hindi)

Reasons: 
drd ke kii kaarण hote haim jaise  chot lgnaa, pooraanii biimaarii aadi। drd (dard) ke kuchh vishesh kaarण nimn haim: 
- kaimsr
- kaan mem smkrmण
- achaank biimaarii
- mmspeshii kii chot
- jlnaa
- puraanaa drd poorv kii kisii chot yaa shaariirik nuksaan mem bhii hotaa hai

Treatments:
​drd hone pr sbse aasaan upaay log drd nivaark lenaa smjhte haim। kii baar drd nivaark bhii poorण roop se drd khtm nhiim kr paataa। drd kii sthiti mem kuchh nimn upaay apnaae jaa skte haim।
- drd ke nidaan evm upchaar (Diagnosis and Treatment) kaa uddeshy rogii kii kaaryprणaalii mem sudhaar krnaa hai jisse ve apne dainik kaam kr skem।
- chot yaa jod़om ke drd mem raaht ke lie thmdaa yaa grm semk krnaa aasaan upaay maanaa jaataa hai।
- thmdaa semk - brph hmaare shriir kii rkt vaahikaaom ko sikod़ detii hai। jisse hmem drd v jln se hmem chhutkaaraa milne ke saath hii chot thiik ho jaatii hai। thmdaa semk kevl taajaa chot ke smy hii krnaa chaahie। ydi chot lge 6-7 ghmte ho chuke haim to thmde semk se bchnaa chaahie। liil pd़ne se rokne v jod़om mem khoon ko iktthaa hone se rokne ke lie thmdaa semk kiyaa jaataa hai।
- grm semk - grmii se nsom mem rkt prvaah tej ho jaataa hai jisse akd़ii huii mmspeshiym dhiilii hone lgtii haim aur drd mem aaraam miltaa hai।
- grm paanii kaa semk bhut adhik srdii ke mausm mem krnaa phaaydemmd hotaa hai। grmii ke mausm mem grm semk nhiim krnaa chaahie। srdii ke mausm mem jod़om pr sthit nsem sikud़ne lgtii haim। aise mem grm paanii ke semk se drd paidaa krne vaale oottk aur nsem khul jaatii haim।
- gmbhiir chotom mem grm semk n lem। yh chot mem ho rhii jln ko aur bdh़aa sktaa hai। aise mem us chot ko thiik hone mem jyaadaa smy bhii lg sktaa hai

Home Remedies:
drd se nijaat paane ke lie hmeshaa pen kilr dvaa khaanaa thiik nhiim haim। pen kilr dvaaom ke strip pr bhii likhaa hotaa hai ki iske ovrdoj seht ke lie nuksaandeh hote haim। drd nivaark dvaaom ke ovrdoj se liivr aur kidnii pr buraa asr pd़taa hai aur adhik sevn se liivr aur kidnii khraab ho sktii hai।
drd mem jyaadaatr pryaas krnaa chaahie ki hm kudrtii aur ghreloo upaay se hii ise km krem। drd se nijaat ke lie kudrt mem aisii naayaab jd़ii-bootii aur aushdhiym hai jo drd ko n sirph km krtii hai blki jd़ se hii khtm kr detii haim।
drd ke ghreloo ilaaj (Home Remedies for Pain)
kmr drd (Pain in Waist)
raat mem 60 graam gemhoo ke daane paanii mem bhigo dem। subh mem bhiige hue gemhoo ke saath 30 graam khskhs tthaa 30 graam dhniyaa milaakr baariik piis lem। is chtnii ke doodh mem pkaa le aur khiir bnaa lem। is khiir ko lgaataar do mhiine tk khaane se kmr drd kaa naash ho jaataa hai। kevl khskhs auऱ mishrii ko braabr maatraa mem piis kr choorण bnaa lem aur ise roj khaaem, kmr drd gaayb ho jaaegii।
kmr drd mem taarpiin ke tel kii maalish bhii bhut laabhdaayk hotii hai।
kmr drd aur gthiyaa mem nity subh akhrot kii giriyom ko achchhii trh chbaakr khaane se bhii kaaphii laabh hotaa hai।
ghutnom kaa drd (Knee Pain)
subh ke smy methiidaanaa kaa baariik choorण ek yaa do chmmch paanii ke saath lem, ghutnom kaa drd khtm ho jaaegaa।
mchhlii ke tel (k़ॉd liivr ऑyl) bhii ghutnom ke drd mem kaaphii asrdaar hai।
subh bhookhe pet akhrot kii giriym khaaem। drd se nijaat milegaa।
ghutnom kaa drd, jod़om kaa drd hddiyom ko ghisne ke kaaण hotii hai। ismem vijysaar kii lkd़ii ke vidhivt istemaal se kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai।
ek kchchaa lhsun khaalii pet paanii ke saath khaaem, drd se nijaat milegaa।
ashvgmdhaa aur saumth ko kootkr iske choorण ko khaaem, kaaphii aaraam milegaa।
gthiyaa (Arthritis Pain)
bthuaa saag ke taajaa pttom kaa rs 15 graam prtidin piine se gthiyaa door hotaa hai। is rs mem nmk-chiinii aadi kuchh n milaaem। subh khaalii pet lem aur shaam mem bhii।
bthuaa kaa saag bnaa ke bhii khaa skte haim aur iske praathe bhii bnaa kr khaa skte haim।
naagaurii asgmdh kii jd aur khmd donom lgbhg braabr maatraa mem lekr koot-piiskr kpd़e se chhaan kr baariik choorण bnaa lem । ise subh-shaam grm doodh ke saath khaaem। gthiye ke drd se raaht milegii।
kchche lhsun kaa sevn krem।
baariik asgmdhaa kaa choorण do bhaag, saumth kaa choorण ek bhaag aur pisii huii mishrii tiin bhaag milaa kr rkh lem। ise do chmmch subh-shaam grm doodh yaa paanii ke saath khaaem, drd gaayb ho jaaegaa।
hr prkaar ke bdn kaa drd (All type of Pain)
lhsun kii chaar kliym chhiilkr tiis graam srsom ke tel mem daal dem। usmem thod़ii ajvaayn milaa kr dhiimii mch pr pkaaem। lhsun aur ajvaayn kaalii pd़ne pr tel utaar kr thod़aa thmdhaa kr chhaan lem। is hlke grm tel kii maalish se hr prkaar kaa bdn drd chhoo-mmtr ho jaataa hai।
lgbhg 10 graam kpoor aur 200 graam srsom kaa tel- donom ko shiishii mem milaa kr kaark se bmd kr dem। shiishii ko dhoop mem rkh dem। jb donom milkr ekrs ho jaaem tb is tel kii maalish se vaat vikaar, nsom kaa drd, piith aur kmr kaa drd, hip-shool, mmspeshiyom kaa drd smet bdn ke sbhii trh ke drd se chhutkaaraa mil jaataa hai।
pet drd (Abdominal Pain)
ajvaayn kaa choorण chhh bhaag aur kaalaa nmk (pisaa huaa) ek bhaag lekr milaa lem। ismem se do graam grm paanii ke saath lem to pet drd mem turmt aaraam milegaa।
amृtdhaaraa kii do-tiin boomde btaashe yaa khmd ke paanii mem daalkr piine se pet drd khtm hotaa hai।
do-tiin chmmch thmdhe paanii mem do-tiin boomd amृtdhaaraa subh-shaam bhojn ke baad lene se dst, mv, mrod़ aur pechish ke drd mem aaraam miltaa hai।
gle kaa drd (Pain in Throat)
phoolii phitkrii do graam (aadhaa chmmch) 250 milii paanii mem daal kr din mem do-tiin baar graaraa krem। isse gle kii soojn auऱ drd door hotii hai। yh smbhv nhiim hai to kevl nmk aur ekh glaas grm paanii mem daal kr graare krne se bhii drd km hotii hai।
dmt kaa drd (Pain in Teeth and Gum)
srsom ke tel kii kuchh boomdom mem ek chutkii saimdhaa nmk ke saath ek chutkii pisii huii hldii milaa lii jaae aur gaadh़aa lep (pest) bnaakr dmto v msood़om kii maalish rojaanaa sbuh-shaam kii jaae to dmto ke drd ke saath kii tkliiphem door ho jaaemgii।
bhiitrii chot yaa hddii tootne pr drd (Internal Pain and Inflamation)
200 graam ublte hue doodh mem aadhaa chmmch hldii milaa kr do-tiin baar ubaal dem। is hldii aur doodh ke gungune mishrण ko piine se chot kaa drd v soojn km hotii hai।
ydi kisii jgh chot ke kaarण soojn ho yaa drd ho to vhm pisaa huaa semdhaa nmk yaa saadhaarण nmk kii potlii ko grm kr semkne se soojn aur drd km hotii hai।
jhm chot lgii hai, moch aaii hai yaa soojn hai vhm hldii kaa choorण aur choonaa milaa kr lgaa diyaa jaae to phaurn drd thiik ho jaatii hai aur soojn bhii km ho jaatii  hai।


Disease: anidraa (Insomnia)

Description: 
achchhii niimd achchhe svaasthy ke lie behd ज़rurii bhii hai। aisaa khaa jaataa hai "If you cannot sleep, you cannot heal", yaani agr aap soemge nhiim to aap shii nhiim ho paaemge। niimd shriir ke lie aaraam krne kaa sbse behtriin triikaa hai। aaiem smjhem apnii niimd ko kriib se।

Reasons: 
anidraa kii mukhy vjh temshn aur tnaav ko maanaa jaataa hai। lekin anidraa ke kii any kaarण bhii ho skte haim jo shaariirik yaa maansik yaa donom trh ke ho skte haim। aaiyem jaanem anidraa kii kuchh khaas vjhom ko: 

Treatments:
niimd aane kii smsyaa se nijaat paane ke lie aksr log niimd kii goliyom kaa sevn krte haim jo shii chiij nhiim maanii jaatii। niimd naa aane (Sleep Disorder) kii ek mukhy vjh tnaav bhii ho sktaa hai। achchhii niimd paane ke lie kuchh upaay nimn haim:
- shaariirik prishrm shriir ko thkaataa hai aur aaraam kii jroort bdh़aataa hai। ath niymit khelkood yaa thlnaa hmaare lie laabhdaayk hai, isse shriir chust rhtaa hai aur thkaan hone ke kaarण niimd achchhii aatii hai।
- bistr evm shyn kksh aaraamdaayk ho, bhut thmdaa yaa grm n ho। is baat kaa dhyaan rkhem ki gddaa aapke lie upyukt ho। 
- sone se phle dhiimaa smgiit bhii shriir ko aaraam detaa hai aur sone mem mdd detaa hai। 
- sote smy sir ke niiche chhotaa tkiyaa rkhem। ek tkiyaa apne ghutnom ke niiche aur doosraa apne ghutne aur jmgh ke biich rkhem। isse shriir kaa vjn nichle hisse kii or aaegaa aur aap aaraam se so skemge।
- sone se ek ghmtaa phle kmre kii laait hlkii kr lem।
- sote smy achchhii aur skaaraatmk baatem sochem।
- raat mem sone se phle doodh piem, jisse achchhii niimd aaegii। chaay-kॉphii kii maatraa ko siimit krem aur din bhr mem do-tiin baar se jyaadaa inkaa sevn n krem।
- smy pr sone aur jaagne kii aadt daalem।
- achchhe dost bnaaem। akelepn se door rhem।
- ydi koii chiiज़ aapko preshaan kr rhii hai aur aap uske baare mem shii triike se nhiim soch paa rhe hom to apnii smsyaa ko sone se phle kaagज़ pr likh lem aur svym se khem ki kl aap is smsyaa se niptemge। 
- agr aap so nhiim paate haim to uth jaaem aur kuchh aisaa krem jisse aapko hlkaa mhsoos ho, jaise – pdh़naa, tiivii dekhnaa yaa hlkaa smgiit sunnaa aur jb aap thkaan mhsoos krem to phir se sone jaaem। 

Home Remedies:
agr sonaa aapke lie jrurii kaam bn jaae to smjhie kuchh gd़bd़ii hai। anidaa aam kaamkaajii bhaartiiyom kii shikaayt bntii jaa rhii hai। imsomeniyaa koii biimaarii nhiim blki khraab jiivnshailii se utpnn huii niimd smbmdhii smsyaa hai। imsomemniyaa agr lmbe smy tk rhe to yh gmbhiir biimaarii kaa rup le sktii hai।
dॉktr khte haim ki behtr svaasthy aur jimdgii ke lie ek aam imsaan ko 7 se 8 ghmte avshy sonaa chaahie। lekin naukr-dhmdhe kaa preshr, vyst dinchryaa aur aage bhaagne kii hod़ mem hm niimd ko hii bhool jaate haim। baad mem jb niimd kaaphii staane lgtii hai to hm sliipimg pils (Sleeping Pills) lene lgte haim। lekin sliipimg pils lene se behtr hai ki hm kuchh aise aasaan ghreloo ilaaj krem jisse shriir kii thkaavt door ho aur hmem behtr niimd mil ske।
anidaa ko bhgaane ke ghreloo ilaaj (Home Remedies for Insomenia)
hrii saag aur sbjii jyaadaa maatraa mem khaaem (Eat green vegetables more)
hrii saag aur sbjii shriir ke lie hii nhiim niimd ke lie bhii jrurii hai। khaaskr jin saagom ke ptte bd़e hom aur usmem lislisaapn ho to yh niimd aane mem kaaphii mdd krtaa hai। poro aur paalk ke saag niymit rup se khaaem, isse behtr niimd aaegii।
maigniishiym aur kailshiym (Magnesium and calcium)
maigniishiym aur kailshiym donom ko hii niimd bdh़aane vaalii kemikl khii jaatii hai। jb yh donom saath mem lii jaae to aur asrdaar hotii hai। maigniishiym khaane se dil kii biimaarii kaa khtraa bhii km ho jaataa hai। raat mem 200 Mg maigniishiym(jyaadaa maatraa n lem, daayriyaa ho sktaa hai) aur 600 mg  kailshiym nishchit rup se khaaem, behtr niimd aaegii।
jmglii slaad pttaa yaa kaahoo (Wild Lettuce)
agr aapko teshn, sirdrd, mmspeshiyom aur jod़om ke drd kii shikaayt rhtii hogii to aap jmglii slaad pttaa ko jrur jaante homgem। yh shriir kii thkaavt, dipreshn aur anidaa mem bhii kaaphii asrdaar hotii hai। sone se phle ise pairom mem 30 se 120 milii graam lgaa lem, thkaavt gaayb ho jaaegii aur chain kii niimd aa jaaegii।
hॉps (Hops)
yh ek prkaar kaa jmglii paudhaa hai jiske phl kaa upyog shraab (biiyr) bnaane ke kaam mem aataa hai। anidaa, temshn aur diprethn ke mriijom ko iske phl kaa rs pilaaii jaatii hai taaki unhem aaraam kii niimd aa ske।
eromaatherepii (Aromatherapy)
sugmdh kaa mstishk se ghraa smbdh hai। bhut saare log apne bed pr tkie ke niiche chmelii ke phool rkh kr sote haim। kii log apne baalknii mem rjniigmdhaa yaa isii trh ke sugmdhit phoolom ke paudhe lgaa kr rkhte haim taaki iske sugmdh se raat mem behtr niimd aa ske। levemdr ke phool bhii kaaphii asrdaar hote haim anidaa ke mriijom ke lie। tkie ke niiche iske phool rkh dene se sugmdh poore kmre mem phail jaatii hai aur niimd behtr aatii hai।
yog aur dhyaan (Yoga or meditation)
yog aur dhyaan ko niymit abhyaas mem laaem। yog mem jyaadaa kthin aasn nhiim krne haim, saadhaarण aasn jisse mn ko shmti mile vhii krem। bed pr jaane, phle 5 se 10 mint dhyaan krem। dhyaan ke dauraan khiim bhtke nhiim aur mn ko sirph apnii sms pr ekaagr krem। raat mem behtr niimd aaegii।
el- thiyaaniin (L-theanine)
griin tii mem el –thiyaanin naamk emiino esid paaii jaatii hai। ise din mem piine se chustii aur taajgii chhaaii rhtii hai mn mem aur raat mem piine se ghrii niimd aatii hai।


Disease: hrniyaa (Hernia)

Description: 
hrniyaa (Hernia) mem pet kii mmspeshiym kmjor ho jaatii haim aur usii kmjor jgh se mtem baahr nikl aatii haim। yh smsyaa purushom v mhilaaom donom mem ho sktii hai, kintu purushom mem adhik paaii jaatii hai। adhikm~sh maamlom mem purushom mem hrniyaa kmr ke bhaag mem hotaa hai। yh kmr kii mmspeshiyom mem kmज़orii aane pr hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- kisii bhaarii vstu ke uthaane pr pet mem soojn kaa ubhr aanaa,
- pet kii chrbii yaa m~tom kaa baahr kii or niklnaa,
- pet ke nichle bhaag mem ubhaar yaa soojn mhsoos honaa
- pet mem phulaavt, drd aur bhaariipn,
- ml-mootr tyaagne mem preshaanii
- lmbe smy tk khd़e rhne yaa baithne mem drd mhsoos honaa,

Reasons: 
- paidaaishii taur pr
- bढ़tii umr
- chot lgnaa
- puraanaa ऑpreshn
- bhaarii vjn uthaanaa
- puraanii khm~sii
- motaapaa (Obesity)
- kbj
- peshaab mem rukaavt
- grbhaavsthaa
- pet kii mmspeshiyom kii kmjorii
- pet kii mmspeshiyom mem vikaar
- aanuvmshiktaa (Hereditiary)

Treatments:
hrniyaa kaa ilaaj (Treatment of Hernia)
- hrniyaa kaa ekmaatr sphl aur kaargr upaay opn aur laiproskopik srjrii ke roop mem uplbdh hai।
- 90 prtisht maamlom mem hrniyaa dobaaraa nhiim hotaa, lekin ds prtisht logom mem ऑpreshn ke baad phir se hrniyaa kii smsyaa utpnn ho sktii hai। islie dॉktr ke nirdeshaanusaar saavdhaanii brtem aur jroort pd़ne pr dॉktr se mulaakaat krne mem n hichkem।

Home Remedies:
pet kii mmspeshiyaa yaa khem pet kii diivaar kmjor ho jaane se jb mt baahr nikl aatii hai to use hrniyaa khte haim। vhm ek ubhaar ho jaataa hai, jise aasaanii se dekhaa jaa sktaa hai। lmbe smy se khmste rhne yaa lgaataar bhaarii saamaan uthaane se bhii pet kii mmspeshiyaa kmjor ho jaatii hai। aisii sthiti mem hrniyaa kii smbhaavnaa bdh़ jaatii hai। iske koii khaas lkshण nhiim hote haim lekin kuchh log soojn aur drd kaa anubhv krte haim, jo khड़e hone pr aur mmspeshiyom mem khimchaav hone yaa kuchh bhaarii saamaan uthaane pr bdh़ sktaa hai।
hrniyaa kii smsyaa jnmjaat bhii ho sktii hai। ise kॉnjenaaitl hrniyaa khte haim। hrniyaa ek vkt ke baad kisii ko bhii ho sktaa hai aur binaa srjrii ke thiik bhii nhiim ho sktaa। ismem pet kii tvchaa ke niiche ek asaamaany ubhaar aa jaataa hai, jo naabhi ke niiche hotaa hai। mt kaa ek hissaa pet kii mmspeshiyom ke ek kmjor hisse se baahr aa jaataa hai। iske alaavaa imguiml hrniyaa, phemorl hrniyaa, epigaastrik hrniyaa, emblaaikl hrniyaa bhii hotaa hai, jo bhut km dikhtaa hai।
hrniyaa ke ghreloo ilaaj (Home Remedies for Hernia)
agr hrniyaa bd़ii ho, usmem soojn ho aur kaaphii drd ho rhaa ho to binaa srjrii ke iskaa ilaaj smbhv nhiim hai। lokin hrniyaa ke lkshण ptaa lgne pr aap use ghreloo ilaaj se km kr skte haim। haalmki, in ghreloo upaayom se sirph praathmik ilaaj hii smbhv hai aur ise aajmaane pr kbhii ulte priणaam bhii ho skte haim। islie ghreloo ilaaj aajmaane se phle dॉktr se jrur smprk kr lem।
mulaithii (Licorice)
kph, khmsii mem mulaithii to raambaaण kii trh kaam krtaa hai aur aajmaay huaa bhii hai। hrniyaa ke ilaaj mem bhii ab yh kaargr saabit hone lgaa hai, khaaskr pet mem jb hrniyaa niklne ke baad rekhaaem pd़ jaatii hai tb ise aajmaaem।
adrk ke jd़ (Ginger Root)
adrk kii jd़ pet mem gaistrik esid aur baail joos se hue nuksaan se surkshaa krtaa hai। yh hrniyaa se hue drd mem bhii kaam krtaa hai।
bboone kaa phool (Chamomile)
pet mem hrniyaa aane se esiditii aur gais kaaphii bnne lgtii hai। is sthiti memm bboone ke phool ke sevn se kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai। yh paachn tmtr ko thiik krtaa hai aur esid bnne kii prkriyaa ko km krtaa hai।
maarsh mailo (Marshmallow)
yh ek jmglii aushdhi hai jo kaaphii miithii hotii hai। iske jd़ ke kaaphii aushdhiiy guण haim। yh paachn ko thiik krtaa hai aur pet-mt mem esid bnne kii prkriyaa ko km krtaa hai। hrniyaa mem bhii yh kaaphii aaraam phumchaataa hai।
haavthorniyaa (Hawthornia)
yh ek hrbl spliimemt hai jo pet kii mmspeshiyom ko mjboot bnaatii hai aur pet ke mdr ke mgom kii surkshaa krtii hai। yh hrniyaa ko niklne se rokne mem kaaphii kaargr hai। haavthorniyaa mem Citrus Seed, Hawthorn aur Fennel milii hotii hai।
ekyoopmkchr (Acupuncture)
hrniyaa ke drd mem ekyoopmkchr kaaphii aaraam phumchaataa hai। khaas nrv pr dbaav se hrniyaa kaa drd km hotaa hai।
brph (Ice)
brph se hrniyaa vaale jgh dbaane pr kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai aur soojn bhii km hotii hai। yh sbse jyaadaa prchln mem hai।
hrniyaa mem in chiijom ko nhiim krem (Don’ts in Hernia)
prbhaavit jgh ko kbhii bhii grm kpd़e yaa kisii bhii grm pdaarth se semk nhiim dem।
hrniyaa mem ksrt krne se prhej krem।
hrniyaa mem jyaadaa tmg aur taait kpd़em nhiim phnem।
bed pr apne tkie ko 6 imch upr rkhem, taaki pet mem sote smy esid aur gais nhiim bn paae।
ek hii baar jyaadaa mt khaaem, thod़ii-thod़ii der pr hlkaa bhojn lem।
khaane ke turmt baad jhukem nhiim।
shraab piinaa poorii trh bmd kr dem।


Disease: spomdilosis (Spondylosis)

Description: 
spomdilosis yaa spॉndilaaitis, aarthraaitis kaa hii ek roop hai। yh smsyaa mukhyt: meru dmd (Spine) ko prbhaavit krtii hai।

Symptoms: 
- agr spaainl kord db gii hai to bledr (Bladder) yaa baaul (Bowl) pr niymtrण khtm ho sktaa hai।
- is rog kaa drd haath kii umgliyom se sir tk ho sktaa hai।
- umgliym sunn ho jaatii haim।
- kmdhe, kmr ke nichle hisse aur pairom ke ooprii hisse mem kmjorii aur kd़aapn aa jaataa hai।
- kbhii-kbhii chhaatii mem drd ho sktaa hai।
- ksherukaaom (Vertebra) ke biich kii mmspeshiyom mem soojn aa jaatii hai।
- grdn se kmdhom aur vhm se hotaa huaa yh drd haathom, sir ke nichle hisse aur piith ke ooprii hisse tk phumch sktaa hai।
- chhiimknaa, khmsnaa aur grdn kii doosrii gtividhiym in lkshणom ko aur gmbhiir bnaa sktii haim।
- drd ke alaavaa smvedn shoonytaa aur kmjorii mhsoos ho sktii hai।
- shaariirik smtuln gd़bd़aa sktaa hai।
- sbse phle dikhaaii dene vaale lkshणom mem se ek grdn yaa piith mem drd aur unkaa kd़aa ho jaanaa hai।
- smy biitne ke saath drd kaa gmbhiir ho jaanaa।
- spomdilosis kii smsyaa hone pr yh sirph joड़o tk hii siimit nhiim rhtii। smsyaa gmbhiir hone pr bukhaar, thkaan, ultii honaa, chkkr aanaa aur bhookh kii kmii jaise lkshण bhii dikhaaii de skte haim।

Reasons: 
- aanuvmshik kaarण
- umr kaa bdh़naa
- bhojn mem poshk ttvom, kailshiym aur vitaamin dii kii kmii ke kaarण hddiyom kaa kmjor ho jaanaa
- baithne yaa khd़e rhne kaa glt triikaa
- lmbe smy tk draaivimg krnaa
- shaariirik shrm kaa abhaav
- msaaledaar thmdii yaa baasii chiijom ko khaanaa
- vilaasitaa poorण jiivnshailii
- mhilaaom mem lgaataar maahvaarii kaa asmtuln
- umr bdh़ne ke saath hddiyom mem kshy yaa vikaar paidaa honaa
- aksr phraikchr ke baad bhii hddiyom mem kshy kii sthiti hone lgtii hai।

Treatments:
spomdilosis kaa ilaaj (Treatment of Spondylosis)
- jiivnshailii mem bdlaav laaem।
- paushtik bhojn khaaem, visheshkr aisaa bhojn jo kailshiym aur vitaamin dii se bhrpoor ho।
- chaay aur kaiphiin kaa sevn km krem।
- paidl chlne kii koshish krem। isse bon maas (Bone Mass) bdh़taa hai। shaariirik roop se skriy (Active) rhem।
- niymit roop se vyaayaam aur yog krem।
- hmeshaa aaraamdaayk bistr pr soem। is baat kaa dhyaan rkhem ki bistr n to bhut skht ho aur n hii bhut nrm।
- spomdilosis se piiड़it log grdn ke niiche bd़aa tkiyaa n rkhem। unhem pairom ke niiche bhii tkiyaa nhiim rkhnaa chaahie।
- aisii mej aur kursii kaa pryog krem, jin pr aapko jhuk kr n baithnaa pd़e। hmeshaa kmr siidhii krke baithem। 
- dhoomrpaan n krem aur tmbaakoo n chbaaem।

Home Remedies:
srvaaikl spmdlaaisis (Cervical Spondolysis) umr bdh़ne ke saath grdn ke jod़ kii hddii-upaasthi ke ghisne ke kaarण hotii hai। yh grdn ke hddii ke disk pltne, ligaamemt mem phraikchr se bhii ho sktaa hai। ismem kaaphii ashniiy drd aur piid़aa hotii hai। grdn kaaphii bhaarii aur kd़aa mhsoos hone lgtii hai। kmdhe se lekr grdn aur sir tk mem drd hotii hai।
bmhom kii mmspeshiyom se lekr haathom kii umgliyom tk mem drd kii smvednshiiltaa mhsoos kii jaatii hai। 60 ke baad yh kisii ko bhii ho sktaa hai। haalmki khraab jiivnshailii, baithne-khd़aa hone ke glt poschr aur anuvmshik kaarणom se yh kbhii bhii ataik kr sktaa hai। aaie jaante haim spmdlaaisis se ld़ne ke ghreloo ilaaj।
niymit vyaayaam (Regular Exercise)
agr aap niymit rup se grdn aur bmh kii ksrt krte rhem to spmdlaaisis ke drd se aaऱaam milegaa। apne sir ko daaem-bme aur upr-niiche ghumaate rhem। apne grdn ko daaem aur bme kmdhe pr baarii-baarii se jhukaaem। ds mint tk yh vyaayaam rojaanaa 2 se 3 baar krem। kaaphii aaraam milegaa। aap hlke erobiks jaise sviimimg bhii aadhe ghmte tk roj kr skte haim, isse grdn kii spmdlaaisis mem aaraam milegaa।
grm aur thmde paanii kii pttii (Hot and cold compress)
grdn ke prbhaavit kshetr jhm drd ho aur kd़aapn mhsoos hotaa ho vhm phle grm paanii aur baad mem thmde paanii kii pttii se dbaav daalem। grm paanii kii pttii se bld srkuleshn tej hogaa aur mmspeshiyom kaa khimchaav km hogaa aur drd se raaht milegii। thmde paanii kaa pttii se soojn km hogaa। grm paanii kii pttii 2 se 3 mint tk rkhem aur thmde paanii kii pttii 1 mint। ise 15 mint pr dobaaraa krem।
semdhaa nmk kii pttii yaa snaan (Epsom salt bath)
niymit rup se semdhaa nmk kii pttii yaa isse snaan krne se spmdlaaisis ke drd mem kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai। semdhaa nmk mem maigniishiym kii maatraa jyaadaa hone se yh shriir ke piiech str ko niymtrit krtaa hai aur grdn kii akd़ aur kd़epn ko km krtaa hai। aadhe glaas paanii mem do chmmch semdhaa nmk milaa kr pest bnaa lem aur use grdn ke prbhaavit kshetr mem lgaaem, thod़ii der ke baad kaaphii raaht milegii। yaa gungune paanii mem do kp semdhaa nmk daal kr rojaanaa snaan krem, kaaphii phaaydaa milegaa।
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun mem drd nivaark guण hotaa hai aur yh soojn ko bhii km krtaa hai। subh khaalii pet paanii ke saath kchchaa lhsun niymit khaaem, kaaphii phaaydaa hogaa। tel mem lhsun ko pkaa kr grdn mem maalish bhii kiyaa jaa sktaa hai, isse drd mem kaaphii raaht milegii।

til ke biij (Sesame Seeds)
til mem kailshiym, maigniishiym, maigniij, vitaamin ke aur dii kaaphii maatraa mem paaii jaatii hai jo hmaare hddii aur mmspeshiyom ke seht ke lie kaaphii jrurii hai। spmdlaaisis ke drd mem bhii til kaaphii kaargr hai। til ke grm tel se grdn kii hlkii maalish 5 se 10 mint tk krem, phir vhm grm paanii kii pttii daalem, kaaphii aaraam milegaa aur grdn kii akd़ bhii km hogii।
aur bhii haim kii tips (Some more tips)
subh shaam bhojn ke baad thod़ii maatraa mem hriitaakii khaaem, drd se nijaat milegii aur grdn kii akd़ km hogii।
shaariirik shrm km krem yaa isse prhej hii kr lem। bhaarii saamaan ekdm nhiim uthaaem

Disease: liivr kaimsr (Liver Cancer)

Description:

Symptoms:

Disease: kmr drd (Back Pain)

Description: 
slip disk yaa kmr drd (Back Pain) koii biimaarii nhiim hai blki yh ek trh se shriir kii ymtrik asphltaa (Mechanical Failure) hai। kmr drd ke sbse mhttvpoorण kaarण riiढ़ se yaa merudmd (Spinal Cord) se juड़e hote haim। spaainl kॉrd yaa riiढ़ kii hddii spaain vrtibraa (Vertebrae) se milkr bntii hai jis pr shriir kaa pooraa vjn tikaa hotaa hai। yh sir ke nichle hisse se shuroo hokr tel bon (Tail Bone) tk hotii hai। hmaarii riidh़ kii hddii mem hr do vrtibraa (Vertebrae) ke biich mem ek disk hotii hai jo jhtkaa shne kaa yaani shaak ebjaarvr (Shock Absorber) kaa kaam krtii hai। aage-piichhe, daayem-baayem ghoomne se disk kaa phailaav hotaa hai। glt triike se kaam krne, pढ़ne, uthne-baithne yaa jhukne se disk pr lgaataar jor pड़taa hai। isse merudmd kii nsom (Nerves) pr dbaav aa jaataa hai jo kmr mem lgaataar hone vaale drd kaa kaarण bntaa hai। is disk ke ghis jaane se ismem soojn aa jaatii hai, aur yh ubhrkr baahr nikl aatii hai। iske baad yh riidh़ kii hddii se pairom tk jaane vaalii nsom pr dbaav daaltii hai। nsem dbne ke kaarण yh drd pairom tk bhii jaa sktaa hai। ismem pair sunn ho jaane kaa khtraa rhtaa hai। drd itnaa kshtdaayk hotaa hai ki mriij apne dainik kaary krne tk mem asmrth ho jaataa hai। kmr drd ( Peeth Ka Dard) ab logom ke lie ek kshtdaayk smsyaa bnii huii hai। aaj hr umr ke log isse preshaan haim aur duniyaa bhr mem iske srl v shj ilaaj kii khoj jaarii hai। dinbhr baithe kr kaam krne se yh smsyaa aur bhii bdh़ jaatii hai। kmr drd agr niiche kii trph bdh़ne lge aur tej ho jaae, to jld se jld dॉktr ko dikhaaem। kbhii-kbhii drd kuchh mint hii hotaa hai aur kbhii-kbhii yh ghmtom tk rhtaa hai। 30 se 50 vrsh kii aayuvrg ke log iskii chpet mem adhik aate haim। ve mhilaa aur purush iske adhik shikaar hote haim, jinhem apne kaam kii vjh se baar-baar uthnaa, baithnaa, jhuknaa yaa saamaan utaarnaa, rkhnaa hotaa hai।

Home Remedies:
kmr kii mmspeshiyom kaa asmtulit honaa hii kmr drd kaa kaarण hotaa hai। kmr drd shii trh se n uthne-baithne, sone yaa kmr pr kshmtaa se adhik dbaav pड़ne se hotaa hai। lgbhg 80 % log kbhii n kbhii kmr drd se preshaan hote haim। kmr drd nyaa bhii ho sktaa hai aur puraanaa bhii ho sktaa hai। sthii taur pr dekhne pr kmr mem hone vaalaa drd bhle hii ek saamaany sii sthiti lgtii hai, lekin ise nj़rmdaaj krne se smsyaa kaaphii bढ़ sktii hai।
jaanie kmr drd door krne ke ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Back Pain):
1. ghutne moड़em (Band knee)- niiche rkhii koii vstu uthaate vkt phle apne ghutne moड़em phir us vstu ko uthaaem। aisaa krne se kmr pr anaavshyk dbaav nhiim pड़egaa aur km tkliiph hogii।
2. lhsun (Garlic)- bhojn mem lhsun kaa pryaapt upyog krem। lhsun kmr drd kaa achchhaa upchaar maanaa gyaa hai। lhsun ke pryog se puraane se puraanaa kmr drd bhii thiik hone lgtaa hai।

6. daalchiinii (Cinnamon)- 2 graam daalchiinii kaa paaudr ek chmmch shhd mem milaakr din mem do baar lete rhne se kmrdrd mem raaht miltii hai।
7. shriir ko grm rkhem (Warm Body)- kmr drd puraanaa ho to shriir ko grm rkhem aur grm vstuem khaaem। aisaa krne se kmr drd mem behd raaht miltii hai। srdiyom mem drd jyaadaa ho to dhyaan rkhem ki drd vaalaa hissaa hvaa ke smprk mem n aae।
8. brph kii sikaaii (Ice Foment)- drd vaalii jgh pr brph kaa pryog krnaa bhii laabhkaarii upaay hai। isse bhiitrii soojn bhii smaapt hogii। kuchh roj brph़ kaa upyog krne ke baad grm sikaaii praarmbh kr dene se anukool priणaam aate haim।
9. paushtik bhojn (Proper Nutrition)- bhojn me tmaatr, gobhii, chukmdr, khiiraa, kkड़ii, paalk, gaajr, फ़lom kaa prchur maatraa mem upyog krem।
10. bhaap kii sikaaii (Steam Foment)- nmk mile grm paanii mem ek tauliyaa daalkr nichoड़ lem। pet ke bl letkr drd ke sthaan pr tauliye dvaaraa bhaap lene se kmr drd mem raaht miltii hai।
11. maalish (Massage)- roj subh srsom yaa naariyl ke tel mem lhsun kii tiin-chaar kliym~ daalkr (jb tk lhsun kii kliym~ kaalii n ho jaayem) grm kr lem phir thmdaa kr prbhaavit jgh pr maalish krem।
12. nmk (Salt)- kढ़aaii mem do-tiin chmmch nmk daalkr ise achchhe se sek lem। thoड़e mote sootii kpड़e mem yh grm nmk daalkr potlii bmdh lem। kmr pr iske dvaaraa sek krem।


Disease: siine mem drd (Chest Pain)

Description: 
siine mem drd ( Chest Pain) kii baat aate hii hm dil ke daure (Heart Attack) kii baat sochne lgte haim, mgr siine mem drd kii kaarणom se ho sktaa hai। phephड़e, mmspeshiym~, pslii, yaa nsom mem bhii koii smsyaa utpnn hone pr siine mem drd hotaa hai। kisii-kisii pristhiti mem yh drd bhyaank roop dhaarण kr letaa hai jo mृtyu tk kaa kaarण bn jaataa hai। lekin ek baat dhyaan mem rkhem ki khud hii rog kii phchaan n krem aur siine mem drd ko njrmdaaj n krem, turnt chikitsk ke paas jaayem।

Symptoms: 
- siine kaa drd svym kii rogom kaa lkshण hai।

Reasons: 
enjaainaa (Angina) : hृdy (Heart) ke kaarण jb siine mem drd hotaa hai tb chikitsaa shaastr ke anusaar isko enjaainaa khte haim। enjaainaa se grst rogii ko siine mem drd kuchh hii der tk hotaa hai yaa pristhiti bigd़ jaane pr drd kii avdhi bdh़ jaatii hai। saadhaarणth yh drd kmdhe, bm~h, piith, pet ke ooprii bhaag mem hotaa hai। enjaainaa mem dhmniyom ke sikud़ jaane ke kaarण rkt kaa hृdy mem aavaagmn baadhit ho jaataa hai। jb dhmniyom mem rkt kaa thkkaa jmne lgtaa hai tb sm~s lene mem mushkil hone lgtii hai aur siine mem drd shuroo ho jaataa hai। agr pristhiti ko smbhaalaa nhiim gyaa to mृtyu tk ho sktii hai। enjaainaa kaa drd saadhaarणth aanuvmshiktaa ke kaarण, mdhumeh, haaii kolestrॉl, phle se hृdy smbmdhit rog se grst hone ke kaarण hotaa hai।
uchch rktchaap: jo dhmniym~ rkt ko phephd़om tk le jaatii hai usmem jb rkt kaa chaap bdh़ jaataa hai tb siine mem drd hotaa hai aur is avsthaa ko uchch rktchaap (Pulmonary Hypertension) khte haim।
esiditii (Acidity): yh saadhaarणt gaistro isophegl riphlks dij़iij़ (grd) (bhaataa rog) ke kaarण hotaa hai।
phephd़om mem rog (Lung Disease) : jb rkt dhmniyom mem thkkaa jmne lgtaa hai tb phephd़om ke tishu yaa ootkom mem rkt kaa prvaah rukne lgtaa hai, aisaa hone se bechainii hone lgtii hai aur sm~s lene mem mushkil hotaa hai, jo baad mem drd kaa kaarण bntaa hai।
dr ke kaarण (Fear Psycosis): kbhii-kbhii dil mem drd atydhik dr, achaank koii sdmaa, dil kii dhd़kn ke bdh़ne, atydhik psiinaa aur sm~s mem tkliiph ke kaarण bhii hotaa hai।
tnaav: tnaav ke kaarण dil kii dhd़kn tej ho jaatii hai, sm~s lene mem tkliiph hone lgtii hai aur rkt chaap bdh़ jaane ke kaarण bhii hृdy mem rkt smchaar kii gti ko nuksaan phum~chtaa hai, in sb kaarणom se bhii siine mem drd hotaa hai।

Treatments:
- siine mem drd (Chest Pain) kaa siidhaa smbmdh hmaare aniyojit aur asvsth khaan-paan se hai। khaan paan mem sudhaar ke saath saath hmem niymit roop se vyaayaam krnaa chaahie।

- khaane mem nmk kii maatraa ko km krem aur agr ho ske to bilkul chhod़ dem।
- dhoomrpaan hृdy smbmdhii biimaarii ko bdh़aane mem ahm bhoomikaa nibhaataa hai। ath isko chhod़naa phaaydemmd hai।

Home Remedies:
siine mem drd (Chest Pain) hmeshaa haart ataik kaa maamlaa nhiim hotaa। siine yaa chhaatii mem drd ke aur bhii kii kaarण ho skte haim। esiiditii, srdii, kph, tnaav, gais, bdhjmii aur dhoomrpaan se bhii chhaatii mem drd hotii hai। vaise jb kbhii bhii chhaatii mem drd ho to ttkaal d़ॉktr se smprk krnaa chaahie taaki haart ataik kii shmkaa ko door kiyaa jaa ske।

chhaatii drd ke ghreloo ilaaj (Home Remedies for Chest Pain)

lhsun ko vmdr medisiin khaa gyaa hai jo hr trh kii bimaariyom mem raambaaण kaa kaam krtaa hai। seht ke lie to raambaaण hai hii haart ke lie to sbse jyaadaa laabhkaarii hai। lhsun mem kii trh ke vitaamin, minrls-kailshiym, phaasphors, aayrn, thiyaamin, raaibophlaavin, niyaasin aur vitaamin sii kaa khjaanaa hai। iske alaavaa ismem slphr, aayodiin aur kloriin kii maatraa bhii paaii jaatii hai।

Disease: phephड़om kaa kaimsr (Lung Cancer)

Description: 
maanaa ki maanv shriir mem koshikaaom kaa vikaas ek niymtrit prणaalii ke roop mem hotaa hai lekin kuchh koshikaaom kaa ek aisaa smooh hotaa hai jo ki aniymtrit roop se bdh़taa hai aur viksit hotaa hai। in koshikaaom ko kaimsr koshikaaem khte haim। ye do prkaar kii hotii hai jinhem binaain tyoomr (Benign Tumour) aur melignent tyoomr (Malignant Tumour) khaa jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- mguliyom aur mgoothom ke sirom kaa bdh़ jaanaa (dijitl kltbimg)
- aavaaj kaa phtnaa
- kuchh maamlom mem nimoniyaa honaa
- khmsii mem khoon kaa aanaa (hemoptaaisis),
- thkaan (kmjorii) mhsoos honaa
- nirmtr khmsii bne rhnaa,
- vjn mem kmii yaa bhookh n lgnaa, niglne mem kthinaaii honaa

- shriir kii raasaaynik smrchnaa mem asaamaanytaaem honaa
- sms lene mem kthinaaii yaa ghrghraaht honaa
- sir mem drd yaa dauraa pड़naa, chehre, grdn yaa ooprii mgom mem soojn aanaa
- siine, kmdhe yaa bmh mem drd rhnaa
- hddiyom mem drd rhnaa

Reasons: 
- phephd़e ke kaimsr kaa khtraa un sb ko ho sktaa hai jo dhoomrpaan krte haim। agr aap sigret, paaip, biid़ii v sigaar kaa dhumaa phephd़e tk naa bhii le jaaem, to bhii inse gle v mumh kaa kaimsr (Cancer) phailne kaa khtraa hotaa hai। dhoomrpaan bmd krke is khtre ko km kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
- dhoomrpaan krne vaalom ke aaspaas maujood hote haim yaa dhuem ke vaataavrण mem kaam krte haim, unhem bhii phephd़e ke kaimsr kaa khtraa hai। iskaa sbse jyaadaa dr chhote bchchom ko hotaa hai।
- esbests (Asbestos), yooreniym (Uranium) , aarsenik (Arsenic) v petrol (Petrol) kii riphaainrii yaa kaarkhaane mem kaam krte haim।
- jinhem tyoobrkyoolosis (Tuberclosis) ho, unhem bhii iskaa khtraa rhtaa hai। iske alaavaa redio ektiv gais redॉn kii vjh se bhii phephd़e kaa kaimsr hotaa hai।

Treatments:
kaimsr paae jaane ke baad log aksr preshaan ho jaate haim। kaimsr (Cancer) ke nidaan aur upchaar ke dauraan aur uske pshchaat vyaavhaarik aur bhaavnaatmk shaaytaa bhut mhtvpoorण hotii hai। privaar ke sdsyom, svaasthy peshevrom yaa vishesh shaaytaa sevaaom ke maadhym se yh shaaytaa uplbdh ho sktii hai।

Home Remedies:
phephd़e ke kaimsr (Lungs Cancer) ke ilaaj ke krm mem kii mriijom ko sms lene mem preshaanii hotii hai yaa sms hii nhiim le paate haim। ismem sms kii nlii jo phephd़e ko ऑksiijn phumchaatii hai, vo hii jaam ho jaatii hai। aisii sthti mem mriijom ko alg se ऑksiijn naak ke dvaaraa diyaa jaataa hai aur isse mriij kaaphii aaraam mhsoos krte haim। lekin yh upaay hmeshaa ke lie nhiim haim।
lmgs kaimsr ke mriijom kii smkhyaa tejii se bdh़ rhii hai। dhoomrpaan aur nshe ke atydhik sevn se phephd़e mem jb taar kii maatraa kaaphii bdh़ jaatii hai to phephd़e kaa kaimsr (Lungs Cancer) hotaa hai। agr tiibii kaa ilaaj shii se nhiim hotaa hai yaa tiibii kii dvaaii kaa kors mriij aadhe mem hii chhod़ detaa hai to phephd़e ke kaimsr kii smbhaavnaa bdh़ jaatii hai।
lmgs kaimsr kaa ilaaj kiimotherepii yaa phir srjrii hii hai, mgr lmgs kaimsr ke baad bhii agr mriij apne khaan-paan mem bdlaav laae aur nshe kii aadt ko chhod़ de to kaaphii hd tk mriij ek behtr jimdgii jii sktaa hai।
phephd़e ke kaimsr ke ghreloo ilaaj (Home remedies For Lung Cancer)
khaan-paan (Diet)
phephd़e ke kaimsr ke mriijom ke lie sehtmmd bhojn kchchii sbjii, aur kchche phl hote haim। saabut anaaj khaanaa bhii thiik rhtaa hai। slaad kaa jyaadaa se jyaadaa sevn krnaa phaaydemmd rhtaa hai। aise mriijom ko hmeshaa saaph aur svchchh paanii piinaa chaahie। phephd़e ke kaimsr mem baadaam nhiim khaanaa chaahie। dophr mem khtte phl yaa saaitrs phroots (Citrus Fruits) ke joos piine chaahie।

nonii (Noni)
yh ek traapikl phood hai jo phephd़e ke kaimsr mem kaaphii asrdaar hotaa hai। ise khaayaa bhii jaataa hai aur iske joos bhii piie jaa skte haim।

Disease: thkaan (Fatigue)

Description: 
thkaan ek saamaany avsthaa hai, adhik shaariirik yaa maansik prishrm krne se shriir mem thkaan aa jaatii hai aur shriir sust ho jaataa hai। thkaan, kmjorii se alg hai। aaraam krne pr thkaan chlii jaatii hai jbki kmjorii bnii rh sktii hai।

Symptoms: 
- kmjorii mhsoos honaa
- kisii kaam mem mn n lgnaa
- nkraatmk soch kaa bdh़naa
- hr smy niimd aanaa

Reasons: 
- shaariirik str pr iske kii kaarण ho skte haim jaise eniimiyaa, thaairaaid, shugr aur kolestrॉl kaa bड़aa huaa str।

- yh hlke bukhaar kii vjh se bhii ho sktaa hai jo imphekshn kaa ntiijaa hotaa hai।
- bhut jyaadaa shugr yaa riphaaimd kaarbohaaidrets jaise chaavl, maidaa aadi khaanaa, lmbe mtraal pr khaanaa khaanaa aur shii trh kaa bhojn n khaane se bhii aadmii thkaan mhsoos krtaa hai।
- maansik str pr hone vaalii thkaan kaa arth hai ki aap tnaavgrst haim।
- avsaad (Depression) kii sthiti mem bhii bhut adhik thkaan, sirdrd aur kmjorii mhsoos hotii hai। avsaad kii vjh se thkaavt honaa aaj kii jiivnshailii mem bhut saamaany hai। 
- agr aap do-tiin hphtom tk hr smy thkaan mhsoos krte haim to mnochikitsk se praamrsh uchit hogaa।
- din mem kii baar chaay-kॉphii kaa sevn krne vaale logom ko thkaan jldii hotii hai। kaiphiin vaalii chiijom ke adhik sevn se bld preshr aur dhd़kn kii gti tej hotii hai jisse thkaan jldii hotii hai।
- grmiyom mem shriir mem paanii kii kmii yaani dihaaidreshn bhii aapko jldii thkaa sktii hai। islie shriir mem paanii kii kmii n hone dem।

- khaan-paan aur apnii jiivnshailii pr dhyaan dene kii khaas jroort hai। jroorii nhiim ki hr baar thkaan kaa kaarण koii shaariirik smsyaa ho, kii baar thkaan kaa kaarण maansik bhii hotaa hai।

Treatments:
thkaan door bhgaane kaa sbse behtr upaay hotaa hai aaraam krnaa। iske saath kuchh any upaay apnaa kr bhii aap thkaan ko door bhgaa skte haim। yh upaay nimn haim:
- raat mem achchhii v bhrpoor niimd lenaa, thkaan ko door krne kaa sbse achchhaa triikaa hai। 7-8 ghmte kii niimd jroor lem taaki agle din ke lie aapko pryaapt oorjaa mile।

- skriy rhem, aals chhod़em।
- niymit ksrt krem। 

Home Remedies:
thkaavt-aalsy se aap jimdgii se niraash mhsoos krte haim। hmeshaa gusse mem haare hue imsaan kii trh vyvhaar krte hai। aap bhii chaahte haim ki ek achchhe nsl ke ghod़e kii trh res lgaaem, lekin aapko mhsoos hotaa hai ki aapke pmv kiichd़ mem  phmse hue haim। aap ichchhaashkti bhii krte haim lekin vo kaam nhiim krtaa। maansik aur shaariirik thkaavt vaise to saamaany biimaarii hai , mgr kuchh gmbhiir biimaarii mem bhii aise lkshण dikhaaii pd़te haim।

subh-shaam niymit yog krem। khaaskr piith ke bl let kr pair ko sir se umchaa krnaa aur phir use dhiire-dhiire niiche krnaa। ghutnom ko naak mem staanaa। ye kuchh aise vyaayaam haim jisse aap trotaajaa mhsoos krte haim। yog mem bhraamrii bhii kaaphii phaaydemmd rhtaa hai।

adhik vsaa vaale bhojn khaanaa km krem। isse motaapaa bdh़tii hai aur shriir mem hmeshaa thkaavt mhsoos hotii hai।
binaa chhiile hue aaloo ke slaais kaat kr ise raat bhr paanii mem bhiimgne chhod़ dem। subh is joos ko pii lem। ismem kaaphii maatraa mem potaashiym rhtii hai jo shriir mem minrls kii kmii ko door krtii hai। minrls ke sevn se shriir kii mmspeshiyaa kaaphii skriy rhtii hai aur aap thkaavt nhiim mhsoos krte haim।

Disease: khoon kaa thkkaa (Blood Clotting)

Description: 
shriir mem khoon kaa thkkaa (Blood Clotting) bnne aur uske ghulne kii prkriyaa shj roop mem chltii rhtii hai। hmaare plaajmaa mem maujood pletlets aur protiin, chot kii jgh pr rkt ke thkke kaa nirmaaण krke rkt ke bhaav ko rokte haim। agr aisaa n ho to chot lgne pr shriir mem khoon kaa bhaav roknaa kthin ho jaae। aamtaur pr chot ke thiik hone pr rkt kaa thkkaa apne aap ghul jaataa hai। pr jb is prkriyaa mem ad़chn aatii hai to khoon kaa thkkaa bnaa hii rh jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- ghbraaht honaa
- psiinaa aanaa
- sir chkraanaa

Reasons: 
khoon kaa thkkaa kevl chot lgne ke kaarण hii bntaa। iske kii any kaarण bhii hote haim jaise 
khoon kaa thkkaa bnne ke kaarण (Causes of Blood Clotting)
- agr aap grbh nirodhk golii (Oral Contraceptive Pills) lete haim।
- agr aapko motaapaa hai।
- agr aapko menopoj (menopause) ho chukaa hai।
- smaachaar ptr 'd mirr' ke anusaar ek ne adhyyn mem khaa gyaa hai ki jo log lgaataar 10 ghmte tk kaam krte haim aur is dauraan koii viraam nhiim lete to unmem khoon kaa thkkaa jmne kaa khtraa dogunaa ho jaataa hai। yh adhyyn 21-30 saal aayu siimaa ke logom pr kiyaa gyaa। adhyyn mem shaamil 75 phiisdii logom ne maanaa ki ve kaam ke dauraan viraam nhiim lete।

Treatments:
khoon kaa thkkaa bnne pr turmt dॉktr se slaah krem। yh biimaarii behd khtrnaak ho sktii hai islie phle achchhii trh jmch kraane ke baad hii upchaar shuru krem।

Home Remedies:
rkt kaa thkkaa jmnaa rktnlikaa ke bmd ho jaane se hotaa hai aur agr ttkaal iskaa ilaaj nhiim kiyaa gyaa to yh jaanlevaa ho jaataa hai। mote logom mem bld klॉt hone kaa khtraa jyaadaa rhtaa hai, lekin kii aur rog-pristhitiyom mem rkt kaa thkkaa jmtaa hai jo kaaphii khtrnaak hotaa hai।
binaa srjrii ke bld klॉtimg kaa koii ilaaj hii nhiim hai aur kbhii-kbhii to shriir ke us hisse yaa mg mem chhed kr yaa kaat kr iskaa ilaaj kiyaa jaataa hai।  khaaskr sir mem chot lgne ke baad agr bld kl़ॉt hotii hai to yh kaaphii gmbhiir ho jaatii hai , jismem mriij ko bren hemrej kaa khtraa rhtaa hai aur maut tk ho sktii hai।
dhyaan rhe ki bld klॉtig hone ke baad koii ghreloo upchaar kaam nhiim krtaa hai। haalmki, bld klॉt n ho yaa jin logom iskaa khtraa jyaadaa hai unke lie kii ghreloo upchaar haim।
bld klॉtimg se b़chne ke ghreloo ilaaj (Home remedies to prevent from Blood clotting)
skimd milk yaa chhaalii utaaraa huaa doodh (Skimmed milk)
skimd milk yaa chhaalii utaare doodh mem phait yaani vsaa nhiim hotii aur ismem kailshiym bhii rhtaa hai, jisse rkt kii nlikaa mem phait jmaa hone kaa khtraa nhiim rhtaa hai aur kailshiym se bld ke pletlets shii dh़mg se kaam krte haim। rkt nlikaa mem phait jmaa nhiim hone se rkt kaa prvaah shii dh़mg se hotaa hai।
motaapaa km krem (Loose obesity)
kaaphii vsaa yukt bhojn krne se motaapaa bdh़taa hai aur iskaa ntiijaa hotaa hai ki rkt nlikaa ke diivaar pr phait kii prt jm jaatii hai। agr rkt nlikaa ke mumh kii chaud़aaii km huii to rkt ke prvaah mem kthinaaii hogii aur ntiijaa bld klॉt hogaa। bld klॉt hone se dil kaa dauraa pd़ sktaa hai aur bren haimrej kaa khtraa rhtaa hai।
niymit vyaayaam krem (Exercise Regularly)
niymit rup se vyaayaam krne se shriir mem phailii sbhii rkt nlikaaom mem rkt kaa smchrण shii dh़mg se hotaa hai।
dhoomrpaan se krem taubaa (Avoid Smoking)
dhoomrpaan krne se ऑksiijn kaarbn daaiऑksaaid mem bdltaa hai aur isse rkt nlikaa kii mmspeshiym kmjor hotii hai ntiijaa bld klॉtimg kii smbhaavnaa bdh़ jaatii hai।
pyaaj aur lhsun kaa sevn (Eating onion and garlic)
pyaaj aur lhsun khaane se shriir mem phaaibrin kii kmii hotii hai aur iske priणmsvrup pletlets shii dh़mg se bnte haim aur bld kii klॉtimg nhiim hotii hai।
haaidrotherepii (Hydrotherepy)
bld klॉt vaale sthaan pr agr grm auऱ thmde paanii kaa paik lgaataar diyaa jaae to smbhv hai vhm rkt kaa smchrण ho sktaa hai।
msaaj (Massage)
agr aap niymit rup se shriir kii msaaj krvaate haim to shriir mem rkt kaa prvaah suchaaru dh़mg se hotaa hai। rkt kii nlikaaem bhii blॉk nhiim hotii hai auऱ bld klॉt kaa khtraa km rhtaa hai।


Disease: mmspeshiyom mem drd (Muscle Pain)

Description: 
aaj kii vyst aur bhaag-daud़ bhrii jimdgii mem mmspeshiyom mem drd (Muscle Pain) ek aam smsyaa hai। yuvaaom mem yh smsyaa tejii se bdh़ rhii hai। yh drd kuchh logom ko kbhii-kbhii staataa hai, jbki jyaadaatr log isse sthaayii roop se preshaan rhte haim। mmspeshiyom kaa drd kisii bhii umr ke vykti ko ho sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- shaariirik kmjorii khaas kr mmspeshiyom kii,  niimd n aanaa

Reasons: 
- aniymit jiivn shailii aur glt khaan-paan is smsyaa kaa sbse bd़aa kaarण hai। 
- shaariirik prishrm yaa kthor shrm ke kaarण tnaav, thkaan yaa mmspeshiyom mem chot, inphlooemjaa, laaim disiij, mleriyaa, demgoo, mmspeshii kaa phod़aa tthaa smkrmण kii vjh se bhii drd ho sktaa hai। 
- ilektrolaait kaa asmtuln jaise-potaishiym yaa kailshiym kii maatraa bhut km honaa bhii iskaa kaarण ho sktaa hai।

Treatments:
mmspeshiyom mem drd hone pr semk aur maalish se aaraam miltaa hai। agr isse bhii aaraam naa mile to nimn upaay apnaane chaahie:
- mmspeshiyom mem drd ho to thod़ii chhlkdmii krem । 
- ghrii sms lem aur donom haathom ko siidhaa oopr uthaaem। yh prkriyaa kii baar dohraaem। aisaa krne se mmspeshiyom mem rkt prvaah mem sudhaar hotaa hai, jisse aap rilaiks mhsoos kremge। 
- bhojn mem doodh, taaज़aa phl, sbjiym aadi paushtik bhojn lenaa chaahie। 
- ek-do ghmte tk kaary krne ke baad thod़aa aaraam krem tthaa thlem। 
- ek hii sthiti mem lmbe smy tk baithkr kaam n krem। 
- motaape ko niymtrit krem। 
- dinchryaa sudhaarem aur dvaaom ke upyog kii jgh vyaayaam krem। 
- shraab tthaa sigret ke sevn se bchem।  
- atydhik tnaav aur mmspeshiyom pr adhik jor daalne vaale kaary n krem। 
- phaast phood kaa sevn km se km krem। 
- jim mem prshikshit trenr kii dekh rekh mem hii vyaayaam krem। 
- kold drimk kaa km se km sevn krem, yh aapke shriir ke kailshiym ko thiik se pchne nhiim detaa hai। 
- khoob paanii piem, kaiphiin utpaadom aur alkohl ke sevn se bchem, kyomki isse dihaaidreshn (Dehydration) ho sktaa hai। 
- bhaarii-bhrkm shaariirik gtividhiyom ke baad mmspeshiyom ko protiin kii jroort hotii hai, taaki shriir mem enrjii kaa str bnaa rhe। aise mem protiinyukt nechurl khaady utpaadom kaa sevn krnaa chaahie।

Home Remedies:
jb kbhii bhii hm kshmtaa se adhik kaam krte haim yaa jyaadaa aals krte haim, donom hii pristhitiyom mem mmspeshiyom mem drd (muscle pain) ho sktaa hai। iske alaavaa vyaayaam glt triike se krne yaa vyaayaam ke shurooaat mem, bld phlo se smbmdhit smsyaa hone, kailshiym (Calcium), maigniishiym (Magnesium) aur poteshiym (Potassium) kii kmii hone, dihaaidreshn aadi ke kaarण bhii mmspeshiyom mem tnaav aur khimchaav smbhv hai।
mslpen ligment (Ligament, ootk jo ki do yaa do se jyaadaa hddiyom ko aaps mem joड़te haim) kii chot hai। mmspeshiyom mem drd tb hotaa hai jb in ootkom pr jyaadaa jor pड़taa hai। yhm hm aapko kuchh ghreloo nuskhom se mmspeshiyom ke drd kaa ilaaj btaaemge lekin ashniiy ho aur jyaadaa piiड़aa ho rhii ho to dॉktr ke paas jaanaa hii behtr upaay hai। kuchh ghreloo nuskhe nimn haim-
1. epsm sॉlt (Epsom salt)
grm paanii kii ek baaltii mem yaa tb mem ek kp epsm nmk daal kr prbhaavit sthaan ko is paanii mem tkriibn 15 mint ke lie dubaa kr rkhem। ek hphte mem is prkriyaa ko do se tiin baar kr skte haim। lekin hृdy se smbmdhit, shugr yaa uchch rktchaap (high blood pressure) kii smsyaa se piiड़it vykti is vidhi ko n krem।
2. grm aur thmdaa sek (Hot and cold fomentation)
grm paanii se nhaane se mmspeshiyom kii sikaaii hotii hai aur unhem aaraam bhii miltaa hai। is trh se mmspeshiyom kii akड़n bhii door hotii hai। lekin iske ult ydi soojn mhsoos ho rhii ho to brph ke tukड़om ko ptle kpड़e mem lpetkr usse sikaaii krnii chaahie।
3. maigniishiym yukt khaanaa (Magnesium rich food)
maigniishiym kii km maatraa se bhii mmspeshiyom mem drd aur khimchaav ho sktaa hai। iske lie khaane mem kddoo ke biij (pumpkin seeds), kaalii biins (black beans), soorjmukhii ke biij (sunflower seeds), baadaam aur kaajoo ko apne aahaar mem shaamil krnaa chaahie। jisse shriir ko prchur maatraa mem maigniishiym mil ske।
4. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)
seb ke sirke kii kuchh maatraa ek gilaas paanii mem milaakr piine se msls ke drd se raaht miltii hai। iske alaavaa ydi is trh piinaa kthin lge to ek gilaas paanii mem do chmmch sirkaa, ek chmmch shhd aur kuchh pttiym pudiine kii milaakr bhii pii jaa sktii haim।
5. ऑyl (Oil)
msl pen mem raaht ke lie kaimomaail, peprmimt, levemdr aadi tel mem ek yaa do chmmch, naariyl yaa ऑliv ऑyl milaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaanaa chaahie।
6. cherii joos (Cherry juice)
msl pen se raaht ke lie cherii joos bhii piinaa chaahie। cherii joos piine se msls kaa khimchaav km hotaa hai saath hii yh mmspeshiyom ko raaht bhii detaa hai।
7. msaaj (Massage)
msaaj krne se shriir kaa rktsmchaar behtr hotaa hai jo ki drd ko tejii se thiik krne mem mdd krtaa hai। ydi msaaj krne ke lie achchhe telom kaa pryog kiyaa jaae to asr dogunaa ho jaataa hai।
8. mirch (Chilli)
mirch mem maujood kaipsesin (capsaicin) bhii drd kii khaas dvaa hai। baajaar mem mirch se taiyaar kii trh kii drd nivaark kriim miltii haim, lekin inhem aap ghr bhii taiyaar kr skte haim। iske lie naariyl yaa jaitoon ke tel ko grm krke ismem ek bड़aa chmmch laal mirch milaakr ise thmdaa krem। iske baad ismem eloveraa jel milaaem। is trh se taiyaar utpaad ko ydi prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaakr hlke haath se maalish kii jaae to behd aaraam miltaa hai।
9. aaraam (Rest)
kii baar kuchh n krke sirph aaraam krnaa bhii shriir ko bhut laabh de sktaa hai। ydi shriir mem akड़n mhsoos ho to km se km do din aapko shriir ko poorii trh aaraam denaa chaahie। isse shriir hlkaa mhsoos krtaa hai aur tnaav km hotaa hai jiskaa siidhaa asr mmspeshiyom pr bhii pड़taa hai।


Disease: prostet kaimsr (Prostate Cancer)

Description: 
prostet kaimsr purushom ko hotaa hai। ye kaimsr shurooaatii daur mem ptaa chl jaae, to aasaanii se thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- koolhe (hips), jmgh kii hddiym (thaaiij) v piith mem lgaataar drd honaa
- peshaab krte smy drd v jln honaa
- peshaab krne mem dikkt honaa
- baar baar peshaab jaanaa, khaaskr raat mem
- viiry yaa mootr mem khoon aanaa
- seks ke dauraan viiry niklte vkt drd honaa
- seks ke smy limg mem kthortaa naa aanaa

Reasons: 
- bढ़tii umr: prostet kaimsr 40 kii umr ke baad sbse jyaadaa hotaa hai। umr bढ़ne ke saath hii prostet glaimd bढ़ne lgtaa hai, jo kaimsr hone kii smbhaavnaa ko bढ़aataa hai। 50 saal kii umr paar kr rhe logom mem yh bhut tejii se phailtaa hai। prostet kaimsr (Prostate Cancer) ke hr 3 mem se 2 mriijom kii umr 65 yaa usse jyaadaa hotii hai।
- aanuvmshik biimaarii: prostet kaimsr aanuvmshik bhii hotaa hai। ghr mem agr kisii bhii vykti yaa rishtedaar ko prostet kaimsr hotaa hai to bchchom mem iskii hone kii smbhaavnaa jyaadaa hotii hai।
- khaanpaan: aadhunik jiivnshailii mem khaan-paan bhii prostet kaimsr ke phailne kaa prmukh kaarण bn gyaa hai। jo aadmii laal mms (red miit) yaa phir jyaadaa vsaayukt deyrii utpaadom kaa pryog krte haim, unmem prostet kaimsr hone kii smbhaavnaa jyaadaa hotii hai। jmk phood kaa sevn bhii prostet kaimsr hone kii smbhaavnaa ko bढ़aataa hai।
- dhoomrpaan : dhoomrpaan krne se muॅmh aur phephड़e kaa kaimsr to hotaa hai, lekin dhoomrpaan prostet kaimsr ko bhii bढ़aataa hai। 

Treatments:
prostet kaimsr kaa bchaav (Treatment of Prostate Cancer)

Home Remedies:
prostet kaimsr (Prostate cancer) buht jyaadaa sunne mem nhii aataa lekin yh ek khtrnaak biimaarii hai। haalmki iskaa ilaaj smbhv hai। ek umr ke baad aadmiyom mem prostet svbhaavik roop se bढ़ jaate haim। 50 kii umr ke baad lgbhg 40 phiisdii purooshom mem prostet kaimsr kii smbhaavnaaem ho jaatii haim।
haalmki yh jaanlevaa ho aisaa nhiim hai lekin ek sthiti ke baad yh khtrnaak bhii ho jaataa hai। yh jitne jyaadaa bढ़te haim inmem kaimsr kaa khtraa bhii utnaa hii hotaa hai kyomki prostet ke mdr maujood sels (jo kaimsr kaa bढ़aavaa dete haim) bhii prostet ke saaij ke anusaar bढ़ne lgte haim। iske lie kii ghreloo ilaaj bhii haim, jinhem apnaakr hm prostet kaimsr se bchaav kr skte haim।
1. adrk (Ginger)- adrk kii jड़ prostet kaimsr se bchaav ke lie behd prbhaavii hai। adrk mem emtiiphlemetrii, emtiiऑksiidemt aur emtiiproliphiretiv (antiproliferative) guण hote haim jo kaimsr ko bढ़aavaa dene vaale sels ko khtm kr dete haim। aise mem adrk khaanaa prostet kaimsr se bchaav aur aaraam donom de sktaa hai।
2. khoob pey pdaarth piiem (Drink lots of fluid)- dhyaan rhe ki aapko dihaaidreshn n hone paae। iske lie n kevl paanii khoob piinaa hai blki any heldii pey bhii aapkii bhut shaaytaa kr skte haim। sbjiyom aur phlom ke joos ke saath hii heldii soop bhii behd phaaydemmd haim।
3. tmaatr (Tomato)- tmaatr mem ektiv ttv laaikopiin (lycopene) hotaa hai jiske kaarण tmaatr mem emtiiऑksiidemt (antioxidant) kii maatraa bhii jyaadaa hotii hai। yh ttv kaimsr ko phailne aur bढ़ne se bhii roktaa hai। upchaar ke lie kchchaa tmaatr yaa tmaatr kii sॉs, chtnii, kaichap yaa slaad aur sbjii ke roop mem bhii khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
4. anaar (Pomegranate)- risrch mem bhii saabit ho chukaa hai ki prostet kaimsr se bchaane mem anaar behd phaaydemmd haim। yh ovr aal kaimsr se bhii bchaav krtaa hai। anaar mem maujood ttv kaimsr ko paidaa krne vaale sels ko maar dete haim jisse kaimsr nhiim hotaa। anaar ke daanom ko yoom hii khaayaa jaa sktaa hai yaa anaar kaa joos nikaalkr bhii piiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
