5. kddoo ke biij (Pumpkin seeds)- kddoo ke biij dyooretik (diuretic) roop se kaary krte haim jo ki kii biimaariyom mem laabhkaarii haim। khaaskr mootr aur prostet se smbmdhit rogom mem behd laabhkaarii haim। kddoo ke biijom mem bhut saa jimk (zinc) hotaa hai jo ki imyoonitii bढ़aane mem mdd krtaa hai, jisse prostet kaimsr se tejii se rikvrii smbhv hotii hai। upchaar ke lie kddoo ke biijom ko iktthaa krke unhem kchchaa hii khaaem। iske alaavaa in biijom kii chaay bnaakr bhii pii skte haim। is chaay ko laabh hone tk rojaanaa piiem।
6. soyaa (Soya)- soyaa mem saaytostrojn (phytoestrogen) hotaa hai jo ki testostiiron (testosterone) kaa straav tej krtaa hai। is kaarण prostet glaimd mem rkt smchaar tej hotaa hai jisse kaimsr paidaa krne vaale sels kii smkhyaa ghttii chlii jaatii hai।
7. vitaamin dii (Vitamin D)- vitaamin dii kii uchit maatraa hone se prostet kaimsr hone kaa khtraa nhiim rhtaa। yh n kevl prostet kaimsr se rkshaa krtaa hai blki hone ke baad isse upchaar bhii smbhv hai। phortiphaaid (fortified) daalem aur thmde paanii mem rhne vaalii mchhliym vitaamin dii kii achchhii strot hotii haim। iske saath hii aap vitaamin dii 3 ke spliimemt bhii le skte haim।
8. griin tii (Green tea)- griin tii ek aisii hrb hai jismem bhut se guण hote haim aur yh prostet kaimsr ke upchaar mem bhii shaayk hai। griin tii mem poliiphinols (polifenoles) uchit maatraa mem hote haim jo kaimsr paidaa krne vaale sels ko maar dete haim।
9. phaitii phish (Fatty fish)- phaitii phish omegaa 3 kii achchhii strot hotii hai, jo ki kaimsr se bchaav mem shaayk hai। iske alaavaa phlaik siid bhii omgaa 3 ke achchhe strot hote haim। shriir mem omegaa 3 kii maatraa bढ़aane ke lie phish ऑyl ke kaipsool spliimemt ke roop mem bhii lie jaa skte haim।


Disease: haipetaaitis (Hepatitis)

Description: 
livr shriir kaa ek mhttvpoorण mg hai। vh bhojn pchaane mem mhttvpoorण bhoomikaa nibhaataa hai। shriir mem hone vaalii chyaapchy kriyaaom (Metabolic Process) mem livr (Liver) vishesh shaaytaa krtaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- atydhik kmjorii v thkaan
- mkh, jiibh, mootr v tvchaa mem piilaapn
- paachn smsyaaom jaise ultii
- bhookh mem kmii
- chid़chid़aapn

Reasons: 
haipetaaitis ko saamaanyt: paanii se honii vaalii biimaarii maanaa jaataa hai jo poorii trh glt hai। dॉktrom ke anusaar nimn kaarणom se bhii haipetaaitis ho sktaa hai: 
haipetaaitis ke kaarण (Causes of Hepatitis)
- aanuvmshik,
- kuposhण,
- shraab,
- phaitii liivr

Treatments:
haipetaaitis se bchaav ke lie saaph-sphaaii behd aavshyk hai। khaane aur piine mem hmeshaa saaph chiijom ke pryog se isse bchaa jaa sktaa hai। haipetaaitis se bchaav ke any upaay nimn haim:
- livr ko svsth rkhne ke lie saaph-suthraa bhojn aur saaph paanii jroorii hai।
- baahr kaa khaanaa khaane se bchem, lekin khaanaa bhii pd़e to saaph-sphaaii dekhkr hii khaaem।
- haipetaaitis e (Hepatitis A Vaccine) kaa tiikaa jroor lgvaanaa chaahie।
- kisii doosre kii suii, rejr aur toothbrsh istemaal nhiim krnaa chaahie।
- rkt chdh़aane pr is baat kaa vishesh dhyaan rkhem ki nii suii ho aur rkt smkrmit n ho।
- adhik tel, ghii, hldii aur mirch msaale kaa bhojn n krem।
- hrii pttiidaar sbjiym khaaem, mausmii aur gnne kaa rs piem।
- naariyl paanii, chaavl, dhii yaa chhaachh, uble aaloo aur chhaine vaalaa rsgullaa khaaem।
- piilaa bukhaar
- liivr kaimsr   

Home Remedies:
hepetaaitis rog, liivr mem soojn aur jln (inflammation) ke kaarण hotaa hai। liivr shriir ko svsth rkhne mem mhtvpoorण kaary krtaa hai। poshk ttvom ko storej krne ke saath hii shriir mem oorjaa ke smchaar ko kmtrol krnaa aur kolestrॉl aadi kaa nirmaaण bhii liivr hii krtaa hai। liivr yaani gurde mem preshaanii tb aatii hai jb haanikaark pey yaa bhojn adhik maatraa mem khaayaa jaataa hai। shraab yaa any nshiile pdaarth liivr pr buraa asr daalte haim। isse imyoon sistm bhii kmjor ho jaataa hai। kii baar yh aanuvmshik smsyaa bhii ho sktii hai।
hepetaaitis ke lkshणom mem pet ke daayiim or ke hisse mem bhaariipn lgtaa hai, piiliyaa ho sktaa hai, thkaavt mhsoos hotii hai tthaa khujlii hotii hai। hepetaaitis kaa upchaar ghreloo saamgrii se bhii smbhv hai lekin sthiti agr kaaboo mem n aae to chikitsk ke paas jaanaa hii thiik hotaa hai। aaie aapko btaate haim hepetaaitis ke upchaar ke lie kuchh ghreloo upaayom ke baare mem-
1. ajvaayn aur jiiraa (Ajwain aur jeera)
ek chmmch ajvaayn aur ek chmmch jiiraa piiskr paaudr bnaa lem। ismem ek chutkii nmk milaaem। is choorn ko rojaanaa do baar khaaem। isse imyoonitii bढ़egii aur hepetaaitis mem aaraam hogaa।
2. likoris paaudr aur shhd (Liquorice powder and honey)
ek bड़aa chmmch likoris paaudr mem do chmmch shhd milaakr prtidin khaaem। hepetaaitis ke upchaar mem yh bhii behd phaaydemmd hai। iske saath hii likoris kii jड़ ko paanii mem ubaalkr uskii chaay bhii bnaaii jaa sktii hai।
3. lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun rkt ko saaph krtaa hai aur shriir se vishaakt pdaarthom ko baahr nikaaltaa hai aise mem rojaanaa subh khaalii pet lhsun kii ek se do klii chbaaem। saath hii khaanaa bnaane mem bhii lhsun kaa pryog msaale ke roop mem jroor krem।
4. hldii (Haldi)
hldii inphlememtrii (inflammatory) guणom se bhrpoor hotii hai। hldii kaa istemaal bhii hepetaaitis se rkshaa kr sktaa hai। hldii ko doodh mem daalkr piine se bhii bhut laabh hotaa hai। haalmki piiliyaa hone mem hldii lene kii mnaahii hotii hai।
5. kaalii gaajr (Black carrot)
kaalii gaajr ke bhii bhut phaayde haim। vitaamin se bhrpoor kaalii gaajr se khoon kii kmii poorii hotii hai tthaa rkt smchaar sudhrtaa hai। hepetaaitis mem bhii gaajr ko slaad ke roop mem khaane se bhut phaayde hote haim।
6. griin tii (Green tea)
griin tii yaani hrbl chaay guणom se bhrpoor hotii hai। griin tii mem emtiiऑksiidemt (antioxidant) hote haim jo shriir ke saath hii mstishk ko bhii svsth rkhte haim। hepetaaitis ke upchaar aur bchaav ke lie griin tii ko apnii dinchryaa mem shaamil krem।
7. mvlaa (Amla)
mvlaa vitaamin sii se bhrpoor hotaa hai jo liivr ko hr trh se phaaydaa phumchaataa hai। mvlaa kaa pryog chyvnpraash mem bhii kiyaa jaataa hai jisse imyoonitii bढ़e aur paachn shkti mjboot ho। aise mem mvlaa kaa pryog dainik aahaar mem bhii kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। mvlaa joos, chtnii, achaar aadi ko dainik aahaar mem shaamil krem।
8. alsii ke biij (Flax seed)
alsii ke biij shriir mem haarmon kaa smtuln donom bnaae rkhte haim aur unhem rkt mem shii triike se bhejne kaa kaam bhii krte haim। phlaiks siid mem saaytokmstiityooemts (phytoconstituents) hote haim jo ki haarmon kii baaimdimg kaa kaam krte haim aur liivr pr atirikt bhaar nhiim pड़ne dete। phlaiks siid ko yoom hii tost ke oopr, slaad me yaa daal aadi mem daalkr khaayaa jaa sktaa hai। yh liivr ko mjboot bnaane mem shaayk hai jisse hepetaaitis rog se bchaav hotaa hai।


Disease: piile dm~t (Yellow Teeth)

Description: 
dmt sirph hmem bhojn chbaane mem hii mdd nhiim krte, blki hmaare vyktitv ko bhii prbhaavit krte haim। saaph, svsth v sumdr dmt chehre kaa aakrshण hote haim। lekin agr dmt piile ho to yh shrmimdgii kaa bhii kaarण bn skte haim।

Symptoms: 
- piile dm~t

Reasons: 
dmtom mem piilaapn aanaa hmaare glt rhn-shn ke kaarण to kii baar saaph-sphaaii naa rkhne ke kaarण hotaa hai। kuchh any kaarण bhii haim  jinke kaarण dmt piile hote haim, jaise: 
piile dmtom kaa mukhy kaarण (Causes of Yellow teeth in Hindi)
- tmbaakoo, gutkaa, shraab aadi ke jyaadaa sevn krne se dmt piile ho skte haim। 
- kuchh logom mem umr bdh़ne ke saath-saath dmtom pr plaik kii prt chdh़tii jaatii hai। isse bhii dmt piile dikhne lgte haim। 
- jyaadaa maatr mem chaay, kॉphii aur kold drimk kaa sevn krne se bhii dmt piile hone lgte haim। 
- phlorosis : desh ke kii shhrom ke paanii mem phloraaid kii maatraa adhik hone ke kaarण dmtom kaa rmg bdrmg ho jaataa hai। unmem oopr piile evm sphed chiktte dikhaaii pड़te haim। 

Treatments:
agr dmtom ko saaph krne ke baad bhii dmtom se piilaapn naa jaae to nimn upchaar apnaane chaahie:
- vhaaitnr, shaainr aur vishesh kemikls ke jriye dmtom kii chmk aasaanii se lautaaii jaa sktii hai।
- demtl bliichimg se dmtom kaa piilaapn, piile-laal dhbbe, gutkaa, tmbaakoo aadi ke daag aasaanii se khtm kie jaa skte haim।
- piile dmtom ko sphed krne kaa ghreloo upchaar, bekimg sodaa hai। grm paanii mem bekimg sodaa milaa kr usse kullaa (Gargle) krem। jb mumh se paanii baahr nikaalem tb apne dmtom ko umgliyom se rgड़em, isse dmt chmk jaaemge।
- dmtom ko svsth rkhne ke lie phloraaid yukt toothpest aur mulaaym brsh se din mem do baar dmt saaph krne kii aadt daalem।
- iske saath jiibh kii sphaaii bhii krem, kyomki baiktiiriyaa jyaadaatr yhiim pnpte haim।
- din mem ek baar phlॉs bhii krem। isse dmtom ke biich phmse bhojn ke tukd़e nikl jaate haim।
- adhik grm chiijem n khaaem।
- jyaadaa kd़k brisl vaale brsh se dmt saaph n krem।
- mm~saahaarii khaanaa khaane ke baad kullaa jroor krem। isse dmtom mem phmse reshe bhii nikl jaaemge aur gmdh bhii।
- dmtom mem tkliiph n ho, tb bhii saal mem ek baar dmtom kaa chekap jroor kraaem।
- kuchh bhii khaane-piine ke baad saaph paanii se kullaa krem।
- jyaadaa puraanaa brsh msood़om aur dmtom ko nuksaan phumchaa sktaa hai, islie hr tiin mhiine mem brsh bdl lem।

Home Remedies:
sphed aur chmkte dmt kisii kii bhii prsnelitii mem nikhaar laa skte haim। bhut se log piile dmtom ke kaarण logom ke saamne hmsne se bchte haim yaa mumh pr haath rkhkr hmste haim। dmt jyaadaatr umr ke kaarण, dmtom kii thiik se sphaaii n hone ke kaarण, bhut jyaadaa chaay yaa kॉphii piine ke kaarण athvaa tmbaakoo aur sigret piine ke kaarण piile ho jaate haim।
kbhii kbhii kisii biimaarii ke kaarण bhii dmt piile ho jaate haim। haalmki piile dmtom ko sphed bnaanaa koii mushkil kaam nhiim hai। thoड़ii sii mehnt se aap piile dmtom ko sphed bnaa skte haim। aaie aapko kuchh ghreloo nuskhe btaate haim jo aapke dmto kii sphedii aur chmk ko bnaae rkhemge।
1. bekimg sodaa- (Baking Soda)
bekimg sodaa dmtom ko sphed bnaane kaa sbse aasaan triikaa hai। yh dmtom se plaak ko khtm krke dmtom kii sphedii aur chmk bnaae rkhtaa hai।
kaise upyog krem
- roj brsh krte smy apne pest mem thoड़aa saa bekimg paaudr daalem aur brsh krem। dmtom kii sphedii laut aaegii।
- ek kp paanii mem bekimg sodaa aur haaidrojn pr ऑksaaid (hydrogen peroxide) milaakr maauth vॉsh (mouthwash) kii trh bhii istemaal kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
2. smtre kaa chhilkaa- (Peel of Orange)
smtre ke chhilke se roj dmtom kii sphaaii krne se kuchh hii dinom mem piile dmt chmkne lgemge।
kaise upyog krem
- roj raat ko sote smy smtre ke chhilke ko dmtom pr rgड़em। smtre ke chhilke mem vitaamin sii (vitamin c) aur kailshiym ke saath maaikroऑrgenijm (micro organism) hotaa hai jo dmtom kii mjbootii aur chmk bnaae rkhtaa hai।
3. strॉberii- (Strawberry)
strॉberii mem bhii vitaamin sii prchur maatraa mem hotaa hai jo ki dmtom ko sphed bnaane mem shaayk hai।
kaise upyog krem
- strॉberii ke kuchh tukड़om ko piiskr, is lep ko dmtom pr lgaakr msaaj krem। ise din mem do baar krne se kuchh hii dinom mem piile dmt sphed hone lgte haim।
- bekimg sodaa aur strॉberii ke plp ko milaakr bhii dmtom pr rgड़ne se dmtom kaa piilaapn khtm hotaa hai।
4. niimboo- (Lemon)
niimboo ke praakृtik bliichimg (natural bleach) ke guण dmtom pr bhii asr dikhaate haim। piile dmtom ke lie niimboo ke chhilke ko dmtom pr rgड़aa jaa sktaa hai, yaa niimboo ke paanii se graare bhii kie jaa skte haim।
kaise upyog krem
- niimboo ke saath nmk milaakr dmtom kii msaaj krem।
- do hphtom tk rojaanaa do baar krne se dmt chmkne lgemge।
5. nmk- (Salt)
nmk ko puraane smy se hii dmto kii sphaaii ke lie istemaal kiyaa jaataa rhaa hai। yh dmtom ke khoe minrls lautaataa hai jisse dmtom kaa sphed rmg bnaa rhtaa hai।
kaise upyog krem
- rojaanaa subh toothpest kii trh nmk ko dmtom kii sphaaii ke lie istemaal kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। nmk ko chaarkol mem milaakr bhii dmtom kii sphaaii kii jaa sktii hai jisse dmt sphed hote haim।
- nmk aur bekimg paaudr milaakr bhii mmjn taiyaar kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
6. tulsii- (Basil)
tulsii mem bhii dmtom ko sphed bnaane kaa guण hotaa hai। iske saath hii tulsii paayriyaa aadi se bhii dmtom kii rkshaa krtii hai।
kaise upyog krem
- tulsii ke pttom ko sukhaakr paaudr bnaa lem। is paaudr ko rojaanaa istemaal krne vaale toothpest mem milaakr dmtom kii sphaaii krem।
- tulsii ke pttom kaa pest bnaakr usmem srsom kaa tel (mustard oil) milaaem। is pest se dmtom kii sphaaii krne pr bhii bhut phaaydaa hotaa hai।
7. seb- (Apple)
seb ko daait mem shaamil krne se bhii dmtom kii sphedii lautaaii jaa sktii hai। seb kii krmchiines dmtom ko praakृtik taur pr skrb krtii hai। rojaanaa ek yaa do seb jroor khaaem aur khoob chbaa chbaa kr khaaem। isii trh gaajr aur khiiraa bhii kchchaa khaane se dmt sphed tthaa mjboot bnte haim।


Disease: tii. bii. (Tuberculosis)

Description: 
tyoobrkyulosis (Tuberculosis) maaykobektiriym tyoobrkyulosis naamk jiivaaणu ke kaarण hotaa hai। tii.bii. rog ko any kii naam se jaanaa jaataa hai, jaise tpedik, kshy rog tthaa ykshmaa।

Symptoms: 
- agr aapkaa vjn, bgair koshish kiye huye, pichhle 2 mhiinom mem, 5 kilograam se adhik ght gyaa hai
- agr aapko khmsii mem khoon aataa hai
- agr aapko khmsii mem blgm aataa hai
- agr aapko tiin hphte se adhik se khmsii hai
- agr aapko bhookh km lgtii hai
- agr aapko raat mem adhik psiinaa aataa hai
- agr aapne apne blgm kaa kbhii tii bii kaa jmch krvaayaa hai, jise poज़itiv khaa gyaa ho

Reasons: 
tiibii  kii kaarणom se phailtaa hai lekin iske prmukh kaarणom mem apryaapt v apaushtik bhojn, km jgh mem adhik logom kaa rhnaa, gmdgii, gaay kaa kchchaa doodh piinaa aadi haim। iske any kaarण nimn haim: 
tiibii ke kaarण (Causes of Tuberculosis)
- tii bii ke mriij ke jhm-jhm thookne se iske vishaaणu svsth vykti ke shriir mem prvesh krke use rogii bnaa dete haim।
- kpड़aa mil mem kaam krne vaale shrmik yaa reshe-roe ke smprk mem rhne vaale log,
- bunkr, dhool ke smprk mem rhne vaale log tthaa mdherii kothriyom yaa chaalom mem rhne vaale log bhii is rog kaa shikaar ho jaate haim।
- mdiraapaan, dhoomrpaan tthaa roggrst pshu kaa mms khaane vaale log bhii tiibii kaa shikaar ho skte haim।
- asaavdhaaniivsh rogii kaa khoon any kisii rog ke shriir mem chढ़aane se vh vykti roggrst ho jaataa hai। 

Treatments:
tiibii kaa upchaar (Treatment of Tuberculosis in Hindi)
- ydi tiin athvaa adhik sptaah se khm~sii ho rhii ho to kफ़ kii do baar jm~ch kraaem। ye jm~ch srkaarii kफ़ sookshmdrshii kendrom pr ni:shulk kii jaatii hai।
- sbhii dvaaom ko niymit roop se, btaaii gii poorii avdhi tk lem।
- khm~ste yaa chhiimkte smy roomaal kaa pryog krem।

Home Remedies:
tiibii yaani tyoobrkulosis (Tuberculosis), ek prkaar kaa imphekshn hotaa hai jo ki maaykoiktiiriym tyoobrkulosis (mycobacterium tuberculosis) baiktiiriyaa ke kaarण phailtaa hai। tiibii adhiktr phephephड़om mem hotii hai lekin yh shriir ke kisii bhii hisse mem ho sktii hai। tiibii ke mriij ke kph mem khoon aanaa tiibii kaa aam lkshण hai iske alaavaa smsom kaa tej chlnaa, vjn kaa km honaa, bukhaar honaa, kidnii aur siine mem drd honaa aadi bhii tyoobrkulosis ke lkshण haim।
vaise to tiibii se poorii trh nijaat ke lie chikitsk se praamrsh aavshyk hai lekin kuchh ghreloo upchaarom ke dvaaraa bhii tiibii ko thiik krne kii prkriyaa tej kii jaa sktii hai। aaie aapko btaate haim tiibii ke upchaar ke lie kuchh ghreloo nuskhe-
1. lhsun (Garlic)- lhsun mem slphyoorik esid (sulphuric acid) prchur maatraa mem hotaa hai jo ki tiibii ke kiitaaणuom ko maarne mem skshm hai। iske saath hii lhsun mem eliisin (allicin) aur ejoinii (agoeni) bhii hote haim jo ki tiibii ke pnpne vaale kiitaaणuom kaa khtm krne kaa kaam krte haim। itnaa hii nhiim lhsun ke emtiibaiktiiriyl guण imyoonitii ko bhii bढ़aate haim।
kaise krem upyog
aadhii chmmch lhsun, ek kp doodh aur chaar kp paanii ko ek saath milaakr ubaalem। ise tb tk ubaalem jb tk yh mishrण ek chauthaaii rh jaae। is mishrण ko din mem tiin baar piiem।
grm doodh mem lhsun kaa rs milaakr bhii piiyaa jaa sktaa hai। iske baad paanii n piiem।
grm doodh mem lhsun ko ubaalem। iske baad lhsun ko chbaakr bche hue doodh ko pii lem।
2. kelaa (Banana)- kelaa poshk ttvom aur kailshiym kaa bhut achchhaa strot hai। yh tiibii ke mriij kaa imyoon sistm bdhaa़ne mem shaayk hai। iske saath hii bukhaar aur kph se bhii raaht detaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
ek pke hue kele ko ek kp naariyl ke paanii mem mslkr milaaem। iske baad ismem dhii aur shhd milaaem। ise din mem do baar khaaem।
kchche kele kaa joos bnaakr rojaanaa piiem।
kele ke tne kaa joos bnaakr bhii piiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
3. mvlaa (Amla)- mvlaa mem emtiiphlemetrii (anti inflammatory) aur emtiibaiktiiriyl (antibacterial) guण hote haim। jo shriir kaa imyoon sistm mjboot krke shriir ko oorjaa prdaan krte haim।
kaise krem upyog
mvlaa ke biij nikaalkr, joos bnaaem aur ismem ek chmmch shhd milaakr subh subh piiem।
4. smtraa (Orange)- smtre mem bhii jroorii minrls (minerals) aur kmpaaumd (compound) hote haim। smtre mem maujood slaain (salain) shriir ko imphekshn se bchaataa hai saath hii imyoon sistm ko mjboot krtaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
taajaa smtre ke rs mem thoड़aa saa nmk aur shhd milaakr rojaanaa subh shaam piiem। smtre ko chhiilkr uskii slaais pr bhii nmk chhiड़k kr khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
5. shriiphaa (Custard apple)- tiibii ke upchaar ke lie shriiphaa bhii behd phaaydemmd hai। shriiphe kaa plp nikaalkr ise khaanaa chaahie।
kaise krem upyog
do shriiphom kaa plp nikaalkr use paanii mem ubaal lem, iske saath pchchiis kishmish (kishmish) ko bhii ubaal lem। jb paanii ek tihaaii rh jaae tb ise chhaankr ismem paaudr shugr milaaem। is pey mem ilaaychii aur daalchiinii milaakr din mem do baar piiem।
6. kaalii mirch (Black pepper)- kaalii mirch phephड़om (lungs) kii sphaaii kaa kaam krtii hai। jisse tiibii ke dauraan hone vaale siine ke drd se raaht miltii hai। iske saath hii yh tiibii ke kiitaaणuom ko maarne kaa kaam bhii krtii hai।
kaise krem upyog
mkkhn mem aath se ds kaalii mirch phraaii krem। ismem ek chutkii hiimg milaaem aur paaudr bnaa lem। is mishrण ko tiin braabr bhaagom mem bmt lem। kuchh kuchh ghmte ke mtraal pr iskii ek ek doj khaaem।
7. akhrot (Walnut)- akhrot tiibii ke mriijom ko taakt detaa hai, unkii imyoonitii bढ़aataa hai aur jldii thiik hone mem bhii mdd krtaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
akhrot ke paaudr mem kuchh klii lhsun kii milaakr kuchl lem। ismem kleriiphaaid mkkhn (clarified butter) milaakr khaaem।
akhrot ko yoom bhii khaayaa jaa sktaa hai yaa iske paaudr ko slaad mem daalkr khaaem।
8. pudiinaa (Mint)- pudiinaa mem maujood emtiibaiktiiriyl (antibacterial) guणom ke kaarण ismem bhii tiibii ke rog ko thiik krne kaa adbhut guण hotaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
ek chmmch pudiine ke rs mem do chmmch shhd milaaem, iske saath hii is ghol mem maalt vinegr (malt vinegar) aur aadhaa kp gaajr kaa joos milaaem। is ghol ko kuchh kuchh ghmtom pr poore din piiem।


Disease: phroज़n sholdr (Frozen Shoulder)

Description: 
kmdhe kaa drd ek bhut hii aam shikaayt hai। aisaa maanaa jaataa hai ki kmdhom ke aaspaas jod़om mem soojn aane ke kaarण yh drd hotaa hai। aise drd mem kbhii-kbhaar kmdhe sunn bhii pd़ jaate haim। yh sthiti kii baar mhiinom tk rh jaatii hai।

Symptoms: 
- kmdhom kaa sunn pd़ jaanaa
- kmdhom ko ghumaane mem asmrthtaa mhsoos honaa
- raat mem kmdhom mem tiivr drd honaa

Reasons: 
- daaybitiij ke mriijom mem, hृdy smsyaa se grsit logom mem paarkisn biimaarii ke mriijom mem ho sktii hai।
- grdn mem hone vaalii srvaaikl disk kii smsyaa bhii aise drd kaa kaarण ho sktii hai।
- vo mriij, jinhem kmdhom pr kisii prkaar kii chot lgii ho yaa kmdhom kii kisii prkaar kii srjrii huii hai, unmem phrojn sholdr kii aashmkaa adhik hotii hai। 

Treatments:
kmdhom kii jkड़n mem aksr maalish yaa semk se aaraam miltaa hai। agr isse aaraam nhiim miltaa hai to nimn upaay apnaane chaahie:
- drd ko andekhaa n krem। yh lgaataar ho to dॉktr ko dikhaaem।
- saamaany kmdhom ke drd mem drd nivaark dvaaom se hii raaht mil jaatii hai। aisaa drd kmdhom mem soojn ke kaarण hotaa hai, islie soojn km krne vaalii dvaaem bhii raaht phumchaa sktii haim। lekin drd kii dvaaom kaa pryog kevl aapaat sthiti mem hii krem।
- kmdhom ko grm yaa thmdaa sek dem।
- drd se jld aaraam ke lie ekyoopmkchr chikitsaa kaa shaaraa le skte haim।
- phrojn sholdr kii chikitsaa kaa sbse achchhaa upaay phijiyotherepii (Physiotherapy) maanaa jaataa hai। phijiyotherepii mem kmdhom mem khimchaav utpnn kr kmdhom ko dobaaraa gtimaan bnaanaa hotaa hai। aisaa krne ke lie kmdhom ke vibhinn bimduom ko vyaayaam dvaaraa dhiire-dhiire saamaany sthiti mem laane kaa pryaas kiyaa jaataa hai।
- phrojn sholdr (Frozen Shoulder) kii chikitsaa smy pr nhiim kii gii to mriij ko pooraa jiivn is smsyaa ke saath bitaanaa pd़ sktaa hai।  


Disease: srvaaikl spॉndilaaitis (Cervical Sypondolysis)

Description: 
umr ke saath hddiyom mem ghisaav v bdlaav aa jaataa hai। yh grdn kii hddiyom mem bhii hotaa hai। hddiyom mem ghisaav, antr ho jaane yaa inke joड़ vaale bhaag kii mmspeshiyom mem soojn se grdn kaa drd yaani srvaaikl spmdaailosis (Cervical Spondolysis) hotaa hai। yh sb grdn kii us hddii mem hotaa hai jise srvaaikl spaain khte haim। riiढ़ kii hddii kaa grdn vaalaa yh bhaag merudणd (Spine) kii saat ksherookaaom (Vertebrae) evm unke mdhy kii disk se bntaa hai। grdn kii 85 prtisht gtividhiym~ oopr kii do ksherookaaom ke kaarण hotii hai। grdn ke drd se hone vaalii preshaanii ismem baadhaa phumchaatii haim। srvaaikl spmdaailosis phle 40 vrsh se adhik aayu ke logom ko hotaa thaa kintu vrtmaan smy kii jiivnchryaa evm aajiivikaa ne bchche aur bड़om sbhii ko grdn mem drd kaa mriij bnaa diyaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- grdn mem akd़n,
- grdn ghumaane mem cht kii aavaaj aanaa
- grdn ghumaane mem dikkt
- chkkr aanaa
- drd v bhaariipn
- nsom mem khimchaav se haathom mem kmpn aadi lkshण dikhte hai
- sir ke piichhe bhaag mem drd
- haathom kaa sunn pड़ jaanaa, jaan n rhnaa

Reasons: 
- sote smy mote tkie kaa upyog iskaa ek kaarण hai।
- baithne kii glt sthiti ke kaarण, lmbe smy tk ek jaisii sthiti mem baithnaa। kmpyootr pr jyaadaa der tk kaam krne vaale vykti, dmt chikitsk, vaahn chaalk, helmet dhaark aadi ko yh any logom kii apekshaa jyaadaa hotaa hai।
- vidyaarthii evm aise vykti jo bhaarii baig piith yaa kmdhe pr ltkaae rhte haim, ve isse piiड़it hote haim।
- kisii chot yaa phraikchr ke kaarण yh drd hotaa hai।
- kuchh any rogom mem bhii yh drd prkt hotaa hai।
- ek jaisii sthiti mem lgaataar tiivii, kmpyootr, viidiyo gem aadi ke upyog se hotaa hai।

Treatments:
- grdn evm kmdhe kaa vyaayaam niymit krem।
- shii sthiti mem baithem।
- pair jmiin pr evm piith kursii ke pृshth bhaag pr siidhii rkhem।
- jhukkr yaa ek jaisii sthiti mem lgaataar kaam n krem।
- biich-biich mem kmdhe, grdn ko ghumaaem।
- mote tkie v msnd kaa upyog km yaa bmd kr dem।
- grdn ke drd vaale bhaag kii grm kpड़e se sikaaii krne yaa brph ghisne se drd thiik ho jaataa hai, phir bhii drd bnaa rhe to hddii rog visheshjञ se milem aur upchaar laabh lem।

Home Remedies:
srvaaikl spmdlaaitis (cervical spondylosis) ko grdn kii gthiyaa (neck arthritis) ke naam se bhii jaanaa jaataa hai। is rog mem grdn ke joड़ mem drd kii shikaayt rhtii hai। yh joड़ kaartilej, ootk aur srvaaikl spaain mem juड़e rhte haim। 
srvaaikl spmdlaaitis adhiktr umr bढ़ne ke saath hone lgtaa hai lekin kii dphaa grdn pr dbaav pड़ne, baithne-uthne ke glt poshchr se, dhoomrpaan krne, vjn ke bhut jyaadaa hone, jenetik kaarणom aur aalsii rhn shn se bhii shuroo ho sktaa hai। haalmki kuchh ghreloo upaay apnaakr srvaaikl spondiiloysis kaa upchaar smbhv hai। aaie jaante haim kuchh aise hii upchaarom ke baare mem-
1. niymit vyaayaam (Daily excersise)- niymit vyaayaam n krnaa bhii srvaaikl spmdlaaitis hone kaa bड़aa kaarण hai। niymit vyaayaam se grdn ke drd ko km kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। 
(ydi kisii bhii trh ke vyaayaam se drd bढ़ jaae to vyaayaam ko chhoड़ dem)
2. grm aur thmdii sikaaii (Hot and cold fomentation)- grdn drd se nijaat ke lie grdn kii grm aur thmdii sikaaii krne se bhii bhut aaraam miltaa hai। grm sikaaii krne se rkt smchaar behtr hotaa hai vhiim thmdii sikaaii se soojn aur chubhn km hotii hai।
kaise krem upchaar-
grm sikaaii ke lie grm paanii kii botl ko tauliyaa mem lpet kr grdn kii sikaaii krem।
thmdii sikaaii krne ke lie brph (ice) ke tukड़om ko tauliyaa mem lpetkr, us tauliyaa se sikaaii krem।
sikaaii krte vkt km se km do se tiin mint tk grdn kii lgaataar sikaaii honii chaahie।
15 se 20 mint mem dobaaraa dohraaem। is vidhi ko aaraam hone tk din mem do baar krem।
3. lhsun (Garlic)- ydi srvaaikl spmdlaaitis ke lkshण njr aaem to lhsun kaa istemaal behd achchhe priणaam de sktaa hai। iske aushdhiiy guण grdn ke drd, soojn aur jln ko thiik krte haim। 
kaise krem upchaar-
lhsun kii do klii hr subh khaalii pet paanii ke saath khaaem।
khaanaa bnaane vaale kisii bhii tel mem lhsun kii kuchh kliym daal kr bhoon lem। is tel ko gungunaa hone tk thmdaa krem aur prbhaavit hisse kii maalish krem। is vidhi ko din mem do baar kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
4. hldii (Haldi)- hldii ke aushdhiiy guण kisii se chhipe nhiim hai lekin achchhii baat yh bhii hai ki yh srvaaikl spmdlaaitis ke drd mem bhii utnii hii prbhaavii hai। hldii rkt smchaar tej krke grdn ke drd se aaraam detii hai aur grdn kii akड़n ko bhii km krtii hai।
kaise krem upchaar-
ek chmmch hldii ko doodh mem daalkr ubaalem aur thmdaa hone pr ismem shhd milaaem, ise din mem do baar piiem।
5. til (sesame seed)- srvaaikl spmdlaaitis ke upchaar ke lie aayurved kii best aushdhi hai til। ismem kailshiym, maigniishiym, maigniij, kॉpr, jimk, phॉsphors aur vitaamin ke (vitamin k) tthaa dii (vitamin d) prchur maatraa mem paae jaate haim। isii kaarण yh hddiyom ke saath saath poore shriir ke lie phaaydemmd hai।
kaise krem upchaar-
til ke tel ko gungunaa krke lgbhg 10 mint prbhaavit hisse kii msaaj krem। is kriyaa ko dinbhr mem tiin se chaar baar krem।
grm siism ke tel mem kuchh boomde levemdr ke tel kii daalkr bhii msaaj kii jaa sktii hai।
til ko hlkaa saa bhoonkr roj subh chbaaem। iske alaavaa grm doodh mem bhune hue til daalkr bhii piiyaa jaa sktaa hai। ek din mem lgbhg do gilaas doodh piiem।
6. adrk (Ginger)- srvaaikl spmdlaaitis ke ilaaj ke lie adrk bhii behtriin prbhaav dikhaataa hai। yh rkt smchaar (blood circulation) ko tej krtaa hai jisse grdn ke drd se raaht miltii hai।
kaise krem upchaar-
ek din mem lgbhg tiin kp adrk kii chaay piiem। adrk kii chaay bnaane ke lie paanii mem adrk ubaalem aur thmdaa krke ismem shhd milaaem। is pey ko piiem।
prbhaavit hisse kii adrk ke tel se msaaj bhii kii jaa sktii hai।
7. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)- seb saaidr sirkaa bhii srvaaikl spmdlaaitis se raaht dene mem bhut achchhaa asr dikhaatii hai। yh grdn ke drd aur soojn se raaht detaa hai।
kaise krem upchaar-
kisii kpड़e ko se saaidr sirkaa mem bhigokr prbhaavit sthaan pr lpetem aur kuchh ghmtom ke lie chhoड़ dem। din mem do baar is vidhi ko krem।
do kp seb ke sirke ko gungune paanii mem daalkr nhaayaa bhii jaa sktaa hai। 
ek gilaas paanii mem kchchaa seb kaa sirkaa aur shhd milaakr piine se bhii laabh hotaa hai।


Disease: vaakvikaar (Dyslexia)

Description: 
disleksiyaa koii biimaarii nhiim hai aur n hii yh koii maansik ayogytaa hai। disleksiyaa (Dyslexia) pdh़ne-likhne se smbmdhii ek vikaar hai, jismem bchchom ko shbdom ko phchaanne, pdh़ne, yaad krne aur bolne mem preshaanii aatii hai। ve kuchh akshrom aur shbdom ko ultaa pdh़te haim aur kuchh akshrom kaa uchchaarण bhii nhiim kr paate। unkii pढ़ne kii rphtaar aur bchchom kii apekshaa kaaphii km hotii hai ।

Symptoms: 
- agr aapkaa bchchaa inmem se ek yaa do preshaaniyom se gujr rhaa hai aur vo sthaayii smsyaa nhiim hom to thod़ii mdd se hii bchche ko raaht mil sktii hai, chaahe vo ghr pr kii gii mdd ho yaa kkshaa mem
- uchchaarण saaph nhiim honaa
- uttejit rhnaa
- kvitaa vaale shbdom mem dikkt
- kaaphii thkaa honaa yaa ekaagrtaa (ek chiij़ pr dhyaan lgaane) mem kmii
- gintii, shbd, din aur mhiinom ke naam smjhne mem dikkt
- daaem aur bme mem mtr smjhne mem dikkt honaa
- dishaa aur nirdesh smjhne mem preshaanii
- doosre bchchom ke mukaable der se bolnaa shuru krnaa
- nmbrom ke krm aur gणit ke chinhom mem uljhn
- nii chiijem siikhne mem derii
- pdh़aaii ke dauraan shbdom kii gltiym lgaataar krnaa
- praaimrii pdh़aaii ke dauraan lkshण pdh़ne
- baatchiit krne mem dikkt
- binaa soch vichaar ke kaary krnaa yaa kisii kaary ko krne yojnaa nhiim bnaanaa
- ydi ghr pr aap apne bchche ke vyvhaar ke baare mem strk haim to shikshkom se jaankaarii liijie ki kyaa skool mem bhii vo aisaa hii vyvhaar krtaa hai.
- logom se bolchaal krne mem dikkt, apne aaspaas kii chiijom ke prti asmvednshiiltaa jiske kaarण durghtnaa kii smbhaavnaa bnii rhtii hai
- vrणmaalaa aur smkhyaa ko siikhne mem dikkt honaa
- shbdom aur dhvni ke mel ko kaaphii der se smjhnaa
- shbdom kaa mtlb smjhne mem derii, jyaadaatr shii shbdom ko nhiim pkd़ paanaa
- shbdom kii phchaan mem dikkt jaise (b/d), ulte (m/w), milte julte (felt/left) aur vaiklpik (house/home) shbd
- smy ke baare mem yaad rkhne kii kmii
- skool se phle ke lkshण

Reasons: 
- vmshaanugt (Herediatary), yh tmtrikaa tmtr (Nervous System) kii smsyaa hai, jo jnm poorv kaarkom pr nirbhr krtii haim। 
- maataa ke smtulit aahaar kii kmii, dhoomrpaan kaa sevn bhii iske kaarण ho skte haim।
- bchchom mem kuposhण bhii iskaa ek bd़aa kaarण hai।

Treatments:
- kuchh kes mem bchche ke jnm se phle hii disleksiyaa kaa mdaajaa lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai। aise mem dॉktr un grbhvtii mhilaaom ko paushtik aahaar lene kii slaah ke saath saath kuchh vishesh dvaaom se smbmdhit slaah dete haim।
- jin maamlom mem jnm ke baad disleksiyaa kaa ptaa lgtaa hai, un bchchom ko jyaadaa smy dekr smbhaalaa jaa sktaa hai। in bchchom kii smjh dhiimii hotii hai, islie inhem jyaadaa smy dene kii aavshyktaa hotii hai।
- disleksiyaa se piiड़it bchchom ke saath apnaa pdh़ne kaa apnaa triikaa bdlem, chiijom ko aasaan krke btaaem, tod़-tod़kr smjhaaem। chitrom aur khaaniyom kaa shaaraa lem। jin akshrom ko phchaanne aur likhne mem smsyaa hotii hai, unhem baar-baar likhvaae।
- vokeshnl trenimg kraaem।


Disease: pittaashy kii pthrii (Gallstones)

Description: 
pittaashy (Gall Bladder) pitt (Bile) bhmdaarण ke lie ek chhotii sii thailii hai (pitt jigr dvaaraa utpaadit ek paachk rs hai jo khaane mem maujood vsaa ke tootne mem pryog kiyaa jaataa hai)। pittaashy mem vsaayukt khaady pdaarthom kii maatr adhik hone se pittaashy kii pthrii (kolestrॉl, pitt vrणk aur kailshiym lvण se bnaa chhotaa saa ptthr) kaa nirmaaण hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- drd chhaatii, kmdhe, grdn mem bhii phail sktaa hai
- pet aur piith mem achaank drd uthnaa
- vsaayukt bhojn khaane ke baad pet ke drd mem tejii aanaa,   piiliyaa, bukhaar

Reasons: 
- pitt mem kolestrॉl kii atydhiktaa (Over Saturation)
- pitt mem lesithin
- aur pitt lvण kii km aapoorti (Undersupply)।  

Treatments:
pittaashy kii pthrii kisii bhii smsyaaom kaa kaarण nhiim hai lekin ydi pittaashy kii pthrii smkrmण paidaa kr rhaa hai to aapreshn jroorii hai।

Home Remedies:
assii phiisdii pitt kii thailii kii pthrii kolestrॉl (cholestrol) ke jmne yaa skht hone ke kaarण hotii hai। pitt kii pthrii ke kaarण pet mem ashniiy drd hotaa hai, kii baar ultii (vomit) bhii ho sktii hai। rogii kaa khaanaa pchne mem dikkt hone lgtii hai jisse pet mem apch (indigestion) aur bhaariipn rhtaa hai।
pitt kii thailii mem pthrii hone ke baare mem yhii khaa jaataa hai ki binaa ऑpreshn ke ise nikaalnaa mushkil hai। aise mem ydi aapko gॉl bledr ston kii shikaayt hai to jaahir hai aapne bhii ऑpreshn kaa vichaar bnaayaa hogaa, lekin ऑpreshn se phle kuchh ghreloo upaay apnaakr dekhem, smbhv hai ki pthrii gl jaae। kuchh ghreloo upaay n kevl pthrii ko glaa demge blki paachn ko duroost krke drd ko bhii thiik kr demge। aaie jaante haim, aise hii ghreloo upaayom ke baare mem।
1. seb kaa joos aur seb kaa sirkaa (Apple and Apple cider vinegar)- seb mem pitt kii pthrii ko glaane kaa guण hotaa hai, lekin ise joos ke roop mem seb ke sirke ke saath lene pr yh jyaadaa asrkaarii hotaa hai। seb mem maujood mailik esid (mallic acid) pthrii ko glaane mem mdd krtaa hai tthaa seb kaa sirkaa livr mem kolestrॉl nhiim bnne detaa, jo pthrii bnne ke lie jimmedaar hotaa hai। yh ghol n kevl pthrii ko glaataa hai blki dobaaraa bnne se bhii roktaa hai aur drd se bhii raaht detaa hai।
upchaar ke lie- ek gilaas seb ke joos mem, ek chmmch seb kaa sirkaa milaaem। is joos ko rojaanaa din bhr mem do baar piiem।
2. naashpaatii kaa joos (Pear juice)- naashpaatii ke aakaar kii pitt kii thailii ko naashpaatii dvaaraa hii saaph kiyaa jaanaa smbhv hai। naashpaatii mem maujood paiktin (pectene) kolestrॉl (cholesterol) ko bnne aur jmne se roktaa hai। yoom bhii naashpaatii guणom kii khaan hai jiske kii svaasthy laabh haim।
upchaar- ek gilaas grm paanii mem, ek gilaas naashpaatii kaa joos aur do chmmch shhd (honey) milaakr piiem। is joos ko ek din mem tiin baar piinaa chaahie।
3. chukmdr, khiiraa aur gaajr kaa joos (Beetroot, Cucumber and carrot juice)- joos therepii ko pitt kii thailii ke ilaaj ke lie ghreloo upchaarom mem sbse jyaadaa istemaal kiyaa jaataa hai। chukmdr n kevl shriir kaa mjbootii detaa hai blki gॉl bledr ko saaph bhii krtaa hai saath hii livr ke kolon (colon) ko bhii saaph krtaa hai। khiiraa mem maujood jyaadaa paanii kii maatraa livr aur gॉl bledr donom ko ditॉksiiphaaii (detoxify) krtii hai। gaajr mem bhii vitaamin sii aur uchch poshk ttv (high nutrient) hone ke kaarण yhii guण hote haim।
upchaar- ek chukmdr, ek khiiraa aur chaar gaajr ko lekr joos taiyaar krem। is joos ko prtidin do baar piinaa hai। joos mem prtyek saamgrii kii maatraa braabr honii chaahie, islie sbjii yaa phl ke saaij ke hisaab se maatraa ghtaaii yaa bढ़aaii jaa sktii hai।
4. pudiinaa (Mint)- pudiinaa ko paachn ke lie sbse achchhii ghreloo aushdhi (home remedy) maanaa jaataa hai jo pitt vaahikaa tthaa paachn se smbmdhit any rsom ko bढ़aataa hai। pudiinaa mem taarpiin (terpenes) bhii hotaa hai jo ki pthrii ko glaane mem shaayk maanaa jaataa hai। pudiine kii pttiyom se bnii chaay gॉl bledr ston se raaht de sktii hai।
upchaar- paanii ko grm krem, ismem taajii yaa sookhii pudiine ke pttiyom ko ubaalem। hlkaa gungunaa rhne pr paanii ko chhaankr ismem shhd milaaem aur pii lem। is chaay ko din mem do baar piiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
5. khaan-paan aur dinchryaa mem bdlaav (Changes in diet and daily activity)
rojaanaa 8 se 10 gilaas paanii jroor piiem। chaahe pyaas n bhii lgii ho।
vsaayukt yaa tej msaale vaale khaane se bchem।
prtidin kॉphii jroor piiem। bhut jyaadaa bhii nhiim lekin din mem ek se do kp kaaphii haim। kॉphii bhii pitt vaahikaa ko bढ़aatii hai jisse pitt kii thailii mem pthrii nhiim hotii।
apne khaane mem vitaamin sii kii maatraa bdhaaem। dinbhr mem jitnaa jyaadaa smbhv ho vitaamin sii se bhrpoor chiijem khaaem।
hldii, saumth, kaalii mirch aur hiimg ko khaane mem jroor shaamil krem।


Disease: rebiij (Rabies)

Description: 
rebiiज़ ek nyooro invesiv (Neuro-Invasive) vaayrl biimaarii hai। rebiiज़ kaa vaayrs tmtrikaa tmtr yaani semtrl nrvs sistm (Central Nervous System) pr ataik krtaa hai, jisse piiड़it vykti saamaany nhiim rh paataa।

Symptoms: 
- gle kii mms peshiyom mem khimchaav paidaa ho jaataa hai
- piiड़it vykti kutte kii trh bhaumkne bhii lgtaa hai
- bechainii, mshik pkshaaghaat, bhrm, anidraa aur niglne mem kthinaaii aadi kuchh any lkshण haim
- rebiij kaa shikaar bne jaanvrom kaa dimaagii smtuln bigड़ne lgtaa hai
- rebiij ho jaane pr mriij paanii se drne lgtaa hai

Reasons: 
rebiij pshuom ke kaatne ke kaarण hotaa hai। paaltoo jaanvr, kutte, billii yaa chmkaadड़ ke kaatne se sbse adhik rebiiज़ hotaa hai। 

Treatments:
rebiij se bchaav ke lie jroorii hai iske baarem mem jaankaarii honaa। rebiiज़ (Rabies) aksr pshuom ke kaatne ke kaarण hotaa hai, saath hii aise mem is baat kaa dhyaan rkhnaa chaahie ki yh sirph kaatne hii nhiim chhilne ke kaarण bhii hotaa hai। rebiiज़ hone pr nimn baatom kaa dhyaan rkhnaa chaahie:
- pshuom ke kaatne pr kaate ge sthaan ko paanii v saabun se achchhii trh dho denaa chaahie।
- dhone ke baad kaate ge sthaan pr achchhii trh se timchr yaa povodiin aayodin lgaanaa chaahie। aisaa krne se kutte yaa any pshuom kii laar mem paae jaane vaale kiitaaणu sirotaaipvn laaysaa vaayrs kii gyaalkoprotin kii prtem ghul jaatii haim। isse rog kii maar ek bड़e hd tk km ho jaatii hai, jo rogii ke bchaav mem shaayk hotii hai।
- iske turmt baad rogii ko titens kaa imjekshn lgvaakr chikitsaaly mem le jaanaa chaahie। yhm~ chikitsk kii slaah se kaate ge sthaan pr kaarbolik esid lgaayaa jaataa hai, jisse adhiktm kiitaaणu nsht ho jaate haim।
- iske baad chikitsk kii slaah pr aavshyktaanusaar imjekshn lgaae jaate haim, jo tiin yaa ds din kii avdhi ke hote haim।
- ttpshchaat aavshyktaanusaar nishchit dinom pr bustr doj bhii die jaane kaa praavdhaan hai, jo chikitsk ke vivek v kaate ge pshu kii jiivit yaa mृt hone kii avsthaa pr nirbhr krte haim।
- imjekshn lgaane kii krmbddhtaa mem laaprvaahii ghaatk siddh ho sktii hai।
- is rog kaa prkop pshu ke kaatne ke tiin din ke baad v tiin vrsh ke bhiitr kbhii bhii ho sktaa hai। 

Home Remedies:
raibiij vaayrs se phailne vaalii biimaarii hai jo ki mnushy ke dimaag aur spaainl kord (spinal cord) ko prbhaavit krtii hai। ydi raibiij ke lkshण ubhrne se phle iskaa ilaaj n kiyaa jaae to vykti kii maut bhii ho sktii hai। aise jaanvr jo is vaayrs se aphekted (affected) hote haim, unke slaaivaa (salaiva) yaa dimaagii ootkom (brain membrane) se yh vaayrs doosre logom mem phail jaataa hai। yh biimaarii mnushyom ke saath hii any any stndhaariyom mem bhii ho sktii hai।
jaanvrom  ke kaatne, chaatne, khromch lgaane yaa kisii jkhm ko chaatne se bhii raibiij phail sktii hai। aise mem kisii bhii jaanvr ke smprk mem aane se phle saavdhaan rhnaa chaahie tthaa sbhii paaltoo jaanvrom ko jroorii tiike avshy lgvaane chaahie। aaie aapko btaate haim aise upaay, jinhem apnaakr raibiij se bchaa jaa sktaa hai।
1. paanii aur saabun (water and soap)
ydi kisii jaanvr ke smprk mem aane pr aapko lgtaa hai ki raibiij imphekted thaa, to sbse phle prbhaavit hisse ko paanii aur phir saabun se achchhii trh dhoem। ydi jaanvr ne kaataa ho yaa aapke jkhm pr khromchaa ho to bilkul bhii laaprvaahii n krem। saabun aur paanii se dhone ke baad turmt chikitsk se milem।
2. akhrot (walnut)
akhrot mem kutte dvaaraa hone vaalii raibiij ke jhr ko maarne kii kshmtaa hotii hai। upchaar ke lie akhrot, pyaaj aur nmk kii braabr maatraa lekr piis lem। is mitrण mem thodaa़ shhd milaaem। prbhaavit hisse yaa ghaav pr yh lep lgaaem।
3. levemdr (lavander)
jaanvr ke kaatne ke sthaan pr yaa raibiij prbhaavit hisse pr levemdr ko piis kr lep lgaane se bhii imphekshn se bchaa jaa sktaa hai।
4. lhsun (garlic)
lhsun mem praakृtik taur pr emtiibaayetik (antibiotic) guण hote haim। raibiij ke ghaav ko jldii bhrne ke lie din mem tiin baar lhsun kii klii chbaaem।
5. jiiraa (cumin)
kutte ke kaatne se phailne vaalii raibiij pr jiiraa bhii kaaphii asr dikhaataa hai। do bड़e chmmch jiiraa ko piiskr usmem biis kaalii mirch piiskr milaaem। donom paaudr mem paanii milaakr lep bnaaem aur prbhaavit hisse pr lgaaem। isse bhii ghaav jldii bhrne mem mdd milegii।
6. vitaamin sii (vitamin c)
ydi aap raibiij se imphekted haim to apne aahaar mem vitaamin sii kii maatraa bढ़aaem। iske lie amrood (guawa), laal mirch (red pepper), kiivii (kiwi), phool gobhii (cauli flower), smtraa aur niimboo aadi lem। vitaamin sii spliimemt bhii le skte haim।
7. vitaamin bii (vitamin b)
raibiij ke imphekshn se bchne ko vitaamin bii bhii bhut laabhkaarii hai। raibiij ke upchaar ke lie apne aahaar mem aise bhojn ko shaamil krem jismem vitaamin bii prchur maatraa mem ho। aise khaady pdaarthom ke lie aap bmdgobhii (cabbage), tmaatr, rspbairii, trbooj, anaanaas (pine apple) aur paalk aadi le skte haim। iske alaavaa vitaamin bii ke spliimemt lenaa bhii phaaydemmd hotaa hai।
not- yh sbhii upchaar ghreloo haim। inmem se kuchh upchaar jaanvr ke kaatne ke turmt baad dॉktr ke paas phumchne kii derii kii avsthaa mem phle kie jaa skte haim, taaki imphekshn jyaadaa n bढ़e yaa avsthaa ghaatk n ho। saath hii kuchh upchaar ilaaj ke dauraan lgaataar kie jaa skte haim। lekin raibiij hone kii sthiti mem chikitsk ke paas jaanaa jroorii hai, ghreloo upchaar atirikt laabh ke lie haim।


Disease: jukaam (Common Cold)

Description: 
jukaam vishaaणuom (vaayrs) dvaaraa phailaayaa jaane vaale smkrmण hai jo khaaskr hmaare sms prणaalii ke aage vaale hisse ko prbhaavit krtaa hai। jukaam shriir kii rog-prtirodhk kshmtaa kaa prichaayk hai।

Symptoms: 
- m~kh se paanii bhnaa
- kaan mem drd honaa
- gle mem drd honaa
- naak se paanii bhnaa
- srdrd honaa
- hraart mhsoos honaa

Reasons: 
- hvaa mem maujood baiktiiriyaa yaa vaayrs jb kbhii sms ke jrie shriir mem prvesh krte haim, to elrjii ho jaatii hai। ntiijaa yh hotaa hai ki paanii yaa blgm naak se baahr aane lgte haim।
- hmaare gle mem do trh ke baiktiiriyaa maujood hote haim - kuchh achchhe aur kuchh bure। kbhii-kbhii srdii-grmii bdh़ne, ekdm thmdaa-grm khaane, thmde se grm v grm se thmde maahaul mem jaane, thmdaa paanii jyaadaa piine yaa baarish mem bhiigne se gle ke bure baiktiiriyaa skriy ho jaate haim। ye baiktiiriyaa hii gle mem inphekshn kr dete haim aur jukaam (Jukam) kii vjh bnte haim। 

Treatments:
jukaam ek svbhaavik kriyaa maanii jaatii hai। agr kuchhek din mem yh apne aap thiik ho jaae to ise biimaarii nhiim maanaa jaataa lekin adhik din rhne pr iskaa upchaar kraanaa jroorii hotaa hai। jukaam ke kuchh khaas upaay nimn haim:
- saadhaarण jukaam apne aap pmch din mem thiik ho jaataa hai।
- agr blgm sphed ho to yh elrjii kii nishaanii hai। yh saadhaarण jukaam hotaa hai।
- jukaam ko pmch din se jyaadaa ho jaaem yaa saath mem khmsii, blgm, bdn drd v bukhaar bhii ho, to smjhnaa chaahie ki aam jukaam nhiim hai।
- agr blgm piilaa ho ho v sms kii dikkt ke saath bukhaar bhii ho to baiktiiriyl imphekshn hotaa hai।
- aise mem dॉktr ke paas jaanaa chaahie।
- agr kफ़ ke saath khoon bhii aae to chimtaajnk baat hai। yh tii.bii. kaa lkshण ho sktaa hai। aise mem turnt dॉktr se praamrsh lem।  

Home Remedies:
jukaam smkrmण (Infection) kaa ek prkaar hai jo ki vaayrs ke vibhinn prkaar ke kaarणom se ho sktaa hai। sir drd, naak bhnaa, khmsii, tej bukhaar, m~khom mem jln, gle mem khraash (Sore throat) aur shriir mem drd (Body pain) aadi saamaany jukaam ke kuchh lkshण haim। jukaam se raaht ke lie kii ghreloo upchaar haim jo ki jukaam kii smsyaa se raaht de skte haim।
 yh ghreloo upchaar kisii bhii dushprbhaav ke binaa srdii ke vibhinn lkshणom se prbhaavii raaht prdaan krte haim।
1. lhsun (Garlic)
 - lhsun kaa jiivaaणurodhii aur emtiivaayrl (antiviral) guण srdii ke lkshणom se chhutkaaraa praapt krne mem bhut shaayk hotaa hai। lhsun prtirkshaa prणaalii (immunity) ke lie achchhaa hai aur shvsn maarg (respiratory process) ko kholne mem mdd krtaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
- ek kp paanii mem lhsun kii klii, do chmmch niimboo kaa rs, ek chmmch shhd, aur aadhaa chmmch laal mirch yaa laal mirch paaudr milaaem। ise tb tk roj khaaem jb tk srdii jukaam se aaraam naa ho।
- ek kp paanii mem 4-5 kte hue lhsun kii klii ubaal lem aur ek chmmch shhd daalem। ise din mem do se tiin baar sevn krem।
2. shhd (Honey)
 - shhd mem maujood emjaaim (enzyme) mem, uchch maatraa mem baiktiiriyaa aur vaayrs ko maarne ke guण hote haim। shhd se gle kaa sookhaapn door hotaa hai aur jukaam jldii thiik ho jaataa hai।
kaise krem upyog
- sbse srl upaay ghr pr ek chmmch niimboo kaa rs aur do chmmch shhd milaaem। thmdk aur gle mem khraash se raaht paane ke lie hr do ghmte mem lem।
 ydi aap chaahem, to ek chmmch kchchaa shhd bhii khaa skte haim।
3. msaalaa chaay (Masala chai)
 - kichn mem rkhe msaalom se bnii chaay jukaam mem bhut jldii raaht detii hai।
kaise krem upyog 
 - ek chauthaaii kp sookhaa bhune hue dhniyaa biij piiskr ismem aadhaa chmmch jiiraa aur saumph ke biij aur ek chauthaaii chmmch methii ke biij milaaem। ab ek kp paanii ubaal lem aur ismem aadhaa chmmch taiyaar msaalaa aur aadhaa chmmch mishrii daalem। tiin se chaar mint ubaalem। iske baad doodh daalem aur grm grm piiem।
4. adrk (ginger) 
 - adrk apne emtiivaayrl, espektrent (expectorant) guणom ke kaarण srdii se raaht detaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
- kchchaa adrk khaane yaa ek din mem adrk kii chaay kii baar piine se laabh hotaa hai। adrk kii chaay ke prbhaav ko bdh़aane ke lie, chaay mem niimboo kaa rs aur shhd milaaem।
- adrk, laumg aur nmk kaa ek pest taiyaar krem। aadhaa chmmch khaa skte haim।
- naak bh rhii ho to braabr maatr mem sookhaa adrk paaudr (Dry ginger powder) mkkhn yaa ghii aur gud़ (jaggary) milaakr chhotii chhotii golii bnaaem। subh rojaanaa khaalii pet ek golii khaaem।
5. laal pyaaj kaa siirp (Syrup of red onion)  
 - ghr ke bne laal pyaaj siirp se bhii srdii se piid़it logom ko raaht miltii hai।
kaise krem upyog
- 2-3 laal pyaaj ko baariik gol tukड़om mem kaat lem। ek brtn mem pyaaj kaa ek tukd़aa rkhem aur kchchaa shhd milaaem। jb tk brtn bhr n jaae tb tk prkriyaa ko dohraaem। ktore ko dhk kr rkhem aur 12 se 15 ghmte ke lie chhod़ dem। pyaaj siirp kii trh motii prt mem jm jaaegaa।
6. chikn kaa soop (Chicken soup)
 - chikn soop kii mem kii aavshyk poshk ttv vitaamin haim jo aam srdii ke lkshणom ke upchaar mem mdd krte haim। chikn soop ke uchch emtiiऑksiidemt guण jukaam ko thiik krne kii prkriyaa mem tejii laate haim। srvottm priणaamom ke lie, jaivik sbjiyom aur chikn kaa upyog kr, ghr kaa bnaa chikn soop taiyaar krem।


Disease: bukhaar (Fever)

Description: 
bukhaar aanaa ek behd aam biimaarii hotii hai। vijञaan ke anusaar yh bukhaar rog nhiim blki rog kaa lkshण hotaa hai। jaaniem bukhaar ke baarem mem vistaar se:

Reasons: 
- shvsn smsthaan vaale bukhaar jaise kii jukaam, phloo, gle kii soojn, shvaasnlii shoth, nyoomoniyaa, tii.bii. aadi।
- tvchaa ke smkrmण (Infection) se hone vaale bukhaar jaise kii jkhm mem piip honaa, phoड़e yaa daane vaale bukhaar।
- mchchhr yaa pissoo se hone vaale bukhaar jaise kii mleriyaa (Malaria Fever), phaayleriyaa (Flaria), demgoo (Dengue), chikungunyaa (Chickengunia), mstishk jvr (Meningitis), pleg (Plague), aadi। in sbhii bukhaarom mem phle kmpkmpii hotii hai।
- paachn smsthaan ke bukhaar jaise dst yaa pechish, piiliiyaa, taayphॉiid aadi। pechish mem khoon aur blgm girtaa hai। taayphaaiid khoon ke jॉmch se hii ptaa chltaa hai।
- prjnn aur mootr smsthaan ke bukhaar - ismem peshaab ke smy jln hotii hai।
- any smkraamk bukhaar jaise kii bruselॉsiis, eds, tpedik ke kuchh prkaar, joड़om kaa bukhaar। asmkraamk bukhaarom mem jaise loo lgnaa aur ऍlrjii se hone vaale bukhaar।

Treatments:
bukhaar aane pr rogii ke shriir kaa taapmaan dekhnaa chaahie aur agr taapmaan adhik ho to dॉktr kii slaah lenii chaahie। bukhaar (Bukhar) aane ke dauraan rogii ko nimn saamaany upchaar bhii diyaa jaa sktaa hai:
- rogii ko khoob saaraa svchchh evm ublaa huaa paanii pilaaem, shriir ko pryaapt kailorii dene ke lie glookoj, phlom kaa rs aadi dem।
- aasaanii se pchne vaalaa khaanaa jaise chaavl kii kmjii, saaboodaane kii khiir yaa khichड़ii, jau kaa paanii aadi denaa chaahiye।
- rogii ko achchhe hvaadaar kmre mem rkhnaa chaahiye।
- svchchh evm mulaaym vstr phnaaem। 
- ydi jvr 39.5 digrii se. yaa 103.0 phairenhaait se adhik ho yaa phir 48 ghmtom se adhik smy ho gyaa ho to dॉktr se praamrsh lem।

Home Remedies:
jb bhii shriir kaa taapmaan saamaany se jyaadaa hotaa hai to yh bukhaar khlaataa hai। kii baar mausm mem privrtn yaa smkrmण ke kaarण bukhaar ho jaataa hai। bchchom mem imyoonitii kmjor hone, kaan mem imphekshn hone yaa peshaab mem imphekshn hone pr bhii bukhaar hotaa hai । itnaa hii nhiim saaph- sphaaii kaa abhaav hone se bhii bukhaar hone kii smbhaavnaa rhtii hai।
bukhaar ke saamaany lkshणom mem sir drd (Headache), mmspeshiyom mem drd (Muscle pain) , dihaadreshn (Dehydration) , kii dphaa kmpkpii (Shivring) to kii baar psiinaa aanaa aur kmjorii ho skte haim। yoom to bukhaar kuchh din mem thiik ho jaataa hai lekin phir bhii kuchh ghreloo upaayom kaa apnaakr aap jldii thiik ho skte haim। ghreloo upaayom ke baad bhii ydi bukhaar n utr rhaa ho yaa bढ़ rhaa ho to turmt chikitsk kii slaah lenii chaahie।
bukhaar ke lie ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies for Fever)
thmdaa paanii (Cold Water)
kisii kpड़e ko thmde paanii mem bhigokr shriir ko pomchhe। iske alaavaa thmde paanii kii pttiym sir pr rkhne se bhii laabh hotaa he aur shriir kaa taapmaan km hotaa hai। kpड़e ko smy-smy pr bdlte rhnaa chaahie। saamaany bukhaar ke lie yh behd achchhii prkriyaa hai jo taapmaan ko bढ़ne nhiim detii।
tulsii (Basil)
tulsii bukhaar mem shriir ke taapmaan ko km krne mem bhut shaayk hai। yh hrb baajaar mem maujood any emtiibaayotiks (Antibiotics) kii trh hii kaary krtii hai aur prbhaavii bhii hai।
bukhaar ko thiik krne ke lie tulsii kii biis pttii aur ek chmmch ksaa huaa adrk lekr ek kp paanii mem ubaalem। thmdaa krke ismem shhd milaaem aur pii lem। is vidhi ko din mem do baar krem।
tulsii kii pttii aur kaalii mirch paaudr ko milaakr bhii chaay bnaaii jaa sktii hai jisse shriir kaa taapmaan km hotaa hai। is chaay ko din mem do se tiin baar pii skte haim।
seb saaidr sirkaa (Apple Cider Vinegar)
seb saaidr sirkaa bhii bukhaar ke lie behd sstii aur prbhaavii dvaa hai। seb saaidr sirkaa bukhaar ko tejii se km krtaa hai kyomki ismem maujood esid grmaaht ko shriir kii tvchaa se baahr kr detaa hai। saath hii ismem  maujood minrl shriir ko bukhaar se door bhii rkhte haim।
kisii kpड़e ko ek bhaag sirkaa aur do bhaag paanii lekr usmem bhigoem। atirikt paanii ko nichoड़ dem aur is pttii ko maathe aur pet pr rkhem। ek pttii pair ke tlvom pr bhii rkhii jaa sktii hai। jaise hii kpड़aa grm ho jaae, dobaaraa solyooshn mem dubaaem aur prkriyaa ko dohraaem।
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun kii grm taasiir bhii shriir mem psiinaa laakr, shriir kaa taapmaan km kr sktii hai। yh shriir se haanikaark vishaakt pdaarthom ko bhii baahr nikaalne mem shaayk hai। itnaa hii nhiim lhsun emtiiphmgl (antifungal) aur emtiibaiktiiriyl guणom se bhraa hai jo shriir ko imyoonitii (Immunity) detaa hai।
lhsun kii ek klii ko piiskr grm paanii mem milaaem। 10 mint dhk kr rkhem। paanii ko chhaan lem aur ghoomt-ghoomt krke dhiire-dhiire piiem। ek din mem is pey ko do baar piiem। agle hii din aap bukhaar se raaht mhsoos kremge।
do chmmch oeliv ऑyl (Olive Oil) mem do klii lhsun kii daalkr bhoonem। is tel ko thmdaa krke pair ke tlvom  mem lgaaem।
kishmish (Raisin)
kishmish shriir ke imphekshn se lड़ne aur bukhaar se raaht dene kii kshmtaa rkhtii hai। kishmish mem phiinolik saayetonyootriiyemt (Phenolic Phytonutrients) aur emtiiऑksiidemt (Antioxident) guण hote haim।
aadhe kp paanii mem ek ghmte ke lie 25 kishmish bhigaaem, jb tk ki kishmish nrm ho jaaem। kishmish ko paanii ke mdr hii msl dem aur paanii ko chhaankr alg kr lem। is joos mem aadhe niimboo kaa rs milaaem। mitrण ko ek din mem do baar piiem।
adrk (Ginger)
adrk mem shriir ke taapmaan ko niymtrit krne ke guण hote haim। yoom bhii adrk praakृtik roop se emtii vaayrl (Anti Viral) aur emtiibaiktiiriyl (Anti Becterial) ejemt se bhrpoor hotaa hai।
paanii mem adrk daalkr ubaalem aur use thmdaa krke chhaankr usmem, shhd milaakr pii lem। is trh se bnii chaay ko din mem tiin se chaar baar piyaa jaa sktaa hai।
deढ़ chmmch adrk kaa rs, ek chmmch niimboo kaa rs (Lemon Juice) aur ek bड़ii chmmch shhd milaakr is mikschr ko piem। is mitrण ko bhii din mem tiin se chaar br liyaa jaa sktaa hai।


Disease: gle mem khraash (Sore Throat)

Description: 
mausm bdlte hii gle mem khraash honaa aam baat hai। saamaany shbdom mem gle mem khraash, gle kaa smkrmण (Infection) hai। aamtaur pr gle kaa smkrmण (Infection) vaayrs yaa baiktiiriyaa ke kaarण hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- 100.5 drigii F yaa 38 drigii selsiys se adhik buख़aar honaa
- grdn mem soojn honaa
- gle mem drd honaa
- niglne mem kthinaaii honaa
- pet mem drd honaa
- bhookh n lgnaa honaa
- mitlii yaa ultii honaa
- shriir mem piiड़aa honaa
- sms lene mem kthinaaii honaa

Reasons: 
- bdltaa mausm mem aksr khraash kii smsyaa kaa saamnaa krnaa pड़taa hai। 
- kbhii kbhii khaane piine kii chiiज़om ke vipriit prbhaav ke kaarण bhii gle mem smkrmण ho sktaa hai। 
- iske alaavaa gle mem khraash kii smsyaa anuvmshik bhii ho sktii hai।
- thmde, khtte, evm tle hue khaady pdaarthom ko khaane ke kaarण bhii gle mem skrmण ho sktaa hai।

Treatments:
gle kii khraash kaa ilaaj (Treatment of Sore Throat)
- nmk ke gungune paanii se graare krem। isse gle mem aaraam milegaa।
- adrk, ilaaychii aur kaalii mirch vaalii chaay gle kii khraash (Sore Throat) mem aaraam phumchaatii hai।
- km msaale vaalaa bhojn lem।
- phrij kaa thmdaa paanii n piem, n hii any thmdii chiijem khaaem। 

Home Remedies:
saamaanyth gle kii mdroonii prt mem smkrmण ke kaarण gle mem khraash hotii hai। iske alaavaa kbhii kbhii mausm mem achaank bdlaav hone kii vjh se gle mem khraash hotii hai aur kii baar tomsil (tonsil) yaa gle mem kisii trh ke imphekshn ke kaarण bhii khraash ho sktii hai। vaise to gle kii khraash tiin chaar din mem thiik ho jaatii hai, lekin kuchh ghreloo upaayom se gle kii khraash mem jldii raaht miltii hai। aaie jaanem gle kii khraash door krne ke ghreloo upaay
1. grm paanii aur nmk ke graare (Gargle of warm water and salt)- jb gle mem khraash hotii hai to shleshmaa jhillii (mucous membrane) kii koshikaaom mem soojn ho jaatii hai। nmk is soojn (swelling) ko km krtaa hai jisse drd mem raaht miltii hai। upchaar ke lie ek gilaas gungune paanii mem ek bड़aa chmmch nmk milaakr ghol lem aur is paanii se graare krem। is prkriyaa ko din mem tiin baar krem।
2. lhsun (Garlic)- lhsun imphekshn (infection) paidaa krne vaale jiivaaणuom ko maar detaa hai। islie gle kii khraash mem lhsun behd phaaydemmd hai। lhsun mem maujood eliisin (allicin) jiivaaणuom ko maarne ke saath hii gle kii soojn aur drd ko bhii km krtaa hai। upchaar ke lie gaalom ke donom trph lhsun kii ek ek klii rkhkr dhiire dhiire chooste rhem। jaise jaise lhsun kaa rs gle mem jaaegaa vaise vaise aaraam miltaa rhegaa। lhsun kaa rs nikaalne ke lie biich biich mem dmtom se kuchlte rhem।
3. bhaap lenaa (Steaming)- kii baar gle ke sookhne ke kaarण bhii gle mem imphekshn kii shikaayt hotii hai। aise mem kisii bड़e brtn mem grm paanii krke tauliyaa se mumh dhkkr bhaap lem। aisaa krne se bhii gle kii sikaaii hogii aur gle kaa imphekshn bhii khtm hogaa। is kriyaa ko din mem do baar kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
4. laal mirch (Red chilli)- gle kii khraash ko thiik krne ke lie laal mirch bhii behd phaaydemmd hai। upchaar ke lie ek kp grm paanii mem ek chmmch laal mirch aur ek chmmch shhd milaakr piiem।
5. bekimg sodaa (Baking soda)- gle kii khraash door krne ke lie bekimg sodaa kii chaay behd phaaydemmd hai। kaarण, bekimg sodaa mem emtii baiktiiriyl (antibacterial) guण hote haim jo ki jiivaaणuom ko nsht kr dete haim। iske lie ek gilaas grm paanii mem bekimg sodaa aur nmk milaakr din mem tiin baar graare krem।
6. laumg (Laung or Clove)- laumg kaa istemaal upchaar ke lie sdiyom se hotaa aa rhaa hai। gle kii khraash ke upchaar ke lie laumg ko mumh mem rkhkr dhiire dhiire chbaanaa chaahie। laumg emtiibaiktiiriyl guणom se bhrpoor hotii hai jo gle ke imphekshn aur soojn ko door krtii hai।
7. adrk (Ginger)- adrk bhii gle kii khraash kii behd achchhii dvaa hai। adrk mem maujood emtiibaiktiiriyl guण gle ke imphekshn aur drd se raaht dete haim। gle kii khraash ke upchaar ke lie ek kp paanii mem adrk daal kr ubaalem। iske baad ise hlkaa gungunaa krke ismem shhd milaaem। is pey ko din mem do se tiin baar piiem। gle kii khraash se aaraam milegaa।
8. msaalaa chaay (Masala Chay)- laumg, tulsii (basil), adrk aur kaalii mirch (black pepper) ko paanii mem daalkr ubaalem, iske baad ismem chaay pttii daalkr chaay bnaaem। is chaay ko grm grm hii piiem। yh bhii gle ke lie behd laabhdaayk upaay hai jisse gle mem turmt aaraam miltaa hai।


Disease: ubkaaii (Nausea)

Description: 
ubkaaii aanaa ultii hone kaa ehsaas maatr hai। kuchh logom ko mitlii jyaadaa aatii hai। visheshkr yaatraa ke smy kuchh logom ko ubkaaii kii smsyaa hotii hai। ise moshn siknes (Motion Sickness) bhii khte haim। yh gaadii se yaatraa ke dauraan yaa yaa naav se yaatraa ke dauraan (Sea Sickness) vishesh roop se mhsoos kiyaa jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- dil kii  dhd़kn bdh़ jaatii hai
- psiinaa aane lgtaa hai
- pet mem gd़bd़ii kaa ehsaas hone lgtaa hai

Reasons: 
yaatraa ke dauraan mitlii aanaa behd saamaany baat hai lekin kii vjhom se yh agr lgaataar aae to ek smsyaa ho sktii hai।  mitlii nimn kaarणom se bhii aatii hai:
mitlii aur ultii ke saamaany kaarण (Reason of Nausea)
- aimtii baayotik (Anti Biotic) dvaaiiyom ke kaarण aksr pet mem gd़bd़ii ho jaatii hai jo mitlii yaa ultii kaa kaarण bn jaataa hai।
- kuchh logom ko yaatraa ke dauraan mitlii, ultii kaa anubhv hotaa hai। iske liye iskii dvॉme aadhaa ghmtaa poorv lekr hii chle।
- bdhjmii se, amltaa (Acidity), shraab aadi se bhii mitlii kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
- grbhaavsthaa mem phle timaahii mem mitlii yaa ultii kii smsyaa (nausea during pregnancy) hotii hai। yh apne aap ruk jaatii hai। mitlii aur ultii kii smsyaa grbhdhaarण ke smy shriir mem haarmonl bdlaav ke kaarण hotaa hai। shriir mem vitaamin bii6 kii kmii se bhii grbhvtii mhilaa ko ultii hone kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
- phood elrjii aur phood ashishणutaa (Food Intolerance)
- maaigren mem sir ke bhiitr kisii bhii prkaar ke dbaav se seriibro-spaainl phlooid (Cerebro-Spinal Fluid) prbhaavit hotaa hai jiske kaarण mitlii yaa ultii kii smsyaa utpnn hotii hai।
- pittaashy (Gall Bladder) aur paachk grmthi (Pancreas) mem soojn hone pr pet ke ooprii bhaag mem drd hotaa hai aur mitlii aur ultii hone lgtii hai।
- kbhii kbhii ऍksidemt yaa gmdgii bdboo ke kaarण bhii mitlii aa sktii hai।
- tnaav, bhy aur bechainii ke kaarण shriir kii kriyaa mem asmtuln paidaa ho jaataa hai, jo pet mem gd़bd़ii kaa kaarण bn jaataa hai। jiske phlsvroop mitlii, ultii, dst, kbj aadi smsyaaem hone lgtii haim।

Treatments:
yaatraa ke dauraan mitlii se bchne kaa sbse upyogii triikaa hotaa hai thoड़aa-thoड़aa khaanaa khaayem। iske alaavaa kuchh any upaay nimn hai:
- grbhvtii mhilaayem ko jin mhk vaalii vaale chiijom se mtlii ho rhii haim unko n khaayem।
- thod़e-thod़e maatraa mem khaayem।
- do miil ke biich mem thmdaa pey, jl piiyem।
- ultii krne kaa pryaas krem। ultii krne pr aaraam milegaa hogaa ।
- aap jhm~ bhii ho taajaa hvaa aanii chaahie।
- dhiilaa-dhaalaa kpd़aa phne।
- j़roort se j़yaadaa paanii nhiim piinaa chaahie।
- agr sthiti gmbhir ho jaay to dॉktr se slaah lenii chaahie।

Home Remedies:
mtlii yaa jii michlaane kii preshaanii moshn siknes (Motion sickness), pet ke phloo (Stomach flu) yaa phir aapke dvaaraa khaae ge khaane ke imphekshn se hotii hai। kbhii kbhaar mtlii kisii gmbhiir biimaarii jaise haart ataik, kaimsr yaa kiimotherepii lene ke dauraan bhii ho sktii hai। aaie jaanem kuchh aise ghreloo upchaar jo mtlii yaa jii michlaane kii preshaanii se aapko raaht demge।
1. adrk (Ginger)
adrk jii michlaane yaa ultii mem raaht dene ke lie srvottm aushdhi hai। iske upchaar ke lie adrk kii chaay yaa adrk ko yoom hii chbaanaa bhii laabhdaayk ho sktaa hai। haalmki grbhaavsthaa (Pregnancy) mem adrk istemaal kii mnaahii hotii hai। saath hii do saal se km umr ke bchchom ko bhii adrk nhiim dii jaanii chaahie।
2. niimboo (Lemon)
niimboo bhii jii michlaane kii smsyaa se raaht detaa hai। niimboo mem vitaamin sii uchch maatraa mem hotaa hai jo ki pet ke lie behd phaaydemmd hai। upchaar ke lie ek gilaas paanii mem ek niimboo nichoड़kr piiem। saath hii niimboo ko soomghne se bhii kaaphii phaaydaa hotaa hai।
3. pudiinaa (Mint)
pudiinaa mem emtii baiktiiriyl guण (Antibacterial) hote haim saath hii yh imynitii ko bhii bढ़aataa hai। mtlii yaa jii michlaane kii smsyaa se raaht ke lie pudiine kii pttiym chbaaii jaa sktii haim। iske alaavaa pudiine kii chaay (Mint tea) bnaakr piinaa yaa kaimdii khaanaa bhii laabhprd hotaa hai।
4. doodh-bred (Milk and bread)
mtlii se raaht ke lie doodh bred khaanaa bhii laabhprd hotaa hai। upchaar ke lie bred pr binaa nmk vaalaa mkkhn (Without salt) lgaakr , ek gilaas grm doodh mem is bred ko toड़kr daalem aur dhiire dhiire khaaem। lekin pet mem phloo yaa gais ho to doodh n lem।
5. shhd (Honey)
shhd kii biimaariyom kii uchch dvaa hai। shhd mem bhii emtii baiktiiriyl guण hote haim aur shhd bhii imyoonitii bढ़aane kaa kaary krtaa hai। upchaar ke lie ek gilaas paanii mem seb kaa sirkaa milaakr (Apple cider vinegar) usmem thoड़aa shhd daalkr piine se jii michlaane kii smsyaa se raaht miltii hai।
6. chaavl kaa paanii (Rice water)
adhpke chaavl se nikle mmd ko piine se mtlii se bhut raaht miltii hai। is mmd ko hlkaa gungunaa hii piinaa chaahie।
7. jiiraa (Cumin)
ek gilaas chhaachh yaa dhii mem jiiraa ko bhoonkr daalem। is mishrण ko pii lem। isse jii michlaane kii smsyaa thiik ho jaatii hai।
8. bekimg sodaa (Baking soda)
grm paanii mem deढ़ chmmch bekimg sodaa daalkr piine se mtlii mem bhut raaht miltii hai। grbhvtii mhilaaom ko yh upchaar nhiim krnaa chaahie।
9. pyaaj (Onion)
ek pyaaj kaa joos nikaalkr ismem ek chmmch adrk ko kddooks krke milaaem। pyaaj mem emtii baiktiiriyl (Antibacterial) guण hote haim। jiske kaarण yh pet ke lie behd phaaydmmd hai। ismem mtlii ko thiik krne ke praakृtik guण hote haim।
10. thmdii sikaaii (Cold Fomentation)
iske lie ek kpड़e ko yaa chhotii tauliyaa ko ekdm thmde paanii yaa brph ke paanii (Ice water) mem kuchh ghmtom ke lie rkhem। iske baad is tauliyaa ko prbhaavit vykti kii grdn pr lpetem। ydi vykti letaa hai to grdn ke piichhe rkhem aur ydi baithaa hai to grdn ke saamne। aisaa krne se bhii ultii aur jii michlaane kii smsyaa mem bhut raaht miltii hai।


Disease: aphaaraa (Flatulence)

Description: 
khaan-paan mem aniymittaa aur maidaa yaa suprphaain aate se bne khaady prdaarth khaane ke kaarण hmaare pet mem bhut gais paidaa hone lgtii hai। agr yh gais svaabhaavik triike se pet se baahr nikl jaaye to tkliiph nhiim hotii mgr jb yh gais nhii nikltii hai to pet phool jaataa hai aur aphaare (Gas) kii sthiti bn jaatii hai, tb bड़ii tkliiph hotii hai। 

Symptoms: 
- aphaaraa jaisaa mhsoos honaa
- khaanaa khaane ke baad pet jyaadaa bhaarii lgnaa
- chhaatii mem jln honaa
- jii michlaanaa
- dkaarem aanaa
- pet mem drd honaa
- pet mem bhaariipn mhsoos hotaa hai
- pet se gais paas honaa

Reasons: 
- khaanpaan : suprphaain aate (Packed Aata) kii rotii aasaanii se nhiim pchtii। yh vaayu paidaa krtii haim।
- shraab piine se bhii pet mem gais bntii hai।
- mirch-msaalaa yaa tlii-bhunii chiijem jyaadaa khaane se।
- phliym (Beans), raajmaa, chhole, lobiyaa, moth, ud़d kii daal, phaast phood, bred aur kisii-kisii ko doodh yaa bhookh se jyaadaa khaane se।
- khaane ke saath kold drimk lene se। ismem gaisiiy ttv hote haim।
- tlaa yaa baasii khaanaa।
- tnaav, der se sonaa aur subh der se jaagnaa jaisii khraab jiivnshailii aadtom ke kaarण bhii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
- bhookhe rhne se, khaalii pet bhii gais (Pet me Gas) bnne kaa prmukh kaarण hai। smy asmy khaanaa khaane se bhii gais smbmdhii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
- liivr mem soojn, gॉl bledr mem ston, phaitii liivr, alsr jaise rogom mem bhii pet mem gais kii smsyaa hotii hai।
- motaape, daaybiitiij, asthmaa aadi ke rogiyom ko aksr gais kii smsyaa dekhne ko miltii hai।
- bchchom ke pet mem kiid़om kii vjh se aphaaraa ho sktaa hai।
- aksr penkilr khaane se bhii aphaaraa ho sktaa hai।
- kbj, atisaar, khaanaa n pchne v ultii kii vjh se bhii aphaaraa yaa pet mem gais kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
pet mem gais kii smsyaa se nijaat paane kaa sbse bढ़iyaa triikaa hai khaan-paan shii rkhnaa। agr khaan-paan shii ho to is biimaarii se koii preshaanii nhiim hotii hai। iske saath hii nimn baatom kaa bhii dhyaan rkhnaa chaahie:
- bhojn pchegaa, pet saaph rhegaa to gais km bnegii।
- suprphaain aate kii rotii aasaanii se nhiim pchtii, vaayu paidaa krtii haim। ath mote chokr yukt aate kii rotii khaaem। yh jldii pchegii aur vaayu paidaa nhiim hogii aur aphaaraa jaisii tkliiphem nhiim homgii।
- hre saag jaise bthuaa, paalk, srsom kaa saag khaaem। khiiraa, kkड़ii, gaajr, chukmdr bhii is rog ko shmt rkhte haim। inhem kchchaa khaanaa chaahiye।
- naariyl kaa paanii din mem tiin baar piyem। isse saaraa ksht mit jaaegaa।
- skin kaimsr
- soraaysis


Disease: chiknguniyaa (Chikungunya)

Description: 
chiknguniyaa bukhaar (Chikungunya) ek vaayrs bukhaar hai jo ediij mchchhr eijiptii ke kaatne ke kaarण hotaa hai। chiknguniyaa aur demgoo ke lkshण lgbhg ek smaan hote haim।​ is bukhaar kaa naam chiknguniyaa svaahilii bhaashaa se liyaa gyaa hai, jiskaa arth hai ''aisaa jo mud़ jaataa hai'' aur yh rog se hone vaale jod़om ke drd ke lkshणom ke priणaamsvroop rogii ke jhuke hue shriir ko dekhte hue prchlit huaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- ul‍tii honaa
- ek se tiin din tk bukhaar ke saath jod़om mem  drd aur soojn honaa
- kmpkpii aur thmd ke saath bukhaar kaa achaank bढ़naa
- srdrd honaa

Treatments:
chiknguniyaa hone pr dॉktr kii slaah lenaa sbse jroorii hai। saath hii chiknguniyaa se piiड़it rogii ko nimn upaay apnaane chaahie:
- adhik se adhik paanii piiem, ho ske to gungunaa paanii piiem।
- jyaadaa se jyaadaa aaraam krem।
- chiknguniyaa ke dauraan jod़om mem bhut drd hotaa hai jiske lie daaॅktr kii slaah pr hii drd nivaark (Pain Killer) lem।
- doodh se bne utpaad, doodh-dhii yaa any chiijom kaa sevn krem।
- rogii ko niim ke pttom ko piis kr uskaa rs nikaalkr dem।
- rogii ke kpड़om evm uske bistr kii saaph-sphaaii pr khaas dhyaan dem।
- krelaa v ppiitaa aur giloy ke pttom kaa rs kaaphii phaaydemmd maanaa jaataa hai। 
- naariyl paanii piine se shriir mem hone vaalii paanii kii kmii door hotii hai aur liivr ko aaraam miltaa hai। 
- aisprin bukhaar hone pr kbhii naa lem, isse kaaphii smsyaa ho sktii hai। 
- bchchom kaa khaas khyaal rkhem। 
- bchche naajuk hote haim aur unkaa imyoon sistm kmjor hotaa hai islie biimaarii unhem jldii pkड़ letii hai। aise mem unkii biimaarii ko njrmdaaj n krem।
- bchche khule mem jyaadaa rhte haim islie inphekshn hone aur mchchhrom se kaate jaane kaa khtraa unmem jyaadaa hotaa hai।
- bchchom ghr se baahr poore kpd़e phnaakr bhejem। mchchhrom ke mausm mem bchchom ko nikr v tii - shrt n phnaaem। raat mem mchchhr bhgaane kii kriim lgaaem।
- agr bchchaa bhut jyaadaa ro rhaa ho, lgaataar soe jaa rhaa ho, bechain ho, use tej bukhaar ho, shriir pr raishej hom, ultii ho yaa inmem se koii bhii lkshण ho to phaurn dॉktr ko dikhaaem।
- aamtaur pr chhote bchchom ko bukhaar hone pr unke haath - pmv to thmde rhte haim lekin maathaa aur pet grm rhte haim islie unke pet ko chhookr aur rektl temprechr lekr unkaa bukhaar chek kiyaa jaataa hai। bgl se taapmaan lenaa shii triikaa nhiim hai, khaaskr bchchom mem। agr bgl se taapmaan lenaa hii hai to jo riidimg aae, usmem 1 digrii jod़ dem। use hii shii riidimg maanaa jaaegaa।

Home Remedies:
chiknguniyaa (Chikungunya) ek trh kaa vaayrl bukhaar hai jo ki mchchhrom ke kaarण phailtaa hai। chiknguniyaa alphaavaayrs (alphavirus) ke kaarण hotaa hai jo mchchhrom ke kaatne ke dauraan mnushyom ke shriir mem prvesh kr jaate haim।
chiknguniyaa mem joड़om mem drd (Joint Pain), sir drd (Headache), ultii (Vomit) aur jii michlaane (Nausea) ke lkshण ubhr skte haim jbki kuchh logom mem msooड़om aur naak se khoon (Blood from gums and nose) bhii aa jaataa hai। mchchhr kaatne ke lgbhg baarh din mem chiknguniyaa ke lkshण ubhrte haim। chiknguniyaa ke upchaar ke lie bhut se ghreloo nuskhe haim jinhem apnaakr chiknguniyaa se khud ko bchaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
1. ppiite kii pttii (Papaya Leaf)
ppiite kii pttii n kevl demgoo blki chiknguniyaa mem bhii utnii hii prbhaavii hai। bukhaar mem shriir ke pletlets (platelates) tejii se girte haim, jinhem ppiite kii pttiym tejii se bढ़aatii haim। maatr tiin ghmte mem ppiite kii pttiym shriir mem rkt ke pletlets ko bढ़aa detii haim। upchaar ke lie ppiite kii pttiyom se dmthl ko alg krem aur kevl pttii ko piiskr uskaa joos nikaal lem। do chmmch joos din mem tiin baar lem।
2. tulsii aur ajvaayn (Tulsi and Ajwain)
tulsii aur ajvaayn bhii chiknguniyaa ke upchaar ke lie behd achchhii ghreloo aushdhi haim। upchaar ke lie ajvaayn, kishmish, tulsii aur niim kii sookhii pttiym lekr ek gilaas paanii mem ubaal lem। is pey ko binaa chhaanem din mem tiin baar piiem।
3. lhsun aur sjvaayn kii phlii (Garlic and drum stick)
lhsun aur sjvaayn kii phlii chiknguniyaa ke ilaaj ke lie bhut bढ़iyaa hai। chiknguniyaa mem joड़om mem kaaphii drd hotaa hai, aise mem shriir kii maalish kiyaa jaanaa behd jroorii hai। iske lie kisii bhii tel mem lhsun aur sjvaayn kii phlii milaakr tel grm krem aur is tel se rogii kii maalish krem।
4. laumg (Laung or clove)
drd vaale joड़om pr lhsun ko piiskr usmem laumg kaa tel milaakr, kpड़e kii shaaytaa se joड़om pr bmdh dem। isse bhii chiknguniyaa ke mriijom ko joड़om ke drd se aaraam milegaa, aur shriir kaa taapmaan (body temprature) bhii niymtrit hogaa।
5. epsm saalt (Epsom salt)
epsm saalt kii kuchh maatraa grm paanii mem daalkr us paanii se nhaaem। is paanii mem niim kii pttiym bhii milaaem। aisaa krne se bhii drd se raaht milegii aur taapmaan niymtrit hogaa।
6. mgoor (Grapes)
mgoor ko gaay ke gungune doodh ke saath piine pr chiknguniyaa ke vaayrs mrte haim lekin dhyaan rhe mgoor biijrhit hom।
7. gaajr (Carrot)
kchchii gaajr khaanaa bhii chiknguniyaa ke upchaar mem behd phaaydemmd hai। yh rogii kii prtirodhk kshmtaa (immunity power) ko bढ़aatii hai saath hii joड़om ke drd se bhii raaht detii hai।


Disease: aatmvimoh (Autism)

Description: 
ऑtij़m (Autism) mstishk ke vikaas ke dauraan hone vaalaa ek maansik rog hai jo mstishk ke kii bhaagom ko prbhaavit krtaa hai। jin bchchom mem yh rog hotaa hai unkaa vikaas any bchchom kii apekshaa asaamaany hotaa hai।

Reasons: 
- mstishk kii gtividhiyom mem asaamaanytaa honaa
- mstishk ke rsaaynom mem asaamaanytaa
- aanuvmshik aadhaar
- priणaam btaate haim ki km mtraal pr huii grbhaavsthaaom se jnm lene vaale bchchom mem ऑtij़m viksit hone kaa khtraa bdh़ jaataa hai

Treatments:
shuruaatii smjञaanaatmk (Cognitive) yaa vyvhaarii hstkshep, ऑtij़m se prbhaavit bchchom ke vikaas mem bhut mhtvpoorण hotaa hai। ऑtij़m ko ek biimaarii kii bjaay ek sthiti ke njriye se dekhnaa chaahie।

- khilaunom ke saath khelne kaa shii triikaa dikhaaem~
- baarii-baarii se khelne kii aadt daalem
- dhiire-dhiire khel mem logo kii smkhyaa ko bdh़te jaayem
- chhote-chhote vaakyom mem baat krem
- saadhaarण bhaashaa kaa pryog krem

- phle smjhnaa tthaa phir bolnaa sikhme
- ydi bchchaa bol paa rhaa hai to use shaabaashii dem tthaa baar-baar bolne ke lie prerit krem
- bchche ko apnii jroortom ko bolne kaa maukaa dem
- ydi bchchaa bilkul bol nhii paae to use tsviir kii trph़ ishaaraa krke apnii jroortom ke baare mem bolnaa sikhaaem

- bchche ko tnaav mukt sthaanom jaise paark aadi mem le kr jaayem
- any logom ko bchche se baat krne ke lie prerit krem
- bchche ke saath dhiire-dhiire km smy se bdh़aate hue adhik smy ke lie nj़r milaa kr baat krne kii koshish kre
- tthaa uske kisii bhii prytn ko protsaahit krnaa n bhoolem
- ydi bchchaa koii ek vyvhaar baar-baar krtaa hai to use rokne ke lie use kuchh aisii gtividhiyom mem lgaaem jo use vyst rkhem taaki ve vyvhaar dohraa n ske
- glt vyvhaar dohraane pr bchche ko kuchh aisaa kaam krvme jo use psmd nhii hai
- ydi bchchaa kuchh der glt vyvhaar n kre to use turmt protsaahit krem
- protsaahn ke lie rmg-birmgii, chmkiilii tthaa dhyaan khiichnem vaalii chiijom kaa istemaal krem
- bchche ko apnii shkti ko istemaal krne ke lie shii maarg dikhaaem~ jaise kii use tej vyaayaam, daud़, tthaa baahrii khelom mem lgaaem
- ydi preshaanii adhik ho to mnochikitsk ke dvaaraa dii gii dvaa kaa upyog bhii kiyaa jaa sktaa hai


Disease: khoon kii kmii (Anemia)

Description: 
eniimiyaa kyaa hai (About Anemia in Hindi)

Symptoms: 
- mkhem piilii ho jaanaa
- kmjorii aur thkaavt mhsoos honaa
- chkkr aanaa
- chhaatii mem drd honaa evm siine mem aithn honaa
- tvchaa v naakhoonom kaa piilaa honaa
- maaild (Mild) yaanii hlke eniimiyaa mem lkshण km nj़r aate haim, lmbe smy se hue eniimiyaa ke kii lkshण aasaanii se dekhe jaa skte haim
- let ke uthne pr m~khom ke saamne andheraa chhaa jaanaa
- sms phoolnaa
- sir drd rhnaa
- haathom aur pairom kaa thmdaa honaa
- hृdy kii dhd़kn tej yaa asaamaany honaa

Reasons: 
- kidnii kaimsr: kidnii se iraaythropoyॅtiin (Erythropoietin) naam ke haarmon kaa utpaadn hotaa hai jo asthimjjaa (Bone Marrow) ko red-bld sel ke nirmaaण mem mdd krtaa hai, jin logom ko kidnii kaa kaimsr hotaa hai unke shriir mem~ iraaythropoyॅtiin (Erythropoieti) haarmon kaa nirmaaण nhiim hotaa hai aur iskii vjh se red-bld sels kaa bnnaa bhii km ho jaataa hai jiske priणaamsvroop vykti ko eniimiyaa ho jaataa hai ।
- alpaahaar yaa kuposhण: red-bld sels ke nirmaaण ke lie kii prkaar ke vitaamin v minrls kii jroort hotii hai, inkii kmii se red- bld sels kaa nirmaaण bhii km ho jaataa hai aur phlsvroop hiimoglobin bhii km bntaa hai aur mtth vykti eniimiyaa kaa shikaar bn sktaa hai। kuposhण mhilaaom mem aam smsyaa hai aur grbhvtii mhilaaom mem kuposhण kii smsyaa ke kaarण eniimiyaa kii preshaanii ho sktii hai।
- hiimoglobin ke jiin mem bdlaav: is prkaar ke eniimiyaa ko siikl sel eniimiyaa (Sickle Cell Anaemia) khte haim । asaamaany hiimoglobin ke kaarण red bld sels siikl yaanii hmsiye ke aakaar ke ho jaate haim, siikl sel eniimiyaa ke kii prkaar hote haim jinkaa asr alg-alg str pr alg-alg triike se hotaa hai।
- ​thailaisiimiiyaa: thailaisiimiiyaa aanuvmshik eniimiyaa hotaa hai,is prkaar ke eniimiyaa mem hiimoglobin apekshit maatraa mem bnne ke bjaay km yaa jyaadaa bnne lgtaa hai।
- vaayrl imphekshn, kemotherpii: vaayrl imphekshn, kemotherpii aur kuchh dvaaem lene se bhii asthimjjaa (Bone Marrow ) burii trh se prbhaavit hotii hai isse bld sels kaa nirmaaण bilkul km ho jaataa hai jiske priणaamsvroop eniimiyaa hone kii smbhaavnaaem jyaadaa hotii haim, is prkaar ke eniimiyaa ko aplaastik eniimiyaa (Aplastic Anaemia) khte haim।
- hiimolaaytik eniimiyaa (Hemolytic Anaemia): saamaany red-bld sels kaa aakaar iske thiik se kaam krne ke lie kaaphii ahm hotaa hai , kii kaarणom se red-bld sel nsht ho jaate haim jis avsthaa ko hiimolaaytiiis khte haim, aisii sthiti mem red-bld sels thiik triike se kaam nhiim kr paate haim, hiimolaaytis kii sthiti kii kaarणom se paidaa ho sktii haim, kaarण aanuvmshik aur red-bld sels kaa ati nirmaaण ho sktaa hai iske alaavaa kii avsthaa mem saamaany red-bld sels mem bhii hiimolaaytik eniimiyaa ho sktaa hai।
- vitaamiin bii-12 kii kmii: shriir mem vitaamiin bii-12 kii kmii se prniisiiys eniimiyaa hone kii smbhaavnaa hotii hai। prniisiiys eniimiyaa j़yaadaatr shuddh shaakaahaarii vyktiyom ko aur lmbe v़kt se shraab kaa sevn krne vaalom ko hotaa hai। 
- rktsraav se hone vaalaa eniimiyaa: maahvaarii ke dinom mem atydhik sraav, kisii chot yaa ghaav se sraav, gaistroimtestaainl alsr, koln kaimsr ityaadi mem dhiire-dhiire kh़oon lgaataar risne se eniimiyaa ho sktaa hai। 
- lmbe smy se biimaar hone pr: kisii bhii prkaar kii diirghkaalik biimaarii se eniimiyaa ho sktaa hai। 

Treatments:
eniimiyaa se bchaav kaa sbse behtriin upaay hai paushtik aahaar lenaa। iske saath hii nimn bimdooom pr dhyaan dekr bhii is biimaarii se bchaa jaa sktaa hai:
- eniimiyaa jyaadaatr paushtik aahaar lene se thiik ho jaataa hai, lekin kuchh prkaar ke eniimiyaa mem alg-alg trh se upchaar kraane pd़te haim। aise mem sbse jyaadaa jroorii hai dॉktrii praamrsh।
- saadhaarण taur pr yuvaaom mem eniimiyaa kaa upchaar bhut aasaanii se ho jaataa hai, jbki vysk mem eniimiyaa kii shikaayt jldii se door nhiim ho paatii hai।
- khoon kii kmii door krne ke lie sbse phle khaane mem hrii sbjiym (paalk, methii), phl v slaad kii maatraa bdh़aanii chaahie।
- chukmdr aayrn kaa achchhaa strot hai। isko roj khaane mem slaad yaa sbjii ke taur pr shaamil krne se shriir mem khoon kii kmii nhiim hotii।
- hrii pttedaar sbjii jaise paalk, brokolii, pttaagobhii, gobhii, shljm aur shkrkmd jaisii sbjiym seht ke lie bhut achchhii hotii haim। inke sevn se vjn km hone ke saath khoon bhii bdh़taa hai aur pet bhii thiik rhtaa hai।
- sookhe meve jaise khjoor, baadaam aur kishmish kaa khoob pryog krnaa chaahie। ismem aayrn kii pryaapt maatraa hotii hai।
- phl jaise khjoor, trbooj, seb, mgoor, kishmish aur anaar khaane se khoon bdh़taa hai। anaar khaanaa eniimiyaa (Fruits in Anemia) mem kaaphii phaaydaa krtaa hai।
- aayrn kii goliym yaa aayrn sukroch ke imjekshn, vitaamin bii-12 kii golii yaa imjekshn dॉktrii slaah se lem।

Home Remedies:
mnushyom ke shriir mem lohe kii kul maatraa shriir ke vjn ke mutaabik 3 se 5 graam hotii hai। ydi yh maatraa is smkhyaa se km ho jaatii hai to shriir mem hiimoglobin bnnaa km ho jaataa hai aur shriir mem khoon kii kmii ho jaatii hai। iskaa ek nuksaan yh bhii hai ki shriir kii koshikaaom mem ऑksiijn kii aavaajaahii (Oxygen circulation) km ho jaatii hai jisse shriir kaa pryaapt oorjaa nhiim mil paatii aur vykti eniimiyaa se grst ho jaataa hai।
iske saath hii ydi shriir mem pholik esid aur vitaamin bii 12 kii kmii hai tb bhii vykti eniimiyaa se grst ho sktaa hai। purooshom kii tulnaa mem mhilaaem jyaadaa eniimik paaii jaatii haim। shriir kaa jldii thknaa, chkkr aanaa, tvchaa mem piilaapn, lgaataar rhne vaalaa sir drd aadi kuchh eniimiyaa ke lkshणom mem shaamil haim। aaie aapko btaate haim, eniimiyaa se raaht paane ke ghreloo upaay (Home remedies for anemia)
1. paalk (Spinach)
paalk mem bhrpoor lauh tthaa vitaamin bii 12 hotaa hai। iske saath hii paalk pholik esid (Folic Acid) kaa bhii uchch strot hai। aise mem paalk khaane se khoon kii kmii poorii hotii hai। upchaar ke lie paalk kaa soop bnaakr, yaa paalk kaa saag aadi ko apne roj ke khaane mem shaamil krnaa chaahie।
2. anaar (Pomegranate)
anaar shriir mem hiimoglobin (Haemoglobin) ko bhut tejii se bढ़aataa hai। anaar mem protiin aur kaarbohaaidret kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। ismem aayrn aur kailshiym bhii hotaa hai। yh khoon mem hiimoglobin kii maatraa ko tejii se bढ़aakr rkt smchaar ko thiik rkhtaa hai। eniimiyaa ke upchaar ke lie subh khaalii pet anaar khaaem aur rojaanaa anaar kaa joos piiem।
3. chukmdr aur seb kaa rs (Beetroot and Apple Juice)
chukmdr mem pholik esid uchch maatraa mem hotaa hai jbki seb mem lauh ttv hote haim, aise mem donom hii eniimiyaa kii kmii ko door krte haim। upchaar ke lie ek kp chukmdr ke rs aur ek kp seb ke rs mem ek se do chmmch shhd milaakr din mem do baar piiem।
4. tmaatr (Tomato)
shriir ke lie bhut jyaadaa aayrn kii maatraa lene ke saath hii yh bhii jroorii hai ki aayrn ko aapkaa shriir sokhe। ismem tmaatr ahm bhoomikaa nibhaataa hai। rojaanaa ek se do kchche tmaatr jroor khaaem। ek gilaas tmaatr kaa rs bhii roj piiem aur khaanaa bnaane aur slaad mem bhii tmaatr kaa bhrpoor upyog krem।
5. khjoor (Dates)
khjoor bhii aayrn bhut achchhaa strot hai। sau graam khjoor mem 90 miliigraam aayrn kii maatraa hotii hai। do khjoor ko ek kp doodh mem raat bhr ke lie chhoड़ dem। in khjoor ko subh khaalii pet chbaa chbaakr khaaem। bche hue doodh ko bhii pii lem। khjoor ko grm paanii mem do yaa tiin ghmtom ke lie bhigaakr us paanii ko piinaa bhii phaaydemmd hotaa hai। jin logom ko lektoj (lectose) se elrjii hai aur doodh nhiim le skte, unke lie yh behtr triikaa hai।
6. kishmish (Kishmish)
kishmish bhii eniimiyaa kii behd achchhii ghreloo dvaa hai। kishmish mem aayrn, protiin, phaaibr, sodiym jaise uchch poshk ttv hote haim। upchaar ke lie ek kp paanii mem 10 se 15 kishmish raatbhr ke lie bhigaa dem। subh in kishmish ko shhd milaakr khaa lem aur bche hue paanii ko pii lem।
7. shhd (Honey)
shhd bhii lauh aur vitaamin bii 12 kaa uchch strot hai। shhd ko rojaanaa khaane se bhii shriir mem eniimiyaa kii kmii poorii hotii hai। shhd ko phlom mem milaakr, doodh mem daalkr yaa chiinii kii jgh shhd istemaal krke bhii rkt kii kmii poorii kii jaa sktii hai।


Disease: dimemshiyaa (Dementia)

Description: 
dimemshiyaa (Dementia) vykti ke mstishk ko prbhaavit krne vaalii biimaarii hotii hai। aljaaimrs kii biimaarii (Alziehmers Disease) aur vskyulr dimemshiyaa (Vascular Dementia) iske sbse aam prkaar (Common Type) haim।

Symptoms: 
- apne aap mem gumsum rhnaa, mel-jol bmd kr denaa, chuppii saadhnaa
- kpde ulte phnnaa, saaफ़-suthraa n rh paanaa
- kisii baat ko yaa prshn ko dohraanaa, jidd krnaa, trk n smjh paanaa
- kisii vstu kaa chitr dekhkr yh n smjh paanaa ki yh kyaa hai
- kuchh kaam shuroo krnaa, phir bhool jaanaa ki kyaa krnaa chaahte the, aur bhut koshish ke baad bhii yaad n kr paanaa
- chiiज़om ko glt, anuchit jgh pr rkh chhodnaa (jaise ki ghdii ko, yaa ऑphis phaail ko phrij mem rkh denaa)
- chhotii chhotii smsyaaom ko bhii n suljhaa paanaa
- chhotii-chhotii baat pr, yaa binaa kaarण hii baukhlaa jaanaa, chillaanaa, ronaa, ityaadi
- dimemshiyaa se prbhaavit vykti mem, rog ke bढ़ne ke saath jyaadaa aur adhik gmbhiir lkshण nज़r aate haim। (yaad rkhem ki hr vykti mem alg alg lkshण nज़r aate haim)
- nmbr joड़ne aur ghtaane mem dikkt, gintii krne mem dikkt
- bolte yaa likhte hue glt shbd kaa pryog krnaa, yaa shbdom ke arth n smjh paanaa
- bड़ii rkm ko phaaltoo kii skiim mem daal denaa, paise se smbmdhit ajiib nirणy lenaa, laaprvaahii yaa gairjimmedaarii dikhaanaa
- yh bhool jaanaa ki taariikh kyaa hai, kaunsaa mhiinaa hai, saal kaunsaa hai, vykti kis ghr mem haim, kis shhr mem haim, kis desh mem

Reasons: 
​dimemshiyaa kii kaarणom se ho sktaa hai lekin iskaa mukhy kaarण aanuvmshik hii maanaa jaataa hai। saath hii bढ़tii umr mem is biimaarii se piiड़it hone kii smbhaavnaa bhii bढ़ jaatii hai। iske ahm kaark nimn haim:
