dimemshiyaa ke prmukh kaarण (Causes of Dementia ​in Hindi)
- aanuvmshik: agr privaar mem koii bhii is biimaarii se piid़it ho, to khtre kii smbhaavnaa b़dh jaatii hai
- bढ़tii umr mem is biimaarii ke khtre bढ़ jaate haim। 
- uchch rktchaap se piiड़it rogiyom ko dimemshiyaa ke prti schet rhnaa chaahie। 
- mdhumeh aur motaape ko bhii iskaa mukhy kaarण maanaa jaataa hai। 
- j़yaadaa jmk phood khaane se aur aadhunik jiivnshailii se shriir se jroorii poshk ttv nhiim mil paate jis kaarण dimemshiyaa (Dementia) hone kii smbhaavnaa bढ़ jaatii hai। 

Treatments:
dimemshiyaa se bchaav aur iskaa ilaaj donom hii smbhv hai। jroorii hai to kevl shii smy pr iskii jaankaarii honaa। dimemshiyaa ke dauraan nimn baatom kaa dhyaan rkhnaa jroorii hai:
- dimemshiyaa kaa vykti aur privaar pr kyaa asr pड़egaa, yh smjhem aur sviikaarem।
- dekhbhaal kii vrshom tk chl sktii hai, islie yh jaannaa jroorii hai ki rogii kii dekhbhaal ke alaavaa aur kyaa kyaa jimmedaariym nibhaanii haim aur dekhbhaal ke lie smy aur paise kaa imtjaam kis prkaar kremge।
- islie apnii jimdgii mem usii prkaar se bdlaav laaem taaki rogii kii dekhbhaal ke saath saath aap apnii any jimmedaariym bhii nibhaa skem। iske lie jo bhii siikhnaa hai, vh siikhem, aur khushii khushii apne krtvy kaa nirvaah krem। 

Home Remedies:
dimemshiyaa yaa yaaddaasht kaa jaanaa sbhii ke lie chimtaa kaa kaarण ho sktaa hai। hm sbhii apne dimaag ko svsth rkhnaa chaahte haim। dimemshiyaa ke mriij kii yaaddaasht (memmory) jaane ke saath hii uske vyvhaar mem bhii privrtn hotaa hai jisse n kevl mriij blki privaar ke any sdsy bhii prbhaavit hote haim। aaie jaanem dimemshiyaa se bchne ke lie kuchh ghreloo upchaar-
1. chiinii ko avॉid krem (Avoid sugar)
sbse phle apne khaane se miithaa (sweet), kaarbohaaidret (carbohydrate) tthaa riphaaimd kaarbohaaidret (refined carbohydrate) sbhii ko alg kr dem। jb tk ki aapkaa vjn niymtrit nhiim ho jaataa hai, kaarbohaaidt vaalii chiijom ko khaane se bchem। bhut adhik chiinii kho se bhii dimaagii ootk (brain membrane) kmjor hote haim jiskaa asr yaaddaasht (memmory) pr pड़taa hai।
2. hldii (Haldi)
hldii mem maujood ttv krkyoomin (curcumin) dimemshiyaa se surkshaa prdaan krtaa hai। hldii mem emtiiऑksiidemt (antioxidant) ttv bhii hote haim jo dimaagii vikaas ke lie jroorii haim। aise mem bhojn mem hldii kaa istemaal jroor krem।
3. naariyl tel (Coconut oil)
naariyl tel mem khaanaa bnaane se bhii dimemshiyaa kaa upchaar smbhv hai। naariyl tel mem vsaa kii maatraa bhut jyaadaa nhiim hotii aur yh dimaag ko bhii tej krtaa hai।
4. slmn mchhlii aur mdaa (Salmon fish and egg)
thmde paanii (cold water) mem rhne vaalii mchhlii slmn aur mde kii jrdii (egg yolk) donom hii dimaag ko tej bnaatii haim। aise mem bhojn mem donom ko shaamil kiyaa jaanaa behd jroorii hai। ek din mem do mde jroor khaaem।
5. adrk (Ginger)
adrk bhii dimemshiyaa se bchaav ke lie behd phaaydemmd hai। adrk kii chaay (ginger tea), khaane mem adrk kaa pryog yaa sookhaa adrk (dry ginger), kisii bhii roop mem adrk khaanaa dimemshiyaa mem behd laabhdaayk hai।
6. griin tii (Green tea)
griin tii bhii achchhe svaasthy v achchhe dimaagii vikaas ke lie behd jroorii hai। griin tii piine se shriir mem ऑksiijn (Oxygen) kaa smchaar hotaa hai aur jmii huii vsaa (Saturated fat) door hotii hai। isse yaaddaasht bढ़tii hai aur bhoolne kii smsyaa door hotii hai।
7. baadaam (Almond)
baadaam bhii tej dimaag ke lie phaaydemmd hotaa hai। baadaam ke tel mem vsaa hotii hai jise khaane se chrbii nhiim bढ़tii aur dimaag ko any poshk ttv (nutrient) bhii milte haim, jisse n kevl shriir blki dimaag bhii svsth hotaa hai।


Disease: taaiphaaid (Typhoid)

Description: 
taaiphaaid yaa mt jvr ek gmbhiir biimaarii hai। is biimaarii mem rogii ko tej bukhaar ke saath ultii aur dst aadi kii smsyaa hotii hai। taaiphaaid (Typhoid) ek jaanlevaa biimaarii maanii jaatii hai। aaiem jaanem iske vishy mem adhik jaankaarii।

Symptoms: 
- kbj yaa dst honaa
- kbhii-kbhii shauch mem khoon kaa aanaa
- bukhaar shuroo mem hlkaa, pr dhiire-dhiire tej hotaa jaataa hai
- bhookh km lgnaa aur ultiym aanaa
- rog kii gmbhiir sthiti mem behoshii bhii aa sktii hai
- sir-drd aur bdn-drd
- sookhii khmsii aanaa aur pet mem drd

Reasons: 
maanaa jaataa hai ki taaiphaaid adhikaatr gmdgii ke kaarण phailtaa hai। shauch ke baad smkrmit vykti dvaaraa haath thiik se n dhonaa aur bhojn bnaanaa yaa bhojn ko chhoonaa bhii rog phailaa sktaa hai। kuchh any kaarण nimn haim: 
- un kshetrom mem kaam krnaa yaa yaatraa krnaa jhm yh biimaarii hai।
- glt jiivn-shailii ke kaarण shriir ke rog prtirodhk tmtr kaa kmjor honaa।
- piine ke paanii kaa jiivaaणu se prdooshit honaa।
- shauch ke baad saaph-sphaaii kaa dhyaan naa rkhnaa। 

Treatments:
taaiphaaid kaa upchaar (Treatment of Typhoid in Hindi)
- dॉktr ke praamrsh se bld test ke baad hii dॉktr ke praamrsh ke anusaar hii chikitsaa kraaem।
- taaiphaaid kii dvaa ko biich mem n chhoड़em। bukhaar mem peraasiitaamol kaa istemaal krem।
- rogii ke shriir mem paanii kii kmii n hone paae, iske lie rogii ko paanii aur any trl pdaarth pryaapt maatraa mem dem। 
- rogii ke aaspaas saaph-sphaaii kaa vishesh dhyaan rkhem। 

Home Remedies:
taaiphaaid kaa bukhaar paachn tmtr aur bldstriim (blood stream) mem baiktiiriyaa ke imphekshn ke kaarण hotaa hai। slomonelaa taaiphii (salomonela typhi) naam kaa yh baiktiiriyaa (bacteria) paanii, kisii pey yaa khaane ke saath hmaare shriir ke mdr prvesh krtaa hai aur paachn tmtr mem jaakr yh baiktiiriyaa bढ़ jaate haim। yh baiktiiriyaa shriir ke bhiitr ek jgh se doosrii jgh jaise, livr, spliin, gॉlbledr aadi jghom pr ghoomte rhte haim।
taaiphaaid kaa bukhaar adhikmsht dooshit paanii (polluted water) piine se hotaa hai। taaiphaaid ke lkshणom mem sir mem drd (headache), pet mem drd (pain in stomach) aur bukhaar kaa honaa hai lekin taaiphaaid ke bigड़ne pr ultii (Vomiting), daayriyaa (diarrhea), ml mem khoon aanaa (blood in stool), livr kaa bढ़naa (enlargement of liver) aadi bhii ho skte haim। taaiphaaid mem laaprvaahii nhiim brtnii chaahie tthaa iskaa kors pooraa kiyaa jaanaa bhii jroorii hai kyomki iske dobaaraa hone ke chmses bhii rhte hai। taaiphaaid se nijaat ke lie yhm hm aapko kuchh ghreloo nuskhom ke baare mem btaaemge jinhem apnaakr aap taaiphaaid se raaht paa skte haim।
1. thmdaa paanii (Cold water)
kisii kpड़e ko thmde paanii mem bhigokr shriir ko pomchhe। iske alaavaa thmde paanii kii pttiym sir pr rkhne se bhii laabh hotaa he aur shriir kaa taapmaan km hotaa hai। kpड़e ko smy smy pr bdlte rhnaa chaahie। saamaany bukhaar ke lie yh behd achchhii prkriyaa hai jo taapmaan ko bढ़ne nhiim detii।
not- iske lie brph yaa brph ke paanii kii istemaal n krke, taaje paanii kaa istemaal krem।
2. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)
seb kaa sirkaa bhii bukhaar ke lie behd sstii aur prbhaavii dvaa hai। isse bukhaar ko tejii se door hotaa hai kyomki ismem maujood esid grmaaht ko shriir kii tvchaa se baahr kr detaa hai। saath hii ismem maujood minrl shriir ko bukhaar se door bhii rkhte haim।
kaise krem upyog
kisii kpड़e ko ek bhaag sirkaa aur do bhaag paanii lekr usmem bhigoem। atirikt paanii ko nichoड़ dem aur is pttii ko maathe aur pet pr rkhem। ek pttii pair ke tlvom pr bhii rkhii jaa sktii hai। jaise hii kpड़aa grm ho jaae, dobaaraa ghol mem dubaaem aur prkriyaa ko dohraaem।
4. lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun kii grm taasiir bhii shriir mem psiinaa laakr, shriir kaa taapmaan km kr sktii hai। yh shriir se haanikaark vishaakt pdaarthom ko bhii baahr nikaalne mem shaayk hai। itnaa hii nhiim lhsun emtiiphmgl (antifungal) aur emtiibaiktiiriyl (Antibacterial) guणom se bhraa hai jo shriir ko imyoonitii (Immunity) detaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
lhsun kii ek klii ko piiskr grm paanii mem milaaem। 10 mint dhk kr rkhem। paanii ko chhaan lem aur ghoomt ghoomt krke dhiire dhiire piiem। ek din mem is pey ko do baar piiem। agle hii din aap bukhaar se raaht mhsoos kremge।
do chmmch ऑliv ऑyl (olive oil) mem do klii lhsun kii daalkr bhoonem। is tel ko thmdaa krke pair ke tlvom (sole of feet) mem lgaaem।
5. tulsii (Basil)
tulsii bhii taaiphaaid ke bukhaar ke lie uttm aushdhi hai। iske emtiibaiktiiriyl (Antibacterial) aur emtiibaayotik (Antibiotic) guण baiktiiriyaa ko khtm krte hai, jisse bukhaar jldii bhii thiik hotaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
pudiine kii biis pttiyom mem ek chhotii chmmch adrk (Ginger) ko kddooks krke ek kp paanii mem ubaal lem। is paanii ko gungunaa rhne tk imtjaar krem। iske baad ise chhaankr ismem shhd milaakr piiem। is pey ko din do se tiin baar le skte haim।
6. laumg (Laung or clove)
laumg mem taaiphaaid ko thiik krne ke guण hote haim। laumg ke tel mem emtiibaiktiiriyl (Antibacterial) guण hote haim jo ki baiktiiriyaa ko maar dete haim।
kaise krem upyog
aath kp paanii mem 5 se 7 laumg daalkr ubaal lem। jb paanii aadhaa rh jaae ise chhaan lem। is paanii ko pooraa din piiem। is upchaar ko ek hphte lgaataar krem।


Disease: joom~ (Lice)

Description: 
joom (Head Lice) til ke aakaar kii ek chhotii prjiivii hai jo mnushy ke shriir mem paidaa ho jaatii haim। saamaanyt: yh baalom mem paaye jaate haim। ye bd़ii tejii se chl sktii haim। is kaarण baalom ke biich inhem khojnaa kthin ho jaataa hai। ye sbhii umr tthaa prjaatiyom ke logom ko smkrmit krtii haim।

Symptoms: 
- sir mem khujlii honaa

Reasons: 
juem tejii se, ek vykti se doosre vykti tk phail sktii haim। yh behd tejii se chltii haim। juom ke phailne ke kuchh kaarण nimn haim: 
juem phailne ke kaarण (Cause of Head Lices in Hindi)
- hait, skaarph, kmghii, brsh, heyr klip athvaa bairet, heyr baimd, helmet athvaa kpd़om, kaa adl-bdlkr istemaal krte haim।
- ek hii bistr, plmg athvaa kaaliin kaa pryog krte/krtii haim।
- bhut nikt rhkr khelte haim।
- aise almaarii athvaa lॉkr mem rkhii gii, vstuom kaa pryog krte haim, jin mem juem athvaa unke mde maujood hote haim।

Treatments:
kaise roke joom ko phailne se (Treatment of Head Lice in Hindi)
- saamaany shaimpoo se baal saaph krem। kmdiishnr kaa pryog n krem। iske kaarण juom kii dvaa kaa prbhaav smaapt ho sktaa hai।
- grm paanii se baal dhokr unhem tauliye se sukhaa lem। is tauliye kaa dubaaraa pryog tb tk n krem, jb tk yh dho n liyaa jaae।
- baalom pr sphed sirkaa lgaaem - yh us ‘gomd’ ko dhiilaa krne mem shaayk hotaa hai, jo ‘liikhom’ ko baalom se chipkaae hue hai।
- baalom ko mhiin kmghii se saaph krem, jisse ye mde nikl aaem। baalom ko idhr-udhr krke kmghii krnaa upyogii ho sktaa hai।
- sbhii mdom kaa htaayaa jaanaa aavshyk hai। ismem 2 athvaa 3 ghmte yaa adhik smy lg sktaa haim, tthaa ydi kmghii kaam nhiim krtii hai to aapko haathom sm mde chunne pd़ skte haim।
- privaar mem jitne logom ko joom~em haim sb kaa upchaar ek saath ho। 
- kpड़e bistr aadi dhoop mem rkhem yaa grm paanii mem dhoem। 
- roosii
- roosii
- baalom kaa jhड़naa

Home Remedies:
joom~ ek chhotaa prjiivii (parasite) hai jo baalom kii jड़om aur baalom ke nichle hisse pr chipke rhte haim, jhm yh sir kii tvchaa se khoon ko piikr jimdaa rhte haim। bchchom mem joom~ hone kii smsyaa aam hai। ydi aap joom~ vaale kisii vykti ke smprk mem aate haim to yh aapko bhii ho skte haim। saath hii imphekted vykti kaa saamaan jaise kmghii aur kpड़e aadi istemaal krne se bhii joom~ hone kii smbhaavnaa rhtii hai।
sir mem joom~ hone kaa sbse aam lkshण hai sir mem khujlii honaa aur sir kii tvchaa pr laal chktte pड़naa। yh bhut tejii se bढ़te haim islie inhem jldii khtm krnaa bhut mushkil hotaa hai। kuchh ghreloo upchaar ke dvaaraa joom~ se nijaat paaii jaa sktii hai। aaie aapko btaaem aise hii kuchh ghreloo upchaar ke baare mem-
1. lhsun (Garlic)- lhsun kii tej mhk juom kaa dm ghottii hai aur unhem maar detii hai।
kaise krem upyog
aath se ds lhsun kii kliyom ko piiskr ismem niimboo kaa rs milaaem aur baalom kii jड़om mem lgaaem। aadhe ghmte baad baalom ko grm paanii se dho lem।
lhsun kii kliyom ko piiskr, usmem khaane vaalaa tel milaaem। iske baad ismem shaimpoo yaa kmdiishnr mem milaakr baalom mem lgaaem। aadhe ghmte ke lie baalom ko yoom hii chhoड़ dem aur dho dem।
2. bebii ऑyl (Baby oil)- bebii ऑyl mem kpड़e dhone vaalaa ditrjemt aur kuchh sirkaa milaakr baalom mem lgaane se bhii joom~ kaa ilaaj smbhv hai। bebii ऑyl bhii joom~ kaa dm ghomt detaa hai jisse vh mr jaatii haim।
kaise krem upyog
bebii ऑyl ko baalom mem lgaakr, ptle dmtom vaalii kmghii se baal kaaढ़em। joom~ girnii shuroo ho jaaemgii। iske baad baalom ko ditrjemt aur grm paanii se dho lem। sone jaane se phle baalom mem sirkaa lgaaem aur baalom ko shaavr kaip se dhk lem aur poorii raat yoom hii chhoड़ dem। subh saamaany shaimpoo se baal dho lem। shaimpoo ke baad kmdiishnr krem।
3. ऑliv ऑyl (Olive oil)- ऑliv ऑyl bhii joom~ maarne mem bhut prbhaavii hai।
kaise krem upyog
baalom mem kisii bhii prkaar kaa ऑliv ऑyl sone se phle lgaaem। shaavr kaip lgaakr raat bhr tel ko baalom mem yoom hii chhoड़ dem। subh mem baalom ko kmghii krem, joom~ baahr nikl aaemgii। iske baad baalom ko shaimpoo kr lem।
aadhaa kp ऑliv ऑyl mem aadhaa kp kmdiishnr milaakr ismem kuchh likvid saabun milaaem। ise baalom kii jड़om mem lgaakr ek ghmtaa chhoड़ dem aur baal dho lem aur kmghii krke joom~ baahr nikaal dem। ise ek hphte baad dobaaraa dohraaem।
4. nmk (Salt)- nmk bhii joom~ nikaalne mem behd asrkaarii hai।
kaise krem upyog
ek chauthaaii kp nmk mem itnaa hii sirkaa milaakr is ghol ko baalom mem spre krem। spre kie hue giile baalom pr shaavr kaip phnem aur do ghmte yoom hii chhoड़ dem। iske baad baal dho lem aur baalom pr kmdiishnr krem। hr tiisre din is prkriyaa ko dohraaem।
5. petroliym jelii (Petrolium jelly)- petroliym jelii remgne vaale (roaming around) juom ko turmt maar detii hai।
kaise krem upyog
sone se phle baalom kii jड़om mem petroliym jelii lgaaem। iske baad kpड़e se baalom ko bmdh kr so jaaem। subh bebii ऑyl se jelii htaaem aur kmghii krke joom~ ko baahr nikaalem।
6. naariyl kaa tel (Coconut oil)
naariyl kaa tel remgne vaale juom pr asr dikhaataa hai saath hii inkii smkhyaa ko bढ़ne se roktaa hai।
kaise krem upyog
sbse phle baalom ko seb ke sirke (Apple cider vinegar) se dhoem। baalom ko poorii rh sukhaakr jड़om mem naariyl kaa tel lgaaem। chhh se aath ghmtom ke lie baalom ko yoom hii chhoड़ dem। iske baad baalom ko shaimpoo krke kmghii krem aur joom~ nikaalem।
7. sphed sirkaa (White vinegar)
sphed sirke mem maujood esiitik esid joom~ ko maartaa hai। yh joom ko maarne kaa surkshit aur sstaa triikaa hai। kisii tel mem sphed sirkaa milaakr baalom mem lgaakr kuchh ghmte chhoड़ dem aur phir shaimpoo krem।


Disease: kbj (Constipation)

Description: 
kbj ek behd aam biimaarii bn chukii hai। ml tyaag ek praakृtik kriyaa hai। lekin jb ml tyaag krne mem agr preshaanii aatii hai to us smsyaa ko kbj (Kabj) khte haim। aniymit khaanpaan aur glt jiivnshailii ke kaarण yh biimaarii lgaataar bढ़tii jaa rhii hai।

Symptoms: 
- aimthn ho, drd ho, pet phool jaae yaa mtlii ho
- aisaa mhsoos ho ki aapkii m~tड़iym poorii trh se khaalii nhiim huii ho
- ml tyaag ke lie ज़or lgaanaa pड़e

Reasons: 
- aise aahaar jinmem chrbii aur shkkr jyaadaa hom aur reshe km hom। 
- kaaphii maatraa mem trl pdaarth n lenaa। 
- nishkriy rhnaa। 
- jb aap ko ml tyaag kii ichchhaa ho tb shauchaaly n jaanaa।

Treatments:
kaise door krem kbज़ (Treatment of Constipation in Hindi)
- din mem km se km 8-10 gilaas paanii piinaa chaahie। gungune yaa grm paanii se aapkii m~tom ko aasaanii se kaam krne mem mdd mil sktii hai।
- brain siriyl, hol gren bred, kchchii sbjiym, taaje yaa sukhaaye hue phl, sookhaa mevaa aur pॉpkॉrn jaisii adhik reshe vaalii chiijem khaaie। reshe shriir se ml ko niklne mem mdd krte haim।
- chiiज़, chॉklet aur aणkdem aadi km khaanaa chaahie kyomki inse kbj (Kabj) bढ़ sktii hai।
- ml ko nrm krne ke lie aaloo bukhaare yaa seb kaa rs piijie।
- apnii m~tom ko thiik se kaam krne mem mdd krne ke lie ksrt kiijie।
- kbj mem paidl chlne se laabh hotaa hai।
- jb aap ko ml tyaag krne kii ichchhaa ho, shauchaaly jaaem।
- eniimaa kaa upyog krne se phle apne chikitsk kii slaah lem।

Home Remedies:
- ek chutkii kaalaa nmk gungune paanii mem daalem aur use subh khaalii pet piikr 15 mint tk chhlkdmii krem, kbज़ mem avshy hii raaht milegii।
- apne bhojn mem mote anaaj (Bran) kaa smaavesh krem। mausm ke anusaar uplbdh slaad ko shaamil krne se kbj aur pet kii doosrii tmaam smsyaaom se sthaaii roop se chhutkaaraa paayaa jaa sktaa hai।
- alsii ke biij (Flaxseed) kaa sevn bhii kbज़ se aaraam dilaataa hai। alsii ke biij ko subh kॉrnphleks (Cornflax) ke saath milaakr khaa skte haim yaa phir mutthii bhr alsii ke biij ko grm paanii ke saath subh khaa skte haim।
- kishmish phaaibr(Fiber) se bhrpoor hotii hai aur praakृtik julaab kii trh kaam krtii hai। १०-१२-kishmish ko raat mem paanii mem bhigokr rkh dem aur subh khaalii pet khaaem। grbhaavsthaa (Pregnancy) mem mhilaao ko aksr kbज़ kii shikaayt rhtii hai, grbhvtii mhilaaom (Pregnant Females)ke lie yh bhut laabhkaarii upaay hai।
- amrood (Gauva) bhii kbज़ mem bhut raaht phum~chaataa hai। iske goode aur biij mem phaaibr kii uchit maatraa hotaa hai। iske sevn se khaanaa jldii pch jaataa hai aur esiditii (Acidity) se bhii raaht miltii hai, saath hii pet bhii saaph ho jaataa hai।
- ek gilaas gungune paanii mem niimboo (Lime) aur nmk (Salt) milaakr subh khaalii pet piine se bhii kbज़ mem kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai।


Disease: uchch rktchaap (High Blood Pressure)

Description: 
haaii bld preshr yaa uchch rktchaap kii smsyaa aajkl behd aam hotii jaa rhii hai। uchch rktchaap ke dauraan mriij ke shriir mem rkt kaa prvaah behd tej ho jaataa hai। is sthiti mem aapke hृdy ko adhik kaam krnaa pड़taa hai। aaiye jaanem isse juड़ii any baatem:

Symptoms: 
- ultii hone kii shikaayt aur chidchidaapn
- km mehnt krne pr sm~s phoolnaa,  thkaavt rhnaa
- chkkr aanaa
- tmgom mem drd
- tnaav honaa
- naak se khoon aanaa
- niimd n aanaa
- lgaataar sirdrd honaa, sir chkraanaa
- sms lene mem kthinaaii
- sir ke piichhe v grdn mem drd
- hृdy kii dhd़kn tej rhnaa
- hृdy kshetr mem piid़aa mhsoos krnaa

Reasons: 
uchch rktchaap ke hone mem bhut saare phaiktrs ahm bhoomikaa nibhaate haim jinmem se sbse mhtvpoorण hai aasiin jiivnshailii। shaariirik shrm kii kmii ke kaarण bhii kii baar yh biimaarii logom ko preshaan krtii hai। uchch rktchaap ke kii any kaarण nimn haim: 
uchch rktchaap ke kaarण (Reason for High Blood Pressure)
- dhoomrpaan
- motaapaa
- nishkriytaa
- nmk kaa jyaadaa sevn
- shraab piinaa
- tnaav
- bढ़tii umr
- aanuvmshiktaa
- paarivaarik itihaas
- puraanii kidnii kii biimaarii
- thaairoid disऑrdr 

Treatments:
rktchaap (Blood Pressure) bढ़ne pr kis trh apnaa dhyaan rkhnaa iskii jaankaarii honaa behd jroorii hai। saath hii smy-smy pr dॉktrii jmch is biimaarii se bchaane mem bhut kaargr hotii hai। uchch rktchaap se bchne ke kuchh prmukh upaay nimn haim:
- prtidin ek ghmtaa hlkaa yaa tej kisii prkaar kaa vyaayaam jroor krem।
- khaane mem haaii phaaiibr vaale chiijem lenii chaahie। 
- khud ko ektiv rkhne kaa adhik se adhik pryaas krnaa chaahie। 
- smy-smy pr dॉktr kii slaah lenii chaahie। 

Home Remedies:
uchch rktchaap (High Blood Pressure) yoom to jiivnshailii se smbmdhit ek saamaany biimaarii hai lekin yhii kii any bड़ii bimaariyom kii shuroovaat yaa vjh bhii hai। kii baar uchch rktchaap se vykti kii mृtyu tk smbhv hai।
dil kii bimaariym (Heart Disease),  enjaainaa (Engina) aur strok (Stroke) aadi sbhii smsyaaem uchch rktchaap ke kaarण hotii haim yhm tk kii kii baar shugr ke lie bhii uchch rktchaap jimmedaar hotaa hai।
haalmki ydi apne svaasthy kaa dhyaan rkhaa jaae to kii ghreloo upaayom se bhii uchch rktchaap ko thiik kiyaa jaanaa smbhv hai। aaie jaante haim kuchh aise hii ghreloo upchaarom ke baare mem।
uchch rktchaap ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for High Blood Pressure)
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun ko khaalii pet subh kchchaa hii khaaem। lhsun mem rkt ko ptlaa krne ke guण hote haim jo ki rkt kaa thkkaa jmne se bhii roktaa hai। chikitsk se praamrsh lekr lhsun kr pryog shuroo kr skte haim।
shhjn kii phlii (Drum Sticks)
shhjn mem protiin, vitaamin aur any poshk ttv maujood hote haim jo ki shaariirik svaasthy kii dृshti se behd jroorii haim। shhjn kaa upyog krne kaa aasaan triikaa hai ki iskii phliyom ko daal ke saath bnaakr khaayaa jaae। isse bhii uchch rktchaap nॉrml hotaa hai।
mvlaa (Indian Gooseberry)
mvlaa mem vitaamin sii kii uchch maatraa hotii hai jo ki shriir se kolestrॉl (cholesterol) kii maatraa ko km krtii hai। isse dil svsth rhtaa hai aur uchch rkt chaap niymtrit।
moolii (Radish)
rsoiighr mem pryog hone vaalii aam sbjii hai moolii, lekin ismem uchch rktchaap ko niymtrit krne ke guण hote haim। moolii ko slaad ke roop mem kchchaa yaa dhii ke saath milaakr khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
til (Sesame)
til daaystolik aur sistolik (Diastolic and Systolic) , donom trh ke rktchaap ko niymtrit krtaa hai। til ke tel mem sismin (Sesamin) aur sisminॉl (Sesaminol) donom hote haim jo ki shriir ke tnaav ko km krne mem ahm bhoomikaa nibhaate haim।
til kaa khaane mem pryog krne se uchch rktchaap ko niymtrit kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। til ke lddoo yaa til kaa paaudr slaad yaa daal sbjii mem oopr se chhid़kkr khaane se laabh hotaa hai।
alsii ke biij (Flex Seed)
alsii ke biij omegaa-3 phaitii esid mem se ek hai jisse ismem alphaa linolenik esid (Alfa Linolenic Acid) naamk yaugik kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। yh uchch rktchaap ko niymtrit krne ke saath hii kelॉstrॉl kii maatraa bhii ghtaataa hai jisse hृdy bhii svsth bntaa hai।


Disease: dmt kaa drd (Toothache)

Description: 
dmt hmaare shriir kaa mhtvpoorण hissaa haim। baat muskuraane kii ho yaa kuchh khaane kii binaa dmt sb bekaar hai। lekin kisii bhii kaarण ydi dmtom mem drd ho jaae to vykti baichen ho jaataa hai। dmtom kaa drd yoom to ek aam smsyaa hai, lekin iskaa drd ashniiy hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- chbaane mem drd honaa
- bukhaar, sirdrd
- sms lene mem kthinaaii

Reasons: 
dmtom mem drd ke kii kaarण ho skte haim। dmtom kii thiik se sphaaii n krnaa, dmtom mem kaivitii honaa yaa atydhik miithaa khaanaa। iske saath hii chaay kaaphii jyaadaa piinaa। iske saath hii kuchh any kaarण bhii haim jaise: 
dmtom mem drd kaa kaarण (Causes of Tooth Pain)
1. msooड़om mem imphekshn- ydi kisii bhii kaarण se msooड़om mem imphekshn hai to yh dmt drd kaa kaarण ho sktaa hai। iske kaarण tooth ineml (Tooth Enamel) kii smsyaa bhii hotii hai। isse dmtom mem thmdaa grm lgnaa, mumh kaa svaad bigड़naa, grdn kii glaimd mem soojn aanaa, msooड़om mem soojn aanaaaadi smsyaaem aa sktii haim।
2. kaivitiij- iske kaarण dmtom kii ooprii prt nsht ho jaatii hai। kॉrbohaaiidret vaalaa khaanaa jismem bred, sodaa kek yaa kaimdii aadi dmtom pr chipk jaae aur achchhii trh se saaph n ho to kaivitii (Cavity) ho sktii hai jiskaa priणaam hotaa hai dmtom mem drd।
3. dmt mem kiiड़aa- isse dmt poorii trh khokhlaa ho jaataa hai aur unmem khaanaa bhr jaataa hai। jo ki drd kaa kaarण bntaa hai। drd ke kaarण dmt kaam nhiim krtaa aur un pr ek prkaar kii gmdgii jmne lgtii hai।
4. toote dmt- kuchh khaate vkt yaa kisii any kaarण se ydi dmt toot ge haim to aise dmtom mem drd kii shikaayt aksr rhtii hai। aise dmtom ke ineml kmjor ho jaatii hai jisse ye semsitiv ho jaate haim।
5. philimg- ydi dmtom mem philimg (Tooth Filling) kraaii gii ho to yh bhii kii baar yh dmt drd kaa kaarण ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
​dmt drd hone pr thmde paanii se kullaa krnaa phaaydemmd hotaa hai lekin agr isse poorण aaraam nhiim mil paae to nimn upaay krne chaahie:
- koii penkilr lem।
- aais paik yaa tॉvel mem aais lpetkr use gaalom pr kuchh der ke lie rkhem। agr gaalom mem sooj़n aa jaae aur drd ho to phroj़en piij़ ko aaispaik kii jgh lgaaem~। ye chehre ke aakaar ke anusaar bdl skte haim।
- agr do dinom mem drd nhiim jaataa to dentist (Dentist) ke paas jaaem~। ho sktaa haim j़yaadaa kॅvitii yaa kraik kii vjh se drd ho।
- dmt kaa dॉktr aapke mumh kii jmch kregaa aur eks-re legaa। phir dmt kaa dॉktr dmt ko thiik kregaa yaa nikaal degaa। aapko drd nivaark dvaaem yaa emtiibaayotik lene ke lie khaa jaa sktaa hai। dॉktr kii btaaii gii dvaaem lem।

Home Remedies:
dmtom kaa drd vaise to ek saamaany smsyaa hai, lekin iskaa drd ashniiy hotaa hai। ydi aapko bhii kbhii dmt mem drd ho to ghbraaem nhiim, kuchh ghreloo upaay apnaakr aap is tkliiph se bch skte haim।

1. laumg- ydi dmt mem drd ho to laumg kaa tel rooii mem bhigokr dmt pr lgaaie। koshish kiijie ki tel msooड़om pr n lge kyomki isse hlkii jln mhsoos ho sktii hai।
2. elkohl- jii hm aapne thiik pढ़aa elkohl। ek sip elkohl se kullaa krne pr bhii drd mem aaraam miltaa hai। isse drd vaalaa hissaa sunn ho jaataa hai। lekin sthaaii yh ilaaj nhiim hai।
3. viks- viks ko apne chehre ke us hisse kii trph lgaaie jis trph dmt mem drd ho। iske baad chehre ko dhmk lem। isse drd mem aaraam miltaa hai।
4. aais- brph ke tukड़e se sikaaii krne pr bhii dmt drd mem behd aaraam miltaa hai।
5. kaalii mirch- kaalii mirch ke paaudr ko msooड़om pr rgड़ne se bhii drd kaa hissaa sunn ho jaataa hai aur drd mem aaraam miltaa hai।
6. kchchii pyaaj- kchchii pyaaj ko 3 mint tk drd vaale hisse pr rgड़em, isse bhii drd mem bhut aaraam miltaa hai।
7. lhsun- lhsun kii klii ko chbaakr uske rs ko laar ke saath milkaar kullaa krem। kuchh hii sekemd mem drd mem aaraam milegaa।
8. vniilaa ark- vniilaa ark kii kuchh boomde rooii mem lekr drd vaale hisse pr lgaaem। dmt drd mem aaraam milegaa। 
9. gehoom ke paudhe kaa rs- mkurit gehoom ke paudhe kaa rs bhii kulle ke roop mem pryog kr dmt drd se bchaa jaa sktaa hai। yh msooड़om ke vishm pdaarthom ko nikaalkr jiivaaणuom kii vृddhi ko roktaa hai।
10. pairॉksaaid- dmtom mem drd hone pr pairॉksaaid se kullaa krem। lekin dhyaan rhe ise kbhii niglem nhiim। isse bhii dmt drd mem aaraam miltaa hai।


Disease: demgoo (Dengue)

Description: 
demgoo, maadaa ediij (Female Aedes) mchchhr ke kaatne se hotaa hai। ye mchchhr din mem, khaaskr subh kaatte haim। mriij mem agr jtil trh ke demgoo kaa ek bhii lkshण dikhaaii de to use jldii - se - jldii dॉktr ke paas le jaaem। diiecheph ( DHF - Dengue Hemorrhagic Fever) aur diieses (DSS - Dengue Shock Syndrome) bukhaar demgoo ke do prkaar haim jinmem pletlets (Platelets) kaaphii km ho jaate haim, jiske kaarण shriir ke jroorii mgom pr buraa asr pd़ sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- ultii v shriir pr laal-laal daane nikl aate haim
- kmjorii ho jaatii hai aur chkkr aate haim
- demgoo bukhaar ke lkshण aam bukhaar se thod़e alg hote haim
- demgoo shॉk simdrom (DSS) ke mriijom mem saadhaarण demgoo bukhaar aur demgoo haimrejik bukhaar ke lkshणem ke saath-saath bechainii mhsoos ho
- demgoo hemorejik bukhaar mem uprokt lkshणom ke alaavaa pletlets kii kmii se shriir mem khiim se bhii khoon bhnaa shuroo ho sktaa hai, jaise naak se, dm~tom v msooड़om se, khoon kii ultii v ml mem khoon aanaa aadi
- thkaavt v kmjorii hai
- naad़ii kbhii tej aur kbhii dhiire chlnelgtii hai  aur rkt chaap  (Blood Pressure)  ekdm km ho jaataa hai
- bukhaar bhut tej hotaa hai
- sirdrd, kmr v joड़om mem drd hotaa hai
- hlkii khm~sii v gle mem khraash mhsoos hotii hai

Reasons: 
- khaalii brtnom ko ultaa krke rkhem।
- pkshiyom ke khaane- piine ke brtnom ko hr roj saaph krem।
- agr ghr mem koolr hai to uskaa paanii do yaa tiin din baad avshy bdlem।
- ghr mem sthit haudiyom, taimkrom mem paanii ko saaph rkhne ke lie usmem kloriin kii do chaar goliym daal dem।
- ghr ke aas- paas yaa chht pr pड़e bekaar taayr, tyoob, toote hue mtke, khaalii dibbom aadi mem brsaat kaa paanii ikththaa n hone dem।
- paark mem jaate smy yaa aisii jgh jaate smy jhm mchchhrom ke kaatne kaa khtraa ho, vhm poorii  baajoo ke kpड़e phnne chaahie taaki mchchhr naa kaatem। 
- mchchhrom se bchne ke lie kriim, mchchhrdaanii aur any upaayom kaa istemaal krnaa chaahie। 

Treatments:
demgoo se bchaav kaa sbse behtriin upaay hai gmdgii kaa jmaa naa hone denaa। agr maadaa ediij mchchhr pnpemge hii to demgoo hone kii aashmkaa bhii behd km hogii। demgoo hone pr nimn upaay krne chaahie:
- saadhaarण demgoo bukhaar kaa ilaaj ghr pr hii ho sktaa hai। mriij ko pooraa aaraam krne dem। use hr chhh ghmte mem pairaasitaamol (Paracetamol) dem aur baar- baar paanii aur trl chiijem ( niiboo paanii, chhaachh, naariyl paanii aadi ) pilaaem।
- bchchom kaa khaas khyaal rkhem।
- bukhaar km hone ke baad bhii ek-do din mem ek baar pletlets kaaumt test jroor kraaem। demgoo mem mriij ke rktchaap, khaaskr oopr aur niiche ke rktchaap ke mtr pr lgaataar nigraanii ( din mem 3-4 baar ) rkhnaa jroorii hai। donom rktchaap ke biich kaa phrk 20 digrii yaa usse km ho jaae to sthiti khtrnaak ho sktii hai। rktchaap girne se mriij behosh ho sktaa hai।
- bchche naajuk hote haim aur unkaa imyoon sistm (Immune System of Kids) kmjor hotaa hai islie biimaarii unhem jldii pkड़ letii hai। aise mem unkii biimaarii ko njrmdaaj n krem।
- bchche khule mem jyaadaa rhte haim islie inphekshn hone aur mchchhrom se kaate jaane kaa khtraa unmem jyaadaa hotaa hai।
- bchchom ghr se baahr poore kpd़e phnaakr bhejem।
- mchchhrom ke mausm mem bchchom ko nikr v tii - shrt n phnaaem।
- raat mem mchchhr bhgaane kii kriim lgaaem।
- agr bchchaa bhut jyaadaa ro rhaa ho, lgaataar soe jaa rhaa ho, bechain ho, use tej bukhaar ho, shriir pr raishej hom, ultii ho yaa inmem se koii bhii lkshण ho to phaurn dॉktr ko dikhaaem।
- aamtaur pr chhote bchchom ko bukhaar hone pr unke haath - pmv to thmde rhte haim lekin maathaa aur pet grm rhte haim islie unke pet ko chhookr aur rektl temprechr lekr unkaa bukhaar chek kiyaa jaataa hai। bgl se taapmaan lenaa shii triikaa nhiim hai, khaaskr bchchom mem। agr bgl se taapmaan lenaa hii hai to jo riidimg aae, usmem 1 digrii jod़ dem। use hii shii riidimg maanaa jaaegaa।
- bchche ko demgoo ho to use asptaal mem rkhkr hii ilaaj kraanaa chaahie kyomki bchchom mem pletlets jldii girte haim aur unmem diihaaidreshn (paanii kii kmii) bhii jldii hotaa hai।

Home Remedies:
demgoo ediij mchchhr (Adeej Mosquito) dvaaraa phailne vaalii biimaarii hai jo ki haal ke smy mem tejii se bढ़ rhii hai। demgoo ke baare mem sbse khaas baat yh hai ki iske mchchhr din ke smy kaatte haim tthaa yh mchchhr saaph paanii (Clean Water) mem pnpte haim। demgoo ke dauraan rogii ke joड़om mem tej drd (Pain in Joints) hotaa hai tthaa sir mem bhii drd (Headache) kaaphii tej hotaa hai। bड़om ke mukaable yh bchchom mem jyaadaa tejii phailtaa hai।
demgoo ke dauraan ydi turmt upchaar n kiyaa jaae to yh jaanlevaa bhii ho sktaa hai, kyomki demgoo bukhaar mem pletlets (Platelates) kaa str bhut tejii se niiche girtaa hai jisse kii baar mdroonii rktstraav (Internal Bleeding) hone kii smbhaavnaa bhii rhtii hai।
demgoo se bchaav ke lie kuchh ghreloo upaay bhii haim jinhem apnaakr demgoo se bchaav smbhv hai। aaie aapko bhii btaate haim ki kaun se ghreloo upaay aapko demgoo se bchaa skte haim-
demgoo ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Dengue)
dhniyaa pttii (Coriander Leaves)
demgoo ke bukhaar se raaht ke lie dhniyaa pttii ke joos ko tॉnik ke roop mem piyaa jaa sktaa hai। yh bukhaar ko km krtaa hai।
mvlaa (Indian Gooseberry)
mvlaa mem vitaamin sii kii uchch maatraa hotii hai jisse ki shriir mem ebjॉrb krne kii kshmtaa bढ़tii hai। isse shriir jyaadaa lauh ttv ebjॉrb kr paataa hai jo ki demgoo ke bukhaar ko thiik krne ke lie jroorii hai।
tulsii (Basil)
tulsii ke pttom ko grm paanii mem ubaalkr chhaankr, rogii ko piine ko dem। tulsii kii yh chaay demgoo rogii ko behd aaraam phumchaatii hai। yh chaay dinbhr mem tiin se chaar baar lii jaa sktii hai।
ppiite kii pttii (Papaya Leaves)
ppiite kii pttiym, demgoo ke bukhaar ke lie sbse asrkaarii dvaa khii jaatii hai। ppiite kii pttiyom mem maujood ppen emjaaim (papain enjymes) shriir kii paachn shkti ko thiik krtaa hai, saath hii shriir mem praatiin ko gholne kaa kaam krtaa hai। demgoo ke upchaar ke lie ppiite kii pttiyom kaa joos nikaal kr ek ek chmmch krke rogii ko dem। is joos se pletlets kii maatraa tejii se bढ़tii hai।
bkrii kaa doodh (Goat Milk)
demgoo bukhaar ke lie ek aur buht prbhaavshaalii dvaa hai bkrii kaa doodh। bhut km hochukii pletlets ko bhii bkrii kaa doodh turmt bढ़aane kii kshmtaa rkhtaa hai। demgoo ke upchaar ke lie rogii ko bkrii kaa kchchaa doodh thoड़aa-thoड़aa krke pilaaem, isse pletlets bढ़emge aur joड़om ke drd mem bhii aaraam milegaa।
chiraaytaa (Chirayta)
chiraaytaa mem bukhaar ko thiik krne ke guण hote haim। demgoo ke bukhaar ko bhii chiraaytaa ke istemaal se thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
dhtooraa (Dhatura)
dhtoore kii pttiyom mem demgoo ke bukhaar ko thiik krne ke guण hote haim, lekin iskii khuraak 2 desiigraam se adhik nhiim honii chaahie।
methii ke ptte (Fenugreek Leaves)
methii ke ptte bhii demgoo ke bukhaar ko thiik kr skte haim। methii ke pttom ko paanii mem ubaalkr hrbl chaay ke roop mem iskaa pyog kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। methii se shriir ke vishaakt pdaarth baahr nikl jaate haim jisse demgoo ke vaayrs bhii khtm hote haim।
anaar aur kaale mgoor (Pomegranate and Black Grapes)
demgoo bukhaar mem rkt kii kmii ko pooraa krne aur pletlets ke str ko bढ़aane ke lie anaar aur kaale mgoor kaa rs piinaa chaahie।
smtre kaa joos (Orange juice)
vitaamin sii se bhrpoor smtraa, paachn shktii ko bढ़aavaa detaa hai saath hii shriir kaa imyoonitii bhii bढ़aataa hai। aise mem demgoo rogii ko jld se jld svsth hone ke lie smtre ke rs kaa sevn krnaa chaahie।


Disease: mleriyaa (Malaria)

Description: 
mleriyaa bukhaar ke kaarण prtivrsh kii kii log apnii jaan gmvaa dete haim। gmde paanii mem pnpne vaale mchchhrom ke kaatne se phailnii vaalii is biimaarii ke vishy mem jaankaarii behd kaargr hai। aaie jaanem mleriyaa ke baarem mem:

Symptoms: 
- ultii aanaa honaa
- eniimiyaa honaa
- thmd lgkr bukhaar chdhऩaa
- drd aur aimthn honaa
- psiinaa aanaa
- mleriyaa bukhaar 10-15 din rhtaa hai
- ye bukhaar chdh़taa-utrtaa rhtaa hai

Reasons: 
- aaspaan maujood paanii ko smy pr naa bdlnaa
- rhne ke sthaan ke aaspaas gmdgii honaa
- paanii kaa jmaav honaa
- mchchhrom ke mdom kaa jmaa honaa 

Treatments:
mleriyaa kaa praathmik upchaar (Treatment of Malaria in Hindi)
- mleriyaa mem klorokvin jaisii emtii-mleriyl dvaa (Chloroquine- Anti malarial medicine) dii jaatii hai। in dvaaom ke saaid - iphekts ho skte haim, islie inhem dॉktr kii slaah ke binaa n lem।
- mriij ko pooraa aaraam krne dem। use hr chhh ghmte mem pairaasitaamol (Paracetamol in Malaria) dem aur baar- baar paanii aur trl chiijem ( niiboo paanii , chhaachh , naariyl paanii aadi ) pilaaem।
- mleriyaa bukhaar ke dauraan bchchom kaa khaas khyaal rkhem।
- bchche naajuk hote haim aur unkaa imyoon sistm kmjor hotaa hai islie biimaarii unhem jldii pkड़ letii hai। aise mem unkii biimaarii ko njrmdaaj n krem।
- bchche khule mem jyaadaa rhte haim islie inphekshn hone aur mchchhrom se kaate jaane kaa khtraa unmem jyaadaa hotaa hai।
- bchchom ghr se baahr poore kpd़e phnaakr bhejem। 
- mchchhrom ke mausm mem bchchom ko nikr v tii - shrt n phnaaem। 
- raat mem mchchhr bhgaane kii kriim lgaaem।
- agr bchchaa bhut jyaadaa ro rhaa ho , lgaataar soe jaa rhaa ho , bechain ho , use tej bukhaar ho , shriir pr chktte (Rashes) hom, ultii ho yaa inmem se koii bhii lkshण ho to phaurn dॉktr ko dikhaaem।
- aamtaur pr chhote bchchom ko bukhaar hone pr unke haath - pmv to thmde rhte haim lekin maathaa aur pet grm rhte haim islie unke pet ko chhookr aur rektl temprechr lekr unkaa bukhaar chek kiyaa jaataa hai। bgl se taapmaan lenaa shii triikaa nhiim hai , khaaskr bchchom mem। agr bgl se taapmaan lenaa hii hai to jo riidimg aae, usmem 1 digrii jod़ dem। use hii shii riidimg maanaa jaaegaa।

Home Remedies:
mleriyaa bukhaar ke dauraan tej sir drd (Headache), jor kii thmd ke saath kmp kmpii (Shivring) honaa, mmspeshiyom me bhymkr drd honaa (Muscle pain) aur behd kmjorii jaise lkshण mhsoos hote haim। bukhaar utrte smy psiinaa hotaa hai। shriir kaa taapmaan 104 digrii se bhii jyaadaa ho sktaa hai। jii ghbraanaa aur pitt kii kड़vii ultii honaa aur prtidin nishchit smy pr bukhaar chढ़naa bhii mleriyaa kaa prmukh lkshण hai।
 
jaanie mleriyaa se raaht ke ghreloo upaay (Home Remedies for Malaria)
1. choonaa (Chuna)- tiin graam choonaa lem, ise 60 milii paanii mem gholem। ek niimboo ismem nichoड़em। mleriyaa bukhaar kii smbhaavnaa hone pr yh mishrण piiem। yh nuskhaa prtidin lene se bukhaar se raaht miltii hai।
2. chiraaytaa- (Chirata)- chiraaytaa mleriyaa bukhaar kii sbse asrdaayk aushdhi maanii gii hai। ek paav grm paanii mem 15 graam chiraaytaa milaaem, kuchh laumg aur daalchiinii bhii milaa dem। is paanii ke istemaal se bhii mleriyaa bukhaar utrne lgtaa hai।
3. niimboo (Lemon)- grm paanii mem niimboo kaa rs milaakr piine se bukhaar kii tiivrtaa ghtne lgtii hai।
4. phitkrii (Alum)- thodii sii ph़itkrii tve pr bhoonkr choorण bnaa lem। aadhaa chmmch paaudr bukhaar aane ke 3 ghmte phle paanii se piiem। baad mem hr doosre ghmte pr yh dvaa lete rhne se bukhaar khtm hotaa hai।
5. tulsii pttaa (Basil leaves)- jb bukhaar n ho, 10 graam tulsii ke pttom ke rs mem aadhaa chmmch kaalii mirch kaa paaudr milaakr chaat lem। isse mleriyaa bukhaar khtm ho jaataa hai।
6. shhd (Honey)- ek gilaas paanii lem। ismem ek chmmch daalchiinii, ek chmmch shhd aur aadhaa chmmch kaalii mirch kaa paaudr milaakr grm krem। thmdaa hone pr piiem, yh atymt laabhkaarii nuskhaa hai।
7. dhtooraa (Dhatoora)- dhtooraa kii nii kopl 2 ng lekr guड़ ke saath achchhii trh milaakr iskii golii bnaa lem। inhem din mem 2 baar lene se mleriyaa khtm ho jaataa hai।
8. ann n khaaem (Avoid solid food)- mleriyaa hone pr ann n khaaem। kevl phl aur paanii lete rhem। aisaa krne se bukhaar se jldii laabh miltaa hai।
9. adrk (Ginger)- ek gilaas paanii mem 10 graam adrk aur 10 graam munkkaa daalkr itnaa ubaalem ki aadhaa rh jaay। thmdaa hone pr piiem।
10. amrood (Guava)- ek bड़aa amrud grm raakh mem bhoon lem। yh amrood khaanaa bhii, mleriyaa rogii ke lie laabhkaarii hai।
11. thmdii pttii rkhem (Cold compress)- tej bukhaar kii haalt mem maathe pr thmde paanii kii pttii rkhne se taapmaan niiche aa jaataa hai। thmde paanii mem giilaa kiyaa taavel saare shriir pr lpetne se turmt laabh miltaa hai।
12. pyaaj kaa rs (Onion juice)- pyaaj kaa rs mleriyaa mem laabhkaarii hai। 5 milii rs mem 4 kaalii mirch kaa paaudr milaakr din mem 3 baar piine se laabh hotaa hai।
13. jaamun (Black berry)- jaamun ke peड़ kii chhaal sukhaakr piis lem। 5 graam choorण, guड़ ke saath din mem 3 baar lene se mleriyaa se raaht miltii hai।


Disease: chhiimknaa (Sneezing)

Description: 
chhiimk ko ek saamaany kriyaa maanaa jaataa hai। chhiimk praayh tb aatii hai jb hmaarii naak ke mdr kii jhillii kisii baahrii pdaarth ke ghus jaane se preshaanii mhsoos krtii hai। hmaarii naak mem myooks jhillii hotii hai jiske uttk (Tissues) aur koshikaayem (Cells) bhut smvednshiil hote haim।

Reasons: 
- saamaanyt: thmd mem jukaam honaa hii chhiimk kii vjh hotii hai। 
- dhoop mem jyaadaa rhnaa bhii chhiimk kaa kaarण bn sktaa hai, jii hm tej dhoop se chhiimk kii nsem skriy ho jaatii haim jisse binaa mausm ke dhoop mem chlte vkt bhii chhiimk aa jaatii hai।
- seks bhii chhiimkne kaa kaarण ho sktaa hai। seks ke dauraan pairaasimpethetik nrvs sistm skriy ho jaataa hai jisse seks ke baad kii baar kuchh logom ko bhut chhiimk aatii hai।
- thredimg krvaate smy yaa uske baad chhiimk aatii hai। drasl, bhauhom ke thiik niiche jo ns hotii hai vh shvaas nlii se juड़ii hotii hai। isse juड़ii kisii bhii gtividhi kii prtikriyaa ke roop mem chhiimk aatii hai।
- kii baar tej roshnii dekhne se mkh ke retinaa aur dimaag ko jod़ne vaalii ऑptik ven (Optic Vein) uttejit ho jaatii hai। is vjh se bhii hmem chhiimk aa jaatii hai।

Treatments:
adhik chhiimk se bchne ke upaay (Remedies for Sneezing in Hindi)

Home Remedies:
chhiimknaa (Sneezing), bhle hii aapko preshaan krtaa ho lekin, yh vaastv mem aapko kii trh kii elrjii se bchaane kii svbhaavik prkriyaa hai। chhiimkne se shriir ke mdr maujood kii haanikaark elrjii vaale pdaarth baahr nikl jaate haim jisse chhiimkne kii prkriyaa ek surkshaa tmtr kii trh kaam krtii hai।
chhiimk aane ke kii kaarण ho skte haim jaise- dhum, dhool-mittii, sbjii kaa tej chhaumk yaa kisii chiij kii tej gmdh। iske alaavaa thmd ke mausm mem,  nmii yaa taapmaan mem giraavt, kisii khaane se elrjii yaa kisii dvaa se riekshn।
vjh chaahem jo bhii ho, ek do yaa tiin chhiimk aanaa to saamaany hai lekin ydi aapko ek saath kii chhiimkem aatii haim, itnii ki aap preshaan ho jaate haim aur yh roj kii hii baat hai, to phir is baare mem aapko saavdhaanii kii kh़aas jroort hai।
chhiimkne kii smsyaa se nijaat ke lie hm aapko kuchh ghreloo upaay btaane jaa rhe haim jisse aapko chhiimkne se raaht milegii।
chhiimkne kii smsyaa se raaht ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Sneezing)
peprmimt tel (Peppermint Oil)
ydi jukaam yaa naak mem kisii preshaanii ke vjh se aapko chhiimk aa rhii haim to iske nidaan ke lie peprmimt tel bढ़iyaa upaay hai। peprmimt tel mem jiivaaणurodhii (Anti-becterial) guण hote haim। upchaar ke lie kisii bड़e brtn mem paanii ko ubaalkr usmem peprmimt tel kii 5 boomdem daalem। ek tauliye se sir ko dhk kr is paanii kii bhaap lem। is vidhi se aapko chhiimk aane se raaht milegii।
saumph kii chaay (Fennel Tea)
saumph chhiimkne se raaht ke saath hii kii sms smbmdhii smkrmण se lड़ne kii kshmtaa rkhtii hai। saumph mem bhii kii emtiibaayotik (Anti-biotic) aur emtii vaayrl (Anti-viral) guण hote haim। upchaar ke lie ek kp paanii ubaalkr usmem do chmmch saumph ko kuchlkr daalem। tkriibn ds mint paanii ko kvr krke rkh dem aur uske baad chhaankr piiem। is trh kii chaay ko din mem do baar piiem।
kaalii mirch (Black Pepper)
gungune paanii mem aadhaa chmmch kaalii mirch daalkr yh mishrण din mem do se tiin baar piiem। kaalii mirch kaa paaudr daalkr graare bhii kie jaa skte haim। iske alaavaa soop aadi mem bhii kaalii mirch daalkr piinaa, laabhdaayk hotaa hai।
adrk (Ginger)
adrk chhiimkne kii smsyaa ke saath hii vibhinn trh ke vaayrl aur naak kii any smsyaaom ke lie behd puraanaa aur asrdaayk upaay hai। ek kp paanii mem thodaa़ saa adrk daalkr ubaalem। ise gungunaa rhne pr shhd milkaar piiem। iske alaavaa kchchaa adrk yaa adrk kii chaay bhii pii jaa sktii hai।
kaimomaail chaay (Chamomile Tea)
ydi elrjii ke kaarण chhiimkem aatii haim to kaimomaail chaay kaa ek pyaalaa aapko bड़ii raaht de sktaa hai। kaimomaail elrjii ko turmt khtm krke aapko raaht detaa hai। ek kp ublte paanii mem kaimomaail ke sookhe phool kuchh mint ubaalem। ise gungunaa rhne pr ismem shhd milaaem aur piiem। is chaay ko din mem do baar piyaa jaa sktaa hai।
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun mem emtiibaayotik aur emtiivaayrl guण hote haim,  jo ki shvsn smbmdhii smkrmण (Respiratory Infection) ko thiik krte haim। ydi srdii ke aam smkrmण kii vjh se chhiimke aa rhii  haim to lhsun aapko bhut aaraam de sktaa hai। upchaar ke lie pmch se chhh lhsun kii kliyom ko piiskr pest bnaaem aur ise soomghem। daal sbjii bnaane mem bhii lhsun kaa pryog krem saath hii soop bnaane mem bhii lhsun kii uchch maatraa daalem।
ajvaayn (Carom Seed Oil)
ajvaayn kii pttii ke tel mem jiivaaणom se lड़ne kii tej kshmtaa hotii hai jo ki elrjii ko thiik krne mem mdd krtii hai। upchaar ke lie ajvaayn ke tel kii do se tiin boomd rojaanaa istemaal krne se saains kii smsyaa se bhii nijaat smbhv hai।
methii ke biij (Fenugreek Seed)
ek kp paanii mem methii ke do se tiin chhote chmmch biij ubaal lem। jb paanii ublkr aadhaa ho jaae tb is paanii ko ghoomt-ghoomt krke piiem। is paanii ko ek din mem do se tiin baar piyaa jaa sktaa hai।


Disease: haaipothaairaaid (Hypothyroid)

Description: 
haaipothaairaaid ek chyaapchy vikaar (Metabolic Disorder) hai। thaairaaid grmthi ke kaary ke sbhii phluo, jaise aayodiin ko thaairaaid haarmon mem bdlne ke lie grmthi mem aayodiin ke smgrh kaary ko uttejit krne tthaa haarmon ke nirmaaण aur rkt prismchrण mem uske prvaah ko tiiesech (TSH) haarmon prbhaavit krtaa hai। moolth yh biimaarii khaan paan aur jiivn shailii se smbmdhit hai।

Symptoms: 
- iskii adhiktaa hone pr avtu atikriytaa ho jaatii hai jismem netrotsedhii glgणd ho jaataa hai।
- kmjorii mhsoos honaa (Weakness in Body)
- thणd kaa shn nhii honaa (Intolerance Cold)
- tvchaa kaa shushk honaa (Dry Skin)
- peshiyom aur joड़o mem drd honaa, (Pain in the Joints and Muscles)
- baalom kaa jhड़naa (Baldness)
- rktaalptaa (Anemia) honaa
- striyom mem maasik rktstraav (Extra Discharge During Menses) kaa adhik honaa
- buddhi kii kmii ho jaatii hai
- sunaaii km detaa hai
- vjn kaa bढ़naa

Reasons: 
haaipothaairaaid kii mukhy vjh hmaarii jiivnshailii maanii jaatii hai। aasiin jiivn shailii aur jmk phood ke adhik istemaal ko adhikmsh dॉktr iskii vjh maante haim। 

Treatments:
​haaipo thaayrॉyd se bchne ke lie sbse jroorii hai svsthy aur kriyaashiil jiivnshailii apnaanaa। iske saath hii nimn baatom kaa bhii dhyaan rkhnaa jroorii hai:
- vyaayaam (Exercise): prtidin ek ghmtaa hlkaa yaa tej kisii bhii prkaar kaa vyaayaam jroor krem।
- haaipothyrॉid ke koii bhii lkshण dikhaaii dene pr turmt bld test krvaanaa chaahie aur dॉktr se vimrsh krke haaipothyrॉid kii dvaaii shuroo krnii chhiye।

Home Remedies:
jb thaayrॉid glaimd jroort ke mutaabik thaayrॉid haarmon straavit nhiim krtii to yh rog haaypothaayrॉid khlaataa hai। ise medikl ke kshetr mem haaypothaayrॉidijm bhii khaa jaataa hai।
haaypothaayrॉidijm mem rogii ko thkaan,  srdii,  kbj,  shushk tvchaa, mmspeshiyom mem aimthn,  achaank se vjn bढ़naa,  avsaad,  rookhe aur jhड़te baal aur naakhun, aadi smsyaaem pnpne lgtii haim।
kuchh ghreloo upchaar kii mdd se haaypothaayrॉidijm se nijaat paayii jaa sktii hai, aaie aapko bhii btaate haim aise hii kuchh ghreloo upchaarom ke baare mem।
haaypothaayrॉid se bchaav ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Hyopothyroid)
naariyl tel (Coconut Oil)
naariyl tel mem jroorii phaitii esid hote haim, jo thaayrॉid ko niymtrit krte haim। upchaar ke lie rojaanaa bnaae jaane vaale khaane mem naariyl ke tel kaa istol krem। smbhv ho to rojaanaa ek gilaas doodh mem naariyl tel ko milaakr piem।
seb kaa sirkaa (Apple Cider Vinegar)
seb kaa sirkaa bhii thaayrॉid kii smsyaa se nijaat dilaa sktaa hai। iske ditॉksiiphikeshn  (Detoxification) ke guण alkaalaain (Alkaline) ke smtuln ko bnaakr vjn ko ghtaate haim aur haarmons ko str thiik krte haim। itnaa hii nhii, seb kaa sirkaa kolestrॉl ko bhii niymtrit krtaa hai। ek gilaas gungune paanii mem do chmmch seb kaa sirkaa milaakr piiem। is pey mem aavshyktaa anusaar shhd milaa skte haim।
vitaamin dii (Vitamin D)
vitaamin dii thaayrॉid kii smsyaa se niptne ke lie bhut jroorii hai। iske lie roj km se km 15 mint dhoop mem jroor baithem। isse shriir mem kailshiym kii maatraa bhii bढ़tii hai।
adrk (Ginger)
adrk, jimk, poteshiym, aur maigniishiym kaa achchhaa strot hai। iske lie adrk kii hrbl chaay ko dinchryaa mem shaamil krem। chaay bnaane ke lie ublte paanii mem kuchh tukड़e adrk ke daalem। achchhii trh se ubl jaae to kuchh der thmdaa krem। gungunaa rh jaae tb ismem shhd milaaem aur adrk kii is chaay ko piiem। is chaay ko din mem do se tiin baar piyaa jaa sktaa hai।
mchhlii kaa tel (Fish Oil)
mchhlii kaa tel thaayrॉid haarmon ke str ko bढ़aataa hai। saath hii, yh svsth thaayrॉid phmkshn ko bhii bnaae rkhtaa hai। mchhlii ke tel mem omegaa-3 phaitii esid kaaphii adhik hotaa hai jo ki shriir kii rog prtirodhk kshmtaa ko bhii bढ़aataa haim। dॉktr kii slaah se mchhlii ke tel ke spliimemt lie jaa skte haim।
aayodiin kii maatraa bdhaaem (Increase Iodine)
aayodiin kii ऑrgenik intek bhii haaypothaayrॉidijm mem raaht kaa kaam krtii hai। aayodiin ke ऑrgenik srotom mem pyaaj, ot, tmaatr, lhsun, bmdgobhii, anaanaas aur strॉberii, aadi shaamil haim। in khaady pdaarthom ko roj ke bhojn mem shaamil krem।
kaale akhrot (Black Wallnut)
kaale akhrot minrl, jaise ki aayodiin aur maigniij ke uchch srot hote haim। yh minrl thaairॉid glaimd ko smuchit roop se kaam krne ke lie prerit krte haim। kaale akhrot ko bhii roj khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
tnaav se door rhem (Avoid Stress)
ydi aap thaayrॉid smbmdhii kisii bhii preshaanii se grsit haim to tnaav bilkul n lem। aisaa koii bhii kaary n krem, jo aapko iriitet krtaa ho aur aapke tnaav ko bढ़aataa ho kyomki tnaav se aapkii sthiti aur bhii bigड़ sktii hai।
haaii kailorii phood se bchem  (Avoid High Calorie Food)
biskut, mithaaiiym, kek aur isii prkaar ke any khaane kii chiijem jo haaii kailoriiyukt hotii haim, unhem ekdm avॉid krem। iske saath hii khaane se sphed chaavl, maidaa, tlaa huaa khaanaa aadi se bhii phrej krem। itnaa hii nhiim chaay aur kॉphii kii maatraa bhii ghtaaem, jisse haaypothaayrॉidijm mem aaraam ho।


Disease: ऑstiyoporosis (Osteoporosis)

Description: 
ऑstiyoporosis (Osteoporosis) ek aisii shmt prkृti kii biimaarii hai jiske lkshण saamaanyt: jldii se dikhaaii nhiim dete haim। shriir mem kailshiym (Calcium) kii kmii honaa ऑstiyoporosis kaa prmukh kaarण hai।

Symptoms: 
- agr bhut jldii thk jaate hom
- khaaskr subh ke vkt kmr mem phailaa huaa drd ho
- shriir mem baar-baar drd hotaa ho
- smsyaa bdh़ne pr chhotii-sii chot phraikchr kii vjh ho sktii hai

Reasons: 
- vmshaanugt - agr paarivaarik itihaas ho to is biimaarii ke hone kii smbhaavnaaem bढ़ jaatii haim।
- daait- aisii daait lenaa jismem jismem protiin aur kailshiym kii kmii ho vh bhii ऑstiyoporosis (Osteoporosis) ko bढ़aavaa detii hai।
- daaybiitiij, thaairaaid jaisii biimaariyom kii dvaaii kailshiym kaa adhik avshoshण (Absorption) krtii hai, yh chiij bhii kii baar biimaarii ko bulaavaa detii hai। 
- chhote bchchom kaa bhut jyaadaa sॉpht dimks piinaa bhii ek kaarण hai। 
- aaraampsmd- jinkii dinchryaa jyaadaa kriyaashiil naa ho, unko bhii is biimaarii se khtraa hotaa hai। 
- sigret/ shraab sevn- nshaayukt vyktiyom mem kailshiym grhण krne kii kshmtaa km hotii hai। aise logom ko bhii yh rog ho sktaa hai। 
- vjn- jo atydhik duble hote haim unhem bhii is biimaarii se bchkr rhnaa chaahie। 
- bdh़tii umr - 50 vrsh se adhik ke purush v mhilaa ko iskaa jokhim adhik hotaa hai। 
- dvaaiyom kaa sevn- aisii biimaariym~ jhm~ mriij ko steraaid v haarmon kii dvaaiym~ lenii pd़e, un dvaaiyom ke kaarण bhii kii baar yh biimaarii saamne aa jaatii hai। 

Treatments:
ऑstiyoporosis se bchaav kaa sbse bdhiyaa triikaa shii daait lenaa hotaa hai। iske lie nimn bimdooom pr dhyaan denaa aavshyk hai।
- bhojn mem kailshiym ke alaavaa vitaamin, protiinyukt chiijom khaanii chaahie।
- doodh, dhii, pniir v mde kaa sevn krnaa chaahie।
- niymit vyaayaam krnaa chaahie।
- subh kii dhoop kaa sevn laabhdaayk hotaa hai।
- shraab aur kisii any nshe se door rhnaa chaahie। 

Home Remedies:
ऑstiyoporosis (Osteoporosis) hddiyom mem hone vaalii smsyaa hai, jismem hddiyom kaa biiemdii (Bone Mineral Density) levl km ho jaataa hai, jisse hddiyom ke tootne kaa khtraa bढ़ jaataa hai। ऑstiyoporosis mem hddiym ptlii yaa khokhlii hokr kmjor ho jaatii haim।
hmaarii hddiym kii trh ke minrl se milkr bnii hotii haim, jo ki umr ke saath km hone lgte haim। kii baar to hddiym itnii kmjor ho jaatii haim ki maamoolii sii chot se bhii toot jaatii haim।
ऑstiyoporosis protiin, vitaamin dii aur kailshiym kii kmii kii vjh se hotaa hai aur mhilaaem iskii jyaadaa rogii miltii haim।
aaie aapko btaate haim ki kis trh ghreloo upaayom ko apnaakr aap ऑstiyoporosis se bch sktii haim।
ऑstiyoporosis ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Osteoporosis)
proons (Prunes)
proons yaani sookhe plm, khaane se hddiyom kii kmjorii door hotii hai। proons mem maujood poliiphinols (Polyphenols) hddiyom  ko hue nuksaan kii bhrpaaii krtaa hai। itnaa hii nhiim proons mem boraan (Boron) aur tmbaa (Copper) jaise khnij hote haim jo ki hddiyom ke lie jroorii khnijom mem shaamil haim।
seb (Apple)
seb mem poliiphinols (Polyphenols) aur phlevnoids (Flavonoids) ke saath hii emtii ऑksiidemt bhii hotaa hai jo ki hddiyom kii soojn ko km krke unke ghntv ko bढ़aataa hai। islie roj ek seb khaane kii aadt bnaaem।
naariyl kaa tel (Coconut Oil)
eksprt kii maanem to apne aahaar naariyl tel ko shaamil krne se hddiyom  kaa ghntv bढ़taa hai। saath hii estrojn kii kmii bhii poorii hotii hai। naariyl ke tel mem maujood emtiiऑksiidemt yaugik hddiyom ke dhmche ko surkshit rkhte haim।
baadaam kaa doodh (Almond Milk)
baadaam ke doodh mem kailshyim kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। islie baadaam kaa doodh ऑstiyoporosis ke behd achchhaa upchaar hai। baadaam ke doodh mem hddiyom ke lie jroorii ttv maigniishiym,  maigniij aur pauteshiym bhii shaamil hote haim। aise mem roj ek gilaas baadaam vaalaa doodh niymit roop se piiem।
til ke biij (Sesame Seeds)
apne bhojn mem til ke biij shaamil krne se hddiyom kii kmjorii door hotii hai। til mem bhii kailshiym kii uchch maatraa hotii hai, jo ki hddiyom ke svaasthy ke lie sbse jroorii poshk ttv hai। iske saath hii til mem maigniishiym,  phॉsphors,  maimgniij,  tmbaa (Copper),  jstaa (Zinc) aur vitaamin dii bhii hotaa hai। upchaar ke lie ek mutthii bhune hue til chbaa kr doodh piiem। iske alaavaa khaane bnaane mem bhii bhune hue tilom ko oopr se daalkr khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
anaanaas (Pine Apple)
anaanaas mem ऑstiyoporosis ko rokne ke lie jroorii maimgniij shaamil hai। maimgniij kii kmii se hddiyom kaa ghntv km aur hddiym ptlii ho sktii haim, aise mem anaanaas khaane se maimgniij kii kmii poorii hotii hai। upchaar ke lie hr roj khaanaa khaane se phle ek kp anaanaas ko khaaem। iske saath hii anaanaas kaa joos bhii piyaa jaa sktaa hai।
dhniyaa ke biij (Coriander Seed)
dhniyaa ke ptte aur biij donom mem hii maigniishiym,  aayrn,  kailshiym,  poteshiym aur maimgniij aadi poshk ttv hote haim। dhniyaa ke biijom ko grm paanii mem ubaalkr kuchh der dhk kr rkhem uske baad gungunaa rhne pr usme shhd milaakr piiem। khaane ke chhaumk mem bhii dhniyaa ke biijom kaa istemaal kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। hre dhniyaa kaa istemaal bhii khaanaa bnaane aur chtnii ke roop mem krnaa chaahie।


Disease: brest kaimsr (Breast Cancer)

Description: 
maanv shriir ke avyv aur ootk koshikaaom (sel) se bne hote haim। kaimsr in koshikaaom kaa ek rog hai। brest kaimsr duniyaa mem tejii se phailne vaalii khtrnaak biimaariyom mem se ek hai। brest kaimsr (Breast Cancer) yaa stn kaimsr kii adhiktr rogii mhilaaem hotii haim। purushom ko bhii stn kaimsr ho sktaa hai, lekin iskii smbhaavnaa bhut km hotii hai।

Symptoms: 
- stnom ke baare mem jaan lene kaa srl triikaa hai T L C yaani  T - TOUCH Your Breasts (apne stnom ko chhuem)  kyaa aapko kuchh asaamaany lgtaa hai? kyaa aap stn mem, chhaatii ke ooprii hisse mem, yaa bglo mem koii gm~th (Lump) mhsoos krtii haim? kyaa aapko stnom ke oopr koii prt mhsoos hotii hai jo httii nhiim? kyaa stnom mem saadhaarण saa drd hai।  L - LOOK for changes (kuchh bdlaav to nhii lgtaa)  kyaa stnom ke aakr yaa bnaavt ( shape or texture) mem koii bdlaav hai? kyaa stnom ke aakr yaa aakृti (size or shape) mem koii bdlaav hai (koii ek stn doosre ke mukaable chhotaa yaa bड़aa haim)? stnom kii tvchaa kii bnaavt mem koii bdlaav jaise फ़tii फ़tii sii yaa koii gddaa saa pड़ jaanaa? rmg mem bdlaav jaise kii nippls ke aaspaas surkh laal rmg.ho jaanaa? kyaa nippl kii dishaa shii hai, khiim vh mdr kii trph to nhii muड़ gyaa hai? kisii bhii nippl se trl pdaardh kaa risnaa? nippl ke aas paas kisii prdaarth kaa risnaa yaa ppड़ii kaa jmnaa?  C - CHECK any unusual findings with your doctor (kuchh asaamaany saa mhsoos ho to turmt hii dॉktr se slaah lem) kyaa aapko kuchh asaamaany yaa alg saa mhsoos ho rhaa hai? agr aisaa hai to turmt hii dॉktr se slaah lem। smy smy pr apne stnom kii jmch svym krte rhem aisaa krne se aap unme saamaany taur pr aane vaale bdlaavom aur asaamaany bdlaav ke baare mem jaan jaayemge, aksr maasik dhrm (Menses) ke smy stnom mem kuchh bdlaav avshy aataa hai। lkshणom ke ubhrne kaa imtज़aar n krem, niymit roop se stnom kii jmch krvaaem। yh srvvidit hai ki rokthaam ilaaज़ se behtr hai

Reasons: 
brest kaimsr ke kaarण (Reason for Breast Cancer)
kii log maante haim ki brest kaimsr anuvmshik hotaa hai jo poorii trh shii tthy nhiim hai। stn yaa brest kaimsr ke kuchh ahm kaarण nimn haim: 
- aayu-stn kaimsr hone kaa jokhim aayu ke saath bdh़taa hai।
- ydi aapko phle kaimsr yaa stn kaa koii any rog huaa ho।
- paarivaarik itihaas - kevl 5–10% stn kaimsr hii anuvmshik roop se praapt jiin ke kaarण hote haim।
stn kaimsr kaa khtraa kin mhilaaom ko jyaadaa hotaa hai?
- adhik umr kii mhilaaem।
- jin mhilaaom kii mm, bhn yaa betii ko stn kaimsr huaa ho
- jnm ke smy se hii kromoज़om (guणsootro) mem bdlaav ho।
- mhilaa jise bchche naa hue hom, yaa 30 saal kii umr ke baad bchche hue hom।
- jise 12 saal kii umr se phle hii piiriyds shuru ho ge hom।
- jis mhilaa ko 50 saal kii umr ke baad menopॉj (rjonivृtti) huii ho।
- jis mhilaa kii stn ke ootk kaaphii ghne hom। aapkii memograaphii krke dॉktr ye jaankaarii de skte hai।
- jo mhilaa grbh nirodhk goliyom kaa lmbe arse se istemaal kr rhii ho।
- jo mhilaa din mem 2 se 5 baar shraab kaa sevn krtii ho।
- jis mhilaa ko menopॉj ke baad jyaadaa motaapaa aa gyaa ho।
- jis mhilaa ne haarmon riplesmemt therepii istemaal kii ho।
- jo mhilaaem apne bchchom ko stnpaan nhiim krvaatiim।
haarmon smbmdhii kaark
estrojn aur projestrojn naamk haarmon se lmbe smy tk smprk mem aane se aapkaa stn kaimsr kaa jokhim bढ़ sktaa hai।
jiivnshailii smbmdhii kaark
lmbe smy tk prtidin do peg se jyaadaa shraab piinaa tthaa dhoomrpaan se aapkaa stn kaimsr kaa jokhim bढ़ sktaa hai| vjn jyaadaa honaa bhii stn kaimsr kaa kaarण bn sktaa hai।

Treatments:
- agr aapko thoड़aa saa bhii smshy ho to turmt dॉktr kii slaah liijiye।
- chhote stn

Home Remedies:
stn kaimsr (Breast cancer), sbse aam kaimsr mem se ek hai। stn kaimsr ek kmpleks biimaarii (Complex disease) hai jiske hone ke lie kii phaiktr, jaise aanuvmshik (Heredity), khaan-paan aur jiivn shailii jimmedaar hote haim। chikitsaa visheshjञom kii maanem to aane vaale smy mem stn kaimsr se piiड़it rogiyom kii smkhyaa aur bhii tejii se bढ़gii। haalmki jiivn shailii mem bdlaav krke stn kaimsr se kaaphii hd tk bchaa jaa sktaa hai।
 
jaanie stn kaimsr se bchaav ke ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies for Breast Cancer):
1. griin tii (Green tea)- ek gilaas paanii mem hrbl griin tii ko aadhaa hone tk ubaalem aur phir use piiem। yh phaaydemmd hotii hai aur isse stn kaimsr kaa khtraa kaaphii km ho jaataa hai।
2. mgoor aur anaar kaa joos (Grapes and pomegranate juice)- rojaanaa mgoor yaa anaar kaa joos piine se stn kaimsr se bchaa jaa sktaa hai। in donom phlom ke joos mem kaimsr ke sels ko maarne kii kshmtaa hotii hai, jisse stn kaimsr kaa khtraa km ho jaataa hai।
3. lhsun (Garlic)- lhsun mem phlevons (flavons) aur phlevonols (flavonols) jaise emtii baiktiiriyl ttv hote haim। roj lhsun kaa sevn krne se stn kaimsr kii smbhaavnaa ko rokaa jaa sktaa hai।
4. hldii (Turmeric)- hldii mem krkyoomin (curcumin) naam kaa ttv hotaa hai jo ki vibhinn trh ke kaimsr ko thiik krne mem skshm hai। hldii ke sevn se kaimsr sel bढ़ne kii smbhaavnaa km hotii hai tthaa kaimsr thiik hotaa hai।
5. tmaatr (Tomato)- tmaatr khaane se bhii mhilaaem stn kaimsr se bchii rh sktii haim। tmaatr mem laaykopiin (lycopene) hotaa hai jo ki ek shktishaalii emtiiऑksiidemt hai aur kaimsr ko bढ़ne se roktaa hai।
6. paalk (Spinach)- paalk mem emtiiऑksiidemt lyootin (lutin) hotaa hai jo kaimsr se bchaane mem shaayk hai। hphte mem do se tiin baar paalk khaanaa chaahie jisse stn kaimsr se bchaa jaa sktaa hai।
7. broklii (Broccoli)- broklii mem kaimsr se lड़ne vaale ttv, imdol-3-kaarbinol (indole-3-carbinol) hotaa hai jo ki stn kaimsr ke sels kii groth ko km kr dete haim। broklii ke niymit sevn se kaimsr se bchaa jaa sktaa hai। broklii ke saath pttaa gobhii aur gobhii ko milaakr khaanaa chaahie।
8. akhrot (Wallnut)- akhrot mem bhut se poshk ttv hote haim jo stn kaimsr kii groth ko km kr dete haim islie akhrot kaa rojaanaa sevn krnaa chaahie।
9. blooberii (Blueberries)- blooberii vitaamin aur minrl se bhrpoor hotii haim। inmem emtiiऑksiidemt elejik bhii hote haim jo stn kaimsr se bchaav krte haim। bloobairii ke saath strॉberii aur blaikberii bhii behd phaaydemmd hotii hai।


Disease: sirdrd (Headache)

Description: 
sirdrd ek aam smsyaa hai। sir ke kisii bhii hisse mem drd ho sktaa hai aur yh drd kevl lkshण hotaa hai jo ki sir kii kisii biimaarii ko drshaataa hai। kii baar bhut jyaadaa tnaav lene, thkaavt hone, bhookhe rhne, grmii tej hone yaa kisii aam shaariirik smsyaa jaise ki bukhaar yaa jukaam ke kaarण bhii sir drd ho sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- uchch rkt chaap honaa
- kbj yaa dst honaa
- jyaadaa shraab piinaa
- tnaavgrst honaa
- pet thiik n honaa

Reasons: 
sir drd ke kaarण- (Cause of Headache)
sir kaa drd, dimaag mem rkt koshikaaom (blood vessels) aur shiraaom (nerves) ke aaps mem tkraane se hotaa hai। drd ke smy rkt koshikaa kii ek nishchit siraa aur sir kii mmspeshiym skriy hotii haim aur dimaag ko drd kaa signl bhejtii haim। jisse sir drd mhsoos hotaa hai।
sir drd ke any kaarण (Other Reasons of headache)
1. jb vykti kisii chiij ko lekr khud pr dbaav mhsoos krtaa hai yaa kisii sthiti yaa pristhiti ko lekr asmmjs mem hotaa hai। aise mem uskaa mn ashmt ho jaataa hai aur dimaag pr jyaadaa ghraa prbhaav pड़taa hai jiske kaarण tnaav hotaa hai aur sir drd hone lgtaa hai।
2. dimaag kii rkt vaahiniyom mem bdlaav hone se hone vaale drd ko maaigren kaa drd khaa jaataa hai। is trh ke sir drd mem sir ke kisii ek hisse mem chubhn bhraa drd hotaa hai aur drd ke saath jii michlaane, gais aur ultii jaisii smsyaaem bhii hotii haim। itnaa hii nhiim vykti photophobiyaa (roshnii se preshaanii) aur phonophobiyaa (shor se preshaanii) se bhii preshaanii mhsoos krtaa hai। pryaapt niimd n lene, bhookhe rhne yaa km paanii piine se maaigren ho sktaa hai।
3. kuchh mhilaaem haarmon mem bdlaav ke dauraan gmbhiir sir drd mhsoos krtii haim। yh sthiti monopoj, maasik straav, ovelyooshn aadi ke dauraan bhii ho sktii hai। maasik straav mem utaaraa chढ़aav se bhii is trh kaa sir drd bnaa rh sktaa hai।
4. kuchh khaas trh kii dvaaiyom kaa jyaadaa din tk lene ke kaarण ribaaumd sirdrd kii smsyaa ho ho sktii hai। kii biimaariym aisii hotii haim jinmem dvaaiiym lmbe smy tk chltii haim, aise mem yh mstishk ko prbhaavit kr sktii haim। is trh kaa sir drd dvaaem bmd hone ke saath khud hii bmd ho jaataa hai।
5. dmt drd se bhii sir kii nsem prbhaavit hotii haim। dmt aur sir kii nsem jbड़e pr jaakr miltii haim jisse dmt aur sir ek doosrem ko knekt krte haim। jisse dmt mem kisii bhii trh kii tkliiph hone se sir mem drd hone lgtaa hai।
6. chaay aur kॉphii ke aadi logom ko ydi smy pr chaay n mile to bhii unhem sir drd kii shikaayt ho sktii hai।
7. kuchh logom ko subh uthte hii sirdrd kii shikaayt hotii hai jbki kuchh der baad yh apne aap thiik ho jaataa hai। kii baar raat mem achchhii niimd n lene yaa bhookhe pet sone ke kaarण subh subh sir drd ho sktaa hai।
8. mkhom mem kisii trh kii smsyaa hone, mkh kmjor hone, chshmaa n phnne yaa kmtekt laims mem gड़bड़ii hone se sir drd ho sktaa hai। aisii koii bhii smsyaa jisse mkhom pr tnaav pड़taa ho, sir drd hone kii vjh ho sktaa hai। aise mem ydi koii vykti sir drd se preshaan hai to use apnii mkhom ko bhii jroor chaik kraanaa chaahie।
9. kuchh logom ko aaiskriim yaa bhut thmdii chiijom ko khaane se bhii sir drd kii shikaayt ho sktii hai। aaiskriim yaa bhut thmdii chiijem khaane ke baad maathe ke biich mem bhaariipn mhsoos hotaa hai jisse sir drd shuroo ho jaataa hai। is trh kaa drd aaiskriim khaane ke turmt baar shuroo ho jaataa hai।

Treatments:
sir drd se raaht ke lie tips- (Tips to Prevent Headache)

Home Remedies:
aajkl kii tej bhaagtii jimdgii aur vyst jiivnshailii mem tnaav aur srdrd ek aam biimaarii ho gii hai। srdrd ke kii kaarण hote haim। sir mem rkt phumchaane vaalii naad़iyom mem smkuchn, snaayu tmtr kii asmaany gtividhi, jyaadaa dhoomrpaan krnaa, jyaadaa alkohl lenaa, shriir mem paanii kii kmii, jyaadaa der tk bevjh sonaa, drd nivaark dvaaom kaa jyaadaa sevn krnaa, srdii-jukaam, bukhaar smet aise kii vjh haim, jisse srdrd hotii hai।
yhm yh jaannaa jrurii hai ki saamaany srdrd aur maaigren ke srdrd mem mtr hai। maaigren mem srdrd kaaphii preshaanii vaalaa hotaa hai aur yh ek gmbhiir biimaarii bhii hai। srdrd yaa kisii bhii trh ke srdrd mem jldii elopaithik drd nivaark dvaa khaanaa seht ke lie nuksaandeh hotaa hai, kyomki jyaadaa pen kilr khaane se kidnii aur livr daimej hote haim।
elopaithik dvaaom se behtr hai ki hm aise kuchh ghreloo upchaar ko aajmaaem, jisse srdrd mem n sirph aaraam miltaa hai blki yh jd़ se khtm bhii hotaa hai, binaa koii saaid iphekt।
srdrd ke ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Headache)
srsom tel (Mustard Oil)
srdrd mem srsom tel kaaphii asrdaar hotaa hai। maathe ke jis hisse mem drd ho rhaa ho us trph vaale naak mem srsom ke tel kii kuchh boomdem daal diijie aur uske baad jor se smsom ko oopr kii trph khiimchie। isse srdrd se kaaphii raaht milegii। dhyaan rhe srdrd hone pr bistr pr letkr drd vaale hisse ko bed ke niiche ltkaa kr naak mem tel lenaa chaahie।
daalchiinii (Cinamon)
daalchiinii ko paanii ke saath mhiin piiskr maathe pr ptlaa lep lgaane se srdrd  mem kaaphii raaht miltii hai। lep sookh jaane pr use htaa liijie। tiin-chaar baar lep lgaane pr srdrd honaa bmd ho jaataa hai।
pushkr mool (Pushkar Mool)
pushkr mool ek kudrtii jd़ii bootii hai। ise chmdn kii trh ghiskr lep bnaa lem aur sir pr lgaaem। iske lep ko maathe pr lgaane se srdrd mem kaaphii raaht miltaa hai।
mulethii (Mulethi)
mulethii srdrd mem kaaphii kaam krtaa hai। mulethii ko piiskr choorण bnaa liijie। is choorण ko naak ke paas le jaakr soomghem। isse srdrd chhoo-mmtr ho jaaegii।
saumph-piipl-mulethii (Saunf, Peepal and Mulethi)
piipl ke ptte, somth, mulaithii aur saumph sbko piiskr choorण bnaa liijie। uske baad is choorण mem ek chmmuch paanii milaakr gaadhaa lep bnaa bnaa liijie। is lep ko maathe pr lgaaie। srdrd khtm ho jaaegaa।
msaaledaar chaay (Spicy Tea)
msaaledaar chaay srdrd ke lie ek raambaaण kii trh kaam krtaa hai। ise ghr mem bhii aasaanii se bnaayaa jaa sktaa hai। yh ek ut‍tejk pey pdaarth hai jo dimaag ko schet krtaa hai। chaay mem thod़ii adrkh, laumg aur ilaaichii milaa kr ubaal dem। ho gyaa grmaagrm msaaledaar chaay taiyaar। msaaledaar chaay ko grmaagrm hii piinaa chaahie। isse aapkaa srdrd to gaayb hogaa hii saath mem aap trotaaj़aa bhii mhsoos kremge।
tel maalish (Oil massage)
srdrd mem tel kii maalish bhut asrdaar hotii hai। maalish se sir kii rkt dhmniyom mem rkt prvaah shii se hone lgtaa hai aur srdrd turmt chhoo-mmtr ho jaatii hai। dhyaan rhe sir kii maalish hrbl tel se hii krem aur srdrd hone pr tel ko hlkaa grm kr lenaa chaahie taaki yh jldii asr kre।
niimboo paanii (Lemon Water)
kaaphii maatraa mem shraab piine se aksr logom ko haimgovr ho jaataa hai। haimgovr mem kaaphii tej srdrd hotaa hai। aisii sthiti mem niimboo paanii kaaphii kaam krtaa hai। shraab jyaadaa piine se shriir mem paanii kii kmii ho jaatii hai aur niimboo paanii piine se shriir mem paanii kii kmii bhii door hotii hai aur srdrd bhii thiik hotaa hai।


Disease: bromkaaitis (Bronchitis)

Description: 
jb shvaasnlii tthaa iskii shaakhaaom mem smkrmण yaa elrjii ke kaarण soojn aane ke kaarण shvaas smbmdhii smsyaa hotii hai to us sthiti ko bromkaaitis (Bronchitis) khte haim। yh srdiyom kii ek aam smsyaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- khmsii ke saath bhut gaadh़aa v hre rmg kaa blgm aanaa
- naak bhnaa yaa bmd honaa
- bdn drd honaa
- baar-baar chhaatii mem jln
- bukhaar yaa thmd lgnaa
- lgaataar kaaphii der honaa
- sms phoolnaa
- sms lete smy chhaatii mem ghrghraaht kii aavaaj honaa

Reasons: 
- siine mem sthit shvms nlii aur uskii shaakhaaom mem baar-baar hone vaalaa imphekshn।
- nyoomoniyaa bhii bromkaaitis kaa mukhy kaarण hotii hai।
- tii.bii. kaa imphekshn bhii iskaa ek prmukh kaarण hotaa hai। agr shuruaat mem hii tii.bii. imphekshn kaa smuchit ilaaj ho jaae to bromkaaitis se bchaa jaa sktaa hai।
- kuchh logom mem yh rog jnmjaat hotaa hai।
- iske alaavaa aimtiitripsin naamk emjaaim kii kmii, ryoometaaid ऑrthraaitis aur any aatoimyoon biimaariym bhii bromkaaitis kaa kaarण bntii haim।
- baiktiiriyaa yaa vishaaणu kaa smkrmण bhii bromkaaitis kaa kaarण ho sktaa haim।
- dhoomrpaan aur vaayu prdooshण ke kaarण bhii yh biimaarii ho sktii hai। 
- vaayu mem kisii chiij se elrjii jaise praag kण ityaadi bhii bromkaaitis kaa kaarण ho skte haim।

Treatments:
bromkaaitis se bchaav ke lie shriir ko thmdii se bchaanaa chaahie। saath hii nimn baatom kaa bhii khyaal rkhnaa chaahie:
- dhoomrpaan chhod़ dem। 
- vaayu prdooshण, v dhool se bchem। 
- srdii aur phloo se krem bchaav। 
- blgm ptlaa rkhne ke lie khoob paanii piem। 
- sote smy sir bistr se oomchaa rkhne ke lie tkie kaa pryog krem।
- ydi bukhaar bdh़ jaae aur thmd lgne lge to turmt kisii chikitsk se smprk krem। 

Home Remedies:
bromkaaitis naak aur phephd़e ke biich sms lene vaalii nlii mem soojn ke vjh se hotii hai। yh praay vaairl imphekshn se hotaa hai। gle mem khichkhich, kmto jaisii chubhn aur drd honaa iske lkshण haim। mausm mem bdlaav aur elrjii se bhii bromkaaitis kii shikaayt hotii hai। ismem kbhii-kbhii bukhaar kii bhii shikaayt hotii hai।
bromkaaitis mem khraash yaa drd hone se khaanaa khaane, paanii piine yaa thook niglne tk mem tkliiph hotii hai। isse nijaat paane ke lie dॉktr kii mdd lene se behtr hai ki kuchh ghreloo ilaaj kie jaane chaahie jo kaaphii asrdaar bhii hotaa hai।
bromkaaitis mem khraash ke ghreloo ilaaj(Home remedies for Bronchitis)
shhd (Honey)
shhd mem emtii vaayrl aur emtii baiktiiriyl guण hotaa hai। gle mem khraash hone pr shhd yaa shhd vaalii chaay piine se soojn km hotii hai aur gle ko kaaphii aaraam miltii hai। gle mem khraash mem yh kaaphii phaaydemmd hotaa hai।
adrk (Ginger)
srdii, kph aur gle kii khraash mem adrk gle ko kaaphii aaraam phumchaataa hai। adrk mem emtii imphlaametrii guण hotaa hai। adrk kaa rs, adrk kii chaay piine yaa adrk choosne se gle kii soojn, khraash mem kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai।
hrbl chaay (Herbal Tea)
kaalii mirch, tulsii v laumg se bnii chaay piine se gle mem khraash se nijaat miltii hai। in kudrtii jd़ii-bootiyom se bnii grm chaay kii chuskiyom se gle ko kaaphii raaht miltii hai। vaise hrbl chaay kii biimaariyom mem bhii kaam aataa hai।  
hldii (Turmeric)
thod़ii sii hldii daalkr doodh mem ubaal lem। doodh tb tk ubaalem jb tk hldii pk naa jaaem. phir ise kp mem lekr chaay kii chuskiym lete hue piem। isse gle ke drd mem  aur khraash mem kaaphii raaht milegii।
graaraa (Gargil)
gle mem khraash kii shikaayt hone pr grm paanii mem nmk daalkr graare krem। nmk milaa grm paanii aapke gle mem imphekshn kii vjh se aaii soojn ko km krtaa hai aur aaraam phumchaataa hai। behtr hogaa ki jldii raaht ke lie aap hr tiin ghmte mem graare krem।
trl pdaarth (Liquid)
aap thod़ii-thod़ii der mem kuchh grm trl pdaarth lete rhem। kuchh bhii nhiim to aap thod़ii-thod़ii der mem grm paanii piite rhem। isse aapke gle kii sikaaii hogii aur aapko aaraam milegaa।
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun mem emtii-baayotik aur emtii vaayrl guण hote haim। gle kii soojn aur khraash mem yh kaaphii asrdaar hotaa hai।  lhsun ke do-tiin tukd़e ko paanii ke saath chbaa kr subh khaaem yaa phir doodh mem ubaal kr bhii pii skte haim।
yookilipts tel (Eucalyptus Oil)
gle kii khraash mem bhaap lenaa kaaphii phaaydemmd hotaa hai। grm paanii mem agr yookilipts ke tel ko milaa kr bhaap lem to yh kaaphii asrdaar hotaa hai। gle kii soojn aur khraash ko km krtaa hai।


Disease: ibolaa vishaaणu rog (EVD) (Ebola)

Description: 
ibolaa vaayrs rog yaa ibolaa hemoraahaijik bukhaar ibolaa vishaaणu ke kaarण hotaa hai। ibolaa vishaaणu rog (EVD) yaa ibolaa hemoraahaijik bukhaar (EHF) mem shriir mem nsom se khoon baahr aanaa shuroo ho jaataa hai, jisse shriir ke mdr rktsraav shuroo ho jaataa hai aur isse 90% rogiyom kii mृtyu ho jaatii hai।

Symptoms: 
- aarmbhik lkshण mem jvr, phunsii, sr drd, michlii, ultii aur pet mem drd, poore shriir mem gthiyaa kaa drd, gle mem drd, dst sktaa hai
- is rog kaa imkyoobeshn piriiyd  (Incubation Period) ek hphte kaa hotaa hai। uske baad rogii mem aarmbhik lkshण njr aate haim
- jnnmg mem soojn hotii hai
- tvchaa mem drd kaa anubhv hotaa hai
- netrshleshmlaashoth (kmjemgvaaitis) hai
- poore shriir pr phumshiyom njr aane lgtii haim
- mum~h kaa taalu laal ho jaataa hai
- mum~h, kaan, naak se rktsraav hotaa hai
- rog ke viksit avsthaa mem yh lkshण bhii njr aate hai

Reasons: 
ibolaa se bchaav kaa sbse behtr aur ekmaatr upaay hai isse prbhaavit rogii ke smprk mem aane se bchnaa। kisii rogii ke smprk mem aane se yh rog aur tejii se phailtaa hai। 

Treatments:
​ibolaa kaa abhii tk koii thos ilaaj nhiim milaa hai। bchaav hii is biimaarii kaa sbse behtriin upaay maanaa jaataa hai। abhii tk ibolaa se piiditom ke kes mem nimn kdm uthaae jaate haim:
- is biimaarii ke lie koii vishisht upchaar nhiim hai; smkrmit logom kii shaaytaa kii koshishom mem unhem orl rihaaidreshn therepii (piine ke lie thod़aa-saa miithaa aur nmkiin paanii denaa) yaa imtraavens phluds denaa shaamil hai।
- aksr is vaayrs ke smkrmit hone vaale 50% se 90% tk log maut ke shikaar ho jaate haim।
- iske lie tiikaa viksit krne ke pryaas jaarii haim; haalmki abhii tk aisaa koii tiikaa maujood nhiim hai।


Disease: loo lgnaa (Heat Stroke)

Description: 
grmii mem sbse bड़ii smsyaa hotii hai loo lgnaa। mgrejii bhaashaa mem ise hiit strok (Heat Stroke) aur snstrok (Sun Stroke) bhii khte haim। grmii mem uchch taapmaan mem jyaadaa der tk rhne se yaa grm hvaa ke jhomkom se smprk mem aane pr loo (Loo) lgne kaa dr adhik hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- m~khem bhii jltii haim
- isse achaank behoshii v mtth rogii kii maut bhii ho sktii hai
- bukhaar kaaphii bdh़ jaataa hai
- bldpreshr bhii lo ho jaataa hai aur livr - kidnii mem sodiym potaishiym kaa smtuln bigd़ jaataa hai। aise mem behoshii bhii aa sktii hai। iske alaavaa  lo biipii , bren yaa haart strok kii sthiti bhii bn sktii hai
- loo lgne pr shriir mem grmii , khushkii , sirdrd , kmjorii , shriir tootnaa , baar - baar mumh sookh.naa , ultii , chkkr , tej bukhaar  sms lene mem tkliiph , dst aur kii baar nidhaal yaa behoshii jaise lkshण njr aate haim। loo lgne pr psiinaa nhiim aataa
- shriir kaa taapmaan ekdm bdh़ jaataa hai। aksr bukhaar bhut jyaadaa msln 105 yaa 106 digrii phॉrnhaait tk phumch jaataa hai
- haath aur pairom ke tluom mem jln-sii hotii rhtii hai

Reasons: 
loo lgnaa ke kaarण (Heat Stroke Causes)
loo lgne ke jokhim (Risk Factors of Heat Storkes)
loo lgne ke kaarण dimaag aur mtrik mgom ko kshti phumch sktii hai। vaise to loo kaa shikaar aksr pchaas se oopr kii umr ke log hote haim lekin kii svsth khilaad़ii bhii iskaa shikaar aasaanii se ho jaate haim। km umr ke logom mem semtrl nrvs sistm viksit ho rhaa hotaa hai to jyaadaa umr ke logom mem dooshit hotaa hai, jiske kaarण in donom ko hii loo kaa khtraa sbse jyaadaa rhtaa hai।
loo lgne ke dauraan vykti ko shriir mem paanii kii kmii yaani diihaaidraishn kii shikaayt bhii hone lgtii hai। hiit strok kaa turmt ilaaj naa kraane pr mstishk, hृdy, gurde aur mmspeshiyom ko nuksaan phumch sktaa hai। kii sthitiyom mem mriij़ kii mृtyu bhii ho sktii hai।
grmii mem vibhinn dvaaiyom kaa sevn krne vaale vyktiyom ko bhii loo lgne kaa dr hotaa hai। aisii dvaaem jo rkt dhmniyom (bld vesls) ko smkiirण krem, edrenaalaaiin ke raaste mem avruddh paidaa kr rktchaap ko niymtrit krem, shriir se sodiym aur paanii ko baahr nikaalem aur emtiidiprsemts hom, loo lgne ke khtre ko aur bdh़aatii haim।

Treatments:
loo lgne pr praathmik upchaar (First Aid for Heat Strokes in Hindi)
- aaht vykti ko phle chhmv mem laa kr hvaa kaa imtjaam krem। grmii ke kaarण shriir kaa taapmaan bढ़ jaataa hai। chhaayaa mem laane se shriir kaa taapmaan saamaany aanaa shuru ho jaataa hai।
- usko nmk shkkr aur paanii kaa ghol mum~h se pilaayem, uske kpड़e nikaalkr sirph mdroonii vstr rkhem। shriir pr hlkaa saa grm paanii chhiड़kem।
- giilii chaadr mem lpetkr taapmaan km krne kaa pryaas krem।
- haath pair kii maalish krem jisse rkt smchrण prbhaavit hotaa hai।
- smbhv ho to brph ke tukड़e kpड़e mem lpetkr grdn, bglom aur jmghom pr rkhe। isse grmii jldii nikltii hai।
- dhoop mem ghr se baahr niklem to chhtrii kaa istemaal krem। nmge bdn aur nmge pair dhoop mem naa khd़e hom।
- niimboo paanii, aam pnaa, chhaachh, lssii, naariyl paanii, bel yaa niimboo kaa shrbt, khs kaa shrbt jaise trl pdaarth piite rhem।
- dhiile aur sootii kpd़e phnem।
- khaalii pet baahr naa jaaem aur thod़ii thod़ii der pr paanii piite rhem।
- grmii se ekdm thmde kmre mem naa jaaem।
- din mem do baar nhaaem।
- hrii sbjiyom kaa sevn adhik krem।
- khiiraa, kkd़ii, laukii, taurii jroor khaaem।
- thmde vaataanukoolit kmre mem rhem।
- imlii ke goode ko haath pairom pr mlem।
- shriir kaa taapmaan tej hone pr sir pr thmdii pttii rkhem।
- ghr se baahr niklte smy jeb mem ktaa pyaaj rkhem।

Home Remedies:
agr turmt ilaaj n ho to hiit strok yaani loo lgnaa jaanlevaa bhii ho sktaa hai। jyaadaa grmii se shriir mem thkaavt mhsoos honaa aur loo lgnaa (hiit strok) donom mem mtr hai। hiit strok yaa loo lgnaa gmbhiir sthiti hai। tej dhoop yaa tej taapmaan mem kaaphii der tk snlaait ke smprk mem rhne se shriir kaa taapkrm 37 digrii selsiys (saamaany) se khiim adhik ho jaataa hai। agr shriir kaa taapkrm 40 digrii selsiys se jyaadaa ho jaae to yh jaanlevaa bhii ho sktaa hai, jismem shriir ke kii mhtvpoorण mg daimej ho jaate haim।
tej sirdrd, sms tejii se lenaa, dil kii dhd़kn tej honaa, tvchaa laal ho jaanaa, chkkr aanaa, ultii, kaaphii psiinaa aanaa jaise lkshण jb dikhne lge to smjh jaaie ki yh hiit strok yaa loo kaa ataik hai। hiit strok yaa loo lgne ke baad mriij ko turmt medikl keyr mem rkhnaa chaahie।
vaise loo se bchne ke kii ghreloo ilaaj haim, lekin loo lgne ke baad agr shriir kaa taapkrm 104 digrii phaarenhaait se jyaadaa hai aur shriir mem paanii kii kmii hai to binaa asptaal mem bhrtii kie iskaa koii ilaaj nhiim hai। grmii mem hiit strok yaa loo se bchne ke kii ghreloo ilaaj haim।
pyaaj kaa joos (Onion Juice)
hiit strok kaa sbse kaargr aur asrdaar ghreloo ilaaj hai pyaaj। aayurved mem yh sbse jyaadaa ajmaayaa huaa nuskh़aa hai। kchche pyaaj ke rs ko kaan ke niiche aur chhaatii pr lgaane se shriir kaa taapkrm km hotaa hai। kchche pyaaj ke joos mem jiiraa paaudr aur shhd kii boomd daalkr piinaa bhii kaaphii phaaydemmd hotaa hai loo mem। grmii ke mhiine mem loo se bchne ke lie ek totkaa yh bhii hai ki aap pyaaj ke ek tukd़e ko jeb mem lekr baahr niklem।
kchche aam kaa pnaa (Unripe mango juice)
kchche aam kaa joos raambaaण hai loo se bchaav mem। kchche aam ko ubaal kr yaa pkaa kr uskaa goodaa nikaal liyaa jaataa hai aur phir paanii ke saath gud़, saumph, pudiinaa aur jiiraa milaa kr piiem। kaaphii asrdaar hotaa hai yh। shriir kaa taapmaan bhii km krtaa hai aur kaaphii thmdk phumchaataa hai। kchche aam ke gude kaa lep bhii shriir pr lgaae jaate haim।
imlii aur gud़ kaa desii kold drimk (Tamarind Drink)
imlii mem ilektrolaaits aur minrls kii maatraa kaaphii hotii hai। grmii mem yh shriir mem ilektrolaaits kii kmii ko door krtaa hai। imlii ko mth kr paanii mem gud़ ke saath ghol kr piiem। loo mem yh kaaphii asrdaar hai। raajsthaan shit desh ke kii hissom mem gud़ aur imlii ko paanii mem milaa kr piyaa jaataa hai taaki grmii sir n chdh़e।
niimboo paanii (Lemon juice)
jhm oomche paare ke saath psiinaa bhii bhut aataa hai, vhm paanii piine ke alaavaa kuchh taajgii de sktaa hai to vh hai niimboo paanii। niimboo mem vitaamin sii aur ilektrolaaits paae jaate haim jo hmem hiit stroks se bchaate haim।
naariyl paanii (Coconut water)
grmiyom ke lie  heldii pey hai naariyl paanii।  kailorii bhii nhiim aur taajgii 100 phiisdii। yh shriir ke taapmaan ko bhii km krtaa hai।
dhii kii lssii (Lassi)
dophr mem agr dhoop mem baahr niklnaa ho to dhii kii lssii yaa chhaachh piikr niklem। aisaa krne se dhoop kaa asr km pd़egaa aur loo se bchaav bhii hogaa। chhaachh mem hlkaa saa nmk, chutkii bhr chiinii aur dhniyaa pudiinaa daal kr hlkaa saa thmdaa kr lem, bs bdh़iyaa kold drimk ho gyaa taiyaar।
chmdn kaa lep (Sandalwood Paste)
chmdn ke paaudr ko paanii mem gholkr pest bnaa kr sir aur poore bdn mem lgaaem, kaaphii shiitltaa milegii aur shriir kaa taapmaan bhii km hogaa।
dhniyaa pttaa aur piprmimt kaa joos (Juice of Coriander and Mint Leaves)
dhniyaa pttaa aur piprmimt ke ptte kaa joos nikaal kr ismem thod़aa chiinii milaa kr pii lem। hiit strok ke lie yh ek asrdaar ghreloo ilaaj hai। isse shriir mem shiitltaa mhsoos hogii aur shriir kaa taapmaan bhii km hogaa।
ailoveraa joos (Aloe Vera Juice)
ailoveraa mem sirph emtii baiktiiriyl guण hii nhiim hote haim, blki yh shriir kii rog prtirodhii kshmtaa ko bhii mjboot krtaa hai। loo lgne pr iske joos piine se shriir memm n sirph thmdk phumchtii hai blki yh rog se ld़ne kii taakt bhii detaa hai।


Disease: chhote stn (Small Breast)

Description: 
adhiktr mhilaaem chhote yaa bd़e stnom kii smsyaa ko lekr preshaan rhtii haim। sudृढ़ aur pusht stn (Breast) strii kii sundrtaa mem chaar chm~d lgaate haim।

Reasons: 
mhilaaom mem chhote stn kii mukhy smsyaa aahaar kii kmii ko maanaa jaataa hai। inke alaavaa kuchh kaarण nimn haim: 
- smtulit paushtik aahaar n lenaa
- vyaayaam n krnaa
- haarmonl smsyaa 
- groth iyr yaani yuvaavsthaa mem tnaav lenaa 

Treatments:
chhote stnom kii smsyaa ko kaise krem door (Tips to Increase Breast Size In Hindi)
chhote stnom kii smsyaa ko door krne ke kii upaay hote haim lekin sbse ahm hai yuvaasthaa kii dhliij pr shii khaan-paan aur tnaav naa lenaa। smॉl brest kii smsyaa se nijaat paane ke kuchh upyogii upaay nimn haim: 
khaan paan (Diet to increase Breast Size)
stn chhote rh jaane pr unhem bd़aa krne ke lie vitaamin yukt smtulit paushtik aahaar lem।
chhote stnom ke lie vyaayaam (Excercise for Small Breats)
