tairnaa, rssii kootnaa, rॉd pkd़kr jhoolnaa stn ke smtulit vikaas ke lie vyaayaam hai।
paanii se  bढ़aaem stn (Use of Water to Increase Breats)
stnom pr thmde paanii kii bauchhaarem dem। isse stnom (Stan) kii koshikaaom mem rkt smchaar achchhii trh hogaa aur stnom kaa vikaas shii dhmg se hogaa।
sthaa hii nhaate smy stnom ko gungune paanii se dhoem। iske turmt baad thmde paanii se dhoem। aisaa pmch-chhh baar krem। taapmaan ke jldii se bdlne se stnom kii koshikaaom mem tejii se rkt smchaar hotaa hai aur stn viksit hote haim।
chhote stnom ke lie msaaj (Massage for Small Breast)
raat ko sote smy baadaam yaa jaitoon ke tel kii stnom pr maalish krem। baadaam yaa jaitoon ke tel mem paae jaane vaale vitaamin e, ii, kailshiym, potaishiym, maigniishiym aur emino esid stnom ko pusht bnaate haim, unkaa vikaas krte haim। saath hii maalish se stnom mem shii prkaar se rkt kaa smchaaln hotaa hai। 
mdr dhmse hue nippl ke lie (Remedies for Sore Nipples in Hindi)
kisii-kisii mhilaa ke stnom ke nippl mdr kii trph rh jaate haim। aisii sthiti mem plaastik kii ek botl mem grm paanii bhrem। phir ise khaalii kr dem। botl mem bhaap rh jaaegii। ab botl ke mumh mem nippl ko daalkr, botl ko is trh se dbaakr rkhem, jisse baahr kii hvaa mdr n jaa ske। jaise-jaise botl kii bhaap thmdii hotii jaaegii, vaise-vaise nippl baahr kii or khimchtaa jaaegaa। botl thmdii hone pr htaa dem। pmch-chhh baar aisaa krem। yh upaay niymit krne se mdr kii or dhmse nippl baahr nikl aate haim। haalmki aisii kisii bhii pryog se phle dॉktr se avshy slaah lem। 


Disease: baalom kaa jhड़naa (Hair Fall)

Description: 
saamaanyth prtidin hmaare lgbhg 50 se 100 baal hr din tootte-jhd़te haim। ydi isse jyaadaa baal jhd़te (Hair Fall) haim, to yh chimtaa kaa vishy hai। baal jhd़ne ke piichhe tnaav, inphekshn, haarmons kaa asmtuln, poshk pdaarthom kii kmii, dvaaom ke saaid iphekts, laaprvaahii brtnaa yaa baalom kii shii dekhbhaal n krnaa, ghtiyaa saabun aur shaimpoo kaa pryog aadi kii kaarण ho skte haim।

Symptoms: 
- kmghii krte haim aur baalom kaa guchchhaa aapke haathom mem hotaa hai
- baal aapke kpd़om ke saath bhii chipke hote haim
- baalom mem haath daalte haim, to aapke baal haath mem aa jaate haim

Reasons: 
baalom ke jhड़ne ke kii kaarण hote haim jaise mm-baap se lgii biimaarii, daimdrph, tnaav aadi। dॉktrom ke anusaar adhik maatraa mem baal jhड़ne ke mukhy kaarण nimn maane jaate haim: ​
- purush haarmon
- vmshaanugt gmjaapn:​ agr peremts yaa graimd perets mem se kisii ko baalom ke jhd़ne yaa gmjepn kii smsyaa hai, to bchchom mem bhii aisaa hone kii aashmkaa jyaadaa hogii।
- bdh़tii huii aayu mem bhii baalom kaa jhड़naa aam baat hotii hai। 
- imphekshn aur daimdrph phmgl imphekshn se baal jhd़ skte haim। 
- haalmki thod़ii-bhut daimdrph honaa saamaany hai, khaaskr mausm bdlne pr, grmiyom aur brsaat kii shurooaat mem, lekin jyaadaa hone pr yh baalom kii jd़om ko kmjor kr detii hai। yh draaii aur mॉishchr, donom roop mem ho sktii hai। isse bchaav ke lie saaph-sphaaii kaa pooraa khyaal rkhem।
- prdooshण aur tnaav, baalom ko gmvaane kii ahm vjh hai।
- maansoon siij़n mem aksr baal jhड़ne kii smsyaa aa jaatii hai। 
- asmtulit bhojn krne se shriir ko aavshyk poshण nhiim miltaa jo kii baar baal jhड़ne kaa kaarण bntaa hai। 
- koii shaariirik biimaarii jaise thaairॉyd ke hone pr bhii baal jhड़ne kii smsyaa dekhne ko miltii hai। 
- aniymit jiivnshailii aur saumdry prsaadhnom kaa anuchit istemaal krnaa bhii baal jhdne kii smsyaa ko nyautaa dete haim। 

Treatments:
​kaise rokem baalom kaa jhड़naa (Hair Fall Remedies in Hindi)
- baalom ko jhd़ne se rokne ke lie svsth jiivnshailii apnaayem।
- tnaav km kr, uchit aahaar lekr bhii jhड़te baalom se nijaat paayaa jaa sktaa hai। 
- baal smvaarne kii uchit tkniik apnaakr aur ydi smbhv ho to baalom ko jhd़ne se rokne vaalii dvaaiyom kaa upyog kr baalom ke jhd़ne kii smsyaa ko rokaa jaa sktaa hai।
- kisii bhii prkaar ke smkrmण se bchne ke lie baalom kii sphaaii pr dhyaan denaa chaahie। jhड़te baalom kii smsyaa se rhne ke lie doosrom ke brsh, kmghii, topii aadi kaa upyog nhiim krnaa chaahie। 
- kii baar dvaaiyom kii shaaytaa se vmshaanugt gmjepn ke kuchh maamlom ko bhii rokaa jaa sktaa hai। aisii dvaaiym dॉktr kii slaah se hii lem। 
- roosii
- joom~

Home Remedies:
kaale-ghne aur lmbe baalom kaa raaj hai poshण। baalom kii jd़om ko milne vaalaa poshण। baalom ko poshण klr, daay yaa shaimpoo se nhiim blki jd़ii-bootiyom se dhone yaa kudrtii tel lgaane se miltaa hai। baal jhrne ke to vaise kii kaarण hote haim। lekin mukhy rup se pet kii gd़bd़ii, tnaav, animdraa aur khraab jiivnshailii hai। dvaaom ke saaid iphekt khaaskr kaimsr ke ilaaj ke dauraan kiimotherepii aur prsv ke dauraan bhii baal jhd़te-girte haim।
aaie jaante haim, kuchh aise ghreloo upchaarom ke baare mem jise istemaal krne se n sirph baalom kaa jhd़naa-girnaa bmd hotaa hai blki baalom mem kudrtii chmk bhii aatii hai।
baal kaa jhd़naa rokne ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Hair fall)
memhdii aur mvlaa (Rosemary and Amla)
memhdii aur mvlaa kii braabr maatraa lekr shaam ko paanii mem bhiimgne ke lie chhod़ dem।  raat bhr bhiimgne ke baad subh isse baalom ko dhoem। ise lgaataar aajmaane baal jhd़ne ruk jaate haim aur baal kaale, mulaaym aur lmbe bhii hote haim।
shmkhpushpii (Shankpushpi)
shmkhpushpii se bne tel rojaanaa niymit roop se baalom mem lgaane se sphed baal kaale ho jaate haim। iske tel se maalish krne se baalom kii jd़om ko poshण miltaa hai aur baal jhd़ne bmd ho jaate haim।
shhd aur mdaa (Honey and Egg)
shhd se baalom kii jd़om ko uchit poshण miltaa hai। agr shhd ke saath mde kii jrdii milaa de to iskaa asr dogunaa ho jaataa hai। baalom kii jd़ yaani skailp ko isse jrurii protiin keraatin miltaa hai aur baalom kaa jhd़naa-girnaa bmd ho jaataa hai। 
bhृmgraaj (Bhringraj)
bhृmgraaj baalom ke lie vmdr medisiin ke rup mem jaanaa jaataa hai। iske aushdhiiy guणom se baalom ko kaaphii phaaydaa phumchtaa hai। rojaanaa bhृmgraaj ke tel se baalom kii maalish krne se baal n sirph kaale aur ghne hote haim blki baalom kaa tootnaa bhii ruk jaataa hai।  ise lgaane se baalom mem rusii ko bhii km hotii hai।
shikaakaaii (Shikakai)
shikaakaaii aur mvle ko achchhii trh se koot lem। donom ko raat bhr paanii mem bhiigne ke lie chhod़ dem। subh is paanii ko mslkr chhaan lem aur isse baalom kii maalish krem। shikaakaaii aur mvle se baal kbhii sphed nhiim hote v jinke baal sphed hom to ve bhii kaale ho jaate haim। baalom kaa jhd़naa-girnaa bhii bmd ho jaataa hai।
naariyl tel, ऑliv ऑyl aur niimboo kaa rs (Coconut oil, Olive Oil and Lemon Juice)
naariyl tel aur ऑliv ऑyl kii braabr maatraa lekr ismem niimboo kii kuchh boomde milaa kr baalom kii maalish krem। maalish ke baad phir grm taulie se sir ko 3 mint ke lie dhk lem। yh krne se baalom kaa jhd़naa bmd hotaa hai aur baal kaalaa bhii hotaa hai।
methii (Methi)
methii ke biijom mem baalom ko poshण dene vaale sbhii jrurii ttv maujood rhte haim,jo baalom kii jd़ ko mjbootii prdaan krtaa hai। methii daanom ko piiskr choorण bnaa lem। choorण mem paanii milaakr pest taiyaar kr lem aur is pest ko baalom mem lgaaem। ise lgaane se baalom kaa jhd़naa-girnaa km hogaa aur baal kaale, ghne aur lmbe homge। daimdrph kii preshaanii bhii khtm hogii। 
amrbel (Amarbel)
amrbel baalom ke lie tॉnik kii trh kaam krtaa hai। amrbel ko paanii mem ubaal kr rkh lem। jb paanii aadhaa ho jaae aur amrbel paanii mem poorii trh mil jaae to to ise utaar lem।  subh isse baalom ko dhoem। isse baalom kaa jhd़naa-girnaa ruk jaaegaa। baal lmbe, kaale aur ghne bhii homge। 
triphlaa (Trifala)
triphlaa choorण mem lauh bhsm milaakr subh-shaam khaane se baalom kaa jhd़naa bmd ho jaataa hai aur baalom mem kudrtii rmg bhii aatii hai।


Disease: mirgii (Epilepsy)

Description: 
mirgii ek aisaa rog hai, jismem vykti achaank jmiin pr gir kr praayh arddh moorchhitaavsthaa mem rhtaa hai। rogii ko iskaa poorvaabhaas bhii nhiim hotaa, ki use mirgii (Epilepsy) kaa dauraa pड़ne vaalaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- inhem tiin avsthaaom mem bmtaa jaa sktaa hai। prthm avsthaa-saaraa shriir tn jaataa hai। yh avsthaa 30 sekmd se adhik nhiim hotii, mriij apnii jiibh ko dmtom se chbaa sktaa hai। kii mriijom ko kpड़om mem peshaab yaa paakhaanaa bhii ho jaataa hai। dvitiiy avsthaa- yh adhik ugr hotii hai, do se pmch mintom tk bnii rhne vaalii is avsthaa ke dauraan mriij ko tel jhtke aate haim। uske mumh se jhaag niklkr baahr bhne lgtaa hai, homth aur chehraa niile pड़e jaate haim। tृtiiy avsthaa-jhtke aanaa bmd ho jaataa hai। mriij yaa to hosh mem aa jaataa hai yaa vh phir aisii avsthaa mem rhtaa hai।

Reasons: 
mirgii ke daure mukhyt: dimaagii kmjorii ke kaarण aate haim। yh kmjorii anuvmshik yaa kisii any kaarण se bhii ho sktii hai। mirgii ke daure (Mirgi ke Daure) pड़ne ke kuchh ahm kaarण nimn haim: 
mirgii ke daurom kaa kaarण (Reason for Epilepsy in Hindi) 
- yh rog saamaanyt: mstishk kii kmjorii ke kaarण hotaa hai। 
- mstishk mem rktsraav honaa yaa khoon kaa thkkaa jm jaane (strok) ke kaarण bhii mirgii ke daure aate haim। 
- sir mem chot lgne yaa mstishk smkrmण ke kaarण 
- grbhaavsthaa kii jtiltaaom kii vjh se maataa ko grbhaavsthaa mem hue dimaagii smkrmण
- dimaag mem koii gmth 
- dimaagii bukhaar
- dimaag mem kisii vjh se soojn yaa vishaile pdaarth kaa dimaag mem phum~chnaa 
- atydhik tej bukhaar
- khsraa yaa glsoojaa
- nimn rktchaap ke kaarण bhii mirgii kii biimaarii ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
mirgii ke mriij ko dauraa aataa hai jis dauraan uske shriir kii gtividhiym saamaany nhiim rhtii। is dauraan agr mriij ko shii upchaar naa mile to sthiti chimtaajnk ho sktii hai। mirgii kaa dauraa aane pr nimn upaay apnaane chaahie:
- mriij ko jmiin pr yaa smtl sthaan pr litaa dem। 
- uske aaspaas se tej, nukiilii yaa chubhne vaalii vstuom ko htaa dem। 
- jhtkom ko aane diyaa jaaye। jaise hii jhtke bmd ho jaayem, mriij ko vishraam kii sthiti mem litaa dem aur uskii grdn ek or moड़ dem taaki mumh mem jmaa laar aur jhaag baahr nikl jaae। 
- yaad rkhiye, jhtkom ke dauraan mriij mem mumh mem kuchh n rkhiye, aksr mriij ko dmtom pr dmt kste dekh log uske mumh mem chmmch yaa any vstu rkh dete haim। mgr aisaa krnaa khtrnaak siddh ho sktaa hai kyomki aisaa vstu tootkr sms ke raaste mem jaa sktii hai yaa mriij ke dmt toot skte haim।
- kse hue yaa baadhaa utpnn krne vaale vstrom ko nikaal dem। 
- is biich chikitsk se smprk kr yaa to use vhiim bulaa lem yaa phir mriij ko asptaal le jaaem। 

Home Remedies:
ipiilepsii yaani mirgii mstishk kii ek biimaarii hai। yh mstishk aur snaayu koshikaaom ke biich aapsii taalmel nhiim hone ke kaarण hotaa hai। mirgii hone ke aur bhii kii kaarण hote haim msln- bijlii kaa jhtkaa lgnaa, nshiilii dvaaom kaa adhik sevn krnaa, sir mem tej chot lgnaa, tej bukhaar tthaa esphiiksiyaa jaise rog ke hone se bhii mirgii ke daure aate haim।
snaayu smbmdhii rog, bren tyoomr, smkraamk jvr se bhii mirgii kii biimaarii hotii hai। ismem mriij ko dauraa aataa hai। mirgii ke mriij is baat se preshaan rhte haim ki ve aam logom kii trh jiivn jii nhiim skte। lekin unhem jiivn se preshaan nhiim honaa chaahie। agr jiivnshailii mem skaaraatmk bdlaav kie jaae aur kuchh ghreloo ilaaj niymit rup se aajmaayaa jaae to mirgii ke mriij bhii behtr jimdgii jii skte haim।
mirgii rog ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Epilepsy)
bkrii kaa doodh aur memhdii (Goat’s Milk and Rosemery)
bkrii kaa doodh mirgii ke mriijom ke lie kaaphii phaaydemmd hotaa hai। paav bhr bkrii ke doodh mem 50 graam memhdii ke pttom kaa rs milaakr roj svere do hphtaa tk piine se mirgii ke daure bmd ho jaate haim।
tulsii ke pttiym (Basil Leaves)
tulsii kii biimaariyom mem raambaaण kii trh km krtaa hai। tulsii mem kaaphii maatraa mem emtii ऑksiidemt paae jaate haim jo mstishk mem phrii redikls ko thiik krte haim। mstishk kii kisii bhii prkaar kii biimaarii mem agr rojaanaa tulsii ke 20 pttiym chbaakr khaayaa jaae to yh kaaphii asrdaar hotaa hai।
braahmii bootii (Brahmni Leaves)
braahmii ke ptte hmaare ghrom ke aaspaas khaaskr jhm mittii hote haim, vhm ugte haim। yh aakaar mem gol aur ghumaavdaar hotaa hai। ise roj khaalii pet chbaa kr khaane se n sirph yaaddaasht mjboot hotii hai, blki mirgii ke daure ko bhii yh km krtaa hai।
mgoor kaa rs (Grapes Juice)
mirgii ke mriijom ke lie mgoor kaa rs kaaphii phaaydemmd hotaa hai। lgbhg aadhaa kilo mgoor kaa rs nikaalkr svere khaalii pet piinaa chaahie। ise chhh mhiine tk aajmaane se behtr priणaam milte haim।
mittii kaa lep (Soil Bath)
mittii ko paanii mem giilaa krke mriij ke poore shriir lep lgaa dem। ek ghmte baad nhaa lem। isse mirgii ke daure km aaege aur mriij thod़aa behtr mhsoos kregaa। yh ilaaj kaaphii kaargr hai।
kddoo (Petha)
mirgii ke mriijom ke lie kddoo yaa pethaa sbse kaargr ghreloo ilaaj hai। pethe kii sbjii bhii bnaaii jaatii hai aur aap iskii sbjii kaa bhii sevn kr skte haim, lekin iskaa joos roj़aanaa piine se kaaphii phaaydaa hotaa hai।


Disease: kd bढ़aanaa (Height Gain)

Description: 
bchchom~ mem shaariirik vikaas ek aam prkriyaa hotii hai। bchchom kii lmbaaii yaa kd (Height) kaa saamaany roop mem bढ़naa isii vikaas kaa mhtvpoorण soochk hai। lmbaaii kaa bढ़naa yoom to aanuvmshik hotaa hai lekin kii baar poshण kii kmii yaa kuchh any kaarणom se bchchom kii lmbaaii bhut km rh jaatii hai।

Symptoms: 
- aayu anusaar kd km honaa

Reasons: 
- anuvmshik : bchchom kii lmbaaii maataa aur pitaa kii lmbaaii pr bhii nirbhr krtii hai। amerikaa ke tphts vishvvidyaaly ke ek shodh mem aisaa paayaa gyaa kisii vykti ke kd kaa nirdhaarण krne mem 60 se 80 prtisht yogdaan hmaarii jiins (Genes) kaa aur 20 se 40 prtisht hmaare khaane piine, khaaskr paushtik chiijom aur vaataavrण kaa hotaa hai।
- aahaar aur poshण: ydi uchit aahaar aur poshण ke baad bhii bchchom kii lmbaaii n bdh़ rhii ho to dॉktr se smprk krnaa chaahie। dॉktr bchchom ke vikaas kii groth chaart dvaaraa any bchchom evm unke abhibhaavkom se tulnaa krte haim aur agr aavshyk ho to groth haarmon ke pryog kaa sujhaav bhii dete haim। groth haarmon dvaaraa bchchom kii lmbaaii 20-25 semtiimiitr tk bdh़ jaatii hai। groth haarmon kevl dॉktr ke sujhaav se hii lem । 
- haivii vetliphtimg: chhotii umr mem haivii vetliphtimg se bhii lmbaaii kaa bdh़naa rook jaataa hai। islie koshish krnii chaahie ki bchchom ko chhotii-umr mem jyaadaa bhaarii saamaan naa uthaanaa pड़e। 

Treatments:
- bchchem ke shaariirik vikaas pr poorii trh njr rkhem। agr koii preshaanii ho to jld se jld dॉktr se slaah lem। 
- paushtik aahaar lem: aahaar mem praakृtik protiin kii maatr aapke vjn ke anusaar honii chaahie yaani prti kilograam vjn pr 1 graam protiin hmem din mem avshy lenaa chaahie।
- kuchh yog aasaan bhii lmbaaii bढ़aane mem laabhdaayk siddh hote hai। 

Home Remedies:
oomchaa kd hr koii paanaa chaahtaa hai lekin hr kisii kii lmbaaii achchhii ho, aisaa mumkin nhiim hotaa hai। achchhii lmbaaii se jhm, shaariirik bnaavt achchhii lgtii hai vhiim vykti kaa aatmvishvaas bhii bढ़ jaataa hai। vykti kii lmbaaii yoom to anuvmshik kaarणom pr nirbhr krtii hai lekin kii baar any kaarणom se bhii lmbaaii km ho sktii hai।
 
aaie jaanem lmbaaii bढ़aane ke lie ghreloo upaay (Home remedies for Height Gain)
1. ashvgmdhaa (Ashwagandha)- ashvgmdhaa lmbaaii bढ़aane mem shaayk hai। ashvgmdhaa mem minrl hote haim jo ki lmbaaii bढ़aane mem shaayk hote haim। do chmmch ashvgmdhaa choorण ko ek gilaas grm gaay ke doodh ke saath lem। svaad ke anusaar doodh mem chiinii yaa guड़ milaayaa jaa sktaa hai। 45 din tk rojaanaa sone se phle yh upaay krne se lmbaaii bढ़ne lgtii hai।
2. doodh (Milk)- doodh mem uchch maatraa mem kailshiym, vitaamin e aur protiin hotaa hai jo lmbaaii bढ़aane mem shaayk hotaa hai।
3. shriir ko khiimchem (Stretch your body)- shriir ko khiimchne vaale vyaayaam krne se praakृtik roop se lmbaaii bढ़ne lgtii hai। shriir ko khiimchne ke lie ghutnom ko moड़e binaa pair ke mgoothom ko chhoone kaa pryaas krem। pmjom pr chlem aur isii trh ke any vyaayaam krem।
4. yogaa (Yoga)- lmbaaii bढ़aane ke lie yogaa bhii behd asrkaarii hotaa hai। yogaa krne se tnaav bhii km hotaa hai jo ki shriir kii lmbaaii bढ़aane mem shaayk hai।
5. bhrpoor niimd (Sound sleep)- shriir ke achchhe vikaas ke lie bhrpoor niimd bhii behd jroorii hai। achchhii niimd sone se hyoomn groth haarmon (Human growth hormone) achchhii maatraa mem nikltaa hai jisse vykti kii lmbaaii bढ़ne lgtii hai।
6. smtulit khaan-paan (Proper diet)- poshk ttvom se yukt khaan-paan bhii vykti kii lmbaaii bढ़aane mem shaayk hotaa hai। shriir ko bhrpoor maatraa mem protiin, vitaamin aur minrl milte haim jisse vykti kii lmbaaii bढ़tii hai।
behtr shaariirik vikaas ke lie shii poshchr bnaanaa bhii behd jroorii hai। siidhe aur tnkr baithnaa, chlnaa aur kmdhom ko taankr rkhne se bhii lmbaaii pr skaaraatmk prbhaav pड़taa hai।


Disease: gurde kii pthrii (Kidney Stone)

Description: 
pet ke nichle hisse mem yaa mutraashy mem tej drd pthrii kii nishaanii ho sktii hai। yh ek aisii smsyaa hai jo kisii bhii imsaan ko ho sktii hai। gurde kii pthrii mem jo drd hotaa hai vh behd ashniiy ho jaataa hai। is biimaarii ko smjhnaa aur isse door rhne ke upaay jaannaa behd aavshyk hai।

Symptoms: 
- gurde kii pthrii ke jyaadaatr rogii piith se pet kii trph aate bhymkr drd kii shikaayt krte haim
- drd ke saath jii michlaane tthaa ultii hone kii shikaayt bhii ho sktii hai
- drd baajoo, shroणi, uroo mool, guptmgo tk bdh़ sktaa hai, yh drd kuchh minto yaa ghmto tk bnaa rhtaa hai tthaa biich-biich mem aaraam miltaa hai
- pthrii ke lkshण aur chinh peshaab ke ptthrom kaa aakaar jgh, saaij aur peshaab ke bhaav mem avrodh ke paimaane pr nirbhr krtaa hai
- piith ke nichle hisse mem athvaa pet ke nichle bhaag mem achaank tej drd, jo pet v jmgh ke smdhi kshetr tk jaataa hai
- ydi mootr smbmdhii prणaalii ke kisii bhaag mem smkrmण hai to iske lkshणom mem bukhaar, kmpkmpii, psiinaa aanaa, peshaab aane ke saath-saath drd honaa aadi bhii shaamil ho skte haim ; baar baar aur ekdm se peshaab aanaa, ruk ruk kr peshaab aanaa, raat mem adhik peshaab aanaa, mootr mem rkt bhii aa sktaa hai। mdkoshom mem drd, peshaab kaa rmg asaamaany honaa
- yh drd rh-rh kr uthtaa hai aur kuchh minto se kii ghmto tk bnaa rhtaa hai ise ”riiln kronin” khte haim
- yh rog kaa prmukh lkshण hai, ismem mootrvaahk nlii kii pthrii mem drdo piith ke nichle hisse se uthkr jmghom kii or jaataa hai

Reasons: 
gurde kii pthrii ke kaarण (Reason of Kidney Stone)
peshaab kii pthrii peshaab mem upsthit lvणom v khnijom ke jmaav se bntii haim। jb lvणom aur khnijom kii prtem vibhinn jghom pr jmaa hotii jaatii haim to in mhiin ptthrom kaa aakaar bdh़taa jaataa hai। ye sbhii lvण aur khnij khaane kii chiijom v paanii se shriir mem aae hote hai। kuchh sbjiym jaise paalk, arbii ke ptte aur tmaatrom mem bhut adhik lvण hote haim।
jmiinii paanii mem bhii kaaphii saare lvण hote haim। kuem~ yaa borvel kaa paanii bhii pthrii bnne kaa kaarण hotaa hai। ye lvण dhiire-dhiire krke shriir mem jmaa ho jaate haim aur ptthr bnaa lete haim। 
phॉsphet aur kॉrbonet ke ptthrom kii sth mulaaym hotii hai aur ऑkjelet ke ptthrom kii khurdurii । is kaarण se ऑkjelet ke ptthrom ke kaarण khoon bhii nikl sktaa hai।
gurde kii pthrii ke kaarण (Causes of Kidney Stone)
pthrii ek aam biimaarii hai jo aksr glt-khaanpaan ke kaarण bhii ho jaatii hai। is biimaarii ke kuchh mukhy kaarण nimn haim: 
- hr din paanii kii pryaapt maatraa kaa sevn n krnaa
- kaiphiin aur shraab kaa adhik upyog krnaa
- mootr maarg mem smkrmण honaa

Treatments:
​- pthrii ke mriij ko din mem km se km 5-6 liitr paanii piinaa chaahiye। pthrii hone pr pryaapt jl piiyem taaki 2 se 2.5 liitr mootr roj bne। adhik maatraa mem mootr bnne pr chhotii pthrii mootr ke saath nikl jaatii hai
- aahaar mem protiin, naaitrojn tthaa sodiym kii maatraa km ho। 
- aisaa bhojn krem jinmem aakjelet kii maatraa adhik ho; jaise chaaklet, soyaabiin, moomgphlii, paalk, aadi ke saath kold drimks se door rhem। 
- naarmgii aadi kaa rs (joos) lene se pthrii kaa khtraa km hotaa hai। 
- dॉktr pthrii ke mriijom ko mgoor aur krelaa aadi bhii khaane kii slaah dete haim। 

Home Remedies:
kidnii mem ston yaani ptthr honaa (jise pthrii bhii khte haim) ab ek kॉmn biimaarii ho gii hai। peshaab mem yoorik esid, phॉsphors, kailshiym aur ऑkjelik esid jaise kemikl ke bdh़ne kii vjh se kidnii mem ptthr yaa pthrii hotaa hai। vitaamin dii ke atydhik sevn, shriir mem minrls kii maatraa mem asmtuln, dihaaidreshn yaa phir asmtulit daayt se bhii kidnii mem ston hotaa hai।
peshaab agr kaaphii gaadh़aa ho rhaa ho to yh kidnii mem ptthr hone kaa lkshण hai। pthrii hone pr kaaphii ashniiy drd hotaa hai। peshaab krne mem bhii kaaphii drd hotaa hai। vaise to pthrii hone pr srjrii kii jaatii hai, mgr iske kii ghreloo ilaaj bhii haim।
kidnii mem pthrii ke lie ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies for Kidney Stone)
kurthii daal (Kurthi Daal)
pthrii ko glaane mem kurthii daal kaaphii asrdaar hotaa hai। kurthii daal ko pkaa kr bhii khaa skte haim, lekin kurthii daal kaa paanii piinaa sbse kaargr hotaa hai।
naariyl paanii (Coconut Water)
kidnii ke seht ke lie naariyl kaaphii phaaydemmd hai। naariyl paanii pthrii ko glaataa hai। pthrii hone pr naariyl paanii subh piinaa chaahie।
hrii ilaaichii (Green Cardamom)
hrii ilaaichii ke bhii bd़e aushdhiiy guण haim। ilaaichii kaa sevn kidnii ke biimaarii mem kaaphii phaaydemmd hotaa hai। hrii ilaaychii, khrbooje ke biij kii grii aur mishrii ko paanii mem milaakr piine se kidnii kii pthrii nikl jaatii hai।
jaamun (Blackberry)
jaamun daaibitiij smet kii biimaariyom mem raambaaण kaa kaam krtaa hai। pthrii ke ilaaj mem bhii yh kaaphii asrdaar hai।
mvlaa (Amla)
mvlaa sirph kesh kmti bdh़aane mem hii kaam nhiim aataa hai। iske kii aushdhiiy guण bhii haim। kidnii ke pthrii ko glaane mem yh kaaphii kaargr hai। mvle kaa choorण moolii ke saath khaane se pthrii gl jaatii hai।
jiiraa (Cumin seeds)
jiire kii taasiir seht ke lie kaaphii phaaydemmd hai। hr bhaartiiy ke ghr mem msaale ke rup mem upyog kie jaane vaale jiire ke kaaphii aushdhiiy guण haim। jiiraa ko chiinii ke saath piiskr thmde paanii ke saath piine se kidnii ke pthrii glte haim।
shjn (Moringa Oleifera)
shjn hii ekmaatr aisii sbjii hai jismem prchur maatraa mem emtiibaayotik guण paae jaate haim। chiknpॉks, mijls smet kii trh kii vaairl biimaariyom se bchaane kaa kaam krtii hai shjn। iske sevn se kidnii kii pthrii bhii gltii hai।


Disease: penis kaa saaij (Size Of Normal Penis)

Description: 
biis se chaaliis saal kii umr ke jyaadaatr purush, apne penis kii saaij (Penis Size) ko lekr shmkaa mem rhte haim ki khiim unke limg (Ling) kaa saaij chhotaa to nhii hai। iske kaarण unmem hiin bhaavnaa aam smsyaa hai। is vishy mem purush apne dॉktr se bhii khulkr baat nhii krte haim। yh ek trh kii seks smsyaa (Sex Problem) hai। adhiktr purusho kaa limg kaa saaij saamaany hotaa hai। haalmki, limg ke saaij ko lekr logom mem bhrmtiym (Misconceptions) jyaadaa hai।

Treatments:
penis (Penis) mem agr rkt smchaar shii rhe to limg kaa aakr bड़aa prtiit hotaa hai। kuchh saamaany baatom ko apnii roj़aanaa kii jimdgii mem shaamil krke rmkt smchaar ko bdh़aayaa jaa sktaa hai-
- niymit vyaayaam
- uchit aahaar lem
- sbjiym aur phl
- tnaav rhit jiivnshailii
- yog aasaan 
- penis pmp - aamtaur pr maanaa jaataa hai ki penis pmp penis kii saaij ko bdh़aane mem mddgaar saabit ho sktaa hai। haalmki iskaa hmeshaa pryog khtrnaak ho sktaa hai kyomki isse nsom ko nuksaan phumchne kaa khtraa rhtaa hai।


Disease: roosii (Dandruff)

Description: 
aajkl roosii yaa daimdrph (Dandruff) kii smsyaa bhut aam ho chukii hai। yh hmaare sir kii tvchaa mem sthit mृt koshikaaom se paidaa hotii hai। daimdrph kii vjh se baal jhd़naa tthaa khujlii jaisii smsyaaem paidaa hotii haim। rusii ke vishy mem mithy (Myths of Dandruff in Hindi) aamtaur pr logom kaa maannaa hai kii roosii tbhii hotii hai, jb hmaare sir kii tvchaa rookhii hotii hai। lekin aisaa nhiim hai। roosii hone kaa kaarण hai, yiist, jo ki sir kii mृt tvchaa ko aur sir mem jme hue tel ko khaa kr jiitii hai। roosii kii vjh se hmaare sir kii tvchaa kii koshikaaem jldii-jldii jhड़ne lgtii hai aur hmem lgtaa hai ki hmaare sr mem roosii ho gii hai। 

Symptoms: 
- agr aapko tiin hphte se adhik se khmsii hai
- kbj aur ख़raab pet : kuchh adhyynom se yh ptaa chltaa hai ki kbj aur ख़raab pet hone kii vjh se bhii rusii hotii hai
- daimdrph se sir mem khujlii rhtii hai aur baal girne lgte haim। yh jyaadaatr srdiyom mem hotii hai
- baalom kaa girnaa : aamtaur pr hmaare roज़ 20 se 50 baal girte haim। sr mem rusii hone se bhii baal jhड़te haim,  agr isse jyaadaa baal jhड़te hai to rusii bhii kaarण ho sktii hai
- sr kii sookhii tvchaa :  sr kii sookhii tvchaa rusii hone kaa ek prmukh kaarण hai
- sr mem khujlii: jb rusii honaa shuroo hotii hai to sbse phle sr mem khujlii honaa shuroo ho jaatii hai

Reasons: 
baalom mem rusii hone kii mukhy vjh (Top Reason For Dandruff In Hindi)
baalom kii shii dekhbhaal naa krnaa, shii daait naa lenaa yaa any kii vjhem hotii haim jinkii vjh se sr mem rusii (Rusi) ho sktii hai। in prmukh vjhom mem se kuchh nimn haim: 
1. mausm mem bdlaav- atydhik grm yaa atydhik thmdaa mausm donom hii sir kii tvchaa ko nuksaan phumchaate haim। jis trh mausm kaa utaar chढ़aav hmaare shriir ko prbhaavit krtaa hai usii prkaar sir kii tvchaa ko bhii, jiskaa ntiijaa daimdrph ho sktaa hai।
2. haaijiin- baalom kii thiik se sphaaii n krne yaa sir se smbmdhit upkrणom ko saaph n rkhne jaise kmghii, tauliyaa, heyr brsh aadi iske saath hii kisii aur ke dvaaraa istemaal kie ge kmghii yaa tauliyaa ko istemaal krne se bhii roosii hone kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
3. shii daait- shriir mem poshk ttvom kaa shii smtuln n hone se bhii skailp se roosii numaa ppड़ii utrne lgtii hai। daait mem daal, doodh, taaज़aa phl aur hrii sbjiyom (Diet for Dandruff) kaa istemaal jroorii hai। iske alaavaa baalom mem shii maatraa mem tel n lgaane se bhii daimdrph shuroo ho jaataa hai।
4. ऑyl glaimd kaa bmd honaa- kii baar kisii biimaarii yaa haarmonl asmtuln ke kaarण ऑyl glaimd bmd ho jaate haim jisse roosii hone lgtii hai।
5. smkrmण- baalom kii staailimg ke lie kemikl kaa pryog, heyr klr kaa istemaal, baalom ko nechurl roop se n sookhne denaa, giile baalom ko hii bmdh lenaa aadi kuchh aise kaarण haim jisse daimdrph (Rusi) hone lgtaa hai। isse baalom mem khujlii shuroo hotii hai aur dhiire dhiire smsyaa bढ़tii jaatii hai।
6. heyr klr- heyr klr mem amoniyaa hotaa hai jo ki skailp pr roosii ko jnm detaa hai। heyr klr kaa istemaal eksprt se raay lekr hii krnaa chaahie aur achchhe kism ke heyr klr kaa istemaal krnaa chaahie।
7. psiinaa aur dhool- grmiyom ke dinom mem sir kii tvchaa pr jmaa psiinaa jb dhool ke smprk mem aataa hai to skailp pr gmdgii jmaa honaa shuroo ho jaatii hai। jo ki dhiire dhiire daimdrph kaa kaarण bn jaatii hai। 
8. elrjii- kii baar hm jo tel, shaimpoo, heyr staailimg prॉdkt yaa heyr klr istemaal kr rhe hote haim vh hmem soot nhiim krtaa, ntiijaa elrjii ho jaatii hai jo daimdrph hone kaa bड़aa kaarण hai।

Treatments:
praathmik str pr rusii kii dekhbhaal (First Level Treatment in Hindi)
- apne sr kii sth ko rukhaa hone se bchaane ke lie sr aur baalom mem niymit roop se tel lgaayem।
- baalom ko niymit roop se dhoye, aise krne se yh saaph rhemge aur kisii prkaar kii smsyaa ke aasaar km homge।  
- baalom ko smkrmण se bchaane ke lie doosrom kii kmghii aadi kaa istemaal nhiim krnaa chaahie। 
- joom~
- baalom kaa jhड़naa
- joom~
