Disease: haart ataik (Heart Attack)

Description: 
haart ataik yaa hृdy aaghaat haal ke saalom mem srvaadhik hone vaalii laaiphstaail biimaarii hai। hृdy mem blॉkej ke kaarण hone vaalii is biimaarii se duniyaabhr mem kii log piiड़it haim aur kii jaan gmvaa chuke haim। haart ataik (Heart Attack) ke pchaas prtisht mriijom kii asptaal phum~chne se phle hii mृtyu ho jaatii hai। hr saal bhaart mem 30 laakh logom kii maut dil kii biimaarii se hotii hai।

Symptoms: 
- chhaatii mem drd honaa evm siine mem aithn honaa
- tvchaa pr chipchipaaht, uniimdaapn, siine mem jln mhsoos honaa
- psiinaa aanaa evm sms phoolnaa
- mhilaao mem haart ataik aane pr kuchh any lkshण bhii dekhe  skte hai
- mitlii aanaa, ultii honaa
- haathom,  kmdhom, kmr yaa jbड़e mem drd honaa
- asaamaany roop se thkaan honaa

Reasons: 
haart ataik hone ke kaarणom mem aasiin jiivn shailii (Sedentary Lifestyle) sbse bd़ii vjh hai। shaariirik prishrm kii kmii ke kaarण shriir mem khoon kaa smchaar shriir mem shii ढ़mg se nhiim ho paataa। iske alaavaa haart ataik (Heart Attack) ke kuchh kaarण nimn haim: 
haart ataik ke kaarण (Causes of Heart Attack in Hindi)
- kolestrol kaa bढ़naa
- uchch rktchaap
- daaybitiij
- motaapaa
- tnaav 
- asmtulit aahaar
- vyaayaam yaa shaariirik shrm mem kmii

Treatments:
- haart ataik hone pr rogii ko litaa dem aur jitnaa ho ske uske aaspaas khulaa vaataavrण rkhem। 
- rogii ke kpड़o ko dhiilaa kr dem। 
- smym brtte hue htheliyom se rogii kii chhaatii pr tej aur jor se dbaav daalem। hr dbaav ke baad chhaatii mem maujood kmpreshn ko riliij krne kaa pryaas krem। 
- is prkiyaa ko 25 -30 baar dohraaem। 
- isse rogii kii dhd़knem phir se laut aaemgii। 
- binaa vilmb kiye embulems ko bulaae। 
- dॉktr se phon pr smprk kr dॉktr kii slaah kaa shii triike se paaln krem। 
- uchch rktchaap
- haart blॉkej

Home Remedies:
haart ataik se bchaav ke kuchh ghreloo upaay (Home remedies for Heart attack)
- paanii mem niimboo kaa rs milaakr roj piiem।
- phlom mem amrood, annaas, mausmii, liichii aur seb kaa istemaal krem।
- sbjiyom mem arbii aur chaulaaii jroor khaaem।
- khaane mem dhii jroor khaayem।
- dil ko mjboot krne ke lie desii ghii mem guड़ milaakr khaaem।


Disease: soraaysis (Psoriasis)

Description: 
soraaysis tvchaa kii ooprii sth kaa chrm rog hai jisse tvchaa mem koshikaaom (Cells) kii taadaad bdhne lgtii hai aur tvchaa ke oopr motii prt jm jaatii hai। soraaysis kii biimaarii mem saamaanyth tvchaa pr laal rmg kii sth ubhrkr aatii hai। yh khopd़ii (Scalp), haath-pm~v athvaa haath kii htheliyom, pm~v ke tlvom, kohnii, ghutnom aur piith pr adhik hotii hai। soriyaasis rog (Psoriasis) smkraamk kism kaa rog nhiim hai। rogii ke smprk se any logom ko koii khtraa nhiim hai।

Symptoms: 
- mkhom mem jln
- chlne-phirne mem dikkt aanaa
- jod़om mem drd
- shriir mem laal rmg ke chktte dikhaaii dene lgte haim

Reasons: 
soraaysis rog (A type of Skin Infection) ke mukhy kaarण do hii maane jaate haim ek aanu‌vmshik aur doosraa pryaavrण। 
mukhy kaarण (Main Causes of Psoriasis)
aanuvmshik: dॉktr maante haim ki soraaysis aanuvmshik kaarणom se bhii aa sktaa hai। 
pryaavrण: lgaataar kaimikls aur prdooshण ke smprk mem rhne kaarण bhii soraaysis ho sktaa hai। yh biimaarii srdiyom mem adhik hotii hai। jyaadaa der dhoop mem rhne ke kaarण bhii yh biimaarii ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
soraaysis se bchaav aur upchaar kaa phlaa kendr hai tvchaa kii dekhbhaal krnaa। soraaysis hone pr nimn upaay bhii phaaydemmd hote haim:
- soraaysis ke lkshण dikhne pr visheshjञ chikitsk se slaah lem tthaa uske btaae nirdeshom kaa paaln krem । 
- soraaysis ke rogiyom ko tnaavmukt rhnaa chaahie। kyomki tnaav siidhe-siidhe soraaysis ko prbhaavit kr rog ke lkshणom mem vृddhi krtaa hai। 
- tvchaa ko adhik khushk hone se bhii bchaaem~ taaki khujlii n ho। 
- rog kii tiivrtaa n hone pr saadhaarणth kriim ityaadi se hii rog niymtrण mem rhtaa hai। lekin kbhii-kbhii mum~h se lii jaane vaalii emtiisorik aur simtometik aushdhiyom kaa pryog aavshyk ho jaataa hai। aajkl altraavaaylet laait se upchaar kii vidhi bhii atydhik upyogii aur laabhdaayk ho rhii hai। 
- skin kaimsr
- aphaaraa

Home Remedies:
chrm rogom mem soraaysis sbse krॉnik aur gmbhiir biimaarii hai। yh rkt mem ashuddhi aur tvchaa ke jyaadaa shushk hone kii vjh se hotaa hai। soraaysis se piid़it mriij jimdgii mem bhaavnaatmk str pr kaaphii naakaaraatmk mhsoos krne lgte haim। unhem apne haath-pair yaa jis kisii bhii mg kii tvchaa mem soraaysis hai usko lekr hmeshaa ek shrmimdgii kii bhaavnaa mn mem rhtii hai। kii mriij to baahr jaanaa tk bmd kr dete haim। jbki unhem aisaa nhiim krnaa chaahie। behtr dekhbhaal aur behtr ilaaj se smbhv hai aap is biimaarii ke rhte bhii behtr anubhv kr skte haim।
soraaysis mem tvchaa mem tej khujlaaht, nochne kaa mn aur kbhii-kbhii drd bhii hotii hai। tvchaa jyaadaa shushk hone pr kbhii-kbhii laal chkte aur phlaiks bhii nikl aate haim। jo sookhne pr ppd़ii kii trh jhd़ne lgtii hai। soraaysis kaa koii thos ilaaj nhiim hai, kuchh ghreloo upchaar krne se iske lkshण jrur km ho jaate haim lekin hmeshaa ke lie isse chhutkaaraa nhiim miltaa hai।
soraaysis ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home remedies for Psoriasis)
gungune paanii mem snaan (Bath in Lukewarm Water)
tel, otmiil, semdhaa nmk gungune paanii mem milaa kr baath tb mem 15 mint baith jaae। niklne ke baad poore bdn mem mॉschraaijr lgaa le। isse skin kaa draaines km hogaa aur tvchaa pr ppd़ii bhii nhiim jmegii।
mॉschraaijr (Moisturizer)
soraaysis mem tvchaa turmt-turmt shushk ho jaatii hai aur isse khujlii aur nochne kii prvृti bhii jldii-jldii hone lgtii hai। isse bchne ke lie tvchaa mem hmeshaa nmii bnaae rkhem। tvchaa ko jldii shushk hii nhiim hone dem। poore bdn mem mॉschraaijr kaa lep hmeshaa lgaa kr rkhem।
kutkii chirautaa (Kutki Chirauta)
rkt ashuddhi se hone vaalii sbhii biimaariyom ke lie kutkii chirautaa raambaaण hai। yh piine mem kaaphii kd़vaa hotaa hai aur piine ke saath ultii yaa mitlii jaisaa bhii hone lgtaa hai, lekin yh kaaphii asrdaar hai।
chaar graam chirautaa aur chaar graam kutkii lekr shiishe yaa chiinii ke brtn mem aadhaa glaas paanii daal kr bhiimgne ke lie raat bhr chhod़ dem। subh raat ko bhigoyaa huaa chirautaa aur kutkii kaa paanii nithaar kr kpd़e se chhaankr pii lem aur piine ke baad 3-4 ghmte tk kuchh khme nhiim। lgaataar chaar hphte tk kutkii-chirautaa piine se soraaysis, phod़e-phumsii se lekr pet ke kiid़e tk nsht ho jaate haim। yh rkt ko saaph krtaa hai।


Disease: svaain phloo (Swine Flu)

Description: 
svaain phloo yaa H1N1 (H1N1 Flu) ek smkrmण hai, jo inphlooemjaa e vaayrs (Influenza Virus​) ke kaarण hotaa hai। aamtaur pr yh biimaarii sooarom mem hotii hai, islie ise svaain phloo khaa jaataa hai, lekin kii baar sooar ke siidhe smprk mem aane pr yh mnushy mem bhii phail jaatii hai। yh bhut jldii phailne vaalaa rog hai। isse bchne ke lie smkrmit logom se door rhnaa chaahie।

Symptoms: 
- H1N1 ke rogiyom ko bhut jyaadaa thkaan mhsoos hotii hai।
- H1N1 mem piiड़it vykti mmspeshiym mem drd, akd़n aur piiड़aaom kii tiivrtaa bhut adhik mhsoos krtaa hai।
- H1N1 se piiड़it 80% rogiyom ko thmd bhut lgtii hai।
- H1N1 se piiड़it vykti sookhii khmsii, bhtii naak se preshaan rhtaa hai।
- lgbhg 80% H1N1 maamlom mem rogii bukhaar se tptaa rhtaa hai। bukhaar mem shriir kaa taapmaan 101 digrii tk phumch jaataa hai। dvaa khaane ke baad bhii bukhaar kaa lgaataar bdh़taa hai।
- lgaataar sr mem drd honaa H1N1 kaa ek aam lkshण hai tthaa yh lkshण 80% mriijom mem maujood hotaa hai।

Reasons: 
maanaa jaataa hai ki svaain phloo adhiktr sooarom ke kriib rhne vaale logom mem tejii se phailtaa hai। haalmki kii any kaark bhii hai jo svaain phloo ke lie jimmedaar haim lekin inmem se sbse mhtvpoorण kaarण hai sooarom kaa smprk। kuchh any kaark nimn haim: 
svaain phloo ke kaarण (Causes of Swine Flu)
- smkrmit sooarom ke saath rhne vaale vykti svaain phloo kii chpet mem aa skte haim tthaa aage chlkr ve vykti any logom ko smkrmit kr skte haim।
- biimaarii ke hone kaa khtraa bchchom, bujurgom, grbhvtii mhilaaom aur dil, kidnii, daaybitiij se grst logom mem adhik rhtaa hai। jinkii rog-prtirodhk kshmtaa km hotii hai, ve bhii svaain phloo kaa shikaar ho skte haim।
- yhm yh dhyaan rkhne vaalii baat hai ki shii trh se pke hue red miit se svaain phloo nhiim hotaa lekin agr pkaane mem asaavdhaanii brtii jaae to kuchh smsyaaem avshy aa sktii haim।

Treatments:
svaain se bchaav kaa sbse behtriin triikaa hai isse bchkr rhnaa। smkrmit rogii se door rhkr is biimaarii se aasaanii se bchaa jaa sktaa hai। kuch any upaay nimn haim:
- smkrmit logom se door rhnaa hii is biimaarii kaa bchaav hai। 
- saaph-sphaaii kaa dhyaan rkhnaa behd jroorii hai। 
- khmste yaa chhiimkte smy rumaal kaa pryog krem। 
- gmde haathom se mkh, naak yaa mumh chhoone se bchem aur baahr khaane se prhej krem। 
- biimaar logom se nj़diikii smprk rkhne se bchem
- asptaal yaa any kisii saarvjnik sthaan pr jaane se phle maask phnem। 
- smkrmit vykti ke paas jaanaa agr jroorii ho to maask ke saath-saath dstaane bhii phnem। isse aap biimaarii se surkshit rh skte haim।
- svaain phloo se bchne ke lie bhaart mem svaain phloo vaiksiin maujood hai। svaain phloo kii vaiksiin ek saal tk is biimaarii se aapkii rkshaa krtii hai।
- svaain phloo ke lkshण nज़r aane pr mriij ko turnt asptaal mem bhrtii kraa dem taaki uskaa shii ilaaj ho ske।
- ydi aap inफ़luenज़aa se piiड़it hom to aap any logom ko smkrmण se bchaane ke lie unse door rhem।

Home Remedies:
svaain phloo ne phle maiksiko mem apnaa pmv psaaraa, uske baad poore amerikaa aur bhaartiiy up mhaadviip mem phailte hue mhaamaarii kaa rup le liyaa। mgrejii mem ek khaavt hai n – “Prevention is better than cure”। svaain phloo mem bhii bchaav hii ek maatr ilaaj hai। svaain phloo kaa vaayrs siidhe shvaas nlii pr aakrmण krtaa hai aur yh khtrnaak rup se smkraamk ho jaataa hai।
khaas kr H1N1 vaairs jo ki jaanlevaa bhii hai aur kaaphii smkraamk bhii। yh bchche, jvaan aur boodh़e kisii pr bhii ataik kr sktaa hai aur kaaphii tejii se phailtaa hai। mausmii srdii-kph aur khmsii mem chhiimkne-khmsne ke dauraan iske vaayrs hvaa mem tairne lgte haim। iske vaayrs drvaaje, simk, khid़kii, kpd़e, roomaal, tauliyaa yaa khiim pr bhii ho skte haim। iske smprk mem aate hii koii bhii smkrmण kaa shikaar ho sktaa hai।
jrurii nhiim hai ki H1N1 vaayrs ke smkrmण ke turmt baad koii biimaar pd़ jaae। saat din ke baad bhii iske lkshण dikhaaii dete haim aur mriij biimaar pd़ne lgtaa hai। bchchom mem 10 din ke baad bhii lkshण dikhaaii de skte haim। iske lkshण siijnl phloo kii trh hii hote haim, msln- kph, bukhaar, glaa sookhnaa, naak bhnaa, chhiimk aanaa, sirdrd, bdn drd, kmpkmpii ke saath bukhaar aanaa aur bdn mem akd़n honaa।
svaain phloo mem nimoniyaa kaa khtraa rhtaa hai aur shvsn prणaalii naakaam hone kaa dr rhtaa hai joki jaanlevaa hai। svaain phloo pichhle saal bhaart mem mhaamaarii kii trh pmv psaaraa, khaaskr gujraat, raajsthaan mem isse kii logom kii maut bhii huii।
mgr isse ghbraane kii jrurt nhiim hai। agr aap isse bchaav ke lie turmt upaay krnaa shuru kr dete haim to yh utnaa khtrnaak nhiim ho sktaa hai।
svaain phloo ke ilaaj ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Swine Flu - H1N1)
tulsii (Basil)
tulsii mem rog prtirodhii kshmtaa ko mjboot krne kii shkti hotii hai aur kisii bhii trh ke phloo mem yh raambaaण kii trh kaam krtaa hai। yh gle aur phephd़e ko kisii bhii trh ke smkrmण se bchaataa hai। subh khaalii pet 5-10 tulsii ke ptte ko achchhii trh se dho kr chbaa lem। chaay aur kaadh़e mem bhii tulsii kaa sevn kr skte haim।
giloy (Tinospora Cordifolia)
giloy kaa paudhaa aasaanii se hr jgh mil jaataa hai। giloy ke paudhe kaa tnaa kaatkr use achchhii trh se chhote-chhote tukd़e kr lem। giloy ke tnaa ke tukd़e aur pmch-chhh tulsii ke pttom ko paanii mem ubaal lem। ab ismem kaalii mirch, semdhaa nmk yaa kaalaa nmk milaa lem aur ise grmaa-grm kaadh़e kii trh pii lem। yh aapke rog se ld़ne kii kshmtaa ko to mjboot kregaa hii, smkrmण se bhii rkshaa kregaa।
kpoor (Camphor)
svaain phloo se bchaav ke lie kpoor kaaphii kaargr hai। vysk mhiine mem ek baar yaa do baar phloo ke siijn mem iskaa sevn kr sktaa hai। jvaan log to ise paanii ke saath bhii khaa skte haim lekin bchchom ko kele mem kpoor mth kr khaane denaa chaahie। bchche siidhe kpoor nhiim khaa skte। dhyaan rhe kpoor kaa sevn hr roj n krem। phloo ke siijn mem ek yaa do baar hii iskaa sevn kaaphii hai।
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun to vaise bhii hr mrj kii dvaa hai। isse imyoonitii mjboot hotii hai aur smkrmण kaa khtraa km rhtaa hai। roj subh khaalii pet lhsun kii do dlii kchchaa hii paanii ke saath khaaem, kaaphii phaaydaa kregaa।
hldii-doodh (Turmeric with Milk)
hldii mem kii trh ke guण hote haim। drd nivaark ke saath-saath yh kph-khmsii-srdii mem to asr krtaa hii hai, rog prtirodhii kshmtaa ko bhii mjboot krtaa hai। roj raat ko grm doodh mem hldii daal kr piine se phloo aur smkrmण kaa khtraa km rhtaa hai।
saaph-sphaaii (Hygine)
vaayrl smkrmण bhut tejii se phailtaa hai aur vaayrs khiim bhii ho sktaa hai। kisii bhii chiij ko chhoone yaa khiim baahr jaane ke baad turmt paanii aur emtii septik loshn yaa likvid se haath pair dhone ke baad hii kuchh khaanaa-piinaa chaahie। siijnl phloo ke mhiinom mem naak pr maask yaa rumaal lgaa kr baahr niklnaa chaahie।


Disease: skin kaimsr (Skin Cancer)

Description: 
tvchaa kii koshikaaom mem asaamaany vृddhi ko skin kaimsr (Skin Cancer) khte haim jo praay: shriir ke us mg kii tvchaa mem hotaa hai jhm soory kii kirणem siidhe pd़tii hai। jaise chehraa, homth, grdn, bmh, haath aur mhilaaom kii pair kii tvchaa pr।

Symptoms: 
- ekjimaa yaanii khaaj bhii lmbe smy tk rhe। khaastaur pr agr yh kohnii, hthelii yaa ghutnom pr dikhe to ise lekr laaprvaahii n brtem।
- til mem bdlaav ho, rmg bdlne lge aur is pr khujlii ho yaa phir khoon nikle
- maathaa, gaal, thuddii aur mkhom ke aas-paas kii tvchaa laal ho aur usmem khoob jln ho
- raishej, til yaa brth maarks ke aakaar yaa rmg mem bdlaav
- skin pr dhbbe agr chhh hphtom se jyaadaa rhem
- skin rojeshiyaa yaani bhut adhik laalii aur jln

Reasons: 
skin kaimsr kaa kaarण (Causes of Skin Cancer)
dhoop mem jyaadaa rhne se hotaa hai skin kaimsr (Effects of Sunrays)
jyaadaatr maamlom mem skin kaimsr soory kii praabaimgnii kirणom ke smprk mem aane se hotaa hai kyomki soory kii praabaimgnii kirणem skin sel ke diiene ko kaaphii nuksaan phumchaataa hai jisse tvchaa kii koshikaa asaamaany rup se vibhaajit hone lgtii hai।
snbrn aur tainimg (Sunburn)
soory kii altraavaaylet kirणom mem jyaadaa der tk rhne pr snbrn aur tainimg kaa khtraa rhtaa hai। skin pr tainimg hone se skin sel ke diiene ko kaaphii nuksaan phumchtaa hai, jisse skin kaimsr hone kii smbhaavnaa bdh़ jaatii hai।

Treatments:
skin kaimsr kaa ilaaj (Treatment of Skin Cancer)
- kushthrog
- soraaysis
- aphaaraa

Home Remedies:
jb tvchaa ke sels ebnॉrml triike se bढ़naa shuroo kr dete haim to tvchaa kaa kaimsr hotaa hai। skin kaimsr kaa bड़aa kaarण aapke dvaaraa pryukt kie jaa rhe saumdry utpaad, khaaskr smskriin, ho skte haim। smskriin (sn kriim) mem dhoop se bchne ke lie kii tॉksik kemiikl bhre hote haim jo tvchaa ko jroorii vitaamin dii bhii nhiim lene dete।
kii baar nyootriishnl dephishiyemsii (Nutritional Defficiency) bhii tvchaa ke kaimsr kaa kaarण hotii hai। tvchaa ke kaimsr se kii ghreloo nuskh़om ko aajmaakr bchaav smbhv hai।
tvchaa ke kaimsr se bchaav ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Skin Cancer)
kaalii rspberii ke biijom kaa tel (Black Raspberry Seed Oil)
rspberii ke biij emtiiऑksiidemt guणom se bhrpoor hote haim, jisse inmem kaimsr se bchaav kii taakt hotii hai। kaalii rspberii n kevl kaimsr ko roktii hai blki yh siidhe taur pr kaimsr paidaa krne vaalii jड़ pr prbhaav daaltii hai। saath hii kaimsr se lड़ne ke lie vykti kii imyoonitii (immunity) bhii bढ़aatii hai।
hldii (Turmeric)
hldii mem maujood krkyoomin (Curcumin) ttv kaimsr ke sels ko maarne mem prbhaavii hai saath hii kaimsr ko hone se bhii roktaa hai। khaaskr brest kaimsr, pet kaa kaimsr aur tvchaa kaimsr mem hldii adhik prbhaavii hai।
kuchh chiijom ko avॉid kre (Necessary Precautions)
tvchaa kaimsr se prbhaavit hone pr kisii bhii aise khaane se bchnaa chaahie jo shriir mem inphlemeshn ko bढ़aae, kyomki kaimsr esidik aur tॉksik maahaul mem jyaadaa phailtaa hai। aise mem jyaadaa tle aur msaale vaale khaane se door rhem। saath hii phaast phood, aartiphishiyl shugr, kॉrn siirp, aisaa khaanaa jismem jyaadaa phaitii esid ho, miit aur trms phait aadi vaale khaane se bchnaa chaahie।
vitaamin dii (Vitamin D)
kaimsr se bchaav ke lie vitaamin dii behd jroorii hai। iske lie kuchh der dhoop mem baithem। dhoop mem baithnaa smbhv n ho to, vitaamin dii 3 spliimemt ke roop mem liyaa jaa sktaa hai। vitaamin dii se shriir kii imyoonitii paavr bढ़tii hai aur shriir kaimsr se lड़ne ke lie shktishaalii bntaa hai।
baimgnii baimgn
kaimsr se bchaav mem baimgn bhii behd laabhprd hai। itnaa hii nhiim solaanaase (Solanaceae) privaar kii any sbjiym jaise- tmaatr, aaloo, shimlaa mirch, aadi bhii kaimsr se bchaav mem utnii hii prbhaavii haim। baimgn mem maujood solaasodaain raahmnosaail glaaikosaaid (Solasodine Rhamnosyl Glycosides) kaa pryog to aayurved mem bhii tvchaa ke kaimsr kii kriim bnaane mem kiyaa jaataa hai।


Disease: mumhaase (Pimples)

Description: 
tvchaa ke rom koop yaani chhidr aur tailiiy grmthi ke bmd hone kii vjh se chehre pr pimpls (Pimples) niklte haim। inhem muhmse bhii khte haim। yh koii biimaarii nhiim hai। aam taur pr yuvaavsthaa mem ld़ke-ld़kiyom ke chehre pr pimpls jyaadaa niklte haim kyomki isii umr mem shriir mem haarmonl bdlaav hote haim।

Reasons: 
groth iyrs mem aksr muhmse ho jaate haim lekin agr muhmse adhik ho to yh chimtaa kaa vishy hotaa hai। muhmso (Muhanse) kii smsyaa nimn vjhom ke kaarण bhii ho sktii hai: ​
- kishoraayu ke ld़ke-ld़kiyom mem seks haarmon emdrojen ke sraav kii gti tej hone se। 
- jyaadaa maatraa mem jmk phood aur tel mem phraaii kiyaa huaa bhojn khaane se। 
- aanuvmshik kaarणom se bhii chehre pr pimpls niklte haim। 
- kॉsmetiks kaa chehre pr jyaadaa istemaal। kॉsmetiks lgaane ke baad kliimjimg nhiim krne se bhii chehre pr pimpls (Pimples) nikl aate haim।
- mृt tvchaa koshikaa ke dbaav aur in koshikaaom mem baiktiiriyaa tejii se bdh़ne ke kaarण pimpls nikl aate haim। 
- pimpls kii doosrii bd़ii vjh jiivnshailii aur phood haibit bhii hai। jyaadaa vsaa yaani tel mem phraaii kiyaa huaa khaanaa khaane, chॉklet ke sevn se chehre pr pimpls niklne kii smbhaavnaa rhtii hai।

Treatments:
pimpls hone pr kyaa n krem (Treatment of Pimples)
- apne chehre ko baar-baar n chhuem
- baalom ko chehre aur maathe pr girne n dem
- mekap se tvchaa ke chhidr bmd ho jaate haim islie mekap se prhej brtem aur tvchaa ko sms lene dem
- pimpls ko kbhii bhii dbaane yaa uske mdr ke ps nikaalne kii koshish n krem, aisaa krne pr gmbhiir ghaav ho skte haim
- chehre ko din mem do baar se jyaadaa n dhoem। chehre ko jyaadaa dhone pr tvchaa kii tailiiy grmthi jyaadaa skriy ho jaatii hai aur tvchaa se tel kaa sraav jyaadaa hone lgtaa hai
pimpls hone pr aise krem upchaar (Tips to remove Pimples)
smtre aur niimboo ke chhilke 
chehre pr saabun lgaane kii bjaay smtre ke chhilke kaa paaudr yaa phir taajaa smtre yaa niimboo ke chhilkom ko lgaaem। isse pimpls kii smsyaa se chhutkaaraa milegaa।
eloveraa joos
pimpls vaalii jgh pr eloveraa kaa joos lgaaem। yh tvchaa ko mulaaym bnaane ke saath-saath pimpls ko bhii km kregaa।
lhsun
lhsun pimpls kii ilaaj mem raambaaण kaa kaam krtaa hai। lhsun ke ek daane ko pimpls vaalii jgh pr dhiire-dhiire lgaaem। agr lhsun n ho to iske pest ko chehre pr lgaaem। aadhaa ghmtaa baad chehraa dho lem। kaaphii phaaydaa hogaa।
kchchaa ppiitaa
kchche ppiite ke joos aur uske chhilke ko kॉtn ke kpd़e mem lpet kr mumhaasom vaalii jgh pr lgaaem। kaaphii asr dikhegaa।
mimt ke ptte aur joos
mimt ke ptte aur iske joos lgaane se bhii mumhaase door hote haim। raat ko sote smy lgaataar do hphte tk ise chehre pr aajmaaem। kaaphii asr dikhegaa।
shhd aur niimboo kaa rs
shhd aur niimboo kaa rs bhii pimpls ke ilaaj mem kaaphii kaargr hai। shhd mem niimboo kaa rs milaa kr pimpls vaalii jgh pr lgaaem। pimpls khtm ho jaaemge।
stiim baath aur aais paik
thod़e gungune paanii mem nhaane ke baad chehre pr dhiire-dhiire brph kii maalish krem। isse tvchaa ke chhidr khulte haim।
 
Home Remedies:
tvchaa mem upsthit tel grmthiyom (oil glands) dvaaraa atirikt siibm (sebum) kaa straav hone ke kaarण mumhaase nikl aate haim। is dauraan tel grmthiym baiktiiriyaa se smkrmit bhii ho jaatii haim jinse mumhaase phoolkr laal ho jaate haim aur kii baar unmem mvaad bhii bhr jaataa hai। mumhaase jyaadtr chehre, kmdhe, grdn aur piith pr niklte haim।
vaise to baajaar mem mumhaasom se niptne ke lie kii trh kii kriim, loshn aur chehre ko dhone (face wash) ke utpaad maujood haim lekin inkaa asr adhik yaa lmbe smy tk nhiim hotaa hai। in utpaadom kaa pryog bmd krte hii smsyaa phir se pnpne lgtii hai।
mumhaasom ke lie kii aise ghreloo nuskhe maujood haim, jo tvchaa ke lie bhii nuksaandaayk nhiim hai saath hii mumhaasom ko jड़ se smaapt kremge। aaie jaante haim kuchh aise hii ghreloo nuskhom ke baare mem-
mumhaasom se niptne ke lie ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Pimples)
brph (Ice)
brph mumhaasom kii soojn aur laalimaa ko jld se jld thiik krne kaa guण rkhtii hai। brph prbhaavit kshetr mem rkt prismchrण (blood circulation) duroost krtii hai jisse tvchaa ke ks jaate haim aur tvchaa pr maujood gmdgii aur tel saaph ho jaataa hai। upchaar ke lie kisii ptle kpड़e mem brph kaa tukड़aa lekr prbhaavit sthaan kii sikaaii krem।
niimboo (Lemon)
niimboo mem maujood vitaamin sii mumhaasom ko jldii sookhne mem mdd krtaa hai। upchaar ke lie rooii ko niimboo ke rs mem bhigokr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem yaa daalchiinii paaudr mem niimboo ke rs kii kuchh boomde milaakr raat mem prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaakr so jaaem। subh gungune paanii se chehraa saaph krem।
toothpest (Toothpaste)
mumhaasom ke ilaaj mem toothpest bhii bhut kaargaar upaay hai। lekin iske lie saadhaarण toothpest kaa hii istemaal krnaa chaahie। jel vaale toothpest kaa istemaal krne se bchem। brph se mumhaasom ko sek kr, prbhaavit sthaan pr aadhe ghmte ke lie toothpest lgaakr chhoड़ dem।
stiim (Steam)
stiim lene se bhii chehre ke mumhaase khtm hote haim। jb chehre pr bhaap lii jaatii hai to rom chhidr khul jaate haim, jisse tvchaa khul kr sms letii hai aur is pr maujood gmdgii aur tel saaph ho jaate haim। itnaa hii nhiim pors mem maujood baiktiiriyaa bhii stiim lene se khtm ho jaate haim।
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun ek emtiiseptik,  emtiiऑksiidemt aur emtiivaayrl ejemt hai। lhsun mem maujood slphr (Sulphar) bhii mumhaasom ko jldii thiik krne ke lie upyogii hai। upchaar ke lie lhsun kii klii ko do tukड़om mem kaatkr mumhsom pr rgड़em aur pmch mint ke lie chhoड़ dem। uske baad chehraa dho lem।
bekimg sodaa (Baking Soda)
bekimg sodaa chehre kaa atirikt tel, gmdgii aur mृt tvchaa koshikaaom ko htaane mem mdd krtaa hai। niimboo ke rs ke saath bekimg paaudr lekr mishrण taiyaar krem। is mishrण ko mumhaasom pr lgaaem aur sookhne tk chhoड़ dem। is mishrण ko lgaane se jln mhsoos ho sktii hai islie ise bhut der tvchaa pr nhiim rkhnaa chaahie।
shhd (Honey)
shhd bhii mumhaasom ko jld se jld thiik krne kaa guण rkhtaa hai saath hii, yh emtiibaayotik dvaaom kaa bhii ek strot hai,  islie ismem baiktiiriyaa ko maarne kii bhii kshmtaa hotii hai। upchaar ke lie rooii mem thoड़aa saa shhd lekr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem aur tkriibn aadhe ghmte ke lie chhoड़ dem। shhd mem daaliichiinii kaa paaudr milaakr bhii lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
khiiraa (Cucumber)
khiiraa mem maujood poteshiym ke kaarण khiiraa lgaane se tvchaa ko thmdk miltii hai। khiiraa mem vitaamin e, ii aur sii bhii maujood hote haim। upchaar ke khiiraa ko piiskr, use chehre pr lep kii trh lgaaem। tkriibn 15 mint baad chehraa dho lem। isse chehre ke pors kii sphaaii hogii saath hii tvchaa ke baiktiiriyaa bhii khtm homge।
ppiitaa (Papaya)
ppiitaa, emtiiऑksiidemt aur vitaamin e kaa uchch strot hai। ppiite mem maujood emjaaim chehre pr maujood mumhaasom kii soojn ko km krke chehre ko chiknaa bnaate haim। upchaar ke lie ppiite ko krsh krke chehre pr phes maask kii trh lgaaem aur tkriibn 15 mint baad chehraa dho dem। iske alaavaa ppiite mem shhd milaakr bhii chehre pr lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
daalchiinii paaudr (Cinnamon Powder)
daalchiinii paaudr bhii mumhaasom ke ilaaj ke lie behd achchhii ghreloo dvaa hai। daalchiinii mem emtiibaiktiiriyl guण hote haim। daalchiinii ko seb ke sirkaa ke saath milaakr mumhaasom pr lgaane se mumhaase thiik hote haim। daalchiinii ke saath shhd milaakr bhii chehre pr lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।


Disease: gmjaapn (Baldness)

Description: 
purushom mem gmjaapn (Baldness) ek aam smsyaa hai। drasl gmjaapn ek pristhiti hai jismem purushom ke sir pr yaa to khiim baal nhiim hote haim yaa phir km baal hote haim। gmjaapn ko chikitskiiy bhaashaa mem elipisiyaa (Alopecia) khte haim।

Symptoms: 
- kmghii krte haim aur baalom kaa guchchhaa aapke haathom mem hotaa hai
- tnaav honaa
- baal aapke kpd़om ke saath bhii chipke hote haim
- baalom kaa girnaa : aamtaur pr hmaare roज़ 20 se 50 baal girte haim। sr mem rusii hone se bhii baal jhड़te haim,  agr isse jyaadaa baal jhड़te hai to rusii bhii kaarण ho sktii hai
- baalom kaa jhड़naa (Baldness)
- baalom mem haath daalte haim, to aapke baal haath mem aa jaate haim

Reasons: 
gmjaapn mukhy taur pr baalom kii jd़om (Hair Follicles) ke avruddh ho jaane yaa bmd ho jaane ke kaarण hotaa hai। purushom mem gmjepn kii shikaayt sbse jyaadaa hotii hai। iskii kii vjhe haim:-
- haarmonl bdlaav
- ejimg
- aanuvmshiktaa
- shriir mem aairn v protiin kii kmii
- vjn kaa tejii se ghtnaa
- jyaadaa maatraa mem vitaamin e kaa sevn
- baalom kii jd़om mem smkrmण
- trॉmaa
- grbhnirodhk goliyom kaa jyaadaa sevn
- dvaaom ke saaid iphekt
- tnaav
- mhilaaom mem prsv ke dauraan
- mhilaaom mem menopॉj ke dauraan
- kaimsr ke ilaaj kiimotherepii ke baad
- taait heyr staail
- thaayraaid kii biimaarii
- baalom mem daay, klr aur keraatin heyr triitmemt se
- daayt mem bdlaav krne se
- lmbii aur gmbhiir biimaarii se
- eniimiyaa hone pr
- enaabolik steroids golii khaane se

Treatments:
gmjaapn ke saamaany upchaar (General Treatments for Baldness)
- baalom ke lie dhii kmdiishnr kaa kaam krtaa hai। yh baalom ke gmjepn ko door krne mem kaaphii kaam krtaa hai।
- pyaaj mem maujood slphr sir mem rkt ke prvaah ko tej krtaa hai। jisse gmjpn kii biimaarii thiik ho sktii hai।
- chukmdr ke pttom ko memhdii ke pttom ke saath graaimdr mem piis kr pest bnaa lem। is pest ko sir pr lgaa gungune paanii se dhone se kaaphii asr dikhegaa।
- gmjepn se ld़ne ke lie niimboo ke rs ko kii trh ke telom mem milaa kr lgaaem aur sir kii maalish krem।
- memthii ke biij ko koot kr pest bnaa lem aur sir mem jhm baal nhiim hai vhm lgaa lem। ek ghmtaa tk pest lgaa huaa chhod़ dem। baad mem sir ko paanii se dho lem। kaaphii asr hogaa।
- raat mem sote smy baalom kii maalish naariyl tel se ds mint tk krem।
- gmjaapn ke ilaaj ke lie ailoveraa jel ko sir mem lgaaem aur achchhii trh se sir kii msaaj krem।
- arhr kii daal ko piis kr pest bnaa lem। is pest ko sir ke prbhaavit kshetr mem lgaaem, jld hii asr dikhne lgegaa।
- gmjepn se bchne ke lie armdii ke tel ko sir mem lgaa kr achchhii trh se msaaj krem।
- baalom kaa jhड़naa

Home Remedies:
baalom ke jhd़ne ko rokne ke lie to hm-aap laakhom jtn krte haim, mgr gmjaapn ko mtim niyti maan kr koii upaay krnaa hii chhod़ dete haim। hm maante haim ki iskaa ek hii upaay hai – heyr traasplmt yaa phir srjrii।
aapko itnii jldii niraash hone kii jrurt nhiim hai। heyr traasplmt yaa phir srjrii mem laakhom rupye khrch krne se behtr hai ki agr aap kuchh ghreloo aur kudrtii nuskhom (Herbal and Home Remedies for Baldness) ko aajmaaemge to smbhv hai registaan mem bhii drkht ug aaem।
aaie jaante haim un kudrtii upaayom ke baare mem jisse gmjaapn ko kaaphii hd tk km kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
1. armdii kaa tel (Castor Oil)
armdii kaa tel gmjaapn ko door krne kaa sbse kaargr dvaa hai। yh ek aadrrk yaani mॉschraaijimg ejemt kii trh kaam krtaa hai। yh baal aur tvchaa kii kii aur smsyaaom mem kaam krtaa hai। gmjepn ko bhgaane ke lie aapko bs aur kuchh nhiim apne hthelii pr thod़aa armdii kaa tel lem aur ise sir mem lgaa kr achchhii trh se msaaj krem। yh aapke baalom kii jd़om ko poshण degaa aur bhut jld aapke sir pr baal ugne lgemge।
2. arhr kii daal (Toor Daal)
gmjepn kii ilaaj ke lie arhr kii daal bhii best hai। arhr kii daal ko piis kr pest bnaa lem। is pest ko sir ke prbhaavit kshetr mem lgaaem, jld hii asr dikhne lgegaa।
3. ailoveraa jel (Aloe Vera Gel)
ailo veraa ek hrbl paudhaa hai aur yh baal aur tvchaa ke lie kaaphii hii prbhaavkaarii dvaa hai। ailo veraa jel baalom ke groth mem kaaphii kaam krtaa hai। gmjaapn ke ilaaj ke lie kuchh nhiim bs ailoveraa jel ko sir mem lgaaem aur achchhii trh se sir kii msaaj krem। jld hii asr dikhne lgegaa। yh baalom kii jd़ mem bmd hue chhidr ko khol detaa hai।
4. naariyl tel (Coconut Oil)
naariyl tel baalom kii jd़om ko poshण detaa hai। raat mem sote smy baalom kii maalish naariyl tel se ds mint tk krem। yh hair follicles ko bdh़ne mem mdd kregaa। subh uth kr baalom ko dho lem। aap naariyl tel mem niimboo kaa rs bhii milaa skte haim।
5. kaalii mirch (Black Pepper)
kaalii mirch gmjaapn ke ilaaj mem kaaphii phaaydemmd hai। kaalii mirch aur niimboo ke biij ko milaa kr koot lem aur phir uskaa gaadh़aa pest bnaa lem। is pest ko baalom kii jd़om pr phailaa kr lgaa lem। kaaphii asr hogaa।
6. memthii ke biij (Methee)
memthii ke biij bhii gmjepn ko door krne mem kaaphii kaargr hote haim। memthii ke biij ko koot kr pest bnaa lem aur sir mem jhm baal nhiim hai vhm lgaa lem। ek ghmtaa tk pest lgaa huaa chhod़ dem। baad mem sir ko paanii se dho lem। kaaphii asr hogaa।
7. niimboo (Lemon)
niimboo bhut saare baalom kii preshaanii mem kaam aataa hai। msln, baalom ke jhd़ne-girne mem, rusii ko khtm krne mem, draaii heyr mem। gmjepn se ld़ne ke lie niimboo ke rs ko kii trh ke telom mem milaa kr lgaaem aur sir kii maalish krem to kaaphii asr dikhegaa।
8. chukmdr ke ptte (Beetroot Leaves)
chukmdr ke ptte gmjepn ko door krne kii achook dvaa hai। chukmdr ke ptte ko paanii mem ubaal lem। jb vh kaaphii mulaaym ho jaae to usmem memhdii ke ptte milaa dem aur phir ise graaimdr mshiin mem piis kr pest bnaa lem। is pest ko sir pr lgaa kr kuchh der ke lie chhod़ dem। baad mem gungune paanii se sir dho lem। kaaphii asr dikhegaa।
9. pyaaj (Onion)
pyaaj mem maujood slphr sir mem rkt ke prvaah ko tej krtaa hai। jisse gmjpn kii biimaarii thiik ho sktii hai। kuchh nhii bs pyaaj ko kaat kr uskaa joos nikaal lem aur usmem kuchh shhd milaa lem। aur phir ise baalom kii jd़om pr lgaa lem। yh baalom kii jd़ mem rkt smchaar ko to bdh़aaegaa hii saath hii phmgs aur baiktiiriyaa ko bhii maaregaa।
10. dhii (Curd)
baalom ke lie dhii kmdiishnr kaa kaam krtaa hai। yh baalom ke gmjepn ko door krne mem kaaphii kaam krtaa hai। baalom ko jhd़ne-girne se bhii roktaa hai। baalom mem dhii kaa maask lgaaem kaaphii behtr ntiije aaemge।


Disease: diihaaidreshn (Dehydration)

Description: 
diihaaidreshn yaani nirjliikrण। mnushy shriir mem paanii ke km ho jaane kii avsthaa ko diihaaidreshn (Dehydration) khte haim। vaijञaanik bhaashaa mem diihaaidreshn ko haaipohaaidraishn (Hypohydration) khte haim। shriir mem paanii kii kmii (Pani ki Kami) ke kaarण shriir se khnij pdaarth jaise ki nmk aur shkkr km ho jaate haim। diihaaidreshn ke dauraan, shriir kii koshikaaom se paanii sookhtaa rhtaa hai jiske kaarण shriir ke kaary krne kaa smtuln asaamaany ho jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- ghbraaht yaa kmpkmpii
- kbj
- chkkr aanaa
- mumh kaa baar baar sookh jaanaa
- sookhii tvchaa
- pyaas naa bujhnaa
- sir mem drd
- sustii
- mmspeshiyom mem aimthn
- kmj़orii

Reasons: 
- shriir mem paanii kii gmbhiir smsyaa kii baar jaanlevaa bhii ho sktii hai।
- shriir se pmch prtisht drv khtm hone pr kmj़orii, pyaas, ubkaaii, chid़chid़aapn hotaa hai।
- shriir se ds prtisht drv khtm hone pr sir drd, chkkr aur mgom mem snsnaaht paidaa ho sktii hai। shriir kii tvchaa niilii pd़ne lgtii hai aur shriir kmj़or ho jaataa hai।
- shriir se pmdrh prtisht drv khtm hone pr dekhne aur sunne kii shkti pr asr pd़taa hai। jiibh mem soojn ho jaatii hai aur khaanaa niglne mem dikkt hotii hai।
- shriir se pmdrh prtisht se jyaadaa drv khtm hone pr imsaan kii mृtyu bhii ho sktii hai।
- dst ke kaarण shriir mem hue diihaaidreshn se mnushy kii mृtyu ke aasaar jyaadaa hote haim। gmbhiir diihaaidreshn (Pani ki Kami) kii vjh se mnushy kaa bren daimej yaani uske mstishk ko haani bhii phumch sktii hai। saath hii haaipovolemik shॉk kaa khtraa bhii rhtaa hai jismem shriir ke kii mgom ko haani phumch sktii hai।
- ydi aapko chkkr aa rhe haim, yaa aap kisii bhii kaary ko krne mem khud ko asmrth paa rhe haim to aise smy mem dॉktr ko dikhaanaa behd aavshyk hotaa hai। do din se jyaadaa kbj yaa bukhaar rhne pr turmt dॉktr se smprk krem।

Treatments:
diihaaidreshn ke upaay (Treatment for Dehydration)
- jitnaa ho ske jyaadaa se jyaadaa paanii piem।
- nvjaat bchchom mem diihaaidreshn ke upchaar (pani ki kami ka ilaj) ke lie bchche ko mm kaa doodh v paanii pilaate rhem। paanii mem oaares kaa ghol milaakr pilaaem।
- jyaadaa bhaagdaud़ vaalaa kaam naa krem aur jitnaa ho ske aaraam krem।
- dhoop mem ghr se baahr naa niklem aur thmdii jgh pr baithe rhem।
- doodh, kॉphii, phroot joos jaise pdaarthom kaa sevn krne se bchem।
- ilektrolaaits se yukt sports drimks kaa sevn avshy krem।

Home Remedies:
aapke shriir kii hr koshikaa thiik dhmg se kaam kre iske lie ऑksiijn (Oxygen) ke saath saath paanii kii bhii aavshyktaa hotii hai। jb shriir mem paanii kii kmii hotii hai to yh sthiti dihaaidreshn yaa nirjliikrण khlaatii hai।
mumh sookhaa lge,  homthom pr ppड़ii jm jaae, thkaan ho, tॉylet km jaanaa ho, chkkr aaem to inhem dihaaidreshn ke praarmbhik lkshण smjhkr, pey pdaarth adhik maatraa mem lenaa shuroo kr denaa chaahie।
dihaaidreshn kii smsyaa ko gmbhiirtaa se n lene pr iske ghaatk priणaam ho skte haim।
aaie aapko btaate haim ki dihaaidreshn kii smsyaa ko ghreloo nuskhom se kis trh thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
dihaaidreshn ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Dehydration)
paanii piine kii maatraa bढ़aaem (Increase Water Intake)
dihaaidreshn se niptne kaa sbse phlaa kdm hai ki paanii kii maatraa bdhaaem। poore din mem tkriibn ds gilaas paanii piinaa bhut jroorii hai। ydi aapko pyaas n bhii lg rhii ho tb bhii paanii jroor piem। saadaa paanii piinaa achchhaa n lg rhaa ho to paanii mem niimboo yaa ilektrॉl aadi daalkr bhii paanii piyaa jaa sktaa hai।
dhii (Yogurt or Curd)
ultii, dst aadi ke kaarण hue dihaaidreshn ke lie dhii ek achchhaa upchaar hai। yh ilektrolaaits (Electrolytes) kaa bhii achchhaa strot hotii hai, islie pet ke lie phaaydemmd hotii hai aur aasaanii se pch bhii jaatii hai। upchaar ke lie dhii ko saadaa yaa dhii mem kaalaa nmk aur bhunaa jiiraa daalkr bhii khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
rsiile phl aur sbjiym (Watery Fruit and Vagetable)
ydi dihaaidreshn kii shurooaat hai to rsiile phl aur sbjiyom ke sevn se bhii aaraam smbhv hai। in phl aur sbjiyom mem trbooj, khrbooj, mgoor, smtraa, strॉberii, khiiraa, kkड़ii, ppiitaa moolii, paalk, torii aur tmaatr aadi haim।
kelaa (Banana)
shriir mem dihaaidreshn kii shikaayt potaishiym jaise khnij kii kmii ke kaarण hotii hai। kele mem potaishiym bhrpoor hotaa hai, aise mem yh shriir kii dihaaidreshn kii smsyaa se niptne kaa aasaan upaay hai। upchaar ke lie din mem do kele khaae jaa skte haim yaa kele kii smoothii bnaakr bhii pii jaa sktii hai।
naariyl paanii (Coconut Water)
naariyl paanii kaa ek gilaas dihaaidreshn se niptne mem kaaphii kaargr hai। naariyl paanii mem uchch ilektrolaaits hote haim jo ki naariyl paanii ko haaidretimg pey bnaate haim। ismem chiinii kii apekshaa kailorii bhii bhut km hotii hai।
chhaachh (Butter Milk)
ydi aap dinbhr dhoop mem kaam krte haim yaa aapko kinhiim kaarणom se adhik psiinaa aataa hai to bhii aapko dihaaidreshn kii smsyaa ho sktii hai। is trh kii smsyaa se niptne ke lie chhaachh ek prbhaavii nuskhaa hai। upchaar ke lie din mem ek se do gilaas chhaachh piem।
soop (Soup)
dihaaidreshn se niptne mem sbjiyom ke soop bhii prbhaavii asr dikhaate haim। iske lie soop mem ajvaayn, moolii aur torii jaisii sbjiym daalkr soop taiyaar krem। din bhr mem km se km ek baar soop jroor piem।
niimboo paanii (Lemon water)
niimboo paanii n sirph shriir ko haaidert rkhtaa hai blki shriir ke tॉksin bhii baahr nikaaltaa hai। niimboo paanii piine se taajgii kaa ehsaas hotaa hai। niimboo paanii bnaane ke lie chiinii kii jgh shhd kaa istemaal krem aur ek chutkii kaalii mirch bhii daalem।
jau kaa paanii (Barley Water)
jau kaa paanii bhii shriir ko haaidret rkhne kaa achchhaa upaay hai। jau ke paanii se dihaaidreshn ke dauraan shriir mem huii poshk ttvom kii kmii kii bhrpaaii hotii hai। yii aasaanii se pch jaataa hai aur shriir ko thmdaa rkhtaa hai। upchaar ke lie 4 kp paanii mem ek kp jau bhigaa dem। uske baad is paanii ko lgbhg 45 mint dhkkr ubaalem। jb achchhii trh ubl jaae to is paanii ko chhaankr gungunaa rhne tk thmdaa krem aur ismem shhd milaakr piem। svaad bढ़aane ke lie niimboo kaa rs bhii milaayaa jaa sktaa hai।


Disease: ghmauriym (Prickly Heat)

Description: 
ghmauriyom ko mgrejii mem priklii hiit (Prickly Heat) khte haim। grmiyom ke mausm mem ghmauriym honaa aam baat hai। grmii ke mausm mem shriir se psiinaa adhik maatraa mem bhtaa hai। ydi smy rhte is psiine ko saaph़ naa kiyaa jaae to yh shriir kii tvchaa mem hii sookh jaataa hai jiske kaarण psiine kii grmthiym bmd ho jaatii haim aur shriir mem ghmaurii hone lgtii haim।

Symptoms: 
- shriir mem khujlii honaa
- shriir mem jln yaa kmte sii chubhn mhsoos honaa
- shriir pr laal-gulaabii, chhote daanom kaa ubhrnaa
- adhik psiinaa aanaa
- kpd़om se chubhn honaa
- thkaavt mhsoos honaa

Reasons: 
ghmaurii ke dauraan shriir mem khujlii, hlkii soojn aur chubhn mhsoos hone lgtii hai। ghmaurii ke daane dhoop ke siidhe smprk mem aane se bdh़ jaate haim। aamtaur pr ghmaurii kuchh dinom mem apne aap shii ho jaatii hai lekin kuchh logom mem yh hphtom aur mhiinom tk ke lie ho sktii hai। islie ek hphte tk ghmaurii ke thiik naa hone pr dॉktr se jroor praamrsh lenaa chaahie। 
ghmaurii (Prickly Heat) ke kaarण logom mem thkaavt (Heat Exhaustion) aur dhoop mem chid़chid़aaht kii shikaayt bhii hotii hai। ghmaurii ke kaarण loo lgnaa kaa khtraa bhii paidaa ho sktaa hai।
ghmauriym bhii kii prkaar kii hotii haim jaise milieriyaa kristlaain (Miliaria Crystallina), milieriyaa roobraa (Miliaria Rubra) aur milieriyaa prॉphmdaa (Miliaria Profunda)। milieriyaa prॉphumdaa mem sbse adhik khtraa rhtaa hai aur ise vaaildphaayr (Wildfire Rash) bhii khte haim।

Treatments:
ghmauriyom se bchaav kaa sbse behtr upaay hotaa hai grmii se bchkr rhnaa। iske alaavaa ghmauriyom (Ghamoriyan) se bchaav ke kuchh ahm upaay nimn haim:
- simthetik phaibrik se bne vstrom ko naa phnem।
- sootii aur dhiile dhaale kpd़e phnem।
- khoob paanii piem aur nhaaem।
- baahr se ghr lautne ke kuchh der baad snaan krem।
- shriir ke hissom ko taaज़aa hvaa lgne dem।
- msaaledaar bhojn se bchem। saadaa bhojn hii khaaem।
- baarish ke paanii se snaan krne se shriir pr niklii phumsiym aur daanem door hote haim।
- rojaanaa subh niim kii chaar-pmch pttiym chbaaem।
- shriir pr multaanii mittii kaa lep lgaaem।
- niim kii pttiyom ko paanii mem ubaalkr is paanii se snaan krem।
- naariyl ke tel mem kpoor milaakr is tel se poore shriir kii maalish krem।
- kailaamaain loshn kaa pryog krem।
- giile shriir pr paaoodr naa lgaaem। jroort se jyaadaa paaoodr kaa pryog krne se bhii bchem।

Home Remedies:
grmiyom mem ghmauriyom kii smsyaa aam hai। jyaadaa psiinaa aane yaa grmii mem rhne pr bड़om, bchchom, yhm tk ki nvjaatom (Infants) mem bhii ghmaurii kii smsyaa ho jaatii hai। ghmaurii hone pr chhote-chhote chubhne vaale daanem piith, grdn tthaa shriir ke any hissom pr nikl aate haim।
kii baar baiktiiriyl imphekshn (Bacterial Infection) aur shriir kaa vjn jyaadaa hone se bhii ghmaurii niklne kii smsyaa hotii rhtii hai। yoom to mausm mem bdlaav hote hii ghmaurii kii smsyaa khud b khud thiik ho jaatii hai lekin kii dphaa smsyaa itnii bढ़ jaatii hai ki mausm mem bdlaav hone tk kaa smy kaatnaa bhii mushkil hotaa hai। aise mem kuchh ghreloo upchaarom se ghmauriyom se nijaat smbhv hai।
ghmauriyom se raaht ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Prickley Heat)
otmiil (Oatmeal)
ghmauriyom se nijaat ke lie otmiil bhut bढ़iyaa nuskhaa hai। otmiil se ghmauriyom mem hone vaalii jln (inflammation), chubhn aur khujlii (itching) se raaht miltii hai। upchaar ke lie thmde paanii se bhre hue tb mem ek kp otmiil daalem। jb tk paanii doodhiyaa rmg ho tb tk imtjaar krem aur is paanii mem tkriibn aadhaa ghmtaa baithem। is upaay ko hr roj do baar krem।
thmdaa upchaar (Cold Compress)
ghmaurii prbhaavit sthaan pr thmdii sikaaii krne se bhii turmt aaraam miltaa hai। brph ke kuchh tukड़om ko kpड़e mem lpetkr prbhaavit sthaan pr sikaaii krem। lgaataar tkriibn 10 mint tk aisaa krem। hr chaar se chhh ghmte pr aisaa krem। isse ghmauriym thiik ho jaaemgii।
chmdn kaa paaudr (Sandalwood Powder)
chmdn ke paaudr kii thmdk bhii ghmauriyom se nijaat dilaane mem prbhaavii hai। upchaar ke lie chmdn ke paaudr mem paanii milaakr, lep bnaaem aur prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। iske alaavaa paaudr kii trh chmdn paaudr ko ghmauriyom pr chhiड़kaa bhii jaa sktaa hai।
bekimg paaudr (Baking Powder)
bekimg paaudr bhii ghmauriyom se raaht dene kaa achchhaa upaay hai। yh mृt tvchaa ko htaakr, gmdgii ko saaph krtaa hai jo ki khujlii aur jln kaa kaarण hote haim। upchaar ke lie ek kp thmde paanii mem ek chmmch bekimg sodaa milaakr usmem ek saaph kpड़aa bhigaakr nichoड़ lem। is kpड़e ko prbhaavit sthaan pr tkriibn 10 mint tk rkhem। ek hphte tk hr roj 5 se 6 baar aisaa krem।
multaanii mittii (Fuller’s Earth)
multaanii mittii bhii ghmaurii se nijaat dilaane kaa ek achchhaa ghreloo nuskhaa hai। multaanii mittii ghmaurii kii jln se nijaat dilaatii hai aur khujlii bhii mitaatii hai। upchaar ke lie 5 chmmch multaanii mittii mem gulaab jl milaakr lep bnaaem aur is lep ko prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। is upaay ko prtidin ek baar krem।
eloveraa (Aloevera)
eloveraa bhii ghmaurii se nijaat ke lie behd achchhaa strot hai। eloveraa ke jaate pttom kaa goodaa lekr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। tkriibn 20 mint lgaa rhne dem aur uske baad dho dem। prtidin do baar aisaa krne se ghmauriym thiik ho jaaemgii।
besn (Gram Flour)
besn shriir kaa tel sokh letaa hai jisse ghmaurii ke daane jldii sookh jaate haim। yh mृt tvchaa ko bhii saaph krtaa hai aur jln se raaht detaa hai। upchaar ke lie besn kii kuchh maatraa mem paanii milaakr lep bnaaem। is lep ko prbhaavit sthaan pr 10 se 15 mint ke lie lgaakr chhoड़ dem। is upaay ko hr roj ek baar krem। ek sptaah mem ghmoriym thiik ho jaaemgii।
kchche aam (Raw Mango)
kchchaa aam shriir kii grmii ko thmdaa krne mem behd prbhaavshaalii haim। aise mem kchche aam kaa pnaa (ek prkaar kaa pey) bnaakr piine se grmii mem raaht miltii hai। pnaa bnaane ke lie kchche aam ko ubaalkr uskaa goodaa alg krem aur thmde paanii mem milaa lem। is paanii mem svaadaanusaar chiinii, kaalaa nmk aur bhunaa jiiraa milaaem। ise hr roj do baar piiem।
khiiraa (Cucumber)
khiire mem shriir ko thmdaa rkhne kaa guण hote haim jo ki ghmaurii se bhii bchaate haim। upchaar ke lie khiire ke ptle-ptle tukड़e kaatkr niimboo mile hue thmde paanii mem kuchh der bhigaakr rkhem। iske baad in tukड़om ko prbhaavit sthaan pr kuchh der rkhem। aisaa krne se bhii ghmauriym jldii thiik ho jaatii haim aur khujlii tthaa jln se bhii raaht miltii hai।


Disease: skrvii (Scurvy)

Description: 
yh rog bhojn mem vitaamin sii (Vitamin C) jise eskorbik esid (Ascorbic acid) bhii khaa jaataa hai, kii kmii se hotaa hai। mnushyom mem kolaajen ke bnne aur aayrn ke avshoshण ke lie vitaamin sii kii aavshyktaa hotii hai jo ki hmem vibhinn phlom aur sbjiyom se milte haim, lekin vitaamin sii kii kmii hone se shriir mem rkt kii bhii kmii ho jaatii hai।

Symptoms: 
- msooड़om mem khoon aanaa
- sookhe aur do mumhem baal
- pairaalaaysis jaisaa mhsoos krnaa
- vjn kaa n bढ़naa
- skin disऑrdr

Reasons: 
skrvii ke kaarण (Reasons of Scurvy)
skrvii kaa phlaa kaarण bhojn mem pryaapt vitaamin sii (Deficiency of Vitamin C) kaa n honaa yaa shriir ko pryaapt vitaamin sii n milnaa hai। iske alaavaa shriir pr pryaapt dhyaan n denaa yaa smpoorण bhojn n krne kii vjh se bhii yh rog ho sktaa hai।
vitaamin sii kii kmii sbse phle smudr ke jriye vyaapaar krne vaale vyaapaariyom mem dekhne ko milaa thaa jo lmbe smy tk ghr se baahr rhte the aur unhem prॉpr khaanaa nhiim mil paataa thaa। vitaamin sii paanii mem ghulnshiil hai yaani shriir n to ise bnaataa hai aur n hii stor krke rkhtaa hai islie behtr svaasthy ke lie smy smy pr iskaa shriir mem phumchnaa jroorii hai। any kaarण jinse skrvii rog ho sktaa hai, nimnlikhit haim-
- bchchom ko gaay kaa doodh thiik trh se ubaalkr n pilaane se bhii skrvii ho sktaa hai। 
- khaane mem phl aur sbjiyom kii prchur maatraa n hone pr vitaamiin sii shriir ko nhiim mil paataa। 
- dhoomrpaan yaa shraab kaa jyaadaa sevn krne pr bhii is rog se khtraa rhtaa hai। 
- grbhvtii hone ke dauraan khaane piine kaa dhyaan n rkhne pr bhii skrvii ho sktaa hai। 

Treatments:
skrvii kaa upchaar (Treatment of Scurvy)
kii jmch kregaa aur rog se smbmdhit kuchh svaal poochhegaa। yh bhut jroorii hai ki dॉktr dvaaraa btaae ge dishaa nirdeshom kaa paaln kiyaa jaae aur btaaii gii dvaaom ko bhii niymit smy pr khaayaa jaae। 
iske upchaar ke dauraan aapke shriir mem vitaamin sii kii maatraa ko nॉrml kiyaa jaataa hai। aapke lie vitaamin sii kii prchur maatraa se smbmdhit jaankaarii dॉktr, aapkii umr, jemdr aur aapke svaasthy ko dhyaan mem rkhkr degaa। isii ke anusaar aapko apnaa daait chaart bnaanaa hogaa।
bhut sii chiijem haim jinkaa dhyaan rkhkr skrvii hone se bchaa jaa sktaa hai yaa skrvii hone ke khtre ko km kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
-dhyaan rhe ki daait mem vitaamin sii kii prchur maatraa ho jismem, berii, khtte rsiile phl jaise niimboo, mausmii, smtraa aadi , hrii mirch, hrii pttedaar sbjiym, trbooj aur khrbooj aadi shaamil hom।
-daait mem kii trh ke paushtik chiijem shaamil honii chaahie, jisse shriir ko smpoorण vitaamin mil skem।
-dhoomrpaan ko chhoड़naa

Home Remedies:
skrvii rog vitaamin sii se juड़aa huaa hai। vitaamin sii (eskorbik esid or Ascorbic Acid) kii kmii hone pr skrvii rog hotaa hai। skrvii rog hone kaa doosraa kaarण hai tmtrikaa mem tnaav yaani ki nrvs temshn।
skrvii rog mem msoodom se khoon aanaa, thkaavt aur shriir mem kmjorii honaa aadi kuchh lkshण njr aate haim। aaie jaante haim kaun se ghreloo nuskhom se skrvii rog se nijaat paaii jaa sktii hai।
skrvii se bchaav ke lie ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Scurvy)
hrii mirch (Green Chillie)
hrii mirch mem vitaamin sii kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। hrii mirch khaanaa skrvii rog se bchne kaa sbse achchhaa upaay hai। skrvii ke lie laal mirch kaa pryog n krem kyomki laal mirch hrii mirch ke smaan prbhaavii nhiim hai।
kiivii (Kiwi)
kiivii mem bhii vitaamin sii kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। kiivii ko slaad ke roop mem istemaal krke vitaamin sii kii bhrpaaii kii jaa sktii hai।
mvlaa (Indian Gooseberry)
mvlaa mem bhii vitaamin sii hotaa hai। mvlaa kii sookhii kaimdii yaa mvlaa kaa rs bhii skrvii rog mem phaaydaa detaa hai। itnaa hii nhiim mvle kaa murbbaa khaanaa bhii skrvii rog ke upchaar mem laabhdaayk hai।
amchoor paaudr (Dry Mango Powder)
kchche aam ko sukhaakr, use piiskr paaudr bnaa lem। yh amchoor paaudr khaane se phle, hr roj ek chhotii chmmch khaaem। yh bhii shriir mem vitaamin sii kii kmii ko pooraa krtaa hai।
strॉberii (Strawberry)
strॉberii vitaamin sii kaa uchch strot hotii hai। strॉberii ko slaad, smoodii aadi kisii bhii roop mem khaanaa skrvii rog mem phaaydaa detaa hai।
smtraa (Orange)
smtraa mem eskॉrbik esid kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। rojaanaa subh smtre kaa ek gilaas joos piem। isse shriir mem vitaamin sii kii kmii to poorii hogii hii saath hii any poshk ttv bhii milemge, jo shriir ko svsth bnaaemge।
niimboo (Lemon)
niimboo mem vitaamin sii adhik maatraa mem hotaa hai। aise mem rojaanaa niimboo kaa paanii piinaa shriir mem vitaamin sii kii kmii ko pooraa krtaa hai। svaad ke lie niimboo ke saath shhd bhii milaayaa jaa sktaa hai, lekin niimboo paanii mem chiinii milaakr n piem।
ppiitaa (Papaya)
skrvii rog ke upchaar mem ppiitaa bhii behd prbhaavii phl hai। ppiitaa roj khaane se bhii shriir mem vitaamin sii kii kmii poorii hotii hai aur skrvii rog se bchaav hotaa hai।
ajvaayn ke phool (Thyme)
skrvii ke upchaar ke lie ajvaayn ke phool bhii behd prbhaavii haim। ajvaayn ke phool mem bhii uchch maatraa mem vitaamin sii maujood hotaa hai। ajvaayn ke phool ko  ghreloo nuskhom ke alaavaa kii aayurvedik dvaaom mem bhii pryog kiyaa jaataa hai।
bel (Wooden Apple)
belphl mem saaitrik esid aur okjelik kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। belphl kaa shrbt bnaakr yaa iskaa goodaa nikaalkr khaane se vitaamin sii kii kmii ko poorii hotii hai, jisse skrvii rog se bchaav hotaa hai।
broklii (Broccli)
lgbhg100 graam broklii mem 89 miliigraam vitaamin sii kii maatraa paaii jaatii hai। aise mem apne khaane mem broklii kaa istemaal bhii vitaamin sii kii kmii ko pooraa krke shriir ko skrvii rog se bchaataa hai।
shimlaa mirch (Bel Pepper)
shimlaa mirch mem bhii vitaamin sii kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। piilii shimlaa mirch mem sbse adhik vitaamin sii paayaa jaataa hai, iske baad krmsh laal aur hrii shimlaa mirch mem।
paarsle (Parsley)
dhniyaa kii trh paarsele mem bhii vitaamin sii kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। skrvii rog se bchaav ke lie paarsele kaa pryog bhii ghreloo upchaar ke saath-saath aayurvedik dvaaom mem kiyaa jaataa hai।


Disease: beriiberii (Beriberi)

Description: 
beriiberii (Beriberi) vitaamin bii 1 kii kmii se hone vaalaa rog hai। ye hmaare shriir ke bhut se hissom jaise mmspeshiym, hृdy aur paachn shkti aadi ko prbhaavit krtaa hai। dkshiण poorv eshiyaa ke ve hisse jhm~ kaa mukhy bhojn chaavl hai, vhm ke log isse kaaphii smkhyaa mem piiड़it haim।

Symptoms: 
- bolne mem tkliiph honaa
- maansik roop se kmphyooj rhnaa
- haath yaa pairom mem sunnpn lgnaa

Reasons: 
berii berii rog ke kaarण (Reasons of Berberi)
beriiberii rog kaa prmukh kaarण to vitaamin bii 1 kii kmii kaa honaa hii hai। jo log prchur maatraa mem vitaaminyukt bhojn krte haim unmem yh biimaarii km hotii hai। 
any kaarण(Other Reason of Beriberi)
- shraab ke kaarण bhii smbhv hai ki aapkaa shriir vitaamin bii 1 ko avshoshit (Absorb) n kr paa rhaa ho। aisii avsthaa mem beriiberii rog ho jaataa hai। - dॉktr maante haim ki jenetik kaarणom se bhii shriir mem vitaamin bii 1 kii kmii ho jaatii hai। 
- grbhvtii mhilaa aur koii bhii aisaa vykti jismem haaiprthaayrodijm (Hyperthyroidism) yaani ki thaayrॉid glaimd ke ovr ektiv vaale vykti ko vitaamin bii 1 kii atirikt maatraa kii jroort hotii hai।
- kuchh biimaariym jaise livr dijiij, shriir mem vitaamin bii 1 ko avshoshit nhiim hone detiim। aise smy mem  bhii beriiberii ke hone kaa khtraa rhtaa hai। 
- kidnii daaylisis bhii beriiberii rog hone kaa risk bढ़aa detii hai।

Treatments:
beriiberii kaa upchaar aur bchaav (Treatment of Beriberi)
beriiberii kaa ilaaj thaayminiin spliimemt (Thiamine Supplement) se kiyaa jaataa hai। jismem chikitsk bld test krvaataa hai jisse yh ptaa chltaa hai ki shriir vitaamin ko kitnii achchhii trh se avshoshit kr rhaa hai। dॉktr aapko thaayminiin besd khaas trh ke bhojn ko lene ke baare mem bhii dishaa nirdesh degaa jismem aapko anaaj, mdaa, miit, biit, sookhe meve, tmaatr aur smtre kaa joos aadi lene kii slaah dii jaaegii।
chaavl, adhpkaa aur kchchaa miit aadi vitaamin bii 1 ko aapke shriir mem avshoshit n krne ke lie smsyaa bn skte haim। beriiberii rog se bchne ke lie paushtik aur bailems daait lenii chaahie jismem thaayminiin kii uchit maatraa ho।
grbhvtii aur bchchom ko doodh pilaa rhii mmom ko bhii smy-smy pr shriir mem vitaamin kii jm~ch kraate rhnaa chaahie। saath hii aise vykti jo elkohl kaa sevn jyaadaa krte haim unhem bhii smy smy pr vitaamin kii kmii kii jmch krvaate rhnaa chaahie।

Home Remedies:
beriiberii rog vitaamin bii1 kii kmii ke kaarण hotaa hai। vitaamin bii 1 thiamin (thiamine) ke naam se bhii jaanaa jaataa hai jo ki shriir mem maujood kaarbohaaidret (Carbohydrate) ko glookoj (Glucose) mem privrtit krne ke lie behd jroorii hai।
thiamin kii kmii se shriir mem glookoj kii kmii ho jaatii hai jisse shriir mem oorjaa kii kmii hotii hai aur shriir poorii trh kaary nhiim kr paataa n hii shriir kaa vikaas ho paataa hai। beriiberii mem pairom mem sunnpn (Numbness) kii shikaayt ho jaatii hai।
saath hii, jii michlaanaa aur behoshii kii avsthaaem bhii bn jaatii haim। joड़ suchaaroo roop se kaam nhiim krte aur kii dphaa dimaagii kmjorii bhii smbhv hai। beriiberii rog mem kii ghreloo upchaar prbhaavii haim।
aaie jaante haim aisii hii kuchh ghreloo khaady saamgriyom ke baare mem jo beriiberii mem laabhprd haim।
beriiberii se bchaav ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Beriberi)
baadaam (Almond)
baadaam mem aavshyk thiamin hotaa hai jo ki beriiberii rog se bchaav ke lie behd aavshyk hai। aise mem rojaanaa baadaam khaayaa jaanaa ati aavshyk hai। baadaam mem sbhii jroorii minrl aur vitaamin maujood hote haim jo ki shriir ko suchaaroo roop se kaary krne ke lie prerit krte haim। upchaar ke lie rojaanaa raat mem tkriibn 15 baadaam paanii mem bhigaa dem aur subh unhem chhiilkr dhiire dhiire chbaakr khaaem।
soorjmukhii ke biij (Sunflower Seed)
soorjmukhii ke biijom mem seleniym (Selenium), tainin (Tannis) aur omegaa 3 phaitii esid jaise yaugik hote haim, jiske kaarण yh emtiiऑksiidemt guणom se bhii bhrpoor hote haim। soorjmukhii ke in biijom mem vitaamin bii 1, bii 5 aur bii 6 bhii maujood hote haim। soorjmukhii ke biij kaa svaad akhrot jaisaa hotaa hai, islie ise yoom bhii chbaayaa jaa sktaa hai। rojaanaa ek bड़ii chmmch soorjmukhii ke biijom ko chbaanaa chaahie।
phlii yaa biins (Beans)
biins mem behd poshk ttv hote haim। biins mem protiin, kailshiym, khnij aur thiamin bhii hotii hai jo ki hddiyom aur mmspeshiyom ke behtr svaasthy ke lie behd jroorii hai। poore din mem do baar biins kii sbjii jroor khaaem।
aaloo (Potato)
aaloo bhii poshk ttvom se yukt khaady pdaarth hai। ismem phaaitokemiikls (phytochemicals), aayrn (iron), poteshiym (potessium) , tmbaa (copper), vitaamin sii, vitaamin bii 1 aur vitaamin bii 6 kii uchch maatraa hotii hai। jyaadaa laabh ke lie aaloo ko bek krke khaanaa chaahie। beriiberii rog mem rojaanaa do aaloo bhoon (baked) kr jroor khaaem।
braaun raais-bhooraa chaavl (Brown Rice)
braaun raais yoom to griibom kaa khaanaa maanaa jaataa hai। lekin sphed chaavl kii tulnaa mem braaun raais mem khiim adhik poshk ttv hote haim jo shriir ke lie laabhdyk hote haim। braaun raais mem thiamin bhii uchch maatraa mem hotaa hai। beriiberii rog se bchne ke lie rojaanaa do ktore braaun raais khaanaa aavshyk hai।


Disease: irektaail disphmkshn (Erectile Dysfunctions)

Description: 
smbhog ke smy limg mem irekshn athvaa tnaav khtm ho jaane ko irektaail disphmkshn (Erectile Dysfunctions) arthaat stmbhndosh khaa jaataa hai। irektaail disphmkshn ke kii prkaar ho skte haim jaise- kii logom mem seks ke baare mem klpnaa krne bhr se hii irekshn ho jaataa hai, jbki kuchh logom ko yh rtikriyaa ke dauraan bhii bilkul bhii nhiim hotaa।

Reasons: 
irektaail disphmkshn ke kaarण (Causes of Erectile Dysfunctions)
kuchh logom kaa maannaa hai ki irektaail disphmkshn kaa taalluk umr bdh़ne hotaa hai, jbki vaastv mem aisaa nhiim haim। iidii haaiprtemshn, daaybitiij v avsaad aadi ke kaarण bhii hotaa hai। irektaail disphmkshn shaariirik aur maansik kaarणom se bhii ho sktaa hai।
ydi irekshn smbhog ke alaavaa kisii vishesh smy jaise subh sokr uthne pr, peshaab krte smy, hstmaithun ke dauraan yaa seks ke baare mem sochne pr hotaa hai to ye maansik kaarणom kii vjh se ho sktaa hai।
dhyaan rhe ki tnaav ke kaarण shriir mem kii haarmons kaa str bdh़ yaa bigd़ jaataa hai, jinmem edriinliin aur kॉrtisol prmukh haarmon hote haim। inkii vjh se shriir mem kii anchaahe bdlaav hote haim aur nrvs sistm kii kaaryprणaalii bigd़ jaatii hai, jisse imyoon sistm kmjor pd़ne lgtaa hai।
haalmki maatr 10 prtisht maamlom mem hii iidii kaa smbmdh maansik sthiti se hotaa hai, jbki adhiktr maamlom mem yh haarmonl kaarणom yaa phir daaybitiij v bld preshr aadi rogom ke kaarण hotaa hai।
irektaail disphmkshn ke shaariirik kaarण (Physical Causes of Erectile Dysfunctions)
dॉktrom ke anusaar irektaail disphmkshn ke lgbhg 90 prtisht maamlom mem kaarण shaariirik hote haim, baakii 10 prtisht maamlom mem hii iske kaarण maansik hote haim। iske kii any kaarण nimn haim: 
* shraab, smokimg, shugr aur tnaav iske bd़e kraaण hote haim।
* hॉrmomn mem vismgti irektaail disphmkshn kii ek bd़ii vjh hotii hai।
* limg ke skht hone pr usmem rkt kaa bhaav hotaa hai। jb kbhii limg mem rkt ke bhaav mem kmii aatii hai to vh thiik se skht nhiim ho paataa aur irektaail disphmkshn jaisii smsyaaem shuroo ho jaatii haim।
* nyoorॉljii se jud़ii smsyaaem (nrvs sistm mem aaii kisii kmii) bhii irektaail disphmkshn kaa kaarण ho sktii haim।

Treatments:
irektaail disphmkshn kaa upchaar (Treatment of Erectile Dysfunctions)

Home Remedies:
yoom to is smsyaa ke upchaar kii shuruaat khaan-paan mem sudhaar v vyaayaam, dhyaan v yog aadi krne se kii jaatii hai, lekin ydi isse koii laabh njr n aae to iske chikitskiiy upchaar kiye jaate haim। triitmemt dॉktr iidii kaa upchaar krne se phle is smsyaa ke kaarण kaa ptaa lgaataa hai। iske lie kii trh ke test bhii kie jaate haim। aur phir nimn upchaar maadhymom kii mdd lii jaa sktii hai -
hॉrmon therpii (Hormones Therapy)
agr irektaail disphmkshn kaa kaarण hॉrmon kii kmii yaa gd़bd़ii hai to hॉrmon therpii kii mdd se ise do se 2 se 3 mhiinom ke bhiitr ise thiik kr diyaa jaataa hai। is triitmemt kaa koii khaas saaid iphekt bhii nhiim hotaa hai।
bld splaaii (Blood Supply)
limg mem dhmniyom mem kisii prkaar kii rukaavt kii vjh se rkt ke prvaah mem kmii aa jaatii hai, to aiese mem dvaaom kii mdd se is blॉkej ko khtm kiyaa jaataa hai। isse limg mem rkt kaa prvaah bdh़ jaataa hai aur usmem thiik se tnaav aane lgtaa hai।
vaikyoom pmp, imjekshn therpii aur vaaygraa (Vaccum Pump, Injection Therapy and Viagra)
vaikyoom pmp, imjekshn therpii aur vaaygraa jaise ilaaj ke maadhymom kii mdd se bhii irektaail disphmkshn se nijaat paayii jaa sktii hai। haalmki kuchh dॉktrom kaa maannaa hai ki vaikyoom pmp aur imjekshn therpii ab puraane jmaane kii chiijem ho chukii haim।
seks therpii (Sex Therapy)
jaisaa kaa hm baat kr chuke haimki iidii ke kuchh maamlom mem smsyaa shaariirik n hokr maansik hotii hai। aise maamlom mem seks therpii kii mdd se rogii ko seks smbmdhii vistृt jaankaarii dii jaatii hai, jisse vh apne dainik v dmpty jiivn mem sudhaar krke is smsyaa se bch sktaa hai।
bld preshr yaa hृdy smsyaaom se bchaav (Blood Pressure and Heart Problems)
limg ke skht hone kaa mukhy kaarण usmem rkt kaa thiik prkaar se bhaav hotaa hai। lekin jb kbhii bhii limg mem khoon ke bhaav mem kmii aatii hai, to vh poorii trh skht nhiim ho paataa hai aur irektaail disphmkshn kii smsyaa shuroo ho jaatii hai। bld preshr yaa hृdy smbmdhii smsyaaom hone pr yh jyaadaa hotaa hai islie in smsyaaom se bchnaa chaahie।
tnaav se bchem (Avoid Stress)
tnaav ke kaarण bhii irektaail disphmkshn kii smsyaa hotii hai। islie irektaail disphmkshn se bchne ke lie tnaav mukt rhem। yog, dhyaan v eksrsaaij krem aur khaan-paan mem sudhaar laaem।


Disease: shiighrptn yaa priimech‍yor ijaikuleshn (Premature Ejaculation)

Description: 
priimech‍yor ijaikuleshn (Premature Ejaculation) arthaat shiighrptn purushom ko hone vaalii ek prkaar kii yaun smsyaa hai। is smsyaa mem seks ke dauraan chrm yaa kaamotaap (Orgasm) se poorv hii viiry skhlit (Ejaculate) ho jaataa hai। shiighr ptn kaa seks laaiph pr nkaaraatmk prbhaav pd़taa hai। kyaa hai shiighrptn (Details of Premature Ejaculation in Hindi) achchhe yaumn smbmdhom ke lie jroorii hai ki donom hii paartnr smtusht ho paaem aur chrm ko praapt krem, lekin shiighr ptn (Sighra Patan) kii smsyaa ke chlte purush smy se phle hii skhlit ho jaataa hai aur mhilaa saathii ko yaun smtushti nhiim mil paatii। medikl saaims kii bhaashaa mem khaa jaae to, imtrkors aarmbh hone ke 60 sekmd ke mdr hii agr puroosh kaa viiry-skhlit ho jaae to ise shiighrptn (Premature Ejaculation) khaa jaataa hai। 

Reasons: 
shiighrptn yaa priimech‍yor ijaikuleshn shiighrptn ke kaarण (Causes of Premature Ejaculation)
shiighrptn ke kii kaarण jaise- glt triike se hstmaithun, tnaav yaa chimtaa, mstishkiiy rsaaynom kaa asumtln yaa khraab khaan-paan v jiivnshailii aadi ho skte haim। haalmki shiighrptn (Shighrapatan ) kaa ilaaj smbhv hai, kuchh baatom kaa dhyaan rkhkr shiighrptn kii smsyaa se nijaat paaii jaa sktii hai aur dmpty jiivn ko dobaaraa khushhaal bnaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
shiighrptn ke kii any kaarण ho skte haim jaise - bdh़tii umr tthaa pros‍tet kii sms‍yaa aadi। saath hii dr, asurkshaa, chhupkr seks, shaariirik v maansik preshaanii bhii is smsyaa kaa ek kaarण ho sktii hai। iske kaarणom kii shii jaankaarii honaa jroorii hotaa hai।
shiighrptn ke jokhim (Risks of Premature Ejaculation)
shiighrptn kaa rogii s‍vbhaav mem chid़chid़aa ho jaataa hai, use sirdrd v tnaav jaisii shaa‍riirik sms‍yaaem bhii ho sktii haim। kii baar dekhaa jaataa hai ki shiighrptn se grsit vykti kii kuchh smy ke baad seks mem aroochi bhii hone lgtii hai v shaariirik durbltaa bhii ho sktii hai।
shiighrptn kaa ilaaj smy pr n kie jaane athvaa iskaa thiik prkaar se ilaaj n kie jaane pr rog gmbhiir roop le sktaa hai।
shiighrptn (Premature Ejaculation ) ke kisii bhii str pr purush apnii skhln kriyaa ko niymtrit nhiim kr paate haim, jis kaarण ve apne utthaan ko bnaane mem asphl (Erectile Dysfunction) rhte haim aur us vkt viiry ko skhlit hone se rok nhiim paate jb viirypaat nhiim krnaa chaahie।

Treatments:
shiighrptn yaa priimech‍yor ijaikuleshn ke upaay (Remedies of Premature Ejaculation in Hindi) shiighrptn ke kaarण, prkaar v str ke aadhaar pr iskaa upchaar bhii alg-alg ho sktaa hai। yog v eksrsaaij, kuchh vitaamin v jd़ii-bootiyom, aadi kii mdd se is smsyaa ko door kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। smsrg ke biich-biich mem oorjaa dene vaale trl, jaise glookoj, joos, doodh, aadi kaa sevn krne se bhii aaraam miltaa hai । shiighrptn kaa desii upchaar (Home Remedies of Premature Ejaculation) kii log maante haim ki shiighrptn (Premature Ejaculation​) ke desii upchaar ke taur pr kaumch ke biij, sphed mooslii aur ashvgmdhaa ke biijom ko braabr maatraa mem mishrii ke saath milaakr baariik choorण bnaa kr ek chmmch choorण subh aur shaam ek kp doodh ke saath lene se shiighrptn aur viiry kii kmii aadi smsyaaem door hotii haim। shhd aur adrk kaa saath sevn krne se bhii shiighrptn (Shighrapatan) kii sms‍yaa door hotii hai। lhsun bhii is smsyaa ko door krne mem shaayk hotaa hai। iske liye din mem kch‍chii lhsun kii chaar kliym chbaaem। iske niymit sevn se pet kii sms‍yaa ke saath-saath shiighrptn kii sms‍yaa bhii door hotii hai। saumph ko bhii praakृtik kaamot‍tejk ke naam se jaanaa jaataa hai। saumph ke sevn se kaamech‍chhaa bdh़tii hai aur shiighrptn kii sms‍yaa bhii door hotii hai। yog v vyaayaam (Exercises for Premature Ejaculation) niymit yog v vyaayaam se bhii is smsyaa ko door kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। iske liye aap kegl v‍yaayaam kr skte haim। iske alaavaa yog mem yog kii ashvinii mudraa kaa abhyaas krem। isse aap seks kaa smy bdh़aa skte haim। vjrolii mudraa se bhii ijaikuleshn ke smy ko bdh़aayaa jaa sktaa hai। agr baar-baar smbhog krte smy skhln saathii aur aap donom kii ichchhaa se phle ho rhaa ho to dॉktr ke saamne khulkr apnii sms‍yaa ko btaaem aur apne paartnr se bhii is baare mem khulkr baat krem। is sms‍yaa kaa upchaar poorii trh se smbhv hai। 


Disease: pilaagraa (Pellagra)

Description: 
pilaagraa vitaamin bii 3 kii kmii se hone vaalii biimaarii hai। yh shriir mem niyaasin yaa traaiiptophn kii kmii yaa lyoosin (Leucine) kii adhik maatraa hone se hotaa hai। yh biimaarii shriir ke protiin metaabolijm ko bhii avyvsthit kr detii hai jis kaarण kii biimaariym hotii haim jaise kaarsiinॉid simdrom (Carcinoid Syndrome)।

Symptoms: 
- baalom kaa girnaa : aamtaur pr hmaare roज़ 20 se 50 baal girte haim। sr mem rusii hone se bhii baal jhड़te haim,  agr isse jyaadaa baal jhड़te hai to rusii bhii kaarण ho sktii hai
- shriir mem laal rmg ke chktte dikhaaii dene lgte haim
- insomniyaa
- maansik roop se kmphyooj rhnaa
- nrv daimej
- dhoop ke prti atismvednshiil honaa
- soojn - mum~h mem chhaale honaa
- kmj़orii

Reasons: 
pilaagraa hone ke kii kaarण haim jinmem se kuchh nimn haim: 
pilaagraa ke kaarण (Causes of Pellagra)
* niyaasin (Niacin) yaani vitaamin B3 kii kmii ke lie jimmedaar haim, phlsvroop adhikmsh paitholॉjii mem enedii (NAD) kaa prodkshn bhii bढ़aa hai।
* doosraa kaarण hai jroorii emino esid yaani traaiiptophn (Tryptophan) kii kmii, jo miit, mchhlii, aणdom aur moomgphlii mem prchur maatraa mem paayaa jaataa hai। ise hmaaraa shriir khud hii niyaasin mem privrtit kr letaa hai।
* tiisraa kaarण hai shriir mem lyusin (Leucine) kii adhiktaa jo ki kvinolinet phosphoribosil trmsphrs (Quinolinate Phosphoribosyl Transferase i.e. QPRT) aur niyaasin ko nikotinaamaaid mononukleotaaid (Nicotinamide Mononucleotide) mem bdl detii hai।
dvaaiyom ke kaarण pilaagraa (Medicine Causing Peelagra)
bhut sii dvaaem bhii pilaagraa (Pellagra) kii vjh bntii haim inme emtiibaayotik bhii shaamil haim। iske saath hii yh bhii smbhv hai ki shriir kinhiim kaarणom se niyaasin ko shriir mem avshoshit nhiim kr paa rhaa ho। aise mem behtr hotaa hai chikitsk se milkr is smbmdh mem praamrsh kiyaa jaae aur dॉktr dvaaraa btaae ge dishaanirdeshom kaa paaln kiyaa jaae।
pilaagraa ke any kaark (Reason of Pellagra)
ydi pilaagraa kaa ilaaj smy pr naa ho to 4 se 5 saalom mem mriij kii maut bhii ho sktii hai। kii kaark aise bhii haim jo pilaagraa ke risk ko bढ़aa skte haim, jaise: 
* jyaadaa shraab piinaa
* enoreksiyaa nrvosaa (Anorexia Nervosa) naamk biimaarii se piiड़it honaa
* paachn smbmdhii biimaarii honaa
* khaane mem traaiiptophn (Tryptophan) kii km maatraa lenaa

Treatments:
dॉktrom ke anusaar agr saamaany khaan-paan pr agr dhyaan diyaa jaae to bhii pilaagraa se bchaa bchaa jaa sktaa hai। pilaagraa ke risk ko km krne ke lie nimn baatom kaa khyaal rkhaa jaa sktaa hai: 
pilaagraa se bchaav (Treatment of Pellagra)
* khaane mem niyaasin (niacin) yaani vitaamin bii3 kii maatraa bढ़aane se pilaagraa se bchaa jaa sktaa hai।
* laal miit, mchhlii, pॉltrii, phortiphaaid bred, daal aur moomgphlii aadi mem niyaasin kii bhrpoor maatraa hotii hai।
* ydi aap vitaamin vitaamin bii3 kii km maatraa khaate haim yaa kisii biimaarii ke kaarण aapkaa shriir niyaasin avshoshit nhiim kr paataa hai to turmt chikitsk se milem। iske lie aap niyaasin spliimemt yaa mltiivitaamin yaa minrl spliimemt bhii le skte haim।
in splimemt mem km se km 20 miliigraam niyaasin honaa chaahiye। yoom~ bhii hr roj ek purush ko 16 miliigraam aur mhilaa ko 14 miliigraam niyaasin kii jroort hotii hai।
* tृaayptophn se bhrpoor bhojn niyaasin ke bnne mem bड़aa rol adaa krtaa hai| iske lie aap smudrii khaanaa, miit, mdaa, hrii pttedaar sbjiym aadi khaa skte haim। iske alaavaa daalem, mchhlii, doodh aur yiist ko bhii apne bhojn mem shaamil kr skte haim।
* elkohl kaa istemaal n krem aur ek heldii daait plaan (Healthy Diet Plan) bnaaem।


Disease: rikets (Rickets)

Description: 
sookhaa rog yaani rikets (Rickets), vitaamin dii kii kmii se hotaa hai। yh bchchom mem hone vaalaa rog hai jismem bchchom kii hddiym mulaaym ho jaatii haim। kii baar hddiym itnii kmjor ho jaatii haim ki saadhaarण dbaav se bhii toot jaatii haim। isii kaarण bchchom ke pair teढ़e aur spaain asaamaany hokr muड़ jaatii hai। is prkaar ke rog ko bड़om mem asthi-mृdutaa (Osteomalacia) khaa jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- hddiyom mem drd

Reasons: 
rikets biimaarii kaa ek mukhy kaarn vitaamin dii kii kmii (Deficiency of Vitamin D) hai। aahaarnlii se kailshiym aur phaasphors ke shoshण mem shaaytaa ke lie vitaamin dii jroorii hotaa hai। bchchom kii hddiyom mem mjbootii ke lie bhii kailshiym aur phaasphors kii jroort hotii hai, aise mem jb shriir ke rkt mem kailshiym aur phaasphors kii kmii mhsoos hotii hai to rkt iskii poorti hddiyom se krtaa hai aur apnaa smtuln bnaataa hai। ntiijtn hddiym mulaaym aur hddiyom kii smrchnaa kmjor ho jaatii hai।
rikets ke kaarण (Causes of Rickets in Hindi)
soorj kii roshnii naa milnaa (Sun Light)- sn laait vitaamin dii kaa prmukh strot hai। lekin aajkl ke maahaul mem bchche ghr ke baahr khelnaa psmd nhiim krte। maataa pitaa bhii bchche ko imdor ektivitii mem lgaanaa hii psmd krte haim। aise mem bchchom ko soorj kii roshnii se pryaapt vitaamin dii nhii mil paataa।
khaanaa (Food)- bchchom ko paushtik khaan paan naa mil paane ke kaarण bhii vitaamin dii kii kmii jhelnii pड़tii hai। mchhlii kaa tel, mde kii jrdii aur doodh aadi mem bhii vitaamin dii pryaapt maatraa mem hotaa hai। agr bchchem kii daait plaan mem yh chiijem naa hom to use rikets (Rickets) kaa khtraa ho sktaa hai। 

Treatments:
rikets (Rickets) ke kaarण naa sirph shaariirik durbltaa aatii hai blki kii baar is rog ke kaarण bchchom mem apmgtaa bhii dekhne ko miltii hai। is biimaarii se bchne ke lie kuchh aasaan upaay nimn haim: 
rikets se bchne ke upaay (Treatment of Rickets in Hindi)
* bchchom ko pryaapt maatraa mem vitaamin dii kaa sevn kraaem। 
* kuchh der dhoop mem rhnaa bhii jroorii hai isliye bchchom ko bhii sn baath dem।
* khaane piine pr bhii vishesh dhyaan dem। vitaamin splimemt lie jaa skte hai saath hii mde kii jrdii, mchhlii aue doodh kaa prchur maatraa mem sevn krem।
* iske saath hii chikitsk se bhii praamrsh lem। chikitsk bchche kii hddiyom ko dbaakr unkii nkaaraatmktaa ko dekhte haim।
* sookhaa rog kii pristhiti ko eks re dvaaraa bhii jaanaa jaa sktaa hai। saath hii yoorin aur rkt kii jmch dvaaraa bhii biimaarii aur usmem ho rhe sudhaar kaa ptaa lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।

 
Disease: ghemghaa (Goiter)

Description: 
ghemghaa yaani goitr (Goiter) rog thॉyraaid glaimd ke asaamaany triike se bढ़ne ke kaarण hotaa hai। ghemghaa rog asthaaii bhii ho sktaa hai jo ki smy ke saath khud hii thiik ho jaataa hai lekin kuchh kaarणom mem yh gmbhiir hotaa hai jise chikitskiiy slaah kii jroort hotii hai aur ise andekhaa nhiim kiyaa jaa sktaa।

Symptoms: 
- kphj ghemghaa hone pr jhm paidaa hotaa hai us sthaan kii khaal ke rmg jaisaa hii hotaa hai।
- kphj ghemghaa hone pr bhaarii, thoड़e drd vaalaa, chhoone mem thmdaa, aakaar mem bड़aa tthaa jyaadaa khujlii vaalaa hotaa hai।
- medj ghemghaa hone pr khujlii vaalaa, bdboodaar, piile rmg kii, chhoone mem mulaaym tthaa binaa drd kaa hotaa hai।
- medj ghemghaa hone pr rogii kaa mumh tel kii trh chiknaa hotaa hai tthaa uske gle se hr smy ghurr-ghurr jaisii aavaaj nikltii rhtii hai।
- vaatj ghemghaa hone pr grdn mem soojn aur suii ke chubhne jaisaa drd
- vaatj ghemghaa hone pr glaa aur taalu sookhaa rhtaa hai

Reasons: 
ghemghaa bhut adhik haaiprthaairॉdijm (hyperthyroidism) haarmon ke straavit hone yaa haaipothaairodijm (hypothyroidism) ke bhut km straavit hone yaa ekdm saamaany hone pr bhii ho sktaa hai। ghemghaa rog hone kaa mtlb hai ki thॉyraaid glaimd ebnॉrml triike se bढ़ rhii hai। ghemghaa rog ke vishy mem any mhtvpoorण jaankaarii nimn hai: 
ghemghaa ke vishy mem jaankaarii (Information of Goiters in Hindi)
* khaane mem aayodiin kii kmii se bhii ghemghaa rog hotaa hai।
* ghemghaa rog mem doodh se bne huii pdaarth, iikh ke pdaarth, khttii-miithii chiijem, bhaarii tthaa der mem pchne vaalii chiijem, jyaadaa miithii khaane vaalii chiijem, motaapaa bढ़aane vaalaa bhojn aur jyaadaa rs vaale pdaarth haanikaark haim। aisii chiijem ghemghaa ko bढ़aane kaa kaam krtii haim। 
* ghemghaa rog mem puraanaa laal chaavl khaane se, puraanaa ghii, moomg, prvl, krelaa, tthaa pushtikaark (shkti dene vaalaa) aur jldii pchne vaalaa bhojn krne se laabh miltaa hai। saath hii aayodin kii shii maatraa bhii khaane mem lenaa aavshyk hai। 

Treatments:
ghemghaa rog kaa ilaaj behd aasaan hai। lekin iskii jaankaarii honaa bhii aavshyk hai। ghemghaa rog mem kuchh jroorii aur asrdaar upaay nimn haim:
ghemghaa kaa upchaar (Treatment of Goiter in Hindi)
1. nmk- khaane mem hmeshaa aayodiin vaalaa nmk khaane se ghemghaa rog mem bhut laabh miltaa hai।
2. krjnii- goomjaa yaa krjnii kii jड़ aur biij se nikaalaa huaa tel lgaane se aur naak mem daalne se glgrmthi aur gle kii gmth mem laabh hotaa hai।
3. apraajitaa- sphed apraajitaa kii jड़ ke ek se do graam choorण ko ghii mem mishrit kr piine se athvaa ktu phl ke choorण ko gle ke andr ghrshण krne se ghemghaa rog shmt hotaa hai।
4. piipl- piipl aur thoohr kaa lep krne se medj ghemghaa (motaape kii vjh se gle kii gmthe) thiik ho jaatii haim।
5. devdaaroo- devdaaroo aur indraayण ko ek saath piiskr lep krne se kphj ghemghaa thiik ho jaatii hai।
6. armdii- armdii kii jड़ ko piiskr chaavl ke paanii mem milaakr subh-shaam lep krne se ghemghaa rog thiik ho jaataa hai।
7. smudrphl- smudrphl, shjn ke biij aur dshmool kii saarii aushdhiyom ko sil pr piiskr hlkaa-hlkaa grm lep krne se vaatj glgmd yaani ghemghaa (gais kii vjh se gle kii gmthe) rog thiik ho jaataa hai।
8. amltaas- amltaas kii jड़ ko baariik piiskr paanii mem milaakr glgmd (ghemghaa) tthaa gmdmaalaa (gle kii gmthe) pr lep krne se donom rog thiik ho jaate haim।
9. laukii- laukii ke pke hue phl mem paanii bhrkr ek sptaah tk rkhe rhne dem। uske baad piine se ghemghaa rog smaapt ho jaataa hai।
10. laal armdii- laal armdii kii jड़ ko piiskr chaavlom ke paanii mem milaakr lep krne se ghemghaa rog thiik ho jaataa hai।
11. soorjmukhii- soorjmukhii kii jड़ aur lhsun donom ko piiskr, tikiyaa bnaakr gle pr bmdhne se ghemghaa phoot jaataa hai aur bhkr saaph ho jaataa hai mgr isse drd bhut hotaa hai।


Disease: motaapaa (Obesity)

Description: 
shriir ke mdr asaamaany roop se jmaa vsaa hii obesitii (Obesity) hai। saamaanytaur pr vykti kii lmbaaii ke anupaat mem ydi shaariirik vjn jyaadaa ho to use motaapaa (Motapa) maanaa jaataa hai lekin obes logom ke shriir pr phait mote logom kii tulnaa mem khiim adhik hotaa hai, jo n kevl shriir ko bedaul bnaataa hai blki kii trh kii any shaariirik smsyaaom kaa kaarण bhii bntaa hai।

Reasons: 
bhut se aise kaarण hote haim jo ki prtyksh (directly) yaa aprtyksh (indirectly) roop se obesitii kii vjh hote haim। vyvhaar yaa rhn-shn, aas-paas kaa maahaul aur kii dphaa jenetik kaarणom se vykti obes ho sktaa hai। 
motaape ke kaarण (Causes of Obesity)
rhn-shn (Lifestyle)
aaj kii tej rphtaar jimdgii mem log aasaanii se asvsth laaiph staail ko apnaa lete haim। n khaan-paan pr hii dhyaan de paate haim aur n hii shaariirik mehnt hii koii rh gii hai, aise mem motaapaa aasaanii se logom ko apnii chpet mem le letaa hai।
logom ke khaane mem phaast phood bढ़aa hai jo ki jyaadaatr maidaa aur trh trh ke riphaainrii telom se bnaa hotaa hai, is trh log jyaadaa kailorii kmjyoom krte haim lekin iske ult shaariirik mehnt utnii nhii rh gii hai jiske kaarण bhii shriir mem vsaa jmaa hone lgtii hai aur vykti obes ho jaataa hai।
vaataavrण yaa maahaul (Environment)
maahaul yaa aasaapaas ke vaataavrण kaa bhii shriir ke svaasthy pr bhut prbhaav pड़taa hai। ab phle kii trh siiढ़iym chढ़naa, utrnaa, paidl chlnaa aadi nhiim rh gyaa। ab log chhotii se chhotii doorii bhii kaar aur baaik se ty krnaa chaahte haim। ek phlor chढ़ne ke lie bhii lipht kaa istemaal krte haim।
iske alaavaa taajaa khaanaa khaane kii prmpraa bhii km hotii jaa rhii hai। dibbaa bmd khaanaa yaa phrij mem rkhaa huaa khaanaa, khaane kii aadtem bhii shriir pr achchhaa prbhaav nhiim daaltiim।
jenetik kaarण (Genetic Reason)
vijञaan khtaa hai ki kuchh jenetik kaarण bhii motaape kii vjh hote haim। jiims mem kii trh ke disऑrdr (disorder) bhii obesitii ko jnm dete haim। iske alaavaa ydi maataa-pitaa obes haim to smbhv hai ki bchche bhii obes ho jaaem। aise mem shuroo se hii bchchom ke svaasthy ke prti strktaa brtnii chaahie।
khaane piine kii aadtem (Eating and Drinking Habit)
aapkii khaane piine kii aadtem bhii aapke shriir ko motaa bnaa sktii haim। ek baar mem bhut saaraa khaanaa yaa bilkul n khaanaa, donom hii pristhitiym shriir ke lie thiik nhiim। kii log motaape se bchne ke lie subh kaa naashtaa nhiim krte, jbki aisaa krne se motaapaa aur bhii bढ़taa hai।

Treatments:
kuchh logom ko khaane kaa koii smy nirdhaarit nhiim hotaa। asmy khaane-piine kii aadtem bhii motaape ko bढ़aatii haim। smy se khaanaa aur ek saath khaane kii jgh chhote porshn mem kii baar khaanaa shriir ke lie jyaadaa behtr hotaa hai।
- khaane mem phl (fruit) aur sbjiym (vagetables) jyaadaa lem।
- ek saath jyaadaa khaane kii jgh chhote chhote miil bnaakr khaaem। 
- sechureted phait, trms phet aur aur riphaaimd shugr se door rhem।
- jo bhii khaaem uskii kailorii ko notis krem। 
- rojaanaa vyaayaam (exercise) jroor krem, jॉgimg aur rnimg ko iskaa hissaa bnaaem। 
- tairaakii (swimming) bhii motaape se bchne kaa achchhaa upaay hai। 
- rssii koodem (skip rope)। 

Home Remedies:
motaapaa (Obesity) n kevl aapkii prsnelitii ko bigaaड़taa hai blki kii rogom ko bhii nyotaa detaa hai। aaj kii phaast jimdgii mem adhikmsh log motaape se preshaan haim। motaape ke kaarण hii bld preshr, hृdy smbmdhii biimaariym, tnaav aur aisii hii any smsyaaem shriir ko gher letii haim, ntiijaa aap smy se phle hii booढ़e bhii njr aane lgte haim।
kii log to motaape se itne preshaan hote haim ki unmem aatmvishvaas khtm ho jaataa hai। lekin chimtaa kii koii baat nhiim, kuchh ghreloo nuskh़e aise haim, jinhem apnaakr aap khud ko slim trim bnaa skte haim।
haalmki koii bhii upaay raatom-raat aapko dublaa nhiim kr sktaa, islie smym rkhem aur btaae ge nuskhom ko apnaaem। isse aap do se tiin mhiinom mem hii apnaa vjn km kr skte haim।
motaapaa yaa vjn km krne ke ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Obesity)

ber kii pttii (Indian Plum Leaves)

seb kaa sirkaa (Apple Cider Vinegar)
seb kaa sirkaa bhii vjn ghtaane mem asrkaark hai। niimboo kii trh seb ke sirkaa mem bhii pektin phaaibr hotaa hai jo ki pet ko lmbe smy tk bhraa rkhtaa hai aur vsaa ko jmne nhiim detaa। upchaar ke lie ek botl paanii me ek chhotii chmmch seb kaa sirkaa aur ek chhotii chmmch niimboo kaa rs milaaem। is paanii ko rojaanaa piem। kuchh hii smy mem vjn km hone lgegaa।
grm paanii (Warm Water)
grm paanii se vjn km krnaa sbse aasaan triikom mem se ek hai। din kii shurooaat gungune paanii se krem aur jb khaanaa khaane ke aadhe ghmte baad bhii niimboo kaa rs milaakr grm paanii piem। aisaa krne se khud b khud vjn km hone lgegaa।
raat ke khaane ko khem naa (Say no to late night dinner)
vjn km krne kaa ek aur aasaan triikaa hai ki raat ko khaanaa n khaaem, khaaskr ydi aapko der raat ko khaanaa khaane kii aadt hai to। koshish krem ki raat kaa khaanaa 8 bje tk khaa lem, ydi aisaa krnaa smbhv nhiim hai to khaane kii jgh slaad aur likvid chiijem lem lekin thos aahaar n lem। aisaa krne se bhii tejii se vjn km hotaa hai।
pttaa gobhii (Cabbage)
svsthy triike se vjn km krne kaa triikaa hai bmdgobhii। pttaa gobhii phaaibr se yukt aur kailorii mem km hotii hai। pttaa gobhii mem taartrik esid (Tartaric Acid) hotaa hai jo shriir mem maujood kaarbohaaiddret aur shugr ko vsaa mem privrtit nhiim hone detaa। upchaar ke lie slaad mem jitnaa smbhv ho pttaa gobhii khaaem। pttaa gobhii kii binaa msaale kii sbjii bhii bnaakr khaanaa laabhdaayk hai।


Disease: daark srkl - aakhom ke niiche ke kaale ghere (Dark Circle)

Description: 
kisii ne sch hii khaa hai ki mkhem binaa bole bhii bhut kuchh kh jaatii haim। aise mem mkhom ke niiche ke kaale ghere yaa daark srkl bhii aapke svaasthy ko bym krte haim। mkhom ke niiche kaale gherom kii smsyaa bढ़tii jaa rhii hai। kevl mhilaaem hii nhiim blki puroosh aur tiinej bchchom mem bhii daark srkl kii smsyaa ho rhii hai। kii baar mkhom ke niiche ke kaale ghere kisii biimaarii ke kaarण ho skte haim lekin kii baar aisaa asvsth jiivnchryaa ke kaarण bhii hotaa hai। daark srkl (Dark Circle) n kevl mkhom kii khoobsoortii ko km kr dete haim blki isse chehraa bhii biimaar njr aataa hai। mkhom ke niiche kii tvchaa bhut ptlii hotii hai jisse nsem njr aatii haim। jb in nsom mem rkt kaa bhaav tejii se hotaa hai to yh baahr se ghrii njr aatii haim jiske kaarण kaale ghere (Aankhon ke Kale Ghere) njr aate haim। kuchh logom mem mkhem mdr kii or dhmsii huii hotii hai, aise logom mem bhii daark srkl njr aate haim। ydi aapkii mkhom ke niiche soojn yaa bdrmg tvchaa dikhaaii de jo smy ke saath bढ़ rhii ho to chikitsk ko jroor dikhaaem। smsyaa kis kaarण se hai, yh ptaa lgaane ke baad dॉktr aasaanii se kaale gherom kaa ilaaj kr sktaa hai। 

Symptoms: 
- mkhom ke niiche kaale ghere,
- mkhom ke niiche soojn yaa bdrmg tvchaa

Reasons: 
- shriir mem paanii kii kmii honaa
- dooshण mem jyaadaa rhnaa
- raat ko der se sone kii aadt
- paanii prchur maatraa mem n piinaa
- smtulit bhojn kii kmii
- adhik dhoomrpaan krne yaa any nshiilii aadtom se
- kaiphiin kaa jyaadaa maatraa mem upyog
