thmdii sikaaii- (Cold Compress) mkhom kii thmdii sikaaii krne se bhii smsyaa kaa hl smbhv hai। kisii kpड़e mem brph ke tukड़e ko rkhkr mkh kii sikaaii kii jaa sktii hai। j
yaadaa tkiye (Extra Pillow) mkhom ke niiche kii tvchaa phool rhii ho to sir ke niiche atirikt tkiye lgaakr sir ko uthaakr soem। aisaa krne se niiche kii plkom mem jmaa aaii phld phailegaa aur mkhom ke niiche phoolaa huaa hissaa saamaany hokr daark srkl bhii km homge। 
jyaadaa soem (Sleep Extra) mkhom ke niiche ke kaale gherom (Aankhon ke Kale Ghere) se niptne ke lie der raat tk jaagnaa chhoड़ dem। smy se soem aur aap jitnaa sote haim usse jyaadaa niimd lem। aisaa krne se bhii kaale ghere km homge। 

Home Remedies:
smsyaa bढ़ne pr lej triitmemt yaa kemiikl piil therepii kii jaa sktii hai lekin kii baar kevl ghreloo nuskhom se bhii daark srkl ko htaayaa jaa sktaa hai। haalmki jyaadaatr maamlom mem mkhom ke niiche ke kaale gherom ke lie dॉktr kii mdd kii jroort nhiim pड़tii।

Disease: ichimg yaa khujlii (Itching)

Description: 
tvchaa ke kisii bhii hisse mem tvchaa ko khurchne kii anubhooti honaa hii khujlii hai। khujlii mem ek shriir mem ek trh kaa senseshn hotaa hai jo ki tvchaa ko nomchne (Scratch) yaa khujlaane pr mjboor kr detaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- khsraa jaisii biimaarii hone ke chhh sptaah ke mdr dst honaa

Reasons: 
- grmiyom mem psiinaa aataa rhtaa hai। baahr se ghr lautne pr saaraa shriir psiine se bhiigaa hotaa hai, lekin pmkhe v koolr kii thmdii hvaa se kuchh der mem psiinaa sookh jaataa hai। shriir pr psiinaa sookh jaane se khujlii hone lgtii hai।
- kii-kii din tk snaan nhiim krne, tvchaa pr dhool-mittii jmne se khujlii kii utptti hotii hai। chikitsaa visheshjञom ke anusaar khujlii koii svtmtr rog nhiim। doosre rogom ke kaarण tvchaa shushk ho jaane se khujlii hotii hai।

- kuchh strii-purush ke sir ke baalom mem jue utpnn hotii haim to tiivr khujlii hotii hai।
- ekjimaa v daad mem bhii bhut khujlii hotii hai। 
- mdhumeh rog me jnnmgom ke aas-paas tiivr khujlii hotii hai।
- shiit ritu mem shiitl vaayu ke prkop se jb tvchaa shushk hokr phtne lgtii hai to bhut khujlii hotii hai।
- griishm ritu mem dhoop mem chlne-phirne se ghmoriym niklne pr khujlii hotii hai। elrjii ke kaarण bhii tiivr khujlii hotii hai।

Treatments:
khujlii se nijaat ke tips tthaa upaay (Remedie of Itching)
- khujlii se nijaat ke lie adhik phl-sbjiyom kaa sevn krem।
- srdiyom mem adhik shiitl vaayu ke smprk se khujlii hone pr prtidin snaan se phle srsom v til ke tel se maalish krem।
- chmelii ke tel mem niiboo kaa rs milaakr maalish krne ke baad nhaaem।
- niim ke peड़ pr pkii nibaulii khaane se khujlii kii smsyaa nsht hotii hai।
- tmaatr kaa rs subh aur shaam ko piine se khujlii khtm hotii hai।
- rkt dooshit hone pr khujlii kii vikृti hone pr niim ke koml gulaabii ptte 6 graam, kaalii mirch ke 10 daane piiskr jl ke saath sevn krem।
- niim ke pttom ko paanii mem ubaalkr, chhaankr nhaane se khujlii khtm hotii hai।
- naariyl ke tel mem krpoor milaakr maalish krne se khujlii khtm krtii haim।
- ajvaayn ko paanii mem ubaalkr, chhaankr piine se khujlii khtm hotii hai।
- kchche hre chnom kaa prtidin sevn krem। chne uplbdh naa hone pr mkurit chnom kaa sevn krem।
- lhsun ko tel mem pkaakr, us tel ko chhaankr maalish krne se khujlii nsht hotii hai।
- ushण mirch-msaalom v amliiy rsom se bne khaady pdaarthom kaa sevn n krem।
- chaay, kॉphii, shraab, sirkaa v achaar kaa sevn n krem।
- mms, mchhlii, mde n khaaem।
- chaainiij aur phaast phood kaa sevn n krem।
- dooshit jl v baajaar mem khulii rkhii chiijem n khaaem।
- ghii, tel v mkkhn se bne khaady pdaarthom kaa sevn n krem।
- dooshit jl se n nhaaem।
- psiine se dooshit kpड़e n phnem।

Home Remedies:
imphekshn (Infection), elrjii (Allergy), kisii kiiड़e ke kaatne se (Insect Bite), tvchaa ke shushk hone se (Dry Skin), dhoop meum bhut jyaadaa rhne aadi kaarणom se shriir mem khujlii kii smsyaa ho sktii hai। khujlii se nijaat ke lie baajaar mem kii trh kii kriim maujood haim lekin inkaa phaaydaa bhii kevl istemaal krne bhr tk hotaa hai। uske baad sthiti js kii ts ho jaatii hai।
aaie jaanem khujlii se nijaat ke ghreloo nuskhe (Home remedies for Itching)
1. naariyl kaa tel (Coconut oil)- tvchaa ke shushk hone yaa kisii kiiड़e ke kaatne se, khujlii kisii bhii kaarण se ho, naariyl kaa tel behd phaaydemmd hotaa hai। naariyl ke tel ko khujlii vaale sthaan pr lgaakr hlke haath se maalish krem। itnaa hii nhiim naariyl tel ko poore shriir pr bhii lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
2. petroliym jailii (Petroleum jelly)- ydi tvchaa behd smvednshiil (sensitive skin) hai to khujlii se nijaat ke lie petroliym jailii behd achchhaa upaay hai। ismem koii bhii rsaayn nhiim hotaa aur tvchaa pr behd prbhaavii bhii hotii hai। iske istemaal se n kevl khujlii blki tvchaa kii any smsyaaem bhii hl ho jaatii haim।
3. niimboo (Lemon)- niimboo mem vitaamin sii (vitamin c) uchch maatraa mem paayaa jaataa hai। khujlii se nijaat ke lie niimboo behd achchhe upaayom mem se ek hai। niimboo mem maujood volaataail (volatile) tvchaa kii soojn aur jln ko door krte haim। prbhaavit tvchaa pr niimboo ke rs ko rooii kii shaaytaa se lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
4. bekimg sodaa (Baking soda)- tiin hisse bekimg sodaa mem ek hissaa paanii milaakr ek pest bnaayem। is pest ko prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se khujlii kii smsyaa se raaht miltii hai। lekin tvchaa ktii-phtii ho to bekimg sodaa lgaane se bchnaa chaahie।
5. tulsii (Basil)- tulsii mem thaaymॉl, yoojiinॉl aur kaimphr uchch maatraa mem hote haim jo khujlii aur jln se raaht dete haim। tulsii kii kuchh pttiyom ko achchhii prkaar dhokr, prbhaavit sthaan pr rgड़ne se khujlii aur jln se raaht miltii hai।
6. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)- seb ke sirke kaa istemaal roosii se nijaat ke lie kiyaa jaataa hai, usii prkaar khujlii mem bhii yh laabhdaayk hai। seb ke sirkaa mem emtiiseptik aur emtiiphmgl guण hote haim jo ki tvchaa smbmdhii smsyaaom se nijaat dilaate haim। seb ke sirkaa mem rooii ko bhigaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se khujlii kii smsyaa se raaht miltii hai।
7. eloveraa (Aloevera)- elovraa mॉishchraaijr se bhrpoor hotaa hai jisse rookhii tvchaa se hone vaalii khujlii mem yh asrkaarii hai। eloveraa jel prbhaavit tvchaa pr lgaane se khujlii, jln aur soojn door hotii hai। tvchaa pr eloveraa lgaane ke lie iskii ek pttii ko chaakoo se biich se chiir kr uske mdr se jailii ko baahr nikaalem aur shriir pr hlke haathom se msaaj krem।
8. niim (Neem)- niim kii pttiyom ko paanii mem daalkr ubaalem। iske baad is paanii ko gungunaa rhne pr nhaayem। niim mem praakृtik taur pr emtiiseptik guण hote haim jo khujlii ko door krte haim। iske alaavaa ydi rkt mem kisii prkaar kii ashuddhi ke kaarण khujlii hotii hai to subh subh niim ke chhote yaa kchche ptte chbaayem। nibaurii chbaane se bhii rkt saaph hokr khujlii door hotii hai।


Disease: gle mem drd (Throat Ache)

Description: 
gle mem drd (Throat ache) saamaany srdii kaa smket bhii ho sktaa hai aur vokl kord mem imphekshn yaa strep throt (strep throat) jaisii kisii gmbhiir smsyaa kaa lkshण bhii। ismem gle mem chubhn yaa chhilaa huaa mhsoos hotaa hai aur kuchh khaane mem dikkt mhsoos hotii hai।

Symptoms: 
- gle ke saath knptii tk drd honaa
- gle mem drd honaa
- niglne mem kthinaaii honaa
- hlkii khm~sii v gle mem khraash mhsoos hotii hai
- jbड़aa kholne mem preshaanii honaa
- kii baar kaan mem bhii dikkt honaa
- gle mem chubhn honaa

Reasons: 
1. saamaany srdii jo vaayrl imphekshn se ho sktii hai।
2. aavaaj vaalii grmthiyom lairiimgaaitis (Laryngitis) mem imphekshn honaa।
3. tmsil mem imphekshn hone se।
4. tmsil ke aas-paas ke ootkom mem smkrmण hone se।
5. dhoomrpaan, prdooshण, jor se chillaane ke kaarण।
6. naak kii jgh gle se sms lene ke kaarण ।
7. gle mem kisii trh kii koii chot lgne se।

Treatments:
gle mem drd ke tips (Treatment of Throat Ache)
- gungune paanii mem nmk daalk kr graare krem। 
- grm paanii kii bhaap lem। 
- gle kii sikaaii krem। 
- tulsii aur laumg jaise ghreloo upaayom ko gle ke drd (Gale me Dard) se raaht ke lie istemaal krem। 
- gle mem drd ho to jyaadaa bolem yaa chillaaem nhiim। 
- grm pey jaise chaay, kॉphii aur soop piiem। 
- dhoomrpaan n krem। 
- jhoothaa khaanaa yaa jhoothe brtnom mem khaanaa n khaaem। 
- dhool, prdooshण, dhuem aadi se door rhem। 
gle ke drd mem in baatom kaa rkhem dhyaan (Precautions for Throat Ache)
- limph nod yaani kii jbड़e ke niiche ke hisse mem soojn aaii ho to vishesh dhyaan dem। 
- glaa achaank drd krne lge aur bukhaar aa jaae to bhii vishesh dhyaan denaa chaahie। 
- ek sptaah se adhik smy tk bhii smsyaa bnii rhe to dॉktr kii slaah avshy lenii chaahie। 
- niglne mem dikkt saamaany hai lekin ydi paanii bhii nhiim pii paa rhe to schet rhem। 
- gle ke saath baahrii hisse bhii drd krne lge yaa sms lene mem preshaanii ho rhii ho to turmt dॉktr kii slaah lenii chaahie। 
- joड़om mem yaa kaan mem drd ho to dॉktr kii slaah avshy lenii chaahie। 
- blgm mem khoon aa rhaa ho to ise njrmdaaj nhiim krnaa chaahie। 


Disease: jvaaimt pen- joड़om mem drd (Joint Pain)

Description: 
jvaaimt pen- joड़om mem drd

Symptoms: 
- joड़om ko moड़ne mem preshaanii honaa
- joड़om kaa laal honaa
- joड़om mem khimchaav mhsoos honaa
- joड़om pr kthortaa honaa
- chlne- phirne mem dikkt honaa
- joड़om mem akड़n aanaa
- joड़om mem soojn aur drd
- joड़om mem kmjorii honaa

Reasons: 
kaarण (cause of joint pain)
- umr bढ़ne ke saath
- hddiyom mem rkt kii aapoorti mem rookaavt aanaa
- rkt kaa kaimsr honaa
- hddiyom mem minrl yaani kii khnij kii kmii honaa
- joड़om pr bhut jyaadaa dbaav pड़naa
- joड़om mem imphekshn honaa
- hddiyom kaa tootnaa
- moch aanaa yaa chot lgnaa
- hddiyom mem tyoomr aadi kii shikaayt honaa
- arthraaitis
- brsaaitis
- ऑstiyokomdraaitis
- kaartilej kaa phtnaa
- kaartilej kaa ghis jaanaa

Treatments:
joड़om ke drd se raaht ke lie tips (Tips to prevent joint pain)
1. gtishiil rhem (Keep moving)
joड़om ke drd se raaht ke lie gtishiil rhem, yaani joड़om kii moovmemt hotii rhnii chaahie। lmbe smy tk ek hii sthiti mem rhne se bhii joड़om mem kthortaa mhsoos hotii hai।
2. joड़om ko chot se bchaaem (Prevent joints from injury)
joड़om pr lgii chot, hddii ko toड़ bhii sktii hai, islie joड़om ko chot se bchaakr rkhem। jb bhii koii aisaa khel khelem jismem joड़om pr chot lgne kaa dr ho, to jvaaimt sephtii peds (Joint safety pads) phnem। tenis aur golph khelte smy bhii breses (braces) phnem।
3. vjn ko niymtrit rkhem (Maintain your weight)
ydi aapkaa vjn niymtrण mem rhegaa to aapke joड़ bhii svaasthy rhemge। shriir kaa jyaadaa vjn ghutnom aur kmr pr adhik dbaav daaltaa hai, jisse kaartilej (cartilage) ke tootne kaa dr rhtaa hai। aise mem vjn ko niymtrण mem rkhnaa behd jroorii hai।
4. strechimg jyaadaa n krem (Do not stretch more)
vyaayaam krte smy strechimg krne kii bhii slaah dii jaatii hai, lekin strechimg kevl hphte mem tiin baar krem। strechimg ko ekdm shuroo krne kii jgh, isse phle vaarm ap vyaayaam (warm up exercise) krem।
5. doodh piiem (Drink milk)
joड़om ko mjboot rkhne ke lie doodh jroor piiem। doodh se hddiyom ko kailshyim aur vitaamin dii miltaa hai jisse hddiym mjboot bntii haim। ydi doodh psmd n ho to doodh se bne any khaady pdaarth jaise pniir, dhii aadi bhii khaae jaa skte haim।
6. shii poshchr bnaae rkhem (Maintain right posture)
joड़om ke drd se raaht ke lie shii poshchr mem uthnaa, baithnaa aur chlnaa behd jroorii hai। shii poshchr grdn se lekr ghutnom tk ke joड़om kii rkshaa krtaa hai।
7. vyaayaam (Exercise)
joड़om ke svaasthy ke lie vyaayaam ko dainik dinchryaa kaa hissaa bnaaem। tairaakii (swimming) bhii joड़om ke drd se raaht ke lie achchhaa vyaayaam hotii hai।

Home Remedies:
joड़om kaa drd (Joint Pain) shriir ke kisii bhii bhaag mem ho sktaa hai, ghutne, kmdhe yaa kmr। kii baar gthiyaa joड़om ke drd kaa kaarण hotaa hai jo kii baar tnaav lene, prbhaavit hissom pr jyaadaa dbaav pड़ne, moch aane yaa kisii any prkaar kii chot lgne ke kaarण bhii aisaa ho sktaa hai।
joड़om ke drd mem prbhaavit hissaa laal ho sktaa hai aur vhm soojn bhii aa sktii hai। aaie hm aapko btaate haim ki kaun se ghreloo upaay apnaakr aap joड़om ke drd mem raaht paa skte haim।
joड़om ke drd ke lie ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies for Joint Pain)
maalish (Massage)
maalish se shriir ke drd mem behd aaraam miltaa hai, yhii prkriyaa joड़om ke drd mem bhii laagoo hotii hai। naariyl, jaitoon, srsom yaa lhsun ke tel se prbhaavit hisse kii maalish krem। hlke haathom se dbaav dete hue drd vaale hisse ko mlem। aisaa krne se drd se raaht milegii।
grm aur thmdii sikaaii (Cold and Hot Compress)
joड़om ke drd se nijaat ke lie grm aur thmdii sikaaii krne se bhii bhut aaraam miltaa hai। grm sikaaii krne se rkt smchaar behtr hotaa hai vhiim thmdii sikaaii se soojn aur chubhn km hotii hai।
grm sikaaii ke lie grm paanii kii botl ko tauliyaa mem lpet kr grdn kii sikaaii krem। jbki, thmdii sikaaii krne ke lie brph ke tukड़om ko tauliyaa mem lpetkr, us tauliyaa se sikaaii krem। sikaaii krte vkt km se km do se tiin mint tk grdn kii lgaataar sikaaii honii chaahie। yh poorii prkriyaa 15 se 20 mint mem dohraaem। is vidhi ko aaraam hone tk din mem do baar krem।
lhsun (Garlic)
ydi joड़om mem drd hai to lhsun kaa istemaal behd achchhe priणaam de sktaa hai। iske aushdhiiy guण grdn ke drd, soojn aur jln ko thiik krte haim। lhsun kii do klii hr subh khaalii pet paanii ke saath khaaem। khaanaa bnaane vaale kisii bhii tel mem lhsun kii kuchh kliym daal kr bhoon lem। is tel ko gungunaa hone tk thmdaa krem aur prbhaavit hisse kii maalish krem। is vidhi ko din mem do baar kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
hldii (Turmeric)
hldii ke aushdhiiy guण kisii se chhipe nhiim hai lekin achchhii baat yh bhii hai ki yh joड़om ke drd mem bhii utnii hii prbhaavii hai। hldii rkt smchaar tej krke joड़om ke drd se aaraam detii hai aur grdn kii akड़n ko bhii km krtii hai।
adrk (Ginger)
joड़om ke drd ke ilaaj ke lie adrk bhii behtriin prbhaav dikhaataa hai। yh hrb bhii guणom se bhrpoor hai jo ki rkt smchaar ko tej krtii hai jisse grdn ke drd se raaht miltii hai। ek din mem lgbhg tiin kp adrk kii chaay piem। adrk kii chaay bnaane ke lie paanii mem adrk ubaalem aur thmdaa krke ismem shhd milaaem। is pey ko piem। prbhaavit hisse kii adrk ke tel se msaaj bhii kii jaa sktii hai।
seb saaidr sirkaa (Apple Cider Vinegar)
seb kaa sirkaa bhii joड़om ke drd se raaht dene mem bhut achchhaa asr dikhaataa hai। yh joड़om ke drd aur soojn se raaht detaa hai। kisii kpड़e ko seb ke sirke mem bhigokr drd vaale sthaan pr lpemtem aur kuchh ghmtom ke lie chhoड़ dem। din mem do baar is vidhi ko krem। do kp seb saaidr sirkaa ko gungune paanii mem daalkr nhaayaa bhii jaa sktaa hai। ek gilaas paanii mem kchchaa seb saaidr sirkaa aur shhd milaakr piine se bhii laabh hotaa hai।
laal mirch paaudr (Red Chillie Powder)
laal mirch paaudr bhii joड़om ke drd se raaht dene mem bhut prbhaavii hai। upchaar ke lie ek kp naariyl ke tel ko grm krke, usmem do bड़e chmmch laal mirch paaudr milaaem। is mishrण se prbhaavit hisse pr lgaakr tkriibn 20 mint ke lie chhoड़ dem। jyaadaa aaraam ke lie is mishrण ko prtidin drd vaale hisse pr lgaaem।


Disease: looj moshn- dst (Loose Motion)

Description: 
shauch ekdm ptlaa ho aur baar- baar jaanaa pड़ rhaa ho, to yh dst hai। dst hone pr shauch mem paanii kaa bhaag jyaadaa hotaa hai। kii baar shauch jaate smy pet mem drd (Pain) yaa aimthn (Crumping) bhii mhsoos hotii hai।

Symptoms: 
- kbhii-kbhii shauch mem khoon kaa aanaa
- jyaadaa pyaas lgnaa
- piith ke nichle hisse mem athvaa pet ke nichle bhaag mem achaank tej drd, jo pet v jmgh ke smdhi kshetr tk jaataa hai
- pet mem gd़bd़ii kaa ehsaas hone lgtaa hai
- pet mem soojn honaa।
- bukhaar yaa thmd lgnaa

Reasons: 
dst ke kaarण- (Causes of loose motion)
dst, mtom mem jyaadaa drv ke jmaa hone se hote haim। kii baar mtom dvaaraa trl pdaarth ko thiik trh se avshoshit (absorb) n kr paane yaa mtom se ml ke tejii se niklne ke kaarण bhii aisaa hotaa hai।
dst hone kii do sthitiym ho sktii haim, jismem se ek mem saamaany se kuchh jyaadaa baar shauch jaate haim jbki doosrii sthiti mem lgaataar chhh- saat yaa usse jyaadaa baar shauch jaate haim। yh shauch hr baar ekdm ptlii hotii hai। yh dst, paachn smbmdhii smsyaa ke kaarण haate haim। jiivaaणuom dvaaraa smkrmण tthaa tॉksin aadi phailaane se dst hone shuroo ho jaate haim। kii baar tnaav yaa kisii prkaar ke dr ke kaarण bhii dst shuroo ho skte haim। aise dst ko kronik yaa jiirण dst khte haim।
kuchh any kaarण nimn haim-
- baiktiiriyaa, vaayrs yaa prjiivii ke kaarण
- kuchh emtiibaayotik dvaaom ke kaarण
- kisii trh ke pet ke rog yaa simdrom ke kaarण
- phood imphekshn ke kaarण
- jyaadaa khaa lene se
- kisii trh kii koii elrjii ke kaarण
- bhut jyaadaa shraab piine se
- jyaadaa maatraa mem chaay-kॉphii piine se
- mithaaii jyaadaa khaane se

Treatments:
- khaane se phle haathom ko achchhii trh dhoem
- apne khaane- piine kii chiijom mem turmt bdlaav krem
- chaay, kॉphii aur doodh se bne pdaarth n khaaem
- naariyl paanii, niimboo paanii aur chhaachh aadi jyaadaa se jyaadaa lem
- adhpkaa khaanaa, miit aadi n khaaem
- ydi kisii ko dst haim to, usse haath milaane yaa chhoone ke baad turmt haath achchhii trh dhokr aur sukhaakr hii kuchh khaaem

Home Remedies:
looj moshn yaa dst shriir ko kmjor bnaa dete haim। isse shriir mem paanii kii kmii ho jaatii hai jisse shriir ke jroorii khnij bhii shriir se baahr nikl jaate haim। is kaarण vykti ko kmjorii mhsoos hotii।
dst kii shikaayt kii kaarणom se ho sktii hai jaise-  baasii khaanaa khaane, kisii khaane se elrjii hone, kisii trh kaa tnaav hone, dooshit paanii yaa khaanaa khaane, shraab aadi jyaadaa piine se yaa kbhii kbhii kuchh dvaaiiyom ke sevn se bhii।
aaie hm aapko btaate haim ki ghreloo nuskhom kii shaaytaa se kis trh se aap looj moshn kii smsyaa se raaht paa skte haim।
dst ke upchaar ke lie ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Loose Motion)
srsom ke biij (Mustard Seeds)
srsom ke biij looj moshn rokne mem kaargr hote haim। upchaar ke lie thoड़e se paanii mem srsom ke biij daalkr ek ghmte ke lie alg rkh dem। iske baad is paanii ko tॉnik kii trh piem। looj moshn se raaht milegii।
niimboo paanii (Lemonade)
niimboo kaa rs pet saaph krne mem shaayk hai। upchaar ke lie ek gilaas paanii mem thoड़ii chiinii, thoड़aa nmk aur ek niimboo kaa rs milaakr piem। isse shriir mem paanii kii kmii nhiim hogii aur looj moshn bhii rook jaaemge।
anaar (Pomegranate)
looj moshn ke upchaar ke lie anaar ko chbaakr khaaem। ydi daane chbaanaa psmd n ho to anaar kaa taajaa rs nikaalkr bhii piyaa jaa sktaa hai। isse bhii dst rook jaate haim।
methii (Fenugreek Seeds)
methii jiivaaणurodhii hotii hai jo ki looj moshn rokne mem shaayk hai। upchaar ke lie ek se do chmmch methii ke daane lekr inkaa paaudr bnaa lem। is paaudr ko ek gilaas paanii mem daalkr piem।
saaboodaanaa (Sago)
saaboodaanaa pet drd ke saath hii paachn shkti ko bढ़aavaa dekr looj moshn rokne mem shaaytaa krtaa hai। upchaar ke lie tiin se chaar ghmtom ke lie saaboodaanaa ko paanii mem bhigaa dem। iske baad is paanii ko dinbhr mem chaar se pmch baar  piem।
doodh ko khem naa (No milk or milk product)
jb tk aap looj moshn se preshaan haim, doodh yaa doodh se bne pdaarthom kaa sevn n krem। aapkii mt (intestine), doodh yaa doodh se bne pdaarthom ko pchaa nhiim paaegii, ntiijaa smsyaa aur bhii bढ़ sktii hai।
kchchaa ppiitaa (Raw Papaya)
kchchaa ppiitaa looj moshn se raaht detaa hai saath hii pet kii mroड़ aur pet drd se bhii nijaat dilaataa hai। upchaar ke lie, ppiite ko kddooks krke tiin kp paanii mem daalem। is paanii ko lgbhg ds mint tk ubaalem। yhii paanii aapko din mem tiin se chaar baar piinaa hai। aisaa krne se dst rook jaaemge।
saumth (Dry Ginger Powder)
adrk kaa paaudr yaa saumth paachn shkti ko bढ़aataa hai aur pet drd se raaht detaa hai। upchaar ke lie, ek kp chhaachh mem aadhii chmmch saumth milaaem aur din mem km se km tiin se chaar baar piem।
laukii kaa rs (Bottle Guard Juice)
laukii kaa rs, shriir mem paanii kii kmii nhiim hone detaa islie looj moshn se piiड़it vykti ko laukii kaa rs denaa phaaydemmd hotaa hai।
upchaar ke lie ek taajaa laukii ko chhiilkr, dhokr chhote chhote tukड़om mem kaat lem aur miksii mem daalkr piis lem। iske baad ise chhaankr rs ko kisii brtn mem nikaal lem। laukii ke joos ko svaadisht bnaane ke lie ismem kaalii mirch aur kaalaa nmk milaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
staarch yukt khaanaa (Starch Rich Food)
looj moshn se preshaan haim to staarch yukt khaanaa khaaem। yh khaanaa aasaanii se pch jaataa hai aur pet mem bhaarii nhiim lgtaa। staarchyukt khaane mem giilaa sphed chaavl, uble aaloo aur gaajr aadi khaaii jaa sktii hai।
chaay pttii (Tea)
looj moshn se turmt raaht chaahte haim to chaay pttii ko piiskr, ek chmmch chaay pttii ko khaakr paanii piem। isse looj moshn rook jaaemge। nvjaat (infant) aur chhote bchchom ko chaay pttii ko paanii mem gholkr vh paanii ek yaa do chmmch krke pilaayaa jaa sktaa hai। isse bhii dst rook jaaemge।


Disease: pet drd (Stomach Ache)

Description: 
pet drd mem drd chhaatii aur pelvik riijn (pelvic region) ke biich ubhrtaa hai। yh drd tej, hlkaa, chubhnvaalaa aur mroड़ vaalaa ho sktaa hai। pet mem kisii bhii hisse mem koii bhii tkliiph hone pr pet drd ho sktaa hai। vaayrl yaa baiktiiriyl imphekshn (bacterial infection) jo pet aur mtom ko prbhaavit krte haim, ke kaarण bhii pet drd ho sktaa hai। pet drd aam smsyaa hai lekin kii baar pet kaa drd kisii gmbhiir biimaarii kaa smket bhii ho sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- kisii kaarणvsh shauch n jaa paanaa
- pet kaa nichlaa hissaa skht honaa
- pet kaa phoolnaa
- pet pr koii chot lgnaa
- pet mem gais bnnaa
- baar-baar peshaab jaanaa
- dihaaidreshn
- bukhaar
- ultii

Reasons: 
pet drd ke kaarण (Cause of Stomach Ache)
pet kaa drd kii kaarणom se ho sktaa hai। gle, mt yaa rkt ke kaarण baiktiiriyaa pet mem phumch jaate haim jisse paachn kriyaa prbhaavit hotii hai aur pet drd hotaa hai। isii trh ke imphekshn ke kaarण daayriyaa aur kbj (Constipation) bhii ho sktaa hai। mhilaaom mem maasik straav (Menstruation) ke kaarण bhii pet drd kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
pet mem drd kis hisse mem hai, is sthiti ko dekhte hue bhii nimn kaarण bhii ho skte haim:
- apch
- kbj
- maasik dhrm (Pain in Periods)
- khaane se elrjii
- gais
- alsr
- pitt kii thailii mem pthrii
- haarniyaa
- kidnii mem pthrii
- yooriinrii trekt imphekshn (Urinary Tract Infection)
- apemdiks (Appendix)
- pelvik inphlemaitrii dijiij (Pelvic Inflammatory Disease)

Treatments:
pet drd se raaht ke lie tips (Tips to Prevent Stomach Ache)
- khaanaa smtulit aur jyaadaa phaaibr vaalaa khaaem
- paanii jyaadaa se jyaadaa piiem
- aisaa khaanaa km khaaem jo gais kaa kaarण ho
- rojaanaa vyaayaam jroor krem
- khaanaa khaakr turmt soem nhiim blki kuchh der thlem
- pet kii sikaaii krne se bhii aaraam hotaa hai
pet drd mem dhyaan dene yog baatem (Precautions for Stomach Pain)

Home Remedies:
pet kaa drd ek aam smsyaa hai। gais, bdhjmii (Indigestion), pet mem soojn (Swelling in Stomach), aimthn (Cramps), ultii (Vomiting), aadi prkaar kii smsyaaem hone pr pet drd kii shikaayt shuroo ho jaatii hai।

pet drd ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Stomach Ache)

Disease: tnaav- strais (Stress)

Description: 
kisii baat se preshaan, aaht yaa dukhii hokr, vykti kaa mn se ghn udaas honaa hii tnaav hai। tnaav mn se smbmdhit hai। tnaav (Stress) ek trh kaa dvmd hai jo smtuln aur saammjsy n baithaa paane ke kaarण hotaa hai। jo vykti tnaav se grsit hotaa hai uskaa mn ashmt ho jaataa hai, bhaavnaaem sthir nhiim rh paatiim। shii aur glt kaa phaislaa krnaa mushkil ho jaataa hai। aise mem smbmdhit vykti kii shaariirik aur maansik donom hii sthitiym din-prtidin khraab hotii jaatii haim।

tnaav ke kaarण (Cause of stress)

- rishtom mem draar

Home Remedies:
bhaagdauड़ bhrii dinchryaa mem adhikmsh log, tnaav (Stress) se grsit haim। tnaav se n kevl shaariirik blki maansik sthiti bhii prbhaavit hotii hai। itnaa hii nhiim tnaav ke kaarण vykti ke vyvhaar mem bhii privrtn hote rhte haim jisse smbmdhit vykti ke saath usse juड़e any log bhii prbhaavit hote haim। tnaav se vykti kii yaaddaasht, siikhne kii kshmtaa (Learning ability), tthaa kaary krne kii kshmtaa (Working ability) bhii prbhaavit hotii hai।
aaie aapko btaate haim tnaav se bchaav ke lie ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Stress):
1. griin tii (Green tea)- griin tii mem maujood emtiiऑksiidemt (Anti Oxidents) shriir tthaa dimaag ko shmt krte haim tthaa mood mem skaaraatmk bdlaav laate haim। griin tii mem maujood thiyaaniin (Theanine) strktaa aur dhyaan bढ़aataa hai। ydi kisii ko griin tii psmd n ho to blaik tii bhii pii jaa sktii hai।
2. smtraa (Orange)- smtraa mem vitaamin sii uchch maatraa mem paayaa jaataa hai jo ki imyoonitii (immunity) ko bढ़aane mem shaayk hai। smtre mem vitaamin e aur bii ke saath any svaasthy vrdhk minrl bhii paaye jaate haim। tnaav se raaht ke lie rojaanaa smtre kaa ek gilaas taajaa joos piiem।
3. doodh (Milk)- ek gilaas doodh shriir ko bhrpoor emtiiऑksiidemt aur jroorii poshk ttv detaa hai। yh sbhii poshk ttv vykti ko tnaav se lड़ne kii shkti dete haim aur chitt ko shmt rkhte haim। rojaanaa subh naashte mem tthaa raat ko sone se phle ek gilaas grm doodh piinaa tnaav se raaht detaa hai।
4. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam mem vitaamin bii, ii, maigniishiym, jimk, seleniym (selenium) tthaa any svaasthy vrdhk vsaa paaii jaatii hai। jis kaarण yh tnaav se raaht dete haim। baadaam ko bhoon kr yaa kchchaa bhii khaayaa jaa sktaa hai। ydi aise khaanaa smbhv n ho to baadaam kaa paaudr bnaakr, doodh ke saath khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
5. paalk (Spinach)- paalk mem bhrpoor maatraa mem vitaamin e, bii aur sii se bhrpoor hotii haim। inmem minrl (minerals) bhii prchur maatraa mem paaye jaate haim jo tnaav se lड़ne kii shkti dete haim। ek kp paalk rojaanaa khaane se shriir aur dimaag donom ko raaht miltii hai। paalk kaa soop bnaakr, sbjii, slaad yaa ऑmlet aadi mem daalkr khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।

7. jaamun (Blue berries)- jaamun mem uchch maatraa mem emtiiऑksiidemt hote haim jisse tnaav ghttaa hai। jaamun ko rojaanaa khaane se tnaav, insomniyaa (insomnia) aur any trh ke mood disऑrdr (mood disorder) se raaht miltii hai। jaamun ko slaad aadi mem milaakr khaayaa jaa sktaa hai। tnaav se raaht ke lie jaamun kaa joos bhii piiyaa jaa sktaa hai।

Disease: esiditii yaa amlpitt (Acidity)

Description: 
esiditii (Acidity)

Symptoms: 
- kbhii-kbhii chhaatii mem drd ho sktaa hai।
- khttii dkaarem aanaa,
- khaanaa yaa khttaa paanii (esid) mumh mem aa jaanaa,

- pet mem gais bnnaa

kaarण (Cause of Acidity)

- khaan-paan mem aniymittaa

Home Remedies:
pet mem paachn rs kii jyaadaa yaa km maatraa niklne pr esiditii kii preshaanii hotii hai। esiditii hone pr pet mem drd (Stomach Pain), gais (Gas), mumh se bdboo (Mouth Odour) aur jii michlaane (Nausea) jaisii smsyaaem ho sktii haim। jo log aksr esiditii se preshaan rhte haim unke lie smsyaa gmbhiir ho sktii hai। esiditii msaaledaar khaanaa khaane, aniymit khaane (Irregular Eating) kii aadtem yaa bhut jyaadaa stres lene se bhii hotii hai।
