esiditii se bchaav ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Acidity)
tulsii ke ptte (Basil Leaves)
tulsii ke ptte aapko turmt esiditii, gais aur ultii se raaht de skte haim। upchaar ke lie kuchh tulsii ke ptte chbaa kr khaaem। iske alaavaa tulsii ke kuchh ptte paanii mem ubaalkr, us paanii ko chhaan lem। gungunaa rhne pr shhd milaakr piem। yh bhii esiditii ke lie achchhaa upaay hai।
daalchiinii (Cinnamon)
daalchiinii ek praakृtik emtaasid (Antacid) hai jo paachn shkti ke lie behd achchhii hai aur gais ko door rkhtii hai। upchaar ke lie ek kp paanii mem aadhaa chmmch daaliichiinii paaudr daalkr ubaalem। is paanii ko ek din mem do se tiin baar piem। iske alaavaa soop yaa slaad mem bhii daalchiinii paaudr daalkr khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
chhaachh (Buttermilk)
chhaachh piine se bhii esiditii mem bhut raaht miltii hai। chhaachh mem pet kii amltaa ko smtulit krne ke lie laiktik esid hotaa hai। upchaar ke lie methii ke daanom ko paanii ke saath milaakr pest bnaa lem। is pest ko ek gilaas chhaachh mem milaakr piem। isse pet kaa drd bhii thiik hogaa aur gais se bhii raaht milegii। saath hii, esiditii bhii khtm hogii। svaad bढ़aane aur behtr priणaam ke lie is chhaachh mem kaalaa nmk aur kaalii mirch bhii milaaii jaa sktii hai।
seb kaa sirkaa (Apple Cider Vinegar)
seb kaa sirkaa bhii esiditii ko thiik krne kaa aasaan triikaa hai। upchaar ke lie ek kp paanii mem do chmmch kchchaa seb kaa sirkaa milaakr din mem do baar piem। khaanaa khaane se phle bhii ise piyaa jaa sktaa hai।
laumg (Cloves)
laumg khaane se pet mem haaidroklorik esid kii maatraa bढ़ jaatii hai jisse pet kii amltaa km hotii hai aur esiditii se raaht miltii hai। raaht ke lie khaane ke baad do se tiin laumg ko mumh mem rkhkr hlkaa hlkaa chbaakr choosem।
jiiraa (Cumin)
jiiraa bhii ek behtriin esid nyootraalaaijr (Acid Neutralizer) hai jo esiditii ko km krtaa hai। iske saath hii paachn shkti ko bढ़aakr pet drd se bhii raaht detaa hai। upchaar ke lie jiiraa ko bhoonkr uskaa paaudr bnaaem। is paaudr ko khaanaa khaane ke baad ek gilaas paanii mem milaakr piem। jiiraa paaudr ko chhaachh mem milaakr bhii piyaa jaa sktaa hai।
adrk (Ginger)
adrk mem pet kii amltaa se lड़ne ke guण hote haim jo esiditii se raaht dete haim। upchaar ke lie khaane ke baad adrk kaa ek chhotaa tukड़aa mumh mem rkhkr chbaaem। yaa phir ek kp paanii mem adrk ko kuchlkr daalem aur ubaalem। is paanii ko chhnkr piem।
guड़ (Jaggery)
guड़ mem paachn ke lie behd achchhii khaady saamgrii hai saath hii guड़ khaane se pet kii amltaa bhii km hotii hai jisse esiditii se raaht miltii hai। upchaar ke lie hr roj khaane ke baad ek tukड़aa guड़ kaa khaaem। haalmki yh upaay shugr rogiyom ke lie thiik nhiim hai।
thmdaa doodh (Cold Milk)
doodh pet mem esid ke nirmaaण ko roktaa hai saath hii gaistrik esid ko sthir krke esiditii kii smsyaa hone se bchaataa hai। haalmki esiditii kii smsyaa hone pr sirph thmdaa doodh hii piinaa chaahie। grm doodh utnaa laabhkaarii nhiim hotaa।
saumph (Fennel)
saumph khaane ko pchaane mem shaaytaa krtii hai aur gais ko door rkhtii hai। hr roj khaanaa khaane ke baad saumph ko mumh mem rkhkr chbaaem। saumph ke saath mishrii bhii milaaii jaa sktii hai। aisaa krne se esiditii se raaht miltii hai।


Disease: elrjii (Allergy)

Description: 
elrjii (Allergy)
kisii bhii chiij ke prti atismvednshiil honaa hii elrjii hai, jise svaasthy kii bhaashaa mem etopii (atopy) bhii khte haim। elrjii kisii se bhii ho sktii hai, mausm mem bdlaav se, kisii khaane kii chiij se, paaltu jaanvr se, dhool se, dhuem se, saumdry prsaadhnom se yaa dvaaom aadi se।
elrjii mem shriir kaa imyoon sistm kuchh khaas chiijom ko sviikaar nhiim kr paataa। in chiijom ke prti imyoonitii ayogy trh se prtikriyaa detii hai। imyoonitii dvaaraa dii jaane vaalii prtikriyaa hii elrjii hotii hai। yoom dekhaa jaae to adhiktr elrjii khtrnaak nhiim hotii lekin kbhii kbhii smsyaa gmbhiir ho jaatii hai।
elrjii ko rokaa jaa sktaa hai, lekin iske lie elrjii paidaa krne vaale kaarणom se poorii trh door rhnaa hogaa। yoom to elrjii phailne vaalii biimaarii nhiim hai phir bhii ydi kisii ko naak bhne aur mkhom se paanii aane vaalii elrjii ho to usse smprk bnaakr rkhne mem hii behtrii hai। smbhv ho to uske dvaaraa istemaal kie ge saamaan ko bhii istemaal n krem।

Symptoms: 
- mkh mem khujlii honaa aur mkh kaa laal ho jaanaa
- mkh se paanii aanaa
- egjimaa aur grmiyom mem bukhaar
- gle mem khujlii honaa
- tvchaa pr khujlii honaa
- tvchaa pr pitt uthnaa
- tvchaa pr laal chktte aur daane honaa
- naak ke mdr baar- baar daane niklnaa
- naak mem baar-baar khujlii honaa
- naak se paanii aanaa

Reasons: 
elrjii  ke kaarण- (cause of allergy)
1. dhool (Dust)
dhool ke kण bhut chhote jiiv hote haim jo hmaare- aas paas kii jyaadaatr vstuom pr rhte haim। yh kण uchch aadrtaa mem pnpte haim jo mृt tvchaa, baiktiiriyaa aur phmgs aadi se apnaa khaanaa praapt krte haim।
2. kiit (Insect)
kiitom se elrjii vaale logom ko kiitom ke kaatne se dmk lgne se tvchaa ekdm laal hokr phool jaatii hai। itnaa hii nhiim unhem ultii, chkkr aanaa aur bukhaar bhii ho sktaa hai।
3. khaanaa (Food)
kuchh logom ko rojmrraa mem khaayii jaane vaalii chiijom se bhii elrjii hotii hai, jaise moomgphlii, doodh aur mdaa aadi। khaady pdaarth se elrjii vaale logom ko khaane ke baad jii michlaane, shriir mem khujlii hone yaa daane niklne kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।
4. rbड़ (Latex)
rbड़ se bnaa koii bhii utpaad, elrjii kaa kaarण ho sktaa hai। kuchh logom ko rbड़ se bne utpaad bhii nuksaan phumchaate haim, jaise dstaane, kmdom, medikl upkrण aadi ke istemaal se jln, naak bhnaa, chhiimknaa, sms kii ghbraaht aur khujlii kii smsyaaem ho sktii haim।
5. khushboo (Fragrance)
achchhii khushboo bhle achchhii lgtii ho lekin yh bhii kuchh logom kii elrjii kaa kaarण ho sktii hai। prphyoom, khushboo vaalii mombttiym, kii trh ke byootii prॉdkt aadi kii khushboo se sir drd, jii michlaane aur naak kii elrjii ho sktii hai।
6. jaanvr (Pets)
paaltu jaanvr bhii kii logom kii elrjii kaa kaarण hote haim। jaanvrom ke baal, unke mumh se niklne vaalii laar, roosii aadi se kii gmbhiir preshaaniym ho sktii haim।
7. ghaas (Grass)
kii baar ghaas, peड़ aur phool bhii elrjii kaa kaarण hote haim। yh sb mausmii elrjii kaa kaarण hote haim, jinse khujlii, mkhom mem jln, lgaataar chhiimk aanaa aur khujlii aadi kii smsyaa ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
elrjii se nijaat paane ke lie upaay (Tips to Prevent Allergy)
- dhool, dhumaa aur gmdgii se bchkr rhem।
- kuchh dvaaom jaise espiriin, nimuslaaid aadi ke sevn mem saavdhaanii brtem।
- khttii chiijom, jaise achaar aadi kaa istemaal km krem।
- aise khaady pdaarth jinhem khaane se elrjii hai, unhem n khaaem।
- gmdgii se elrjii vaale logom ko smy-smy pr chaadr, tkiye ke kvr aur prde aadi bdlte rhne chaahie।

Home Remedies:
dhool (Dust), gmdgii (Dirt), mausm mem privrtn (Climate change), siiln, aadi kuchh aise kaarण haim jinse vykti ko elrjii (Allergy) ho sktii hai। pryaavrण mem maujood chiijom ke lie alg-alg smvednshiiltaa hotii hai jiske chlte hmaaraa shriir prtikriyaa krtaa hai। aise mem vijaatiiy pdaarthom kii shriir mem asviikaartaa elrjii hai।
kuchh logom ko khaane kii chiijom se elrjii ho sktii hai। adhik chhiimkem aanaa, sms lete smy aavaaj honaa, shriir mem kisii trh kii soojn, khujlii, chkkr aanaa, jii ghbraanaa, pet mem mroड़ honaa aadi elrjii ke kuchh lkshण haim।
aaie aapko btaate haim elrjii se bchne ke kuchh ghreloo upaae (Home remedies of Allergy):
1.shhd (Honey)- shhd shriir kii rog prtirodhk kshmtaa ko bढ़aataa hai। rojaanaa do chmmch shhd kaa istemaal shriir ko kaaphii laabh phumchaataa hai। ek gilaas gungune paanii mem shhd milaa kr piine se yaa doodh mem shhd milaa kr piine se kaaphii laabh phumchtaa hai।
2. seb (Apple)- rojaanaa ek seb khaane se imyoon sistm (immune system) behtr hotaa hai aur aap elrjii se door rhte haim। seb kaa joos bhii piiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
3.hldii (Turmeric)- elrjii se bchaane mem hldii bhii kaaphii prbhaavshaalii hai। hldii mem taaktvr emtii ऑksiidemt paae jaate haim jo elrjii se lड़ne mem mdd krte haim। ek gilaas grm doodh mem ek chmmch hldii milaakr piine se kaaphii laabh phumchtaa hai।
4. lhsoon (Garlic)- lhsoon bhii ek emtii elrjii khaady pdaarth hai jise apnii daait mem shaamil krnaa aavshyk hai। yh ek emtii bॉyotik, emtii ऑksiidemt aur imyoonitii bढ़aane vaalaa khaady pdaarth hai। lhsoon ko sbjii mem daalkr yaa subh khaalii pet ek do klii paanii ke saath niglne se kaaphii phaaydaa hotaa hai।
5.niimboo (Lemon)- niimboo mem uchch maatraa mem vitaamin sii aur emtii ऑksiidemt paayaa jaataa hai। niimboo imyoon sistm bढ़aataa hai aur elrjii se door rkhne mem kaaphii phaaydemmd saabit hotaa hai।
6. adrk (Ginger)- adrk ke sevn se sms kii biimaarii mem aaraam miltaa hai। aise mem yh asthmaa se smbmdhit elrjii mem kaaphii aaraam phumchaataa hai। rojaanaa adrk kaa sevn krne se elrjii se raaht paaii jaa sktii hai। dॉktr kii slaah pr adrk ke spliimemt bhii lie jaa skte haim।
7. griin tii (Green tea)- griin tii mem maujood emtiiऑksiidemts shriir kii rog prtirodhk kshmtaa ko bढ़aate haim। ismem maujood thiyaaniin bhii elrjii se bchaane mem mdd krtaa hai। ydi kisii ko griin tii psmd n ho to blaik tii bhii pii jaa sktii hai।
8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam mem vitaamin bii, ii, maigniishiym, jimk, seleniym (selenium) tthaa any svaasthyvrdhk vsaa paaii jaatii hai। jis kaarण yh tnaav se to raaht dete hii haim saath hii elrjii se bchaane mem bhii mdd krte haim। rog prtirodhk kshmtaa ko tej kr shriir aur dimaag ko mjbootii dete haim। baadaam ko bhoon kr yaa kchchaa bhii khaayaa jaa sktaa hai। ydi aise khaanaa smbhv n ho to baadaam kaa paaudr bnaakr, doodh ke saath khaayaa jaa sktaa hai।


Disease: motiyaabimd- keterekt (Cataract)

Description: 
keterekt yaa motiyaabimd (Cataract)
motiyaabimd mkh ke lems mem ubhraa sphed rmg kaa dhbbaa hai, jo ki mkh kii dृshti ko prbhaavit krtaa hai। motiyaabimd hone se vykti ko koii bhii vstu dhumdhlii njr aatii hai। motiyaabimd jyaadaatr bujurgom ko hotaa hai। motiyaabimd kevl ek mkh yaa donom mkhom mem bhii ho sktaa hai, yhm tk ki yh ek mkh se doosrii mkh mem bhii phail sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- mkhom ke lems pr sphed prt kaa jmnaa
- ek mkh se do chiijem njr aanaa
- kii dphaa hlkii roshnii bhii bhut tej prtiit honaa
- kisii bhii vstu kaa rmg hlkaa njr aanaa
- koii bhii vstu dhumdhlii njr aanaa
- chshme kaa nmbr baar-baar bdlnaa
- tej roshnii se preshaanii honaa
- raat kii laait mem chhlle numaa aakृti njr aanaa
- raat ko gaaड़ii chlaane mem dikkt honaa
- shaam hote hii mkhom kii roshnii aur bhii kmjor honaa

Reasons: 
mkh ke mdr kaa lems kaimre kii trh kaam krtaa hai। yhii retinaa pr laait ko phoks krtaa hai jisse chiijem saaph njr aatii haim। lems paanii aur protiin se milkr bntaa hai। protiin is trh se lems ke saath juड़ii rhtii hai ki yh lems ko saaph rkhtii hai jisse ki roshnii aar-paar jaa ske।
umr bढ़ne ke saath kii baar kuchh protiin ek jgh iktthii ho jaatii hai aur lems ke ek hisse pr jmaa ho jaatii hai। aise mem motiyaabimd mkh ke lems mem atydhik protiin ke bnne ke kaarण hotaa hai jo lems ko dhumdhlaa bnaa detaa hai। yh lems ke jrie roshnii ko poorii trh jaane nhiim detaa jisse mkh se saaph dikhaaii nhiim detaa। aise mem sbhii ne lems sels, lems ke baahr kii or jmaa ho jaate haim jbki sbhii puraane lems sels, lems ke biichom biich ek jgh iktthaa ho jaate haim, jise motiyaabimd yaa keterekt khte haim।
motiyaabimd hone ke any kaarण (other reason & causes of cataract)
- mkhom mem kisii trh kaa any rog honaa, jaisaa glookomaa aadi
- jnmjaat mkh mem motiyaabimd honaa
- daaybitiij honaa
- shriir mem kisii preshaanii, jaise asthmaa ke lie sterॉid lenaa
- achaank se tej roshnii ke smprk mem aane se yaa lgaataar tej roshnii mem rhne se
- dhoomrpaan yaa shraab aadi kaa jyaadaa sevn krne se

Treatments:
motiyaabimd ke upaay (tips to prevent cataract)
- dhoop yaa tej roshnii se khud ko bchaaem, mkhom pr chshmaa aur sir pr topii phn ke rhem
- kisii bhii trh kaa koii nshaa n krem
- paushtik khaanaa khaaem
- smy-smy pr mkhom kii jmch krvaaem
- tnaav se door rhem
- daaybitiij niymtrण mem rkhem

Home Remedies:
jb mkhom kii baat ho to smsyaa ko gmbhiirtaa se lenaa chaahie, kyomki ydi mkhom kii roshnii ek baar chlii gii to dobaaraa nhiim paaii jaa sktii। motiyaabimd (Cataract) bhii aisii hii gmbhiir smsyaa hai, jismem mkhom ke lems pr ek dhbbaa (spot on the eye lens) aa jaataa hai। jisse aap jo bhii chiij dekhte haim vh aapko dhumdhlii njr aatii hai aur vhm aapko dhbbaa jaisaa njr aataa hai।
yoom to motiyaabimd ko srjrii ke dvaaraa htaayaa jaa sktaa hai lekin kuchh ghreloo nuskhom kii mdd se bhii motiyaabimd kaa ilaaj smbhv hai। ydi shurooaat mem schet hokr yh apnaae jaaem to smbhv hai aapko srjrii yaa ऑpreshn n krvaanaa pड़e।
motiyaabimd ke lie ghreloo nuskh़e (Home Remedies for Cataract)
lhsun (Garlic)
lhsun ke asmkhy svaasthy laabh haim aur yh mkhom ke lie bhii smaan roop se laabhkaarii hai। lhsun kii do se tiin kliym (2 to 3 clove) rojaanaa khaane se mkhom se ekdm saaph dikhaaii dene lgegaa aur kuchh hii dinom mem dhbbe kii shikaayt door ho jaaegii।
paalk (Spinach)
paalk khaane se motiyaabimd kaaphii hd tk thiik ho jaataa hai। paalk mem biitaa kairotiin (Beta Carotene) or emtiiऑksiidemt (Antioxidents) guण hote haim। paalk ko rojaanaa khaane se mkhom kaa motiyaabimd kuchh din mem hii khtm ho jaataa hai aur mkhem phle jaisii ho jaatii haim।
doodh aur baadaam (Milk and Almond)
motiyaabimd se preshaan logom kii mkhem jyaadaatr laal rhtii haim aur smsyaa se niptnaa aur bhii mushkil hotaa hai। aise mem doodh aur baadaam mkhom ko laabh dete haim। upchaar ke lie baadaam ko raat bhr doodh mem bhigaakr chhoड़ dem। is doodh ko subh chhaankr iskii boomde mkhom mem daalem aur baadaam ko chbaa kr khaa lem।
griin tii (Green Tea)
griin tii se mkhom kii roshnii tej ho sktii hai। griin tii saamaany mkhom kii smsyaa mem bhii laabhkaarii hai। rojaanaa tiin se chaar baar griin tii piine mkhom ko svaasthy laabh hotaa hai। griin tii mem maujood emtiiऑksiidemt (Antioxident) mkhom ko nii taajgii dete haim।
kchchaa ppiitaa (Raw Papaya)
kchche ppiite mem ppen (Papain) naam kaa emjaaim hotaa hai jo ki protiin (Protien) ke paachn mem shaayk hotaa hai। motiyaabimd se preshaan logom ko protiin ko pchaane mem dikkt aatii hai, aise mem kchchaa ppiitaa motiyaabimd se grsit logom ko laabh detaa hai। kchchaa ppiitaa rojaanaa istemaal krne se mkhom ke lems ne jaise chmkne lgte haim।
vitaamin sii (Vitamin C)
motiyaabimd ke ilaaj mem vitaamin sii mhtvpoorण bhoomikaa nibhaataa hai। vitaamin sii ke sevn se motiyaabimd smrchnaaom ko rokaa jaa sktaa hai। aahaar mem aise khaady pdaarthom ko istemaal krem, jinmem vitaamin sii jyaadaa se jyaadaa ho। iske alaavaa vitaamin sii spliimemt (Vitamin C Suppliment) ke roop mem bhii liyaa jaa sktaa hai।
kchchii sbjiym (Raw Vegetables)
kchchii sbjiym mkhom ke lie chmtkaar kaa kaam kr sktii hai। kchchii sbjiyom mem poshk ttv aur vitaamin e (Vitamin A) kii uchch maatraa hotii hai jo ki mkhom ke svaasthy ke lie jroorii hai। apne dainik aahaar mem kchchii sbjiyom ko istemaal krne se motiyaabimd ke saath hii mkhom kii any saamaany smsyaaom se bhii niptaa jaa sktaa hai। kchchii sbjiyom ko slaad ke roop mem jitnaa smbhv ho khaaem।
jaamun (Bilberrys)
jaamun se motiyaabimd poorii trh nhiim httaa lekin dृshti kii aspshttaa ko jaamun khaane se thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। jaamun mem emthosaaynosaaids (Anthocyanosides) tthaa phlevnaaids (Flavonoids) kaaphii adhik hote haim jo ki retinaa (Retina) aur mkhom ke laims (Eye Lens) kii rkshaa krte haim।


Disease: srdii aur kph (Cough And Cold)

Description: 
srdii aur kph (Cough and Cold)
naak bh rhii hai, yaa bmd hai jisse ki sms lene mem tkliiph ho rhii hai, gle mem drd mhsoos ho rhaa hai yaa gle mem chubhn aur chhilaa (scratchy throat) jaise mhsoos ho rhaa hai aur khmsii ke saath blgm (muscus) preshaan kr rhaa hai to smjh liijie aap srdii- jukaam aur kph se preshaan haim।

Symptoms: 
- mkhom se khoob paanii aanaa aur jln honaa
- aavaaj bhaarii honaa
- khaane mem svaad aur khushboo mhsoos n honaa
- glaa chhilaa huaa yaa drd mhsoos honaa
- chhiimk aanaa
- naak kaa bmd honaa
- naak se khoob paanii girnaa
- naak se gle kii or blgm kaa girnaa
- mmspeshiyom mem drd yaa khimchaav honaa
- sir bhaarii mhsoos honaa yaa hlkaa drd honaa

Reasons: 
kaarण- (Cause of Cough and Cold)
srdii hinovaayrs (rhinovirus) se phailtii hai jo ki 10 se 40 prtisht tk srdii ko shriir mem prvesh kraataa hai। vhiim koronaavaayrs (coronavirus) lgbhg 20 prtisht srdii ke lie jimmedaar hotaa hai। inke alaavaa respiiretrii simsiitaayl vaayrs (respiratory syncytial virus) aur pairaaimphlooemjaa vaayrs (parainfluenza virus) 10 phiisdii tk srdii ke lie jimmedaar hote haim।
srdii, smkrmण se bhii phailtii hai। ek smkrmit vykti yaa uske dvaaraa istemaal kie ge saamaan ke smprk mem aane se doosre ko bhii srdii kii smsyaa ho sktii hai। yh vaayrs shriir ke mdr phumchkr vykti kii rog kshmtaa ko prbhaavit krte haim aur kaaphii maatraa mem blgm bnaanaa shuroo kr dete haim, jisse glaa aur naak poorii trh prbhaavit ho jaate haim। itnaa hii nhiim smkrmit vykti ke chhiimkne (sneezing), usse haath milaane se bhii srdii ke baiktiiriyaa doosre vykti ko prbhaavit kr skte haim।
srdii aur kph ke lie kii any kaarण (Other causes of Cough and Cold)
- kmre mem siiln yaa ghutn ho
- tej dhoop se aane ke baad turmt thmdaa paanii piinaa
- shriir kii prtirodhk kshmtaa kmjor honaa
- bhut tej prphyoom yaa tel kaa istemaal
- ऑphis yaa ghr ke baahr binaa haath saaph kie khaanaa-piinaa

Treatments:
srdii se raaht ke lie tips (Tips to prevent cough and cold)
- aaraam krem, khoob pey pdaarth lem aur svaasthyvrdhk khaanaa khaaem।
- ydi bukhaar yaa shriir mem drd ho to pairaasitaamॉl lii jaa sktii hai।
- naak pr baam yaa baajaar mem maujood spre kaa istemaal kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। isse bmd naak khulegii aur raaht milegii।
- grm paanii mem nmk daal kr graare krte rhem।
- khaane-piine se phle apne haath achchhii trh dhoem।
- smkrmik vykti ke smprk mem n aaem, jaise ki haath milaane kii jgh nmste kii jaa sktii hai।
- ydi aap khud smkrmit haim to bhiiड़ vaalii jghom pr jaane se bchem aur apnii chiijem jaise roomaal aadi doosrom se door rkhem।
- thmdii aur baahr kii chiijem khaane se prhej krem।

Home Remedies:
mausm mem privrtn, srd-grm hone yaa prdooshण aur elrjii (Allergy) yaa smkrmण (Infection) ke kaarण srdii-khmsii kii smsyaa ho jaatii hai। kii baar smkrmण bhii iskaa kaarण hotaa hai।
aaie jaante haim, srdii khmsii se bchaav ke ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Cough and Cold):
1. hldii (Turmeric)- aadhaa kp grm paanii ko ubaal lem phir usmem ek chmmch kaalii mirch paaudr (black pepper powder), ek chmmch hldii paaudr aur ek chmmch shhd milaaem। ab is mishrण ko do se tiin mint tk ubaal lem aur niymit taur pr kaaढ़e kii trh piiem।
2. adrk (Ginger)- adrk ko ghiskr yaa chhote-chhote tukड़om mem kaatkr ek kp paanii mem daalkr ubaal lem। din bhr mem tiin se chaar baar is ghol ko piiem। shhd aur niimboo ko adrk ke rs mem milaakr piine se bhii kph kii shikaayt door hotii hai।
3. niimboo (Lemon)- ek chmmch shhd mem do chmmch niimboo kaa rs milaakr grm kr lem। din bhr mem kii baar is ghol ko dvaa kii trh lete rhem।
4. lhsun (Garlic)- laumg ke tel aur shhd mem lhsun kii do se tiin klii ko piis kr milaa lem। din bhr mem kii baar thoड़ii thoड़ii maatraa mem iskaa sevn krte rhem।
5. pyaaj (Onion)- ek chmmch shhd mem aadhaa chmmch pyaaj kaa rs lem aur isko milaakr din bhr mem km se km do baar avshy sevn krem। kph aur gle kii khraash se raaht milegii।
6. grm trl pdaarth piiem (Drink warm liquids)- grm paanii piiem ye gle kii soojn (throat sweeling) ke lie phaaydemmd hai। aap chaahem to koii any grm pdaarth bhii pii skte haim।
7. shhd (Honey)- shhd gle ko aaraam phumchaane ke lie ek paarmprik upaay hai। ek gilaas grm paanii mem shhd aur niimboo kaa rs milaakr din mem tiin baar piine se khm~sii se raaht miltii hai।
8. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)- seb kaa sirkaa hr trh kii khm~sii ke lie achchhaa hai। 2 bड़aa chmmch sirkaa 10 tolaa paanii mem milaakr grm krem। ismem ek chmmch shhd daalkr piiem। khmsii mem raaht paane kaa kaargr upaay hai।
9. tulsii ke ptte aur shhd (Honey and basil leaves)- dhule hue tulsii ke kuchh pttom ko koot kr uskaa rs nikaalem aur usme shhd milaaem। ab ise chmmch mem grm krke din mem 3-4 baar lem, is ghreloo upaay se khmsii mem jldii aaraam miltaa hai।


Disease: titns (Tetanus)

Description: 
titns (Tetanus)
mnushyom ke ghaav (Wound) mem smkrmण hone se titns hotaa hai jiskaa kaarण klostriidiym titaanii baiktiiriyaa (Clostridium Tetani Bacteria) hai। yhii jiivaaणu ghaav yaa chot mem vish paidaa krtaa hai jisse titns ho jaataa hai। dhiire-dhiire yhii jhr poore shriir mem phailne lgtaa hai jisse sthiti ghaatk ho jaatii hai। titns ke kaarण kii baar vykti kii mृtyu bhii ho sktii hai। titns mem shriir kii mmspeshiyom mem aimthn mhsoos hotii hai aur rook rook kr drd hotaa hai। haalmki kisii chot ke lgne ke baad ydi turmt titns kaa tiikaa lgvaayaa jaae to isse hone vaalii preshaaniyom se bchaa jaa sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- uchch rktchaap
- grdn mem aimthn honaa
- chiड़chiड़aapn
- chehre kii mmspeshiyom kaa jkड़ jaanaa
- jbड़e kaa bmd ho jaanaa
- niglne mem dikkt honaa
- psiinaa khoob aanaa
- mmspeshiyom mem aimthn aur akड़n mhsoos honaa
- sms lene mem tkliiph honaa
- hृdy gti kaa tej honaa

Reasons: 
titns kaa kaarण (Cause of Tetanus)
klostriidiym titaanii (Clostridium Tetani)chhड़ ke aakr kaa jiivaaणu hai jo duniyaa bhr mem mittii mem paayaa jaataa hai। klostriidiym titaanii titns rog ke lie jimmedaar jiivaaणu hai। yh baiktiiriyaa do roopom mem paayaa jaataa hai, phlaa dormmt yaa nishkriy roop mem doosraa skriy roop mem jo jiivaaणuom kii smkhyaa ko aur bhii bढ़aa detaa hai। kisii bhii trh kii chot mem titns ho sktii hai।
- ghaav se
- srjrii mem
- prsv ke dauraan
- koii phoड़aa hone pr
- suii yaa imjekshn se nshaa krne vaalom ko
- kisii puraane jmg lge lohe se chot lgne se

Treatments:
titns se bchne ke lie tips (Tips to Prevent Tetanus)
- koii bhii aisaa ghaav jisse tvchaa pht gii ho, use turmt paanii aur saabun se saaph kiyaa jaanaa chaahie।
- ghaav ko kbhii khulaa n chhoड़em। khule ghaav ke smkrmण kaa khtraa jyaadaa hotaa hai।
- ydi ghaav se khoon bh rhaa ho to to us pr sootii aur sookhaa kpड़aa bmdhem।
- rkt ko rokne ke lie ghaav ke oopr dbaav daalem, jisse rkt bhnaa rook jaae।
- ghaayl vykti ko turmt titns kaa tiikaa lgvaanaa chaahie।
titns  ke any upchaar (Treatment of Tetanus)
- ghaav ko grm paanii se dhoem aur koii emtiiseptik kriim yaa paaudr lgaaem। 
- taarpiin ke tel se shriir kii maalish krem, ismem pair, jbड़e aur grdn pr hlke haath se dbaav daalte hue maalish krem। 
- ghaav ke oopr tel ko grm krke usmem hldii milaakr lgaaem
- mombttii ke mom ko pighlaakr bhii ghaav pr lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai
- kte sthaan pr niim kaa tel lgaane se bhii titns kaa dr nhiim rhtaa


Disease: moch (Sprains)

Description: 
moch (Sprains)
shriir ke joड़ ke ligaamemt (ligament) yaa snaayu jb kisii chot ke kaarण jroort se jyaadaa khimch jaate haim to is avsthaa ko moch (Sprains or Moch) khaa jaataa hai। jyaadaa khimchaav ke kaarण peshiyom ke phaaibr pht jaate haim aur ligaamemt mem ghaav ho jaataa hai। ligaamemt ek hddii ko doosrii hddii se joड़ne (connect) kaa kaary krte haim।

Symptoms: 
- chot vaalii jgh pr ashniiy drd
- chot vaalii jgh pr sunnpn honaa
- prbhaavit sthaan ko moड़ne yaa chlaane mem preshaanii honaa
- prbhaavit sthaan pr niilaa yaa kaalaa dhbbaa aanaa
- prbhaavit sthaan pr soojn aanaa
- binaa shaare ke chlne phirne mem dikkt honaa

Reasons: 
moch ke kaarण- (Causes of Sprains)
moch shriir ke alg-alg hissom mem alg-alg kaarणom se aa sktii hai। moch saamaany yaa kronik bhii ho sktii hai।
1. emkl mem moch (Ankle Sprains)- oomchii-niichii jgh pr chlne yaa dauड़ne se emkl mem moch aa sktii hai। kii baar haaii hiil phnne se pair achaank se muड़taa hai, yh bhii pair mem moch kaa kaarण ho sktaa hai।
2. ghutne mem moch (Knee Sprains)- bhaagte- bhaagte achaank gir jaane yaa koii bhaarii vstu uthaakr chlne se ghutnom mem moch aa sktii hai। kii baar chlte chlte achaank ghutnaa muड़ jaataa hai। yh bhii ghutne mem moch kaa kaarण ho sktaa hai।
3. klaaii mem moch (Wrist Sprains)- girne ke dauraan haath ke muड़ne, kisii ke dvaaraa haath ko glt triike se khiimchne, khel ke dauraan aadi sthitiyom mem klaaii mem moch aa sktii hai।
4. kmr mem moch (Waist Sprains)- kii baar siiढ़iym chढ़ne utrne mem dikkt hone yaa, kisii oomchii jgh se kmr ke bl girne se yaa jroort se jyaadaa bhaarii chiij ko jhukkr uthaane se kmr mem moch aa sktii hai।
5. mgoothe mem moch (Thumb Sprains)- kii trh ke khel khelne yaa khiim mgoothaa db jaane ke kaarण chot lgne se mgoothe mem moch aa sktii hai।
6. grdn mem moch (Neck Sprains)- achaank se grdn mem jhtkaa lgne, jyaadaa oomchaa tkiyaa lgaane, kisii prkaar se grdn mem chot lgne kii sthiti mem grdn mem moch aa sktii hai।
any kaarण (other causes & reason of sprains)
- kii baar vyaayaam krne se phle vaarmap n honaa aur achaank se kthin vyaayaam shuroo kr denaa bhii moch aane kaa kaarण ho sktaa hai।
- pair mem prॉpr phutviyr n hone se bhii pair ke muड़ne yaa chot lgne kaa khtraa bढ़ jaataa hai jisse moch kii smbhaavnaa rhtii hai।

Treatments:
moch se nijaat ke lie upaay (Treatment of Sprain Pain)
- moch se nijaat ke lie prbhaavit sthaan pr chne bmdh dem। in chnom ko baar- baar bhigaate rhem। jaise jaise chne phoolemge, moch thiik hotii jaaegii।
- moch vaale sthaan pr ermd ke pttom ko hlkaa saa semk kr us pr srsom kaa tel lgaakr, prbhaavit sthaan pr bmdh dem।
- til ke tel mem aphiim milaakr moch vaale sthaan pr bmdh dem।
- moch vaale sthaan pr hldii, choonaa aur shhd ko milaakr lgaane se chot thiik ho jaatii hai।
- moch se nijaat ke lie tejpttaa aur laumg ko piiskr lep lgaaem।
- srsom ke tel mem ajvaayn aur lhsun ko grm krke, is tel se moch vaale sthaan kii maalish krem।
- paan ke ptte pr srsom kaa tel lgaakr use hlkaa grm krem aur moch vaale sthaan pr bmdhem ।
- tulsii pttom ke rs mem srsom kaa tel milaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। turmt aaraam milegaa।
- akhrot ke tel se maalish krne pr bhii chot mem aaraam miltaa hai।
- nmk ko grm krke, kisii mote kpड़e mem bmdhkr, chot vaale sthaan pr bmdh dem। aaraam milegaa।
- nmk aur hldii ko milaakr chot vaale sthaan pr lgaane se bhii aaraam milegaa।
- paan ke ptte yaa aam ke ptte pr tel lgaakr, us pr nmk lgaaem aur grm krke chot vaale sthaan pr bmdh dem। aisaa krne se bhii moch thiik ho jaaegii।
- moch aur soojn mem eloveraa lgaane se bhii aaraam miltaa hai।

Home Remedies:
oomchii eड़ii ke joote-chppl phnne, pair oomche niiche pड़ne, vyaayaam bhut jyaadaa yaa glt trh se krne, bhut jyaadaa chlne, glt trh se uthne baithne aadi aise kuchh kaarण haim, jinse shriir mem moch (sprain) kii sthiti bn jaatii hai। kii dphaa drd ashniiy bhii ho sktaa hai aur prbhaavit jgh pr laal yaa niilaa nishaan aur soojn bhii aa sktii hai। ydi khimchaav kii preshaanii ho to pairom ko thणd se bchaayem aur aise kpड़e kaa chunaav krem jo thणd ke dinom mem aapke pairom ko hvaa n lgne dem।
aaie jaanem moch se raaht ke ghreloo upaay (Home remedies for sprain):
1. grm aur thmdaa semk (Hot and cold compress)- shriir ke drd vaale hisse pr krm se grm aur thmde paanii kaa sek krem, ye tnaavgrst mmspeshiyom ko aaraam phumchaaegaa। ise kii triike se kr skte haim jaise ki tauliye ko grm paanii mem dubaayem aur tnaavgrst mmspeshii pr lgaa skte haim। tnaavgrst mmspeshii mem aaraam ke lie gungune paanii se nhaayaa jaa sktaa hai yaa bhaap le skte haim। brph lgaakr bhii aaraam paa skte haim।
2. mmspeshii ko khiimchnaa (Stretch your muscle)- din prtidin kii saamaany shaariirik prkriyaa ke liye jaane se phle, mmspeshiyom ko khiimchnaa mhtvpoorण hotaa hai। iske lie hlkii hlkii strechimg krem। agr aapko raat mem sote smy pairom mem khimchaav hotaa hai, to achchhaa hogaa ki aap mmspeshiyom ko khiimchne kaa abhyaas krem।
3. trl pdaarth lete rhem (Take enough liquid)- trl pdaarth ke saath paanii ko niymit mtraal pr lekr shriir mem nmii bnaayem rkhem। 8 gilaas paanii piine ke saath aapko phlom kaa joos bhii piinaa chaahiye। pryaapt maatraa mem trl lenaa aapke mmspeshiyom mem km mroड़ paidaa kregaa aur aaraam degaa।
4. kelaa (Banana)- kele mem pryaapt maatraa mem potaishiym hotaa hai। yh shriir ke liye behd achchhaa hotaa hai। agr naashte yaa bhojn ke baad prtidin ek kelaa khaate haim to yh mmspeshiyom ko mroड़ se door rkhegaa aur khimchaav se raaht degaa।
5. grm paid se sikaaii (Hot pad)- ek smy aisaa thaa jb log grm paanii ko paid pr daalkr phir istemaal krte the aur shriir pr lgaakr sbhii prkaar ke drd se door rhte the। lekin ab baaज़aar mem bijlii se chlne vaale grm paid maujood haim। in paid se sikaaii krne se mmspeshiyom kaa khimchaav door hotaa hai aur drd se raaht miltii hai।
6. maalish (Massage)- prbhaavit hisse kii maalish krnaa bhii behd raaht detaa hai। kisii bhii tel ko thoड़aa gungunaa krke, usmem lhsun kii kuchh kliym daalem। kuchh der is tel ko aur grm krem aur gungunaa rhne pr prbhaavit hisse kii hlke haathom se maalish krem। kuchh hii der mem pairom mem khimchaav km hogaa aur drd mem bhii aaraam milegaa।


Disease: nimn rktchaap yaa lo bldpreshr (Low Blood Pressure)

Description: 
nimn rktchaap yaa lo bldpreshr (Low Blood Pressure)
lo bldpreshr yaa nimn rktchaap, ऑksiijn (oxygen) ko dimaag tk jaane se roktaa hai। kevl ऑksiijn hii nhii blki any poshk ttv bhii dimaag tk nhiim phumch paate। bldpreshr ko svaasthy kii bhaashaa mem haaipotemshn (hypotension) ke naam se jaante haim।
yoom to lo bldpreshr koii biimaarii nhiim hotii lekin yh shriir mem pnp rhii any gmbhiir biimaarii kaa smket hotii hai। aise mem jb kisii ke shriir mem rkt-prvaah saamaany se km ho jaataa hai to use nimn rktchaap yaa lo bld preshr khte hai। naarml bld preshr 120/80 hotaa hai। aise mem dil, kidnii, phephड़e aur dimaag mshik roop se yaa poorii trh se kaam krnaa bhii bmd kr skte haim।

Symptoms: 
- mkhom ke aage mdheraa chhaanaa
- ultii aur daayriyaa
- grdn kaa akड़ jaanaa
- chkkr aanaa
- chhaatii mem drd, sms phoolnaa
- haathom aur pairom kaa thmdaa honaa
- hृdy mem misd biits mhsoos kii jaatii hai

Reasons: 
bld preshr km hone ke kaarण (causes of low blood pressure)
1. dil kii biimaarii (heart disease)- bldpreshr km honaa dil kii gmbhiir biimaarii se juड़aa hotaa hai, dil kii biimaarii se haart kii mmspeshiym kmjor ho jaatii haim, jisse haart pryaapt khoon ko pmp nhiim kr paataa aur hmaaraa biipii lo rhne lgtaa hai। dil ke mriijom aur eniimiyaa ke rogii lo biipii ko lekr saavdhaan rhem।
2. aarthostetik haaiprtemshn taaip (arthostetic hypertension type)- ismem mriij ko khड़e hone pr chkkr aate haim, kyomki uskaa bld preshr ekdm se 20 pॉimt niiche aa jaataa hai। yh nrvs sistm pr aadhaarit hotaa hai। lekin kii baar dvaaom ke saaid iphekt se yaa elrjii se bhii ho sktii hai।
3. khoon kii kmii tthaa any kaa (less blood and other reason)- shriir ke mdroonii mgom se khoon bh jaane yaa khoon kii kmii se, khaane mem paushtiktaa kii kmii yaa aniymittaa se, phephड़om ke ataik se, haart kaa vॉlv khraab ho jaane se, lo biipii ho sktaa hai। achaank sdmaa lgne, koii bhyaavh dृshy dekhne yaa khbr sunne se bhii lo biipii ho sktaa hai।
iske alaavaa (other reason & causes of low blood pressure)
- grbhaavsthaa, haarmon asmtuln jaise ki thaayrॉid kii skriytaa km ho jaanaa
- bld shugr dvaaom ke prbhaav se
- strok tthaa liivr smbmdhii biimaariym
- kuchh aavshyk vitaamin jaise bii12 aur aayrn kii kmii

Treatments:
bldpreshr lo hai to kyaa krem (some tips to prevent low blood pressure)
- turmt baith yaa let jaaem, mutthiym bhiimchem, bmdhem, kholem, pair hilaayem।
- nmk aur chiinii vaalaa paanii yaa chaay piiem। pairom ke niiche do tkie lgaakr letem।
- jo log phle se haaii biipii kii dvaa khaa rhe haim, ve dvaa khaanaa bmd kr dem।
- km se km aath gilaas paanii aur any pey roj piiem।
- bhojn mem kaarbohaaidret kii maatraa km kr dem।
- in sb ke alaavaa turnt dॉktrii slaah lem।

Home Remedies:
- nimn rktchaap se piiड़it log nmk jyaadaa khaaem
- lgaataar chkkr aa rhe hom, to paanii jyaadaa piiem
- ek kp shkrkmd kaa joos din mem do baar piiem
- mittii ke brtn mem raatbhr kishmish bhigaakr rkhem। subh kishmish chbaakr khaaem aur paanii pii lem
- subh khaalii pet tulsii ke ptte ke rs mem shhd milaakr khaaem
- raat mem baadaam bhigaakr rkhem, subh in baadaam ke chhilke utaarkr piis lem aur doodh ke saath ubaalem। is doodh ko gungunaa piiem।


Disease: sphed baal- gre heyr (Grey Hair)

Description: 
sphed baal- gre heyr (Grey hair)
umr ke saath baalom kaa sphed honaa praakृtik hai lekin kii baar km umr mem hii baal sphed hone lgte haim। aisaa kii baar haarmonl gड़bड़ii, bdltii laaiphstaail aur prdooshण vaale maahaul ke kaarण bhii ho sktaa hai। maujoodaa smy mem tiinej mem hii bchchom ke baal sphed hone lgte haim।

Symptoms: 
- umr se phle baal sphed ho jaanaa
- baal naajuk honaa
- baal ptle ho jaanaa
- baalom kaa tekschr ख़raab honaa

Reasons: 
kaarण- (Cause of Grey Hair)
melaanin ke aadhaar pr hii baalom kaa rmg kaalaa, sphed yaa bhooraa hotaa hai। jinke baalom mem melaanin kii kmii hotii hai unke baalom kaa rmg hlkaa hotaa hai jinke baalom mem melaanin jyaadaa hotaa hai unke baal kaale hote haim। jin logom ke baal sphed ho jaate haim unke baalom mem melaanin khtm ho jaataa hai। melaanin pigmemt baalom ke phॉliikl mem rhtaa hai। kuchh maamlom mem thॉiraaid, aniimiyaa yaa aanuvmshik kaarणom se bhii baal sphed ho skte haim।
baal sफ़ed hone ke any kaarण (Other Reasons & Causes of Gray Hair)
- vitaamin bii, aayrn aur kॉpr tthaa aayodiin jaise ttvom kii kmii se baal sphed hote haim। jin logom ke khaane mem in minrl kii kmii hotii hai unke baal smy se phle sphed hone lgte haim।
- aise vykti jo bhut jyaadaa gussail hote haim yaa bhut jldii tnaav mem aate unke baal bhii jldii sphed hone lgte haim।
- kuchh vyktiyom mem umr se phle baalom kaa sphed honaa aanuvmshik hotaa hai।
- bhut lmbe smy tk kisii biimaarii se piiड़it rhne yaa jldii jldii biimaar pड़ne vaale logom ke baal bhii umr se phle sphed hone lgte haim।
- baalom kii dekhbhaal thiik prkaar se n kii jaae yaa baalom kii sphaaii kaa dhyaan n rkhaa jaae to bhii baal umr se phle sphed hone lgte haim।
- bhut jyaadaa rsaayn vaale shaimpoo yaa baalom ke utpaad jaise ki heyr klr yaa jel aadi istemaal krne vaale logom ke baal bhii jldii sphed hone lgte haim।
- bhut jyaadaa prdooshण vaale maahaul yaa dhoop mem rhne se bhii baalom kaa rmg uड़ne lgtaa hai।

Treatments:
baalom ko kaalaa krne ke lie upchaar (Tips & Remedies to prevent gray hair)
- kchche ppiite kaa pest sir pr tkriibn 10 mint lgaakr rkhem। aisaa krne se kuchh hii dinom mem baalom kaa jhड़naa rookegaa saath hii baal kaale bhii homge। itnaa hii nhiim baalom se demdrph bhii khtm hogaa।
- baal dhone ke lie kemikl shaimpoo kaa istemaal bmd krem, iskii jgh besn aur doodh yaa dhii kaa istemaal krem। aisaa krne se baalom kaa praakृtik rmg bnaa rhegaa।
- baal dhone ke lie mvlaa paaudr aur niimboo kaa istemaal krem। shikaakaaii aur riithaa milaakr ghr pr hii shaimpoo bhii bnaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
- sir mem laal pyaaj ko piiskr uskaa rs lgaaem। aisaa krne se bhii sphed baal kaale hone lgte haim saath hii baalom kaa jhड़naa bhii bmd ho jaataa hai।
- dhii mem kaalii mirch aur niimboo kaa rs milaakr sir kii tvchaa aur baalom pr lgaaem। tkriibn aadhe ghmte baad baal dho dem, aisaa krne se baal kaale hone lgemge।
- desii ghii bhii sphed baalom ko kaalaa krne kaa srl upaay hai। tel kii jgh desii ghii se baalom kii msaaj krem।
- mvle kaa pryog khaane mem bhii krem। mvlaa khaane se bhii baal kaale hote haim।

Home Remedies:
aajkl umr se phle hii baalom kaa pknaa yaa sphed honaa aam smsyaa bntii jaa rhii hai। baalom kii thiik se dekhbhaal n ho paane aur prdooshण ke kaarण, hmaare baal asmy hii sphed ho jaate haim। baalom ko klr krnaa is smsyaa kaa koii upchaar nhiim hai lekin kuchh ghreloo upchaar aajmaakr aap apne baalom ko sphed hone se rok skte haim।
jaanie sphed baalom ko kaalaa krne ke ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Grey Hair)
1. pyaaj kaa rs (Onion juice)- kuchh dinom tk, nhaane se 1/2 ghmtaa phle rojaanaa sir mem pyaaj kaa pest lgaaem। isse baal kaale hone lgemge।
2. kchchaa ppiitaa (Raw papaya)- sptaah mem km se km 3 din ds mint tk kchche ppiite kaa pest sir mem lgaaem। isse baal nhiim jhड़emge aur kaale bhii hone lgemge।
3. naariyl tel (Coconut oil)- bhृmgraaj aur ashvgmdhaa kii jड़em baalom ke lie vrdaan maanii jaatii haim। inkaa pest naariyl ke tel ke saath baalom kii jड़om mem lgaaem aur 1 ghmte baad gungune paanii se achchhii trh se baal dho lem। isse bhii baal kaale hote haim।
4. niimboo kaa rs (Lemon jiuce)- niimboo ke rs mem mvlaa paaudr milaakr use sir pr lgaane se bhii sphed baal kaale ho jaate haim।
5. desii ghii (Desi ghee)- prtidin shuddh ghii se sir kii maalish krne se bhii sphed baal kaale hote haim।
6. adrk (Ginger)- adrk ko kddooks kr shhd mem milaa lem। ise baalom pr km se km sptaah mem do baar niymit roop se lgaaem। baalom kaa sफ़ed honaa km ho jaaegaa।
7. jaitoon kaa tel (Olive oil)- jaitoon ke tel ko hlkaa grm krem। ismem 4 graam kpoor milaakr is tel se maalish krem। iskii maalish se kuchh hii smy mem roosii khtm ho jaaegii aur baal bhii kaale rhemge।
8. mvlaa (Aamla)- mvle ke paaudr mem niimboo kaa rs milaakr use niymit roop se lgaaem। shaimpoo ke baad mvlaa paaudr paanii mem gholkr lgaane se bhii baalom kii kmdiishnimg hotii hai, aur baal bhii kaale hote haim। mvlaa kisii naa kisii rup me sevn bhii avshy krte rhem।
9. til kaa tel (Sesame oil)- srdiyom mem til adhik se adhik khaaem। til kaa tel bhii baalom ko kaalaa krne mem mdd krtaa hai।
10. kaalii mirch (Black pepper)- aadhaa kp dhii mem chutkii bhr kaalii mirch aur chmmch bhr niimboo rs milaakr baalom mem lgaae। 15 mint baad baal dho lem। sphed baal phir se kaale hone lgemge।
11. memhdii (Henna)- lohe kii kड़aahii mem ek ktorii mehmdii paaudr, do bड़e chmmch chaay kaa paanii, do chmmch mvlaa paaudr, ek chmmch niimboo kaa rs, do chmmch dhii, shikaakaaii v riithaa paaudr, ek mdaa (agr aap lenaa chaahem to), aadhaa chmmch naariyl tel v thoड़aa-saa ktthaa daalkr raat ko bhigo dem। ise subh baalom mem lgaaem, phir do ghmte baad dho lem। isse baal binaa kisii nuksaan ke kaale ho jaaem~ge। aisaa maah mem km se km ek baar avshy krem।


Disease: hddii phraikchr yaa hddii kaa khisknaa (Bone Fracture Or Dislocation)

Description: 
hddii phraikchr yaa hddii kaa khisknaa (Bone fracture or dislocation)
phraikchr (Fracture)- hddii kaa tootnaa hii hddii kaa phraikchr khlaataa hai। hddii kii kaarणom se toot sktii hai, khiim girne se, tkkr lgne se, jhtkaa lgne se yaa achaank se dbaav pड़ne pr।
hddii kaa khisknaa (Dislocation of bone) - do hddiym jb juड़e hue sthaan se khisk jaatii haim to ise dislokeshn yaa hddii kaa khisknaa khte haim। do hddiym ek joड़ pr jaakr miltii haim, lekin is joड़ pr chot lgne ke kaarण isii joड़ se hddiym khisk jaatii haim। hddiyom ke khiskne pr bhii bhut drd hotaa hai aur smbmdhit sthaan pr soojn aa jaatii hai।

Symptoms: 
- ashniiy trh se drd honaa
- aas-paas kii tmtrikaaom mem kshti ke kaarण akड़n
- phraikchr kii jgh pr soojn aa jaanaa
- phraikchr ke aas-paas ke utkom mem asthirtaa
- phraikchr vaale sthaan kaa poorii trh se kaam bmd kr denaa
- behosh honaa

Reasons: 
kaarण- (Causes of bone frtacture or dislocation)
phraikchr ke kii kaarण ho skte haim। hddiyom ke kmjor hone yaa hddiyom se smbmdhit kaimsr, sist, ऑstiyoporosis aadi hone se। phraikchr ke baad hddii mem drd ke bhii kii kaarण ho skte haim-
- hddiyom ke aas-paas ke nrv edimgs, jo hddii ke tootne pr skriy hokr dimaag ko drd kaa smket dete haim।
- hddiym tootne se rktstraav kaa honaa aur soojn aanaa, jisse drd hotaa hai।
- phraikchr hone pr mmspeshiym sikuड़ kr hddii ko bchaane kii koshish krtii haim, yh bhii drd kaa kaarण hotaa hai।
- aisii koii durghtnaa hone pr jisse hddiym prbhaavit hom।
- hddiyom kaa phraikchr vykti kii umr pr bhii nirbhr krtaa hai kyomki jyaadaa umr mem phraikchr ke chmses bढ़ jaate haim।
kuchh sthitiyom mem ashniiy drd bhii ho sktaa hai jaise-
- smkrmण hone pr
- glt triike se plaastr lgaane pr, bhut dhiilaa yaa bhut taait

Treatments:
upchaar- (Tips to prevent bone fracture or dislocation)
- phraikchr vaalii jgh kii brph se sikaaii krem। soojn km hogii aur drd se aaraam milegaa।
- piiड़it vykti ko poorii trh aaraam krnaa chaahie। smbhv ho to smbmdhit jgh ko hilaane-dulaane se bchem।
- grm sikaaii krne se bhii aaraam miltaa hai।
- ydi haath yaa pair kii hddii tootii ho to use oomchaaii pr krke rkhem।
- phraikchr vaale sthaan ke aas-paas kii jgh pr maalish krem।
- aadhaa anaanaas roj khaaem।
- red miit khaane se bchem।
- prijrvetiv khaanaa n khaaem।
saavdhaaniym~- (Precautions)
- kaar mem baithkr hmeshaa siit belt phnem।
- koii khel khelte smy yaa saaikil aur motrsaaikil chlaate smy, smbmdhit sephtii upkrण jroor phnem।
- ydi kisii ko ऑstiiporosis hai, to niymit vyaayaam krem aur hddiyom ko mjboot krne vaalii daait lem।


Disease: chikn pॉks- chechk (Chickenpox)

Description: 
chikn pॉks- chechk (Chickenpox)
chechk ek vaayrl smkrmण (viral infection) hai jisse shriir pr chhaale kii trh daane bnte haim aur unmem khujlii (itching) hotii hai। chechk aise logom ko jyaadaa hotaa hai jo biimaar n pड़te hom yaa jinhomne chechk se bchne ke lie tiikaakrण n krvaayaa ho। phle ke smy mem yuvaa hone tk hr koii chechk rog se ek n ek baar jroor prbhaavit hotaa thaa lekin aaj ke smy mem is trh ke rogom mem kmii aaii hai। jyaadaatr logom ke lie, chechk ek hlkii biimaarii hai। phir bhii, yh tiikaa lgaayaa jaanaa behtr hai। chechk ke tiike chechk aur uskii smbhaavit jtiltaaom ko rokne ke lie ek surkshit aur prbhaavii triikaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- thkaan (kmjorii) mhsoos honaa
- bukhaar, sirdrd
- bhookh mem kmii
- shriir pr laal-gulaabii, chhote daanom kaa ubhrnaa

Reasons: 
kin logom ko hotaa hai adhik khtraa?  (Risk Factors of Chicken Pox)
chechk atydhik smkrmit hotii hai, aur yh tejii se phail sktii hai। vaayrs ke daane ke saath siidhe smprk mem aane se yaa khmsne yaa chhiimkne se hvaa mem baiktiiriyaa phailne se doosrom ko ho sktii hai। chechk (chechak) kaa khtraa tb aur adhik hotaa hai jb: 
- kisii ko kbhii chechk n huii ho।
- chechk ke lie tiikaakrण n krvaayaa ho।
- bchche jo skool yaa hॉstl mem smkrmण se prbhaavit hue hom।

Treatments:
upchaar (Treatments of Chicken Pox)
- ek chmmch bekimg sodaa (baking soda) ko ek gilaas paanii mem gholkr, is paanii ko rooii kii shaaytaa se shriir pr lgaaem। chechk se nijaat milegii।
- chechk ke dauraan hone vaalii khujlii se bchne ke lie otmiil (oatmeal) ko paanii mem daalkr nhaaem।
- chechk (chechak) se hone vaalii khujlii se bchne ke lie kailaamaain loshn (calamine lotion) ko daanom ke oopr lgaaem।
- din mem do se tiin baar prbhaavit sthaan pr shhd lgaaem।
- chechk ko jldii thiik krne ke lie gaajr aur hre dhniyaa kaa soop bnaakr piiem।
- chmdn ke tel mem rooii bhigaakr, prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem।
- hrii mtr ko ubaalkr uskaa pest bnaakr, daanom pr lgaaem, aaraam milegaa।
- eloveraa kaa taajaa rs nikaalkr daanom pr lgaaem।
tips (Tips for Chicken Pox)
- ydi chechk ke saath bukhaar bhii hai to khoob pey pdaarth piiem। paanii, joos aur soop smy smy pr lete rhem। ydi bchchaa smkrmit mm kaa doodh piitaa ho, to mm ko doodh nhiim pilaanaa chaahie।
- daanom ko n khujlaaem aur haathom ke naakhoon chhote rkhem। raat mem sote smy khujlaane se bchne ke lie haathom pr glvs (gloves) phnem।
- khujlii se bchne ke lie shriir ko thmdaa rkhem। hlke kpड़e phnem aur grm paanii se nhaane se bchem।
- is baat kaa bhii dhyaan rkhem ki smkrmण ghr ke doosrom sdsyom tk n phaile। smkrmit vykti ke kpड़e, bistr aadi door rkhem aur unhem ghr ke any sdsyom ke kpड़om se alg hii dhoem।

Home Remedies:
shriir mem tejii se khujlii honaa, laal daane nikl aanaa chikn pॉks yaa chechk (Chicken pox) ke prmukh lkshण haim। 1 vrsh se lekr 10 vrsh tk ke bchchom mem chikn pॉks kaa khtraa jyaadaa hotaa hai। khaan-paan mem huii aniymittaa chikn pॉks ke phailne kaa prmukh kaarण hotii hai। is dauraan naakhoon se chkttom ko htaane kii koshish nhiim krnii chaahie, aisaa krne se yh phailtaa hai।
chechk (Chechak) ke smy khaan-paan kaa uchit dhyaan rkhnaa chaahie। msaaledaar aur ऑylii khaanaa khaane se bchem। chiknpॉks ke kisii mriij ko kbhii esprin nhiim denii chaahie। isse uskii haalt khraab ho sktii hai। chikn pॉks hone pr baahr aur bhiiड़ vaalii jgh pr jaane se prhej krem। ho ske to is dauraan logom se door rhem।
jaanie chikn pॉks se bchaav ke ghreloo nuskhe (Home Remedies for Chicken pox)
nimn upchaarom ko apnaakr is biimaarii se raaht paaii jaa sktii hai:
1. jii kaa aataa (Oat Flour)- chikn pॉks hone pr shriir mem bhut tej khujlii hotii hai। khujlii se bchne ke lie jii ke aate ko paanii mem milaakr snaan krnaa chaahie। 2 liitr paanii mem 2 kp jii kaa aataa milaakr lgbhg 15 mint tk ubaalem, pke aate ko ek kॉtn ke baig mem achchhii trh se bmdhkr bॉth tb mem daalkr nhaaem।
2. bhooraa sirkaa (Brown Vinegar)- aadhaa kp bhoore sirke ko paanii mem daalkr nhaane se shriir mem ho rhii khujlii se nijaat paayii jaa sktii hai। isse daanom kii soojn km hotii hai aur daane sookhne bhii lgte haim।
3. niimboo kaa rs (Lemon Juice)- niimboo kaa rs piine se chikn pॉks mem raaht miltii hai। upchaar ke lie smy smy pr ek gilaas saaph paanii mem niimboo nichoड़kr piite rhem।
4. niim kii pttiym (Margosa Leaves)- niim kii pttiyom ko grm paanii mem daalkr nhaane se khujlii smaapt hotii hai। niim praakृtik roop se emtii baiktiiriyl guणom se bhrpoor hotaa hai। aise mem chikn pॉks thiik krne mem behd phaaydemmd hai।
5. bekimg sodaa (Baking Soda)- aadhaa chmmch bekimg sodaa ko ek gilaas gungune paanii mem milaaem aur is lep ko poore shriir pr lgaakr sookhne dem। isse chiknpॉks jld thiik ho jaataa hai।
6. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple Cider Vinegar)- aadhaa kp seb ke sirke ko hlke grm paanii mem milaakr nhaane se raaht miltii hai। is paanii mem tkriibn 20 mint tk jroor baithem।
7. vitaamin ii tel (Vitamin E Oil)- vitaamin-ii yukt tel ko shriir pr lgaane se chikn pॉks ke dauraan hone vaalii khujlii se raaht miltii hai।
8. gaajr (Carrot)- uble gaajr aur dhniyaa khaane se chikn pॉks se aaii kmjorii km hotii hai। gaajr aur dhniyaa kaa soop bnaakr piine se raaht miltii hai।
9. hrbl chaay (Herbal Tea)- tulsii, gemdaa aur kaimomaail ko milaakr chaay bnaaie phir usmem shhd yaa niimboo milaakr piijie। is chaay ko din mem 3-4 baar piine se raaht miltii hai।
10. hrii mtr (Green Pea)- hrii mtr ko paanii mem pkaakr iske paanii ko shriir mem lgaaie, isse chikn pॉks ke laal chktte smaapt hote haim।
11. adrk (Ginger)- baath tb mem thmdaa paanii lem aur usmem adrk daalkr tiis mint tk chhoड़ dem। uske baad is paanii mem baith jaaem। isse chiknpॉks ke dauraan hone vaalii khujlii mem aaraam miltaa hai।


Disease: haijaa (Cholera)

Description: 
haijaa (Cholera)
haijaa ek smkraamk biimaarii (infectious disease) hai, jo mtom ko prbhaavit krtii hai aur jismem paanii kii trh ptle dst lg jaate haim। haijaa kaa ilaaj smy rhte n kiyaa jaae to vykti mem paanii kii kmii (dehydration) ho jaatii hai, jisse vykti kii maut bhii ho sktii hai। haijaa dooshit paanii piine yaa dooshit khaanaa khaane ke kaarण phailtaa hai। aisaa paanii yaa khaanaa jismem vaaibriyo kolerii baiktiiriyaa (vibrio cholerae becteria) maujood ho, haijaa kaa kaarण bntaa hai।
haijaa (Haija) aisii jgh pr jyaadaa phailtaa hai jhm, saaph sphaaii kaa abhaav ho, siivryukt paanii kii splaaii ho, saag-sbjii siivr ke paanii mem ugaaii jaa rhii hom yaa kisii kaa ghr naale aadi ke paas sthit ho। haijaa, bchchom se lekr bujurgom tk, kisii mem bhii ho sktaa hai। grbhvtii mhilaaom tthaa bchchom mem bhii is rog ke hone kii aashmkaa jyaadaa rhtii hai kyomki unkii prtirodhk kshmtaa km hotii hai। haijaa mem vykti ke shriir se paanii ke saath kii jroorii lvण, sodiym aur poteshiym aadi bhii nikl jaate haim, jisse vykti ke shriir kaa rkt amliiy ho jaataa hai aur vykti kii mृtyu ho jaatii hai।

Symptoms: 
- dst ekdm ptle aur chaavl ke paanii jaise honaa
- dst ke saath ultiym honaa
- prbhaavit vykti ko atydhik pyaas lgnaa
- prbhaavit vykti ko peshaab km aanaa
- shriir kii mms peshiyom mem aimthn honaa

Reasons: 
haijaa kaa kaarण (Causes of Cholera in Hindi)
1- dooshit paanii, bhojn, phl yaa doodh aadi kaa pryog krne se।
2- rogii vykti ke smprk mem rhne se, msln, uske saath khaane, uthne-baithne, uske dvaaraa istemaal kie ge kpड़e phnne, uske dvaaraa istemaal kie ge kisii bhii saamaan ko istemaal krne se।
3- mkkhiym bhii haijaa (Haija) phailne kaa bड़aa kaarण haim। khule mem kii gii shauch yaa gmdgii pr baithkr mkkhiym baiktiiriyaa lekr doosrii jghom pr phailaa detii haim, jisse haijaa phailtaa hai।
4- khaane ko binaa dhke rkhnaa, aur use khaanaa।
5- paanii ko binaa dhke rkhnaa।
6- kchchaa yaa adhpkaa bhojn, khaaskr mms khaanaa।

Treatments:
upchaar (Treatment of Cholera)
haijaa kaa ilaaj krne se phle rogii ko saaph-sphaaii kaa vishesh dhyaan rkhnaa haahie। haijaa aksr saaph-sphaaii kii kmii ke kaarण bhii phailtaa hai। haijaa hone pr nimn upaay apnaane chaahie: 
- dooshit bhojn, paanii yaa kisii any khaady pdaarth kaa istemaal n krem
- baasii bhojn n krem
- prtyek khaady pdaarth aur paanii ko hmeshaa dhk kr rkhem
- shriir mem paanii kii kmii n hone dem।
- biimaarii ho rhii ho to niimboo kii shikmjii, dhii, chhaachh, paanii tthaa oaares aadi piite rhem
- ydi vykti ke dst aur ultii n rook rhe hom, to use turmt asptaal le jaaem
- prtyek vykti ko haijaa (Haija) se smbmdhit tiikaa jroor lgvaanaa chaahie
- rogii ke istemaal se smbmdhit hr chiij ko doosre logom se alg rkhem
- paanii mem phinaail daalkr phrsh ko saaph krem, aisaa krne se kiitaaणu mr jaate haim। 

Home Remedies:
pey pdaarth kii maatraa bढ़aayem। paanii, niimboo paanii, chhaachh aadi piite rhem।
ghr pr oaares taiyaar krem, iske lie chaar kp paanii mem chhh chhote chmmch chiinii aur aadhii chhotii chmmch nmk milaaem aur jitnaa jyaadaa pii skem, piiem।
dhii mem kelaa milaakr khaaem।
adrk ko kddooks krke shhd ke saath milaakr khaaem। ydi shauch mem khoon ke dhbbe aa rhe hom to adrk n khaaem।
ek gilaas paanii mem shhd, niimboo aur nmk milaakr piyem।
10 se 20 miliigraam jimk kii jroort roj hotii hai, aise mem jimk ke spliimemt lem।
pyaaj aur kaalii mirch ko piiskr pest bnaaem। ise din mem tiin baar ek hphte ke lie khaaem।
laumg daalkr paanii ko ubaalem aur chhaankr, is paanii ko piiem।
dhii mem methii paaudr aur jiiraa paaudr daalkr khaaem।
niimboo ke rs mem kchchii hldii kii jड़em 2 ghmte ke lie bhigaa kr rkhem aur baad mem piiskr ek kmtenr mem rkh lem। ek kp paanii mem is pest kii kuchh maatraa ko paanii aur shhd milaakr piiem।


Disease: jrmn miijls yaa roobelaa (German Measles)

Description: 
jrmn miijls yaa roobelaa (German measles)
naak, sms kii nlii aur phephड़om se smbmdhit smkrmण ko roobelaa khte haim। yh ek trh kaa khsraa hai jise roobiyolaa yaa jrmn miijls ke naam se bhii jaanaa jaataa hai। yh behd smkrmit hotaa hai aur tejii se ek vykti se doosre vykti mem phail jaataa hai। smkrmit vykti ke smprk mem aane se yh tejii se doosre vykti ko bhii smkmit kr detaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- gaal ke mdr niile yaa bhoore dhbbe njr aanaa
- jln ke saath laal mkhem
- naak kaa bmd honaa
- nirmtr khmsii bne rhnaa,
- mmspeshiyom mem aimthn aur akड़n mhsoos honaa
- sir drd honaa,
- shriir pr laal-gulaabii, chhote daanom kaa ubhrnaa
- bukhaar

Reasons: 
kaarण aur jtiltaaem- (Cause and Complications of German Measles)
roobelaa kaa kaarण, smkrmit vykti ke smprk mem aanaa hii hai। smkmit vykti ke khmsne aur chhiimkne se rog ke jiivaaणu hvaa mem tairne lgte haim aur iske smprk mem aane vaale kisii bhii vykti ko prbhaavit kr skte haim। chhote bchche, grbhvtii mhilaaem yaa aisaa koii bhii vykti jiskii imyoonitii km ho, roobelaa kaa shikaar ho sktaa hai। roobelaa se piiड़it vykti mem kii jtiltaaem bhii ho sktii haim, khaaskr grbhvtii mhilaa ke shishu mem-
- motiyaabimd
- bhraapn
- shriir ke kii mgom mem diphekt
- maansik roop se kmjorii
- saamaany shaariirik vikaas n honaa
- umgliyom aur ghutnom mem arthraaitis ke lkshण aanaa

Treatments:
tips (Tips to Prevent German Measles)
- shriir ko poorii trh se aaraam dem।
- dostom, shkrmiyom, khaaskr grbhvtii mhilaaom ko apnii biimaarii ke baare mem btaaem aur khud se door rhne kii slaah dem।
- aise logom se bhii door rhem jinkii imyoonitii kmjor ho। 
- smkrmit vykti apne istemaal kii sbhii chiijem doosre logom se door rkhe।
- doosre logom ko smkrmit vykti ke smprk se bchnaa chaahie। saath hii rogii ko khud bhii is smbmdh mem saavdhaanii rkhnii chaahie।
upchaar (Treatment of German measles)
paanii mem niimboo daalkr piiem। 
naariyl kaa paanii piiem। 
likoresii kii jड़ ke paaudr mem shhd milaakr rogii ko chtaaem। 
niim kii pttiyom ko daalkr paanii grm krem, is paanii se smkrmit vykti ko snaan kraaem। 
lhsun kii kliyom ko piiskr usmem shhd milaakr, rogii ko chtaaem। 
mvlaa paaudr ko paanii ke saath milaakr, is paanii se shriir pomchhe। 
jau ke paanii mem baadaam ke tel kii kuchh boomde daalkr piiem। 
dhyaan rkhne yogy baatem (Precautions for german measles)
- rogii ko ekmt kmre mem rkhem, jhm ghr ke any sdsy km jaate hom।
- rogii ko grm paanii piine ko dete rhem। khaaskr subh khaalii pet jroor grm paanii piine ko dem।
- rogii ko smy-smy pr trh trh ke joos piine ko dem।
- imyoonitii bढ़aane vaalaa khaanaa, phl aur sbjiym khaane ko dem।
- rogii ko soorj kii roshnii se bchaa ke rkhem।
- doodh yaa doodh se bne any khaady pdaarth rogii ko n dem।
- rogii kaa kmraa hmeshaa saaph aur hvaadaar rkhem।


Disease: inphlooemjaa (Influenza)

Description: 
inphlooemjaa (Influenza)
inphlooemjaa ko saadhaarण bhaashaa mem phloo (flu) ke naam se jaanaa jaataa hai, jismem shvsn tmtr mem smkrmण (infection in respiratory system) ho jaataa hai। is trh kaa phloo adhiktr srdiyom ke mausm mem vaayrl biimaarii ke roop mem hotaa hai। yh un logom ko jyaadaa prbhaavit krtaa hai jinkii rog prtirodhk kshmtaa kisii biimaarii ke kaarण km huii ho।

Symptoms: 
- asaamaany thkaan mhsoos hon।
- kph
- chkkr aanaa
- chhiimk aanaa
- thmd ke saath bukhaar aanaa,
- tvchaa kaa niilaa pड़naa
- naak bhnaa honaa
- pet yaa chhaatii pr dbaav mhsoos honaa aur drd honaa
- mriij pr behoshii haavii ho
- mmspeshiyom mem drd
- sms phoolnaa
- sms lene mem kthinaaii
- sirdrd honaa
- ultii

Reasons: 
kaarण (Reasons of Influenza)
inphlooemjaa naam ke vaayrs se hii yh rog phailtaa hai। phloo kaa vaayrs naak, mkh aur mumh kii msks membren ke dvaaraa shriir mem prvesh krtaa hai। hr baar jb bhii inmem se kisii bhii mg ko haath lgaayaa jaataa haim, vykti khud ko khud hii phloo ke jiivaaणu se smkrmit krtaa hai।
phloo tiin prkaar kaa hotaa hai, e, bii aur sii। taaip e aur bii vaarshik inphlooemjaa kaa kaarण hote haim jisse lgbhg 20 phiisdii log prbhaavit hote haim। taaip e mem ech1en1, ech2en2 aur ech3en3 shaamil haim। taaip e ke imphlooemjaa mem privrtn hotaa hai jisse prbhaavit vykti ko pryaapt imyoonitii nhiim mil paatii। taaip sii bhii phloo ke lkshण drshaataa hai lekin is trh kaa phloo km hotaa hai। haalmki tiinom trh kaa phloo ek hii trh se phailtaa hai aur inke lkshण bhii ek jaise hii hote haim।
jtiltaaem- (Complications during influenza)
- yuvaa, bchchom tthaa 65 kii umr se adhik ke bujurgom mem jtiltaa ho sktii hai।
- grbhvtii mhilaaom ko bhii phloo kaa khtraa jyaadaa rhtaa hai।
- imphlooemjaa se nimoniyaa, kaan mem smkrmण, saains smkrmण aur bromkaaitis kaa khtraa bढ़ jaataa hai।
- ydi uchch shreणii kaa phloo ho to, emtiivaayrl dvaaem upyukt rhtii haim, anythaa vykti kii maut bhii ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
upchaar (Treatment of Influenza) 
- grm paanii mem niimboo daalkr piiem
- thmdaa aur baasii khaanaa n khaaem
- logom se haath n milaaem
- paanii se bhiigne ke baad shriir ko achchhii trh sukhaaem
- prtidin vyaayaam krem
- shriir kii rog prtirodhk kshmtaa bढ़aane vaale khaady pdaarthom kaa sevn krem
- grbhvtii mhilaaem aur bchchom ko piine kaa paanii ubaalkr dem
- ashvgmdhaa aur kaalmegh jaisii jड़ii bootiym shriir kaa taapmaan km krne mem mdd krtii haim
- paanii mem ajvaayn daalkr ubaal lem। paanii tk tk ubaalem jb tk aadhaa n rh jaae, is paanii ko sms smy pr piite rhem।
tips- (Tips to Prevent Influenza)
- shriir ko poorii trh aaraam dem
- naak ko smy-smy pr saaph krte rhem
- grm paanii kii botl yaa hiitimg paid se sikaaii krem
- binaa haath dhoe kbhii khaanaa n khaaem
- jyaadaa se jyaadaa trl pdaarth lem, soop, niimboo paanii aadi piite rhem


Disease: meninjaaitis (Meningitis)

Description: 
meninjaaitis (Meningitis)
meninjaaitis ko dimaagii bukhaar (Dimagi Bukhar) bhii khte haim। yh aamtaur pr vaayrs, baiktiiriyaa, kvk, prjiivii, aur kuchh jiivom ke smkrmण ke kaarण hotaa hai। shaariirik dosh yaa kmjor prtirkshaa prणaalii ko aavrtk baiktiiriyl meninjaaitis se joड़aa jaa sktaa hai।
yh ek trh kaa imphekshn hotaa hai jo mshtishk aur riiढ़ kii hddii kii rkshaa krne vaale membren mem soojn paidaa kr detaa hai। adhikmsh maamlom mem iskaa kaarण vaayrs hotaa hai। haalmki, dimaagii bukhaar ke kuchh gair-smkraamk kaarण bhii maujood haim।

Symptoms: 
- chhote bchchom mem, nimn lkshणom pr gaur krnaa chaahie- (symptoms in toddlers) - bhut tej yaa kraah kr ronaa - tej yaa asaamaany smse - piilaa yaa daanom vaalaa chehraa - laal yaa baimgnii rmg ke dhbbe
- bड़e bchchom mem, nimn lkshणom ko dekhnaa chaahie- (symptoms in younger children) - grdn mem akड़n - piith aur joड़om mem gmbhiir drd - bhut tej sir drd - chmkdaar roshnii se chiढ़ honaa - bhut thmde haath aur pair - kmpnaa - tejii se sm~s lenaa
- mmspeshiyom mem drd
- haathom aur pairom kaa thmdaa honaa
- bukhaar
- sirdrd
- ultii

Reasons: 
dimaagii bukhaar ke kaarण (Causes of Meningitis)
meninjaaitis mem baiktiiriyaa bldstriim mem prvesh krke dimaag aur spaain kॉrd mem chlaa jaataa hai। kii baar jukaam yaa saains kii smsyaa hone se bhii yh baiktiiriyaa naak aur mumh ke dvaaraa shriir mem prvesh kr jaate haim aur dimaag mem soojn paidaa kr dete haim। dimaagii bukhaar (Dimagi Bukhar) kaa emtiibaayotik dvaaom se ilaaj kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। meninjaaitis ko jmchne ke lie glaas test bhii kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
glaas test- ydi kmch ke gilaas ke kinaare ko shriir ke oopr hue dhbbom pr dbaayaa jaae to yh phed nhiim hote। yh meningokokkl septiikaamiyaa (meningococcal septicaemia) kaa lkshण hotaa hai। is avsthaa se piiड़it vykti ke shriir pr gulaabii rmg ke daane ho jaate haim jo baad mem baimgnii rmg ke bड़e daanom mem tbdiil ho jaate haim।

Treatments:
upchaar (Treatment of Meningitis or Dimagi Bukhar) 
- shriir ko poorii trh aaraam dem। 
- rogii ko mdhere aur shmt kmre mem rkhem। 
- likvid phood n lem। oaares kaa ghol grm paanii mem lem। 
- rogii ko anaar kaa joos dem aur lhsun kaa sevn bhii krvaayem। 
- shriir ke taapmaan ko km krne ke lie brph ke tukड़om ko kpड़e mem lpetkr sikaaii krem। 
- ydi rogii ko ultii ho rhii hom, to use ek trph krvt lekr litaayem jisse ultii kii mhk use n aae।


Disease: haart blॉkej (Heart Blockage)

Description: 
haart blॉkej (Heart blockage)
haart blॉkej mem mnushy kii dhड़kn suchaaroo roop se kaam krnaa bmd kr detii haim। is dauraan dhड़kn rook rook kr chltii hai। kuchh logom me yh smsyaa jnm ke saath se hii shuroo ho jaatii hai jbki kuchh logom mem bड़e hone pr smsyaa viksit hotii hai। jnmjaat blॉkej kii smsyaa ko kongenitl haart blॉkej (congenital heart blockage) jbki baad mem huii smsyaa ko ekvaayrd haart blॉkej (acquired heart blockage) khte haim। aadhunik rhn-shn aur khaane-piine kii aadtom ke chlte adhikmsh logom mem haart blॉkej kii smsyaa aam hotii jaa rhii hai। haart blॉkej ko jmchne ke lie ilektrokaardiyograam (electro cardiogram) test kiyaa jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- chhaatii mem drd, sms phoolnaa
- jldii thk jaanaa
- sirdrd honaa
- chkkr aanaa
- behosh honaa

Reasons: 
blॉkej ke kaarण- (Cause of Heart Blockage)
haart mem blॉkej yaa rookaavt plॉk ke kaarण hotii hai। plॉks, kolestrॉl, phait, phaaibr tishyoo aur shvet rkt kणikaaom kaa mishrण hotaa hai, jo dhiire dhiire nsom kii diivaarom pr chipk jaataa hai। plॉk kaa jmaav gaaढ़epn aur uske toड़e jaane kii prvृtti ko lekr alg-alg trh ke hote haim। agr yh gaaढ़aapn haard hogaa, to aise plॉk ko stebl khaa jaataa hai aur ydi yh mulaaym hogaa to ise toड़e jaane ke anukool maanaa jaataa hai, aur ise anstebl plॉk khaa jaataa hai।
stebl plॉk (Stable Plaque):- stebl plॉk se rookaavt kii maatraa se koii phrk nhiim pड़taa, n hii isse gmbhiir haart ataik hotaa hai। is trh kaa plॉk dhiire dhiire bढ़taa hai, aise mem rkt prvaah ko nii aartriij (artries) kaa raastaa dhoomdhne kaa maukaa mil jaataa hai, jise koletrl vesel (collateral vessal) khte haim। ye vesel blॉk ho chukii aartrii ko baaiipaas kr detii haim aur dil kii mmspeshiyom tk aavshyk rkt aur ऑksiijn phumchaatii haim।
anstebl plॉk (Unstable Plaque):- asthaaii plॉk mem, plॉk ke tootne pr, ek khtrnaak thkkaa bn jaataa hai, aur koletrl ko viksit hone kaa pooraa smy nhiim mil paataa hai। vykti kii mmspeshiym (muscle) gmbhiir roop se daimej ho jaatii haim aur vh kii baar sdn kaardiek deth (sudden cardiac death) kaa shikaar ho jaataa hai।

Treatments:
haart blॉkej se bchne ke lie saamaany tips- (Tips to Prevent Heart Blockage)
- dhoomrpaan n krem, yhm tk ki koii doosraa dhoomrpaan kr rhaa ho, to bhii khud ko bchaayem।
- hृdy ko svsth rkhne ke lie dinchryaa mem vyaayaam ko shaamil krnaa behd jroorii hai।
- aisaa bhojn krem, jisse hृdy ko laabh ho।
- hृdy ko svsth rkhne ke lie shriir kaa vjn niymtrit rkhem।
- roj aadhaa ghmtaa paidl chlem।
- lipht kii jgh, siiढ़iyom kaa istemaal krem।

Home Remedies:
haart blॉkej ke ghreloo upchaar- (home remedies for heart blockage)
ek kp doodh mem lhsun kii tiin se chaar klii daalkr ubaalem। is doodh ko roj piiem।
ek gilaas doodh mem hldii daalkr ubaalem aur gungunaa rhne pr shhd daalkr piiem।
ek gilaas gungune paanii mem niimboo kaa rs, kaalii mirch aur shhd daalkr piiem।
do se tiin kp adrk kii chaay rojaanaa piiem। iske lie paanii mem adrk daalkr ubaalem aur shhd milaakr piiem।
methii daane ko raat bhr paanii mem bhigaakr, subh methii chbaakr khaayem aur bchaa huaa paanii pii jaaem।
khaane mem yaa slaad mem alsii ke biijom kaa istemaal krem।
khaane mem saamaany chaavl kii jgh laal yiist chaavl kaa istemaal krem।


Disease: kaan mem smkrmण (Ear Infection)

Description: 
kaan mem smkrmण (Ear Infection ) kaan shriir ke sbse mhtvpoorण aur smvednshiil mgom mem se ek haim। shriir kaa yh ek aisaa hissaa hai jiskaa dhyaan imsaan sbse km rkhtaa hai। kaan mem smkrmण aksr baiktiiriyl yaa vaayrl smkrmण (Bacterial Viral Infection) ke kaarण hotaa hai jo ki mdhy kaan ko prbhaavit krtaa hai jismem chhotii hddiyom kii phaaड़ii bnii hotii hai। isii mem kaan ke prde ke piichhe hvaa se bhrii jgh hotii hai।

Symptoms: 
- kaan mem drd honaa
- chkkr aanaa
- sir drd
- bukhaar
- sunaaii km detaa hai

Reasons: 
kaan mem smkrmण kii jokhimom ko paidaa krtaa hai। smkrmण agr jyaadaa mdr nhiim gyaa ho to kuchh mint ke upchaar aur prkriyaaom ke dvaaraa ise thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai lekin ydi yh mtrik sthaan tk phumch gyaa hai tb ऑpreshn kii naubt bhii aa sktii hai। kaan mem smkrmण hone ke kaarण piiड़it ko nimn preshaaniym ho sktii hai:
* srdrd: kaan kaa drd aksr sr mem tnaav paidaa krtaa hai।
* bukhaar: kaan mem drd ke kaarण tiivr drd, jln aur bukhaar ho sktaa hai।
* chkkr aanaa: kaan kaa drd kii baar sir mem chkkr aane kaa kaarण bn jaate haim।
* sunne kii kshmtaa: ydi is imphekshn ko lmbe smy tk andekhaa kiyaa jaae to kaan kii sunne kii shkti khtm ho sktii hai।

Treatments:
upchaar (Treatment of Ear Infection in Hindi)
kaan ke smkrmण se bchne ke lie sbse jroorii hai saaph-sphaaii kaa vishesh dhyaan rkhnaa। iske atirikt kuchh nimn baatem pr aml kr bhii kaanom ke smkrmण se bchaa jaa sktaa hai। 
vaiks kii sphaaii (Cleaning of the wax)- kaan mem atirikt vaiks kaan mem baiktiiriyaa ko bढ़aakr, kaan mem smkrmण paidaa krtii hai। kaan kii vaiks ko chikitskom dvaaraa sookshm upkrणom se saaph kraayaa jaa sktaa hai। amoomn log iiyr bd se bhii kaan kii sphaaii kr lete haim lekin ydi veks jyaadaa hai to use iiyr bd se saaph nhiim kiyaa jaa sktaa।
iyr drॉps kaa pryog (Use of Ear Drops)- kii dphaa kaan kii dvaa daalne se bhii kaan ke smkrmण se nijaat mil jaatii hai। chikitsk kaan drd ke lie iyr drॉp dete haim jisse kaan ke drd ke saath hii vaiks bhii nikl jaatii hai।
tips- (Tips to Prevent Ear Infection)
- srdii jukaam mem achchhii trh se haath dhone ke baad hii khaanaa-piinaa khaaem। 
- srdii jukaam mem baahr jaane se bchem। bhiiड़ vaalii jghom pr smkrmण kaa khtraa jyaadaa hotaa hai।
- dhoomrpaan se bchem।
- bchchom mem tiikaakrण smy se krvaaem। unhem nyoomokokl tiike jroor lgvaaem।

Home Remedies:
ghreloo upaay- (Home Remedies)
1- kaan mem drd ho to gaimde ke phool ko piiskr uskaa rs daalne se aaraam hotaa hai।
2- nmk ko grm krke use kpड़e mem bmdh kr kaan kii sikaaii krne se bhii kaan ke drd se aaraam miltaa hai।
3- khaanaa bnaane vaale tel mem lhsun daalkr tel grm krem। is tel kii kuchh boomde tiin se chaar baar kaan mem daalem।
4- tulsii ke pttom kaa rs nikaalkr kaan ke aas paas mlne se bhii aaraam hotaa hai। dhyaan rhe rs ko kaan ke mdr nhiim daalnaa hai।
5- seb ke sirke mem braabr maatraa mem paanii milaakr rooii ko usmem bhigaaem। is rooii ko kaan ke piichhe kuchh der lgaakr rkhem।
6- ऑliv ऑyl ko grm krke, gungune tel kii kuchh boomde kaan mem daalem।
7- grm paanii kii botl se kaan kii sikaaii krem।
8- pyaaj ko grm krke use miksii mem piiskr rs nikaal lem। pyaaj ke rs kii kuchh boomde kaan mem daalem।


Disease: daaybitik retinopaithii (Diabetic Retinopathy)

Description: 
daaybitik retinopaithii (Diabetic retinopathy)
daaybitik retinopaithii ek biimaarii hai, jo mdhumeh (diabeties) se piiड़it vykti kii retinaa (m~kh kaa prdaa jhm tsviir bntii hai) ko prbhaavit krtii hai। yh retinaa ko rkt phumchaane vaalii mhiin nlikaaom ke kshtigrst hone ke kaarण hotaa hai, agr iskaa smy pr ilaaj़ n kraayaa jaae to piiड़it vykti mdhepn kaa shikaar ho sktaa hai। daaybitik retinopaithii duniyaa mem mdhepn kaa sbse bड़aa kaarण hai, jiske maamle hr saal bढ़te jaa rhe haim।

Symptoms: 
- mkhom kaa baar-baar smkrmit honaa
- chshme kaa nmbr baar-baar bdlnaa
- retinaa se khoon aanaa
- sphed motiyaabimd yaa kaalaa motiyaabimd
- sirdrd rhnaa yaa ekaaek mkhom kii roshnii km ho jaanaa
- subh uthne ke baad km dikhaaii denaa

Reasons: 
daaybitik retinopaithii ke kaarण (Causes of Diabetic Retinopathy)
mdhumeh (Diabetes), ydi bhut lmbe smy tk rh jaae to yh shriir ke doosre mgom ko bhii prbhaavit krtaa hai aur yh prbhaavit mg mkhem bhii ho sktii haim। daaybitiij़ rkt vaahikaaom kii diivaar ko prbhaavit krtaa hai, jisse retinaa (jispr chhvi bntii hai) tk ऑksiijn le jaane vaalii naaड़iym kmj़or ho jaatii haim। daaybitiij़ ke mriij़om mem agr shugr kii maatraa niymtrit nhiim rhtii, to vh daaybitik retinopaithii kii smsyaa se grst ho skte haim। is smsyaa kaa ptaa tb chltaa hai jb yh biimaarii gmbhiir roop le letii hai।
mdhepn kaa ek prmukh kaarण hai ‘daaybitik retinopaithii’ bhii hai। daaybitik retinopaithii ke do mukhy chrण hote haim। shurooaatii chrण ko naan prolipheretiv daaybitik retinopaithii (enpiidiiaar) khte haim। is chrण mem retinaa kshetr kii nlikaaem kshtigrst ho jaatii haim। saamaanyt biimaarii kaa yh shurooaatii chrण hotaa hai, jismem lkshणom kaa ptaa nhiim chltaa hai।
kuchh maamlom mem kshtigrst rkt nlikaaom ke phtne se retinaa ke mdhy bhaag mem rkt फ़ail jaataa hai। is sthiti ko daaybitik maikyulopaithii khte haim, isse dृshti prbhaavit hotii hai aur dhumdhlaa dikhne lgtaa hai। iske unnt aur viksit chrण ko proliipheretiv daaybitik retinopaithii (piidiiaar) khte haim। yh daaybitik retinopaithii kii sbse sbse gmbhiir chrण hai। is chrण mem retinaa kshetr mem kmj़or avmchhniiy rkt nlikaaem tej़ii se pnpne lgtii haim jo retinaa kii ऑksiijn aapoorti mem baadhaa paidaa kr use kshtigrst krtii haim। is kaarण retinl ditechmemt yaa glookomaa bhii ho sktaa hai। kriib 20 phiisdii mdhumeh piiड़itom mem piidiiaar kii vjh se gmbhiir dृshti dosh ho sktaa hai jo mdhepn kaa kaarण bnaataa hai।

Treatments:
surkshaa ke lie kuchh tips (Tips to prevent diabetic retinopathy)
- smy- smy pr mkhom kii jmch kraayem, yh jmch bchchom mem bhii aavshyk hai।
- rkt mem kॉlestrol aur shugr kii maatraa ko niymtrit rkhem।
- agr aapko mkhom mem drd, mdheraa chhaane jaise lkshण dikhaaii dem to turmt chikitsk se milem।
- daaybitiij़ ke mriij़ ko saal mem km se km ek baar apnii mkhom kii jmch kraanii chaahie।
- daaybitiij़ hone ke ds saal baad hr tiin mhiine pr mkhom kii jmch kraayem।
- grbhvtii mhilaa agr daaybitik hai to chikitsk se smprk krem।
saamaany upchaar (Treatment for diabetic retinopathy)
- vitaamin e yukt khaady pdaarthom kaa sevn adhik krem
- paalk ko apne bhojn mem shaamil krem
- kaale mgoor ke biijom kaa rs piiem
- slaad jyaadaa se jyaadaa khaaem


Disease: glookomaa (Glaucoma)

Description: 
glookomaa (Glaucoma)
glookomaa, kaalaa motiyaa yaa kmch bimdu rog, tmtr mem gmbhiir evm nirmtr kshti krte hue dhiire-dhiire dृshti ko smaapt hii kr detaa hai। kisii vstu se prkaash kii kirणem mkhom tk phumchtii haim, v uskii chhvi dृshti ptl (Retina) pr bnaatii hai। retinaa se yh soochnaa vidyut trmgom dvaaraa mstishk tk netr tmtuom dvaaraa phumchaaii jaatii hai। mkh mem ek trl pdaarth bhraa hotaa hai yh trl pdaarth mkh ke gole ko chiknaa kie rhtaa hai ydi is trl pdaarth kaa risaav ruk jaae to mkh ke mdr kaa daab bढ़ jaataa hai। glookomaa mem mtr netr pr daab, prbhaavit mkhom kii daab shne kii kshmtaa se adhik ho jaataa hai, iske priणaamsvroop netr tmtu ko kshti phumchtii hai, jisse dृshti chlii jaatii hai।
kisii vstu ko dekhte smy glookomaa se grsit vykti ko kevl vstu kaa kemdr dikhaaii detaa hai। smy ke saath sthiti bd se bdtr hotii jaatii hai। saamaanyt: log is pr bhut km hii dhyaan dete haim, lekin jb dhyaan dete haim tb tk bhut der ho chukii hotii hai। saamaany taur pr yh rog binaa kisii lkshण ke viksit hotaa hai v donom mkhom ko ek saath prbhaavit krtaa hai। haalmki yh rog 40 vrsh se adhik aayu ke vyskom ke biich paayaa jaataa hai, phir bhii kuchh maamlom mem yh nvjaat shishuom ko bhii prbhaavit kr sktaa hai। mdhumeh, aanuvmshiktaa, uchch rktchaap v hृdy rog is rog ke prmukh kaarणom mem se haim। vishv str pr kaalaa motiyaa lgbhg chhh kroड़ logom ko prbhaavit krtaa hai aur bhaart mem yh mdhtv kaa doosraa sbse kaarण hai।

Symptoms: 
- tyooblaait yaa blb kii roshnii chaarom or se dhumdhlii dikhne lgtii hai, mkhom mem tej drd bhii hone lgtaa hai।
- dhumdhlaapn, kii rogiyom ko raat mem dikhnaa bhii bmd ho jaataa hai
- mitlii yaa ultii honaa
- sirdrd

Reasons: 
glookomaa ke kaarण (Causes of Glaucoma)
maanv mkh mem sthit kaarniyaa ke piichhe mkhom ko shii aakaar aur poshण dene vaalaa trl pdaarth (Aqueous Humor Fluid) hotaa hai, lems ke chaarom or sthit siiliyrii uttk is trl pdaarth ko lgaataar bnaate rhte haim yh trl pdaarth putliyom ke dvaaraa mkhom ke bhiitrii hisse mem jaataa hai is trh se mkhom mem is trl pdaarth kaa bnnaa aur bhnaa lgaataar hotaa rhtaa hai।
svsth mkhom ke lie yh aavshyk hai mkhom ke bhiitrii hisse mem kitnaa dbaav rhe yh trl pdaarth kii maatr pr nirbhr rhtaa hai। glookomaa rogiyom kii mkhom mem is trl pdaarth kaa dbaav atydhik bढ़ jaataa hai kbhii-kbhii mkhom kii bhaav nlikaaom kaa maarg rook jaataa hai, lekin siiliyrii ootk ise lgaataar bnaate hii jaate haim, aise mem jb mkhom mem dृshti-tmtu ke oopr trl kaa dbaav achaank bढ़ jaataa hai to glookomaa ho jaataa hai। ydi mkhom mem trl kaa itnaa hii dbaav lmbe smy tk bnaa rhtaa hai to isse mkhom ke tmtu bhii nsht ho skte haim। smy rhte ydi is biimaarii kaa ilaaj nhiim kraayaa jaataa hai to isse dृshti poorii trh jaa sktii hai।

Treatments:
saamaany upchaar (Treatment and tips to prevent Glaucoma)
- khaane mem paalk jyaadaa khaaem
- vitaamin e mkhom ke svaasthy ke lie behd jroorii hai। aise khaady pdaarth khaaem jinse vitaamin e kii poorti ho।
- saumph bhii svsth mkhom ke lie achchhaa ghreloo nuskhaa hai।


Disease: bvaasiir (Piles)

Description: 
bvaasiir (Piles) ek asaadhy rog hai। ise hemorhoyds (Haemorrhoids), paails yaa moolvyaadhi bhii khte haim। bvaasiir ko aayurved mem arsh yaani diirghkaaliin praaणghaatk biimaarii khaa jaataa hai। bvaasiir mem mt ke mtim hisse yaa mlaashy (gudaa) kii bhiitrii diivaar mem rkt kii dhmnii aur shiraaom mem soojn ho jaatii hai aur vo tnkr phail jaatii hai। ml tyaag ke vkt jor lgaane yaa dvaab dene se yaa kbj ke kd़e ml se rgd़ khaane se rkt kii nsom mem draar pd़ jaatii hai aur ntiijaa usmem se khoon kaa sraav hone lgtaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- khujlii mlaashy mem atkne kii anubhooti

- drd evm rktsraav
- bvaasiir mem jln tthaa drd hone lgtaa hai
- baadii bvaasiir mem msse kaale rmg ke hote haim
- baahrii bvaasiir mem gudaadvaar ke baahr kii or ke msse mote-mote daanom jaise ho jaate haim
- mnovikaar
- mlaavrodh
- mssom mem khaaj aur soojn hotii hai।

Reasons: 
bvaasiir ke kaarण (Causes of Piles)

kbj (Constipation)
bvaasiir kii sbse bd़ii vjh pet mem kbj bnnaa hai। kbj kii vjh se ml sookhaa aur kthor ho jaataa hai jiskii vjh se uskaa nikaas aasaanii se nhiim ho paataa। mltyaag ke vkt rogii ko kaaphii vkt tk shauchaaly mem ukdoo baithe rhnaa pd़taa hai, jisse rkt vaahniyom pr jor pd़taa hai aur vh phoolkr ltk jaatii hai। ml ke dbaav se vhm kii dhmniym chptii ho jaatii haim aur jhilliym phail jaatii haim। jiske kaarण vykti ko bvaasiir (Haemorrhoids) ho jaatii hai।
tlaa-bhunaa huaa bhojn (Fried and roasted food)
jyaadaa mirch- msaale, tlii huii aur chtptii chiijem khaane, mms, mdaa, rbd़ii, mithaaii, mlaaii jaise der se pchne vaale bhojn krne se bhii bvaasiir rog hotaa hai। aavshyktaa se adhik bhojn krnaa bhii bvaasiir kaa prmukh kaarण hai।
grm paanii (Hot water)
shauch krne ke baad mldvaar ko grm paanii se dhone se bhii bvaasiir rog ho sktaa hai।
dvaaiym (Medications)
dvaaiyom kaa adhik sevn krne ke kaarण bhii bvaasiir (Bawasir) rog ho sktaa hai। khaaskr dispepsiyaa aur kisii julaab kii golii kaa adhik dinom tk istemaal krne se।
niimd mem kmii (Insomania)
niimd poorii nhiim hone ke kaarण pet mem khaanaa shii trh se pch nhiim paataa aur ntiijaa kbj ho jaataa hai। kbj se bvaasiir kii shikaayt ho jaatii hai।
aanuvmshiktaa (Heridetry)
bvaasiir (Bawasir) kii biimaarii aanuvmshik hai। agr privaar mem aapke daadaa-daadii, naanaa-naanii, maataa-pitaa kisii ko bhii bvaasiir thii yaa hai to aapko bhii yh biimaarii ho sktii hai। yh rog piidh़ii dr piidh़ii hotaa rhtaa hai।
any vjhem (Other Causes of Piles)
- grbhaavsthaa me bhrooण kaa dbaab pड़naa।
- shraab aur any nshiile pdaarthom ke sevn se bhii bvaasiir hotaa hai।
- bvaasiir gudaa ke kaimsr kii vjh se yaa mootr maarg mem rukaavt kii vjh se yaa grbhaavsthaa mem bhii ho sktaa hai।

Treatments:
dekhbhaal aur upchaar (Treatments and Tips to Prevent Piles )
- sbse phle kbj ko door kr ml tyaag ko saamaany aur niymit krnaa aavshyk hai। iske liye trl pdaarthom, hrii sbjiyom evm phlom kaa bhutaayaat mem sevn krem। baadii bvaasiir (Haemorrhoids) ke mriij tlii huii chiij़em, mirch-msaalom yukt bhojn n krem।
- raat mem sote smy ek gilaas paanii mem isbgol kii bhoosii ke do chmmch daalkr piine se bhii laabh hotaa hai।
- gudaa ke bhiitr raat mem sone se phle aur subh ml tyaag ke poorv mlhm lgaanaa bhii ml nikaas ko sugm krtaa hai।
- gudaa ke baahr ltke aur sooje hue mssom pr glisriin aur maigneshiym slphet ke mishrण kaa lep lgaakr pttii bmdhne se bhii kaaphii aaraam miltaa hai aur phaaydaa hotaa hai।
- mssom ko htaane ke lie bhii kii vidhiym uplbdh hai। mssom mem imjekshn dvaaraa aisii dvaa kaa prvesh kiyaa jaataa hai jisse msse sookh jaate haim।
- mssom pr ek vishesh upkrण dvaaraa rbr ke chhlle chdh़aa die jaate haim, jo mssom kaa rkt prvaah rokkr unhem sukhaakr nikaal dete haim।
- ek any upkrण dvaaraa mssom ko brph़ mem privrtit kr nsht kiyaa jaataa hai।
- srjrii dvaaraa bhii mssom ko kaatkr nikaal diyaa jaataa hai।
- bvaasiir (Piles) ke mriij ko sbse phle 2 din tk rsaahaar chiij़om kaa sevn krke upvaas rkhnaa chaahie। iske baad 2 sptaah tk binaa pke huaa bhojn kaa sevn krke upvaas rkhnaa chaahie।

- bvaasiir rog ko thiik krne ke lie kuchh upyogii aasn hai jaise- naad़iishodhn, kpaalbhaati, bhujmgaasn, praaणaayaam, pvnmuktaasn, shlbhaasn, suptvjraasn, dhnuraasn, shvaasn, srvmgaasn, mtsyaasn, hlaasn, chkraasn aadi।
