Disease: mkhom kaa imphekshn (Eye Infection)

Description: 
mkhom kaa imphekshn (Eye Infection)
mkhom mem imphekshn haanikaark sookshm jiivaaणu baiktiiriyaa aur vaayrs ke kaarण hotaa hai। ye haanikaark sookshm jiivaaणu maansoon ke mhiine mem sbse jyaadaa skriy hote haim। ye mkhom kii ooprii bhaag, putlii, kॉrniyaa aur plkom pr aakrmण krte haim jisse mkhom mem soojn, jln hotii hai। mkh jrurt se jyaadaa laal ho jaatii hai aur mkhom se jrurt se jyaadaa paanii kaa dischaarj hone lgtaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- mkhom se paanii niklnaa
- mkhom se mvaad niklnaa
- dhumdhlaa vijn
- mkhom kaa sookh jaanaa
- plkom pr soojn
- mkhom mem khoojlaaht
- mkhom mem drd aur jln
- mkhe laal honaa

Reasons: 
mkhom ke imphekshn ke kaarण (Causes and Reasons of Eye Infection)
mkhom ke imphekshn se sbse jyaadaa mkhom kii plkem prbhaavit hotii hai। plkom ke mdrunii hisse mem soojn hone se mkhom kii sumdrtaa to khtm hotii hii hai, smy pr ilaaj nhiim kraane se ghaav hone kaa bhii khtraa rhtaa hai। imphekshn jb mkhom ke mdr msoo kii grmthi ko prbhaavit krtaa hai to soojn se msoo kii grmthi bmd ho jaatii hai aur yh kaaphii drd krne lgtaa hai। sbse jyaadaa gmbhiir sthiti tb hotii hai jb imphekshn kॉrniyaa ko prbhaavit krtii hai। ismem kॉrniyl alsr kaa khtraa rhtaa hai aur mkhom kii roshnii tk chlii jaatii hai।
kmjektivaaitis (Conjunctivitis)- kmjektivaaitis mkhom kaa sbse kॉmn imphekshn hai jise pimk aaii bhii khte haim। yh ek vaayrl imphekshn hai jo kaaphii tejii se phailtaa hai। agr mm ko iskaa imphekshn hai to nvjaat ko bhii yh imphekshn ho sktaa hai।
vaairl keraatitiis (viral keratitis)- pimk aaii kii trh yh bhii ek k़ॉmn aaii imphekshn hai jo hrpis ke vaayrs (Herpes simplex virus) ke kaarण hotaa hai। yh bhii kaaphii tejii se phailtaa hai।
phmgl keraatitiis (Fungal keratitis)- yh ek phmgl imphekshn hai jo mkhom mem kmtekt laims lgaane se ho sktaa hai। 2006 mem yh imphekshn us smy chrchaa mem aayaa thaa jb ek khaas trh ke kmtekt laims solyooshn ke istemaal se kaaphii log is imphekshn ke shikaar ho ge the। vaise mkhom mem phmgl imphekshn kisii bhii trh ke chot se yaa phir ऑrgenik maitr ke jaane se hotaa hai।
traakomaa (Trachoma)- yh imphekshn kaaphii gmbhiir hotaa hai aur gndii jgh mem tejii se phailtaa hai। gmdgii pr pnpne vaale mkkhiyom aur kiid़om ke mkh mem ghusne se yh imphekshn hotaa hai। traakomaa mkhom ke niiche vaale plk ko smkrmit krtaa hai, agr yh lmbe smy tk rhaa to kॉrniyaa tk mem ghaav hone tk kaa khtraa rhtaa hai jisse mriij hmeshaa ke lie mdhaa ho sktaa hai।
imdophthelaamitiis (Endophthalmitis)- jb mkhom kaa imphekshn mkh ke mdr kaaphii ghre tk asr daal detaa hai to use imdophthelaamitiis khte haim। yh vaayrl aur baikteriyl donom trh ke smkrmण se hotaa hai। mkhom mem ghrii chot lgne se bhii iskaa khtraa rhtaa hai।

Treatments:
dekhbhaal aur ilaaj (Care and Treatment of Eye Infection) 
mkhom ke imphekshn kaa ilaaj ab kaaphii srl aur aasaan ho gyaa hai। emtiibaayotik aaii drॉp, mlhm aur semk se kii trh ke smkrmण kaa shii triike se ilaaj ho jaataa hai। kii trh ke vaayrl imphekshn kuchh dinom tk rhne ke baad khud hii thiik ho jaataa hai to gmbhiir imphekshn hone pr dॉktr ko dikhaanaa jroorii hotaa hai।
mkhom kii dekhbhaal ke saamaany upchaar- (Tips to Prevent Eye infection)
-triphlaa jl se mkhom ko dhote rhem, kaaphii kaam kregaa।
-imlii ke biij ko chmdn kii trh piiskr mkhom kii plkom pr lep lgaane se kaaphii raaht miltii hai।
-subh uthte hii mumh mem thmdaa paanii bhrkr mumh phulaakr thmde jl se mkhom pr chhiimte maarem। aisaa din mem tiin baar krem। yh mkhom ke imphekshn ke lie kaaphii asrdaar hai।
-sphed pyaaj ke rs mem shhd aur krpoor milaakr shiishii mem rkh lem aur ise raat mem sote smy mkhom mem daalem। mkhom ke sbhii trh ke imphekshn mem yh kaaphii kaargr ilaaj hai।
-do rttii phitkrii ko baariik piiskr gulaab jl mem gholkr rkh lem। is nechurl aaii drॉp kii do-do boomd din mem tiin baar mkhom mem daalem। yh sbhii trh ke imphekshn mem kaargr hotaa hai। mkh kaa soojn, laalii ko km krtaa hai aur mkhom mem kiich aur mvaad kaa aanaa bmd ho jaataa hai।
any tips- (Other Tips to prevent Eye Infection)
-jiskii mkhe laal haim unke saamne jaane se bchem। agr unke saamne ge haim to mkhom mem mkh daal kr baat nhiim krem। unse milne ke baad turmt m~khom saabun se haath dhoem aur phir m~khom ko thmde paanii se dhoem।
-kmjektivaaitis (conjunctivitis) ke smy skool, ऑphis aur saarvjnik jghom pr emtii vaairl spre kaa chhid़kaav baar-baar krte rhnaa chaahie।
-agr aap kmtekt laims lgaate haim to apne mkhom ko chhoone se phle haathom ko achchhe trh se saaph kr lem।
-piiड़it vykti se door rhem aur uskaa tauliyaa, rumaal, bed, tkiyaa ko hmeshaa emtii-septik likvid se saaph-suthraa rkhem।

Home Remedies:
m~kh mem hone vaalaa imphekshn, gmde haathom se m~kh ko mslne se, prdooshण se, kisii doosre ke dvaaraa istemaal kie ge kaajl lgaane yaa chshmaa phnne se tthaa mkhom kii achchhii prkaar sphaaii n krne se hotaa hai।
jaanie aaii imphekshn se nijaat paane ke ghreloo upaay (Home remedies for eye infection):
1. grm paanii (Hot Water)- hlke grm paanii ke istemaal se m~kh ko dhoem, isse m~khom ke oopr jmne vaalii gmdgii ht jaatii hai। iske baad ruii kii mdd se m~khom ko pochhem।
2. gulaab jl (Rose Water)- gulaab jl se m~kh ko dhone se m~khom kaa imphekshn km ho jaataa hai। do boomd gulaab jl m~khom mem daalem। is upaay ko rojaanaa din mem do baar krem।
3. paalk aur gaajr kaa rs (Spinach & Carrot Juice)- paalk aur gaajr kaa rs m~khom ke smkrmण ke lie kaaphii laabhdaayk hotaa hai kyomki inme paae jaane vaale vitaamin m~khom ke lie kaaphii mhtvpoorण hote haim। paalk ke 4 yaa 5 pttom ko piiskr uskaa rs nichoड़ lem। 2 gaajr ko bhii piiskr rs nikaal lem। ek gilaas mem aadhaa kp paanii lem aur usmem gaajr aur paalk ke rs ko milaa kr piiem। aisaa rojaanaa krne se mkh kaa smkrmण km hone lgtaa hai।
4. mvle kaa rs (Aamla juice)- m~khom mem smkrmण hone pr mvle kaa rs piine se bhut laabh miltaa hai। 3 se 4 mvle ke phl ko piis kr uskaa rs nikaal lem। ek gilaas paanii mem us rs ko milaa kr piiem। mvle ke rs ko subh khaalii pet aur raat mem sone se phle din mem do baar istemaal krem। kuchh hii dinom mem mkhom kaa imphekshn door ho jaaegaa।
5. shhd aur paanii (Honey and Water)- shhd se m~khom ko dhonaa chaahie। isse mkhom ko behd laabh phumchtaa hai। ek gilaas paanii mem 2 chmmch mdhurs ko milaakr khulii m~khom mem chhpke maarem। aisaa krne se mkhom kaa smkrmण door hogaa aur mkhom kii gmdgii bhii saaph hogii।
6. hldii aur grm paanii (Turmeric and Water)- grm paanii mem hldii ko milaakr ruii se m~khom ko pomchhnaa chaahie। hldii praakृtik roop se emtii baiktiiriyl aur emtii septik guणom se bhrpoor hotii hai। yh mkhom kii sphaaii bhii krtii hai aur smkrmण se bhii door rkhtii hai।
7. aaloo (Potato)- aaloo mem prchur maatraa mem staarch hotaa hai, jiske istemaal se m~khom ke smkrmण ko thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। aaloo ko ptle- ptle tukड़om mem kaat lem। raat mem sone se phle us kte hue aaloo ko 15 mint tk apnii m~khom ke oopr lgaa kr rkhem aur baad use utaar dem।


Disease: piiliyaa (Jaundice)

Description: 
piiliyaa (Jaundice)
piiliyaa ek aisaa rog hai jo ek vishesh prkaar ke vaayrs aur kisii kaarणvsh shriir mem pitt yaani rkt mem biliirubin (Bilirubin Disorder) kii maatraa bढ़ jaane se hotaa hai। ismem mriij ko piilaa peshaab hotaa hai। uske naakhoon, tvchaa aur mkhom kaa sphed bhaag piilaa pड़ jaataa hai aur mriij ko kaaphii kmjorii, kbj, jii michlaanaa, sirdrd, bhookh n lgnaa aadi shikaayt hone lgtii hai।
yh bhut hii sooksh‍m vishaaणu (Virus) se hotaa hai। shuroo mem jb rog dhiimii gti se v maamoolii hotaa hai tb iske lkshण dikhaaii nhiim pd़te haim, lekin jb yh gmbhiir ho jaataa hai to mriij kii mkhe v naakhoon piile dikhaaii dene lgte haim। jin vaayrs se yh hotaa hai uske aadhaar pr mukh‍yth piiliyaa tiin prkaar kaa hotaa hai (Types of Jaundice) vaayrl haipetaaitis e, vaayrl haipetaaitis bii tthaa vaayrl haipetaaitis nॉn e v nॉn bii। shriir mem esiditii ke bdh़ jaane, kaaphii dinom tk mleriyaa rhne, pitt nlii mem pthrii atkne, jyaadaa shraab piine, adhik nmk aur tiikhe pdaarthom ke sevn se aur khoon mem rktkणom kii kmii hone se bhii piiliyaa (Piliya) rog hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- mkh ke sphed bhaag kaa piilaa ho jaanaa
- aamaashy mem soojn honaa
- jii michlaanaa
- tvchaa kaa rmg piilaa ho jaanaa
- daahinii psliyom ke niiche bhaariipn aanaa aur drd honaa
- pitt ke kaarण ml kaa rmg phiikaa yaa sphed ho jaanaa
- pet mem drd honaa
- bhookh nhiim lgnaa
- vjn lgaataar km honaa
- shaam mem thkaa-thkaa mhsoos krnaa aur 102 digrii ke aaspaas bukhaar rhnaa

Reasons: 
piiliyaa rog ke kaarण (Causes and Reasons of Jaundice)
jb shriir mem laal rkt koshikaaem 120 din ke saaikil mem ek nechurl prkriyaa ke tht toottii hai to vest baai prodkt ke rup mem biliirubin (Bilirubin Disorder) kaa utpaadn hotaa hai। biliirubin ke jrie shriir kii saarii gmdgii livr se chhn kr baahr nikltii hai। yh gmdgii peshaab aur ml ke jrie baahr nikltii hai। agr livr mem smkrmण hai yaa phir rkt mem biliirubin kii maatraa 2.5 se jyaadaa ho jaatii hai to livr ke gmdgii saaph krne kii prkriyaa avruddh ho jaatii hai aur isii pristhiti mem piiliyaa kii biimaarii ho jaatii hai।
piiliyaa rog ke any kaarण (Other Reasons & Causes of Jaundice)
agr kisii smkrmण se laal rkt koshikaa apnii saamaany prkriyaa se phle hii tootne lgtii hai to rkt mem biliirubin kii maatraa bdh़ne lgtii hai। is pristhiti ko prii heptik jॉndis khte haim। mleriyaa, skil sel eniimiyaa, theliisiimiyaa mem aur kii aanuvmshik kaarणom se bhii rkt mem biliirubin kii maatraa achaank bdh़ne lgtii hai jisse piiliyaa (Piliya) rog hotaa hai।
agr kisii kaarण se livr ko nuksaan phumchaa hai to livr se biliirubin bnne kii kshmtaa hii km ho jaatii hai। ise imtraa-hepaatik jॉndis bhii khaa jaataa hai। vaayrl haipetaaitis (Viral Hepatitis), liivr kaa alkohlik honaa (Alcohol), tej bukhaar (Fever), liivr kaimsr (Liver Cancer), glt dvaaom ke sevn aur pairaasitaamol (Medicine Side effects) ke jyaadaa sevn se bhii imtraa-hepaatik jॉndis hote haim। motaapaa mem liivr saairosis hone kaa khtraa rhtaa hai। jisse imtraa-hepaatik jॉndis kii smbhaavnaa rhtii hai।
gॉl blaadr mem ptthr, painkriyaaj kaa shii dhmg se kaam nhiim krnaa, painkriyaaj kaimsr yaa phir gॉl blaadr ke kaimsr mem bhii livr dvaaraa baai prodkt biliirubin ko shriir se nikaalne kii prkriyaa bmd ho jaatii hai। ntiijaa rkt mem biliirubin kii maatraa kaaphii bdh़ jaatii hai aur gmbhiir piiliyaa rog ho jaataa hai।

Treatments:
dekhbhaal aur ilaaj (Care and Treatment for Jaundice)
- dihaaidreshn hone pr aaii vii phlooyds (IV fluids in case of dehydration)
- emtii baayotiks (antibiotics)
- emtii vaayrl dvaa (antiviral medicines)
- bld trmsphyoojn (blood transfusions)
- sterॉyds (steroids)
- kiimotherepii, redieshn therepii aur nvjaat ke lie phototherepii (chemotherapy/radiation therapy & phototherapy for newborns)
- doodh v paanii ubaal kr piiem।
- taajaa v saaph aur grm bhojn krem।
- s‍vch‍chh shauchaaly kaa hii pryog krem।
- siirimj ko 20 mint tk ubaal kr hii lgvaaem।
- piine ke lie hmeshaa svchchh aur baiktiiriyaa rhit paanii kaa hii istemaal krem।
- khaanaa bnaane, prosne, khaane se phle v baad mem aur shauch jaane ke baad mem haath saabun se ach‍chhii trh dhonaa chaahie।
- bhojn jaaliidaar almaarii yaa dhk‍kn se dhk kr rkhnaa chaahie, taaki mkkhiyom v dhool se bchaayaa jaa skem।
- rogii bch‍chom ko dॉk‍tr jb tk yh n btaa dem ki ye rog muk‍t ho chooke hai s‍kool yaa baahr nhiim jaane de।
- rk‍t dene vaale v‍yktiyom kii poorii trh jmch krne ke baad hii rkt lem। agr rkt mem biliirubin kii maatraa jyaadaa hogii to aapko bhii piiliyaa ho sktaa hai।

Home Remedies:
piiliyaa rog sookshm vishaaणu ke kaarण hotaa hai। is rog ke hone pr vykti ke naakhun aur mkhem piilii dikhaaii detii haim। chikitsaa kii bhaashaa mem piiliyaa ko vaayrl haipetaaitis (Viral Hepatitis) khte haim। piiliyaa rog saaph-sphaaii ke abhaav mem yaa dooshit paanii aur bhojn ke sevn ke kaarण hotaa hai।
piiliyaa rog ke hone pr vykti ko bhookh n lgnaa, bukhaar rhnaa, jii michlaanaa, sir mem drd honaa, peshaab kaa piilaa aanaa tthaa kmjorii v thkaan lgnaa, jaise lkshण njr aate haim। piiliyaa hone pr vykti kaa liivr prbhaavit hotaa hai। ydi smy rhte piiliyaa rog kaa upchaar n kiyaa jaae to vykti kii mृtyu bhii ho sktii hai।
jaanem piiliyaa se bchaav ke ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies for Jaundice)
1. tmaatr kaa rs (Tomato juice)- piiliyaa hone pr ek gilaas tmaatr ke rs mem ek chutkii nmk aur kaalii mirch milaakr subh khaalii pet piiem। aaraam milegaa।
2. moolii kii pttii (Radish leaves)- moolii kii pttiyom ko piiskr, uskaa rs nikaalem। lgbhg aadhaa liitr moolii kii pttiyom kaa rs rojaanaa piiem। ds din ke bhiitr rogii ko piiliyaa se aaraam milegaa।
3. ppiite kii pttii  (Papaya leaves)- ek chmmch ppiite kii pttii ke pest mem ek chmmch shhd milaakr, rojaanaa tkriibn do hphtom tk khaaem। piiliyaa ke upchaar ke lie yh behd phaaydemmd ghreloo nuskhaa hai।
4. gnnaa (Sugarcane)- gnnaa, paachn kriyaa ko duroost krtaa hai saath hii liivr ko bhii behtr triike se kaary krne mem mdd krtaa hai। upchaar ke lie ek gilaas gnne ke rs mem niimboo kaa rs milaakr rojaanaa do baar piiem।
5. tulsii kii pttii (Basil leaves)- tulsii kii ds se pndrh pttii kaa pest bnaakr, gaajr ke rs mem milaa lem। is rs ko rojaanaa, do se tiin hphtom tk piiem। piiliyaa rog se raaht milegii।
6. jau (Barley)- ek kp jau ko tiin liitr paanii mem achchhii trh ubaal lem aur tiin ghmte tk dhk kr rkh dem। is paanii ko din mem kii baar piiem।
7. niimboo  (Lemon)- niimboo liivr ko kshtigrst hone se bchaataa hai। ek gilaas paanii mem do niimboo nichoड़em aur piiem।
8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam kii 8 girii, 2 khjoor aur 5 ilaaychii ko paanii mem raatbhr bhigaakr rkhem। subh sbke chhilke utaarkr, piiskr, pest taiyaar krem। ismem thoड़aa saa mkkhn aur chiinii milkr khaaem।
9. hldii (Turmeric)- ek gilaas gungunaa paanii lem aur usmem hldii milaayem, is paanii ko din bhr mem tiin se chaar baar piiem। piiliyaa ke upchaar ke lie behd prbhaavii upaay hai।
10. chhaachh (Buttermilk)- piiliyaa hone pr chhaachh behd laabhkaarii hai। dhii ko mthkr chhaachh taiyaar krem aur ismem kaalii mirch aur bhunaa jiiraa milaakr piiem।
11. kelaa  (Banana)- pke hue kele ko kuchlkr, usmem shhd milaayem। is trh ke kele ko din mem do baar khaaem।
12. gaajr kaa rs (Carrot juice)- gaajr kaa taajaa rs nikaalkr piiem, piiliyaa mem raaht milegii।
13. bel kii pttii (Wood apple leaves)- bel kii pttii ko piiskr paaudr bnaa lem। is paaudr ko paanii mem milaakr rojaanaa piiem। piiliyaa ke upchaar ke lie behd prbhaavii upaay hai।
14. kaimomaail chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaail piiliyaa rog mem behd laabhkaarii hai। kaimomaail kii pttiyom kii chaay bnaakr piine se piiliyaa rog jldii thiik hotaa hai। is chaay ko piiliyaa thiik hone ke baad bhii piinaa jaarii rkh skte haim।
15. mvlaa (Gooseberry)- mvlaa vitaamin sii se bhrpoor hotaa hai। piiliyaa rog mem mvle kaa sevn krne se behd laabh hotaa hai। mvle ke sevn se liivr bhii mjboot hotaa hai।


Disease: doordrshitaa yaa doordृshti dosh (Hyper Myopia)

Description: 
doordrshitaa yaa doordृshti dosh (Hyper Myopia)
doordrshitaa yaa doordृshti dosh, mem koii bhii vykti door kii chiiज़om ko aasaanii se aur saaफ़ dekh skte haim jbki ismem kriib kii chiiज़e dhumdhlii (blurr) dikhaaii detii haim। doordृshti dosh ko svaasthy kii bhaashaa mem haaipropiyaa (hyperopia) khte haim। doordृshti dosh kitnaa gmbhiir hai yh aapke dekhne kii kshmtaa pr nirbhr krtaa hai।
dekhne ke lie m~kh ke do bhaag jimmedaar hote haim, kॉrniyaa aur lems। kॉrniyaa m~kh ke saamne kaa paardrshii hissaa hotaa hai jbki lems m~kh ke mdr bnaa hotaa hai jo ki chiiज़om ko dekhne pr unke shep mem bhii bdlaav krtaa hai। kॉrniyaa aur lems donom ek saath kaary krte haim aur aane vaalii roshnii ko milaate haim aur ise retinaa pr phoks krte haim। retinaa, aaii bॉl yaanii m~kh ke gole ke piichhe hotaa hai। jb m~kh mem prkaash prvesh krtaa hai to us pr thiik se phoks nhiim ho paataa, yhii door dृshti dosh hotaa hai। ydi m~kh kaa golaa saamaany se chhotaa ho tb bhii door dृshti dosh ho sktaa hai। door dृshti dosh bhut aam smsyaa hai jise aasaanii se thiik bhii kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- asaamaany thkaan mhsoos hon।
- m~kh ke chaarom aur jln yaa drd
- tnaavgrst honaa
- dhumdhlaa dikhnaa (m~kh ke ekdm paas kaa)
- pढ़ne likhne mem dikkt honaa

Reasons: 
doordrshitaa yaa doordृshti dosh ke kaarण (Causes & Reasons of Hyper Myopia)
doordrshitaa yaa doordृshti dosh mem door kii chiijem saaph aur paas kii chiijem dhumdhlii njr aatii haim। mkh ke vishraam kii sthiti mem, prkaash kii smmtr kirणem dृshtiptl kii smvednshiil prt se kuchh piichhe phoks hotii haim। isii kaarण vykti ko paas kii chiijem dekhne mem preshaanii hotii hai। iske alaavaa ydi maataa pitaa ko door dृshti dosh hai to yh bchchom ko bhii prbhaavit kr sktaa hai। iske alaavaa umr bढ़ne ke saath bhii yh smsyaa shuroo ho sktii hai। doordrshitaa ko door krne ke lie sbse aasaan triikaa chshmaa yaa kॉntaikt lems hotaa hai। lems ke pryog se m~khom mem prvesh krne vaalii roshnii pr behtr trh se kemdrit kr paate haim।

Treatments:
doordrshitaa yaa doordृshti kii rokthaam ke lie tips (Treatment & Tips to Prevent Hyper Myopia)
- let kr nhiim pढ़naa chaahie।
- pढ़ne likhne ke dauraan behtr roshnii honii chaahie।
- hrii sbjiym aur phlom kaa pryog khaane mem jroor krem।
- tiivii yaa kmpyootr pr lgaataar kaam naa krem, lgaataar naa dekhem।
- tiivii yaa kmpyootr pr kaary krte vक़t bhii kmre mem pryaapt roshnii honaa jrurii hai।

Home Remedies:
doordrshitaa yaa doordृshti dosh ke ghreloo upaay- (Home Remedies for Hyper Myopia)
m~khom kii raushnii tej ho iske lie vitaamin se poorण bhojn krem।
doodh aur dhii jaise khaady pdaarth jroor khaaem।
mdaa bhii m~khom ke lie behd phaaydemmd hai।
saumph, mishrii aur baadaam ko braabr maatraa mem milaakr paaudr bnaaem aur subh- shaam khaaem।
baadaam aur gaumd se bne lddoo bhii m~khom ke lie phaaydemmd haim।
m~khom kii roshnii tej krne ke lie slaad (salad) jroor khaaem।
m~khom ke vyaayaam (Eye exsercise) jroor krem।


Disease: mumh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer)

Description: 
mumh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer)
maauth alsr ko mumh mem chhaalaa aanaa khte haim। mumh ke mdr jo nrm aur mulaaym ootk hote haim, jise myooks membren (mucous membrane) khte haim, usii mem chhaale pd़te haim। yh aksr khaane ke dauraan yaa kaaphii grm khaane se gaal ke chmd़e ke ktne se hotaa hai।
mumh mem agr chhaale ho jaaem to kuchh bhii khaane mem kaaphii preshaanii hotii hai। khaanaa to door paanii piinaa bhii mushkil ho jaataa hai। chhaale hone pr mumh mem tej jln aur drd hotaa hai। kuchh logom ko to bhojn nlii tk mem chhaale ho jaate haim। mumh mem chhaalaa (Muh ke Chhale) aanaa ek naarml biimaarii hai, jo kuchh dinom baad apne aap thiik ho jaatii hai। kuchh logom ko chhaale baar-baar aate haim। aise logom ko apnii poorii dॉktrii jmch kraanii chaahie, taaki shii ilaaj kiyaa jaa ske। mumh mem chhaale hone ke kii kaarण hote haim। kii baar pet kii grmii se bhii chhaale ho jaate haim।

Symptoms: 
- chbaane aur brsh krne mem preshaanii
- bhookh mem kmii
- msaaledaar, khttaa aur nmkiin chiij khaane pr tej jln
- mumh ke mdr sphed aur laal gol-gol chhaale

Reasons: 
mumh mem chhaalom ke kaarण (Causes of Mouth Ulcer)
kbj (Constipation)
lmbe smy tk kbj rhne se mumh mem chhaale aa jaate haim। aayurved ke anusaar mumh mem chhaale pet kii khraabii tthaa pet kii grmii kii vjh se hote haim। kbj iskii mool vjh hai।
gaal yaa jiibh kaa ktnaa (Injury in Cheek and Tounge)
kii baar koii chiij khaate smy dmtom ke biich jiibh yaa gaal kaa hissaa aa jaataa hai, jiskii vjh se chhaale ho jaate haim। aise chhaale mumh kii laar se apne-aap thiik ho jaate haim।
dvaaom ke saaid iphekt (Medicine Side Effects)
dvaaom ke saaid iphekt kii vjh se bhii mumh mem chhaale hote haim। lmbe smy tk emtiibॉyotik dvaaom sevn krne se mumh mem chhaale aane kii smbhaavnaa jyaadaa hotii hai।  jyaadaa emtiibॉyotik ke sevn se hmaarii mtom mem laabhdaayk kiitaaणuom kii smkhyaa ght jaatii hai, ntiijaa mumh mem chhaale ho jaate haim।
dmtom kii glt smrchnaa (Wrong Structure of Teeth)
dmtom kii glt smrchnaa kii vjh se bhii mumh mem chhaale hote haim। ydi dmt aaड़e-tirchhe, nukiile yaa aadhe toote hue haim aur iskii vjh se ve jiibh yaa mumh mem chubhte haim yaa unse lgaataar rgड़ lgtii rhtii hai, to vhm chhaale ho jaate haim।

Treatments:
ilaaj aur dekhbhaal (Treatment of Mouth Ulcer)
- jb tk chhaale khtm nhiim ho msaaledaar aur khttaa khaanaa bmd kr dem।
- khoob paanii piiem।
- gungune nmk-paanii se kullaa krem।
- mumh ko hmeshaa saaph rkhem।
- drd hone pr pen kilr dvaa le skte haim।
- chhaale vaale jgh pr emtii-septik jel lgaaem।
- mediikedet maauth vaash se mumh saaph krem, kullaa krem।
- subh subh gaay ke doodh se bne dhii ke saath ek kelaa khaane se aaraam miltaa hai।
- khoob tmaatr khaaem। tmaatr kaa rs ek glaas paanii mem milaakr kullaa krne se chhaale mit jaate haim।
- ydi chhaale saamaany haim, to vitaamin 'bii' kॉmpleks tthaa pholik esid kii goliym 2-3 din tk lene se chhaale thiik ho jaate haim।
- chhaale pr boro glisriin bhii lgaaii jaa sktii hai yaa poteshiym prmaimgnet ke ghol se kullaa krne pr chhaale khtm hote haim।

Home Remedies:
mumh ke mdr kii sth ke kisii bhii trh se ktne yaa uske oopr koii phoड़aa niklne se alsr yaa chhaalaa ho jaataa hai। mumh kaa alsr hone pr vykti kaa mumh tthaa jiibh prbhaavit ho jaate haim jisse vykti ko kuchh bhii khaane yaa piine mem preshaanii hotii hai।
jaanie mumh ke chhaalom se bchaav ke ghreloo nuskhe (Home remedies for mouth ulcer):
1. naariyl kaa doodh (Coconut milk)- naariyl kaa doodh mumh ke alsr mem drd se raaht detaa hai saath hii jln ko door krtaa hai। upchaar ke lie ek chmmch naariyl ke doodh mem thoड़aa saa shhd milaakr alsr ke oopr lgaaem। is upaay ko din mem tiin se chaar baar krem। iske alaavaa naariyl ke doodh se kullaa krne pr bhii aaraam miltaa hai।
2. dhniyaa ke biij (Coriander seed)- dhniyaa ke biij bhii mumh ke alsr se raaht dete haim। alsr se hone vaalii jln ko bhii door krte haim। upchaar ke lie paanii mem dhniyaa ke biij daalkr ubaalem aur is paanii ko chhaankr alg rkhem। is paanii ko mumh mem ghumaa ghumaa kr kullaa krem। is upaay ko bhii din bhr mem tiin se chaar baar krem।
3. bekimg sodaa (Baking soda)- bekimg sodaa yaa sodiym baaii kaarbonet bhii mumh ke alsr se nijaat dilaa sktaa hai। esidik khaane- piine se hone vaale alsr mem yh behd laabhkaarii hai। upchaar ke lie ek chhotii chmmch bekimg paaudr mem paanii milaakr pest taiyaar krem aur prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem।
4. shhd (Honey)- mumh ke alsr se raaht dene mem shhd bhii behd prbhaavii hai। shhd mem emtii ऑksiidemt aur emtii maaikrobl guण hote haim। upchaar ke lie rooii ke phaahe ko shhd mem dubaakr, prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem। isii trh glisriin aur vitaamin ii tel ko bhii lgaayaa jaa sktaa hai।
5. eloveraa (Aloevera)- eloveraa kaa rs, prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se alsr se hone vaale drd se raaht miltii hai। eloveraa praakृtik emtiiseptik kii trh kaary krtaa hai jisse chhaale jldii thiik hote haim।
6. dhniyaa pttii (Coriander leaves)- dhniyaa pttii ko kchchaa chbaane se mumh ke alsr se raaht miltii hai। dhniyaa pttii mem फ़ॉlik esid ke saath vitaamin bii 1, bii 2, bii 6 aur vitaamin sii paayaa jaataa hai। dhniyaa pttii ko dmdii ke saath lgbhg 10 mint tk chbaanaa chaahie। iske pryog se mumh se aane vaalii durgmdh se bhii raaht miltii hai।
7. tulsii (Basil)- tulsii mem emtii vaayrl, emtii baiktiiriyl aur emtii phmgl guण paae jaate haim। upchaar ke lie 5 se 6 tulsii kii pttiyom ko dhokr achchhii prkaar chbaakr khaaem aur uske baad thoड़aa paanii pii lem। is upaay ko din mem do baar, subh aur shaam krem।
8. brph (Ice)- brph, alsr ke kaarण mumh mem hone vaale drd se raaht detii hai। brph ko prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se, smbmdhit jgh thoड़ii der ke lie sunn pड़ jaatii hai jisse alsr se hone vaalii jln aur drd se raaht miltii hai।


Disease: alsr (Ulcer)

Description: 
alsr (Ulcer)
pet yaa chhotii mtom mem hone vaale alsr ko peptik alsr (Peptic Ulcer) ke roop mem jaanaa jaataa hai। pet ke peptik alsr ko gaistrik alsr bhii khte haim। alsr aahaar aur tnaav yaa phir pet mem aml (acid) kii atirikt maatraa jmaa hone se hotaa hai। aamaashy kaa alsr pet ke alsr se jyaadaa kॉmn biimaarii hai। peptik alsr aamaashy aur pet ke biich kii ptlii surkshaa diivaar mem ghaav ke baad chhed ho jaane se hotaa hai। lmbe smy tk emtiibaayotiks, drd aur sterॉyd kii dvaa khaane ke alaavaa shraab ke sevn se pet aur aamaashy kaa alsr hotaa hai। pet mem esid aur emjaaim ke bnne se chhotii mt ke upr aamaashy ke paas chhed yaa ghaav ho jaataa hai jise alsr khte haim।
adhikmshth yh helikobaiktr paailorii (helicobacter pylori) naam ke ek jiivaaणu ke smkrmण se hotaa hai। kuchh logom mem alsr ke lkshण aasaanii se jbki doosrom mem ye jldii nhiim dikhaaii pd़te haim। kbhii-kbhii alsr unhem bhii ho jaataa hai, jinhomne iske kisii bhii lkshण kaa anubhv nhiim kiyaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- agr pet kaa drd alsr ke kaarण ho rhaa hai, to raat mem aur jb bhii aap bhookhe hom, yh achaank tiivr ho sktaa hai।
- khaanaa khaane ke do ghmte baad bhookh mhsoos krnaa।
- gais aur dkaar mem vृddhi।
- thkaavt kaa ahsaas honaa।
- pet bhraa huaa mhsoos honaa, aur dher saaraa trl pdaarth pii paane mem asmrthtaa।
- bhookh mem kmii।
- vjn ghtnaa।
- siine kii hddiyom aur pet kii naabhi ke biich kisii bhii sthaan pr drd।
- hlkii mtlii (nausea), jo subh jaagne pr sbse aam hotii hai।

Reasons: 
alsr ke kaarण (Causes of Ulcers)
koii bhii ek khaas kaarण nhiim hotaa hai jo alsr ke lie uttrdaayii hotaa hai। bhut saare kaarण ke prbhaav se alsr paidaa hotaa hai। lekin yh spsht hai ki pet aur aamaashy ke baach emjaaim aur paachk rs ke asmtuln se jo esid bntaa hai usii se alsr bntaa hai।
aam taur pr adhikmsh alsr H. Pylori baikteriyaa ke smkrmण se hii hotaa hai। yh baikteriyaa pet aur chhotii mt ke biich jo surkshaa diivaar hotii hai, vhiim rhtaa hai। aamtaur pr yh koii nuksaan nhiim phumchaataa hai। lekin iske smkrmण se kbhii-kbhii pet ke mdrunii sth aur mt mem soojn ho jaatii hai jo baad mem alsr kaa rup dhaarण kr letaa hai।
pen kilrs aur emtii imphlaametrii dvaa ke lgaataar sevn se chhotii mt aur pet ke biich kii surkshaa diivaar mem soojn aur chhed ho jaataa hai jisse alsr hone kii smbhaavnaa rhtii hai।
aur bhii haim kii vjh (Other Reason for Ulcer)
shraab aur dhoomrpaan kaa jyaadaa sevn
kisii gmbhiir biimaarii kii vjh se
redieshn therepii kii vjh se
kise ho sktaa hai alsr (Whom May be More Prone to Ulcer)
pet ke alsr ke dher saare kaarण hone pr bhii jin logom mem iske viksit hone kaa adhik khtraa hotaa hai, ve haim:
ech paailorii baiktiiriyaa se smkrmit log।
niymit roop se drgs yaa suii se dvaaom kaa sevn krne vaale log।
alsr ke paarivaarik itihaas vaale log।
niymit roop se shraab piine vaale log।
liivr, gurde, yaa phephd़om se jud़ii biimaariyom vaale log।
50 saal se adhik umr ke log।

Treatments:
dekhbhaal aur ilaaj (Treatment for Ulcer)
- pohaa aur saumph ko braabr maatraa mem milaakr choorण bnaa liijie, 20 graam choorण ko 2 liitr paanii mem subh gholkr rkhie, ise raat tk pooraa pii jaaem। al‍sr mem aaraam milegaa।
- pttaa gobhii aur gaajr ko braabr maatraa mem lekr joos bnaa liijie, is joos ko subh-shaam ek-ek kp piine se peptik alsr ke mriijom ko aaraam miltaa hai।
- al‍sr ke mriijom ke lie gaay ke doodh se bne ghii kaa istemaal krnaa phaaydemmd hotaa hai।
- al‍sr ke mriijom ko baadaam kaa sevn krnaa chaahie, baadaam piiskr iskaa doodh bnaa liijie, ise subh-shaam piine se al‍sr thiik ho jaataa hai।
- shjn ke pt‍te ko piiskr dhii ke saath pest bnaakr lem। is pes‍t kaa sevn din mem ek baar krne se al‍sr mem phaaydaa hotaa hai।

Home Remedies:
alsr (ulcer) shriir kii ooprii tvchaa yaa myooks jhillii pr ubhraa huaa ghaav hotaa hai। alsr jyaadaatr helikobaiktr paaylorii (Helicobacter pylori) naam ke jiivaaणu dvaaraa hotaa hai। pet kii mt (Intestine) mem kii prkaar ke drvy niklte haim jo bhojn ko pchaane mem shaayk hote haim lekin jb yh drvy jyaadaa maatraa mem niklte haim to pet v mt kii koml tvchaa ko jlaane lgte haim। iske kaarण pet mem ghaav bn jaataa hai।
jaanie alsr se bchaav ke ghreloo upaay (Home remedies for ulcer):
1.pohaa (Bitten rice)- pohaa alsr ke upchaar mem behd phaaydemmd hai। pohaa aur saumph ko braabr maatraa mem milaakr paaudr bnaa lem। is paaudr kii 20 graam maatraa ko 2 liitr paanii mem gholkr rkh diijie। dophr se raat tk is paanii ko pooraa khtm krem। alsr se raaht milegii।
2. pttaa gobhii aur gaajr (Cabbage and carrot)- pttaa gobhii mem lektik esid hotaa hai jisse emiino esid bntaa hai jo pet mem rkt kaa prvaah bढ़aataa hai। iske saath hii pttaa gobhii mem vitaamin sii (vitamin c) bhii uchch maatraa mem hotaa hai। pttaa gobhii aur gaajr ko braabr maatraa mem milaakr joos taiyaar krem aur subh shaam ek-ek kp piiem।
3. naariyl (Coconut)- naariyl mem emtiibaiktiiriyl guण paaye jaate haim, jo ki alsr paidaa krne vaale baiktiiriyaa ko maar dete haim। naariyl ke doodh aur paanii mem bhii emtii- alsr guण paaye jaate haim। alsr ke upchaar ke lie rojaanaa naariyl paanii piiem। naariyl ke tel kaa sevn bhii alsr se bchaataa hai।
4. gaay kaa doodh (Cow milk)- hldii mem emtii baiktiiriyl guण hote haim, gaay ke doodh mem hldii milaakr piine se bhii alsr rogiyom ko laabh miltaa hai।
5. baadaam (Almond)- alsr rogiyom ko baadaam piiskr, khaane se laabh hotaa hai। baadaam ko piiskr uskaa doodh jaisaa bnaakr piiem।
6. shjn (Drum stick)- shjn kii phlii bhii svaasthy ke lihaaj se behd phaaydemmd hai। ismem emtii baiktiiriyl guण hote haim jo rogom se lड़ne mem shaayk hote haim। shjn kii phlii ko piiskr, dhii ke saath milaakr khaane se alsr rog mem aaraam miltaa hai।
7. shhd (Honey)- kchchaa shhd bhii pet ke alsr mem behd laabhkaarii hai। shhd mem glookoj pairॉksaaid (glucose peroxide) paayaa jaataa hai, jo pet mem maujood haanikaark baiktiiriyaa ko khtm kr detaa hai। iske saath hii shhd ke sevn se pet kii jln se bhii aaraam miltaa hai।
8. kelaa (Banana)- kelaa mem emtiibaiktiiriyl ttv paae jaate haim। kelaa khaane se esiditii se bhii raaht miltii hai। kchchaa aur pkaa donom hii trh kaa kelaa khaane se alsr rogiyom ko behd aaraam miltaa hai। kchche kele kii sbjii bnaakr usmem ek chutkii hiimg milaakr khaaem।
9. lhsun (Garlic)- lhsun pet ke alsr mem behd laabhkaarii hai। upchaar ke lie do se tiin lhsun kii kliyom ko kuchlkr, paanii ke saath khaaem।
10. belphl (Wood apple)- pet ke alsr mem belphl aur uskii pttiyom kaa sevn bhii behd laabhdaayk hai। pttiyom mem maujood tenins pet ko, kisii bhii trh ke nuksaan se bchaataa hai। belphl kaa rs bhii pet kii jln aur drd ko door kr, alsr se bchaataa hai।


Disease: daayriyaa (Diarrhea)

Description: 
daayriyaa (Diarrhea)
lgaataar looj moshn yaani ptlaa dst aanaa, ultii honaa daayriyaa khlaataa hai। daayriyaa vaayrl, baikteriyl smkrmण ke kaarण to hotaa hii hai lekin sbse kॉmn kaarण hai khaan-paan mem gd़bd़ii, prdooshit paanii aur mt kii gd़bd़ii। din mem agr tiin se adhik baar paanii ke saath ptlaa dst ho rhaa ho to yh daayriyaa kaa lkshण hai।
daayriyaa mem shriir mem paanii kii kmii ho jaatii hai jise dihaaidreshn khte haim jo kaaphii gmbhiir hotaa hai। isse shriir kmjor ho jaataa hai, shriir mem smkrmण phailne kaa khtraa kaaphii bdh़ jaataa hai। smy pr ilaaj nhiim hone pr mriij kii jaan bhii jaa sktii hai।
aam taur pr daayriyaa 3 se 7 dinom tk preshaan krtaa hai। daayriyaa vaise to kbhii bhii ho sktaa hai, lekin brsaat mem vaayrl daayriyaa jyaadaa preshaan krtaa hai। iskii vjh gmdaa paanii aur khaanaa-piinaa hai। daayriyaa achaank ho jaataa hai aur kors pooraa hone ke baad hii khtm hotaa hai। pet mem jyaadaa esiiditii bnne se bhii daayriyaa hotii hai। yh sbhii umr ke logom ko preshaan krtaa hai। ekyoot daayriyaa (Acute Diarhea) vyskom ko saal bhr mem ek baar aur bd़e bchchom ko do baar hotaa hai। is biimaarii mem sbse jyaadaa khtraa dihaaidreshn se hotaa hai, jismem shriir se saaraa paanii aur khtm ho jaataa hai। mt mem paanii jaane se phle hii vo paas ho jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- mtom mem soojn se huaa daayriyaa
- ptlaa dst yaa looj moshn (paanii kii trh) agr do hphte tk rhe।
- dst ke saath khoon, mv aur potaa aataa hai। isse shriir kaaphii kmjor ho jaataa hai।
- ultii, mitlii aane ke saath ptlaa dst aataa hai। yh pet aur mt mem esiditii bnne se hotaa hai।

Reasons: 
daayriyaa ke kaarण (Causes & Reasons of Diarrhea)
vaayrl daayriyaa (Viral Diarrhea)
vaayrl imphekshn se sbse jyaadaa daayriyaa hotaa hai। iske lkshण kbhii saamaany to kbhii kaaphii gmbhiir ho jaate haim। ptlaa dst, looj moshn, pet mem mroड़ aanaa aur bukhaar iske saamaany lkshण haim। vaayrl daayriyaa 3 se 7 din tk rhtaa hai।
vaayrl daayriyaa nimn vaayrl smkrmण ke kaarण hote haim
rotaavaayrs (Rotavirus)- nvjaat bchchom mem rotaavaayrs vaayrl smkrmण se vaayrl daayriyaa kaa khtraa rhtaa hai। isse bchne ke lie bchchom ko emtii rotaavaayrs imjekshn bhii lgaayaa jaataa hai।
norovaayrs (Norovirus)- yh vaayrl daayriyaa vyskom aur skool jaate bchchom ko sbse jyaadaa preshaan krtaa hai। nrsimg hom, de keyr semtr aur restoremt mem iske smkrmण kaa khtraa sbse jyaadaa rhtaa hai।
edenovaayrs(Adenovirus)- yh vaayrl smkrmण hr umr ke logom ko hotaa hai।
baiktiiriyl smkrmण se daayriyaa (Bacterial infections)
baiktiiriyl smkrmण se huaa daayriyaa kaaphii siiriys hotaa hai। baiktiiriyl smkrmण prdooshit paanii, bhojn, phood pvaaijnimg se hotii hai। baiktiiriyl smkrmण se huii daayriyaa mem lgaataar ultii aanaa, lgaataar looj moshn hote rhnaa, dst ke saath sirph paanii aane kii shikaayt se mriij kii haalt kaaphii gmbhiir ho jaatii hai। baiktiiriyl smkrmण se pet mem gais bhii bn jaatii hai। gmbhiir baiktiiriyl smkrmण mem kbhii-kbhii dst ke saath khoon, potaa aur mv bhii aatii hai।
aur bhii haim kii vjh (Some more causes)
mtom mem soojn ke baad bhii daayriyaa hotaa hai
ii-kolaaii ke smkrmण se bhii daayriyaa hotaa hai
alkohl sevn ke saaid iphekt mem bhii daayriyaa hotaa hai
daaybitiij ke mriij ko bhii daayriyaa kii shikaayt rhtii hai
rediyotherepii, kiimotherepii mem bhii daayriyaa kii shikaayt hotii hai
kisii khaas emtiibaayotiks ke sevn se bhii daayriyaa hotaa hai, khaaskr vaise emtii baayotiks jo mt pr prbhaav daalte haim
prjiivii jo prdooshit paanii aur khaane ke jrie hmaare pet mem jaataa hai, vo hmaare paachn tmtr ko bigaad़ detaa hai aur jisse daayriyaa kii shikaayt hotii hai
kaimsr kii dvaa, vjn ghtaane kii dvaa, bld preshr kii dvaa ke saaid iphekt kii vjh se bhii daayriyaa hotaa hai
elrjii se bhii daayriyaa hotii hai, khaaskr vaise chiij khaane se msln- aartiphishiyl sviitnr yaa doodh mem laiktoj kii maatraa rhne se daayriyaa ho sktaa hai।

Treatments:
ilaaj aur dekhbhaal (Treatment and Care for Diarrhea)
- daayriyaa hone pr tel-msaalom vaale khaane se prhej krnaa chaahie।
- daayriyaa mem doodh yaa doodh se bne pdaarth nhiim khaanaa chaahie, mriij kii haalt aur bigd़ jaatii hai।
- kele, chaavl, seb kaa murbbaa aur tost kaa mishrण jise braat khte haim, iske sevn se daayriyaa mem raaht miltii hai।
- kchchaa kelaa aur chaavl mtom kii gti ko niymtrit krne aur dst rokne mem shaaytaa krte haim।
- pryaapt maatraa mem trl pdaarth lem lekin agr phir bhii daayriyaa bdh़ rhaa ho to turmt dॉktr se smprk krem। 

Home Remedies:
jb vykti kii paachn kriyaa (Digestive System) suchaaroo roop se kaary krnaa bmd kr detii hai, tb use ultii aur ptle dst hone lgte haim। yhii sthiti daayriyaa khlaatii hai। daayriyaa, baiktiiriyl tthaa vaayrl imphekshn (Bacterial and Viral Infection) ke kaarण hotaa hai, jo dooshit bhojn yaa khaane ke dvaaraa vykti ke shriir mem phumch kr, paachn kriyaa ko prbhaavit krte haim।
daayriyaa kai dauraan vykti ke pet mem drd hotaa hai, pet mem aimthn, jii michlaanaa aadi smsyaaem bhii ho sktii haim। daayriyaa ke dauraan vykti ko dii-haaidreshn (Dehydration) ho sktaa hai, jisse sthiti aur bhii bigड़ sktii hai। daayriyaa ke lkshण vykti mem do se chaar din mem ubhrte haim।
jaanie daayriyaa se bchaav ke lie kuchh ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies of Diarrhea)
niiche diye ge upchaarom ke dvaaraa daayriyaa biimaarii mem raaht paaii jaa sktii hai:
1. dhii (Yogurt)- dhii mem maujood baiktiiriyaa, shriir mem maujood vishaile baiktiiriyaa kaa naash kr, daayriyaa se bchaate haim। daayriyaa ke upchaar ke lie do ktorii dhii khaane se hii behd aaraam miltaa hai। saade chaavl mem dhii milaakr bhii khaaii jaa sktii hai।
2. adrk (Ginger)- adrk kaa pryog phood pॉijnimg (food poisoning) hone pr bhii kiyaa jaataa hai, aise mem daayriyaa se raaht dene mem bhii adrk kaaphii prbhaavshaalii hai। adrk ke pryog se pet kii aimthn (stomach cramps) aur drd se bhii raaht miltii hai। upchaar ke lie adrk ko kddooks krke, usmem shhd (honey) milaakr khaaem। iske tumrt baad paanii n piiem। adrk kii chaay (binaa doodh kii) bhii kaaphii aaraam detii hai।
3. methii daanaa (Methidana)- daayriyaa ke ilaaj ke lie methii daanaa behd phaaydemmd btaayaa gyaa hai। ek chhotii chmmch methii daanaa ko chbaakr, ek bड़ii chmmch dhii khaane se daayriyaa se nijaat miltii hai। iske alaavaa ek chmmch methii daanaa aur jiiraa (cumin) ko bhoon kr paaudr bnaa lem aur do bड़ii chmmch dhii mem milaakr khaaem। is mishrण ko din bhr mem tiin baar khaane se behd aaraam miltaa hai।
4. seb kaa sirkaa (Apple cider vinegar)- seb kaa sirkaa bhii daayriyaa mem behd phaaydemmd hai। seb ke sirke kaa esidik guण, daayriyaa ke baiktiiriyaa ko khtm kr detaa hai। upchaar ke lie ek gilaas paanii mem ek chmmch sirkaa milaaem aur pii lem। is mishrण ko ek din mem do se tiin baar tb tk piiem jb tk daayriyaa thiik n ho jaae।
5. kelaa (Banana)- kele mem kaaphii maatraa mem paiktin ttv (pectin content) aur pauteshiym hotaa hai, islie daayriyaa mem kelaa khaane kii slaah dii jaatii hai। daayriyaa hone pr do se tiin pke hue kelaa roj khaaem।
6. kaimomaail chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaail daayriyaa ke upchaar mem behd phaaydemmd hai। daayriyaa ke upchaar ke lie kaimomaail kii chaay bnaakr piiem।
7. sphed chaavl (White rice)- saadaa, sphed giile chaavl bhii daayriyaa ke dauraan khaane kii slaah dii jaatii hai। is trh ke chaavl supaachy hote haim। is trh ke chaavl khaane se dst km aate haim। saadaa chaavl ko thoड़aa giilaa krke khaaem। svaad ke lie chaavl mem dhii milaakr khaa skte haim।
8. gaajr kaa soop (Carrot soup)- gaajr kaa soop bhii daayriyaa mem behd phaaydemmd hai। daayriyaa ke dauraan shriir mem huii poshk ttvom (nutrients) kii kmii ko pooraa krne ke saath hii gaajr kaa soop imyoonitii (immunity) ko mjboot krtaa hai। soop bnaane ke lie, gaajr ko kaat kr ubaal lem aur jb gaajr ublkr paanii mem ghul jaae tb, paanii ko chhaan kr alg kraa lem। ismem svaadaanusaar nmk, bhunaa jiiraa aur kaaliimirch paaudr milaaem।


Disease: sustii (Lethargy)

Description: 
sustii (Lethargy)
kii baar shriir mem sphoorti (energy) nhiim rhtii। shriir ekdm thkaa huaa mhsoos krtaa hai, aur bhut kmjorii mhsoos hotii hai। kii baar aals itnaa hotaa hai ki hmeshaa niimd aatii rhtii hai। isii avsthaa ko lithaarjii yaa sustii khte haim। tnaavpoorण maahaul yaa poshण kii kmii ke kaarण shriir kmjor hone lgtaa hai। kii baar raat mem achchhii niimd n sone pr bhii agle din thkaa huaa mhsoos krte haim। lekin jyaadaa sustii shriir ke lie behd haanikaark bhii hai। kii baar yh sustii maut kii vjh bhii ho sktii hai, kyomki jyaadaa sustii se bren ke sels bhii sust hone lgte haim aur dhiire dhiire kaary krnaa bmd kr dete haim। poore shriir kii svbhaavik prkriyaa dhiimii pड़ jaatii hai, jo kii smsyaaom kaa kaarण ho sktii hai। aise mem shriir ko ektiv bnaaye rkhnaa behd jroorii hotaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- ekmt achchhaa lgnaa
- kmjorii mhsoos honaa (Weakness in Body)
- kisii kaam mem mn n lgnaa
- chhote se chhotaa kaam krne mem chiड़chiड़aanaa
- hr smy niimd aur aals aanaa
- hr smy lete rhne kaa mn honaa
- mn mem hmeshaa nkaaraatmk vichaar aanaa

Reasons: 
sustii ke kaarण (Causes of Lethargy)
sustii kaa anubhv sbhii ko hotaa hai, lekin thoड़aa aaraam krne yaa raat kii niimd ke baad, aglii subh tk sustii door ho jaatii hai। ydi iske baad bhii sustii bnii rhe to yh biimaarii kaa smket ho sktaa hai। kisii bhii vykti kii sustii kaa asr n kevl uske shaariirik blki maansik v saamaajik str pr bhii pड़taa hai। sustii, vyst dinchryaa, khraab jiivn shailii, biimaariym, aniymit v asmtulit khaan-paan v any kaarणom se ho sktii hai। aamtaur pr achchhii niimd lene aur aur dinchryaa mem bdlaav se is smsyaa ko kaaphii hd tk thiik kiyaa jaa sktaa hai lekin kii baar chikitsk kii slaah lenii hii pड़tii hai।
is smsyaa ke any kaarण (Reasons of Lethargy)
kmjorii kii vjh se।
jyaadaa tnaavgrst rhne se।
niimd poorii n hone kii vjh se।
shriir mem vitaamin kii kmii se।
shriir mem khoon kii kmii kii vjh se।

Treatments:
sustii se bchne ke upaay (Tips to Prevent from Lethargy)
- roj yog aur vyaayaam krem।
- subh kii taajii hvaa mem thlem।
- tnaavmukt rhne kaa pryaas krem।
- khaane mem vitaamin kii maatraa bढ़aaem।
- km se km 8 ghmte kii niimd jroor lem।
- mvle kaa murbbaa bhii shriir ko sphoorti detaa hai।
- hlkaa smgiit, hlkii aavaaj mem sunem। isse bhii maansik sustii door hotii hai।
- kii baar sugmdhit telom kii maalish se bhii shriir kii sustii aur sustii mitaaii jaa sktii hai।
- smtulit aur paushtik bhojn krem, jismem hrii sbjiym, daalem, dhii aur mausmii phl shaamil hom।
- apnii umgliyom ke porom se chehre kii msaaj krem। aisaa krne se bld srkuleshn bढ़egaa, jisse vykti ektiv mhsoos kregaa।

Home Remedies:
bhaagdauड़ bhrii aadhunik jimdgii aur kii trh ke tnaav, n kevl shaariirik blki maansik roop se bhii vykti ko thkaa dete haim। thkaavt hr kisii ko hotii hai prntu kii logom ko poore shriir mem drd kii shikaayt rhtii hai। drd ko km krne ke lie log aksr penkilr le lete haim। ye dvaaem tumrt aaraam detii haim prntu lmbe smy tk iskaa pryog nuksaan phumchaa sktaa hai।
aaie jaanem thkaavt se bchaav ke lie ghreloo nuskhe (Home remedies for lethargy)
1. griin tii (Green tea)- thkaavt ko door krne ke lie ek kp griin tii piinaa behd prbhaavii hai। niymit roop se griin tii piine se vjn bhii kmtrol mem rhtaa hai। mmspeshiyom mem drd (muscle pain) hone pr aap griin tii behd laabhkaarii hai।
2. adrk kii chaay (Ginger tea)- adrk kii chaay kudrtii penkilr ke roop mem kaary krtii hai। yh vykti ko trotaajaa bhii mhsoos kraatii hai। tulsii ke kaaढ़e mem adrk milaakr bhii piiyaa jaa sktaa hai।
3. saumph (Saunf)- kisii pkvaan mem svaad bढ़aane ke saath hii saumph sms mem taajग़ii laane mem bhii behd prbhaavkaarii hai। saumph kaa pryog rsoii mem j़roor hotaa hai। saumph khaane se pet saaफ़ rhtaa hai aur aap khud ko trotaajaa mhsoos krte hai।
4. ajvaayn (Ajwain)- ajvaayn ke ptte bhii drd nivaark dvaa kii trh kaam krte haim। yh shriir ke toote-phute kii mg kii mrmmt krne aur joड़om ke drd mem bhut laabhprd hote haim।
5. kddoo ke biij (Pumpkin seed)- kddoo ke biij mem maigniishiym hotaa hai, jo aals v thkaavt se lड़ne mem mdd krtaa hai। aadhe ghmte kii eksrsaaij mem agr aap thkaa huaa mhsoos krtii haim to iskaa mtlb hai ki aapmem maigniishiym kii kmii hai। vyaayaam ke dauraan shriir mem ऑksiijn ke nirmaaण ke lie maigniishiym jroorii hai। iskii kmii kii vjh se thkaavt jldii hotii hai।
6. akhrot (Wallnut)- akhrot mem omegaa 3 phaitii esid paayaa jaataa hai। omegaa 3 phaitii esid n kevl thkaan aur aals se raaht detaa hai, blki yh avsaad se bhii bchaataa hai। islie akhrot khaane se aapkii jhpkiyom kii smsyaa door hogii।
7. anaaj (Whole grain)- anaaj mem phaaibr kii maatraa adhik hotii hai। islie aals aur thkaan mitaane mem yh mddgaar saabit hotaa hai। anaaj mem kॉmpleks kaarbohaaidret (complex carbohydrate) hote haim। ye thkaan se lड़ne mem mddgaar hote haim।
8. laal mirch (Red chilly)- laal mirch mem vitaamin sii paayaa jaataa hai, jo thkaan door krtaa hai। laal mirch se dimaag ektiv rhtaa hai aur hm hmeshaa trotaajaa mhsoos krte haim।
9. dhii (Curd)- dhii mem maujood achchhe baiktiiriyaa paachn tmtr (immune system) ko mjboot rkhte haim। 4 sptaah tk din mem do baar ydi dhii khaayaa jaae to shaariirik aur maansik seht ke saath rog prtirodhk kshmtaa bhii bढ़tii hai aur thkaan km hotii hai।


Disease: mstishk kaa dauraa (Cerebral Stroke)

Description: 
hmaare shriir mem mstishk aur naaड़iyom ko praaणvaayu (Oxygen) aur poshk ttvom kii nirmtr aapoorti rkt vaahikaaom se rkt ke dvaaraa kii jaatii hai। jb bhii in rktvaahikaaom mem kisii kaarण kshti phum~chtii hai yaa avrodh nirmaaण hotaa hai tb mstishk ke kuchh hissom ko rkt kii aapoorti bmd ho jaatii hai। jis trh hrdy ko rkt kii aapoorti n hone pr hृdyghaat aa jaataa hai, usii prkaar mstishk ke kuchh hisse ko 3 se 4 mint se jyaadaa rkt n milne pr praaणvaayu aur poshk ttvom ke abhaav mem nsht hone lgtaa hai, ise hii mstishk kaa dauraa bhii khte haim।

Symptoms: 
- kmjorii mhsoos honaa (Weakness in Body)
- dishaa aur nirdesh smjhne mem preshaanii
- sirdrd honaa
- bhrm kii sthiti
- bolne mem tkliiph honaa
- jii michlaanaa aur ultii honaa
- shriir ke ek hii trph ke chehre, haath yaa tmg mem sunnpn
- dhiire yaa aspsht bolnaa
- achaank lड़khड़aanaa, chkkr aanaa, shriir kaa smtuln bigड़naa
- ek yaa donom m~khom se dekhne mem kthinaaii

Reasons: 
mstishk ke daure ke kaarण (Causes & Reasons of Cerebral Stroke)
mstishk kaa dauraa hone ke mukhyt: 2 kaarण hote haim, jo nimn haim:
1. arkttaa mstishk kaa dauraa (Ischemic stroke)- dauraa pड़ne kaa sbse aam kaarण hai। yh dimaag ke kisii rktvaahinii ke smkiirण hone yaa avrodhr nirmaaण hone ke kaarण hotaa hai। yh bhii do prkaar kaa hotaa hai-
1.1. thrombotik strok (Thrombotic stroke)- is prkaar ke mstishk ke daure mem mstishk kii rkt vaahinii mem khoon ke jm jaane ke kaarण yaa thkke ke kaarण avrodh ho jaataa hai। jin rogiyom mem khoon ke mdr kolestrॉl kaa prmaaण jyaadaa hotaa hai, aise rogiyom kii rktvaahinii mem bhiitrii str pr vsaa jmaa ho jaatii hai jise plaak khte hai। is pr khoon kaa thkkaa jmaa ho jaane pr dhiire-dhiire poorii rktvaahinii mem avrodh hone lgtaa hai aur mstishk ke us hisse ko rkt n milne pr thrombotik strok pड़ jaataa hai।
1.2. imbolik strok (Embolic stroke)- is prkaar ke mstishk ke daure mem rkt kaa thkkaa yaa imjekshn yaa slaain dvaaraa gltii se rkt vaahinii mem prvesh kiyaa huaa hvaa kaa chhotaa bulbulaa mstishk ke kisii chhotii rktvaahinii mem phsne ke kaarण rktvaahinii mem avrodh nirmaaण ho jaataa hai aur mstishk ke us hisse ko rkt n milne pr imbolik strok pड़ jaataa hai।
2. rktstraav mstishk kaa dauraa (Hemorrhagic stroke)- mstishk kii kisii rktvaahinii mem rktstraav hone ke kaarण hone vaale is prkaar ke mstishk ke daure behd gmbhiir hote hai। uchch rktchaap, rkt vaahinii kii jnmjaat vikृti yaa rkt vaahinii mem phulaav ke kaarण mstishk mem rktstraav ho sktaa hai। iske do prkaar haim-
2.1. imtraa- kraaniyl haimrej (Intra-cranial hemorrhage)- is prkaar mem mstishk ke kisii rktvaahinii mem rktstraav hone ke kaarण mstishk ke us hisse ko rkt kii aapoorti mem kmii aane ke kaarण bren sels ko kshti phum~chtii hai। is prkaar ke mstishk ke daure kaa prmukh kaarण uchch rktdaab hai। lgaataar kii smy tk uchch rktchaap ke kaarn rktvaahinii kmjor aur kड़ii ho jaatii hai aur priणaamt: pht jaatii hai।
2.2. sb- aarknoid haimrej (Sub-archnoid hemorrhage)- is prkaar mem mstishk aur kpaal ke biich ke str mem kisii rktvaahinii mem rktstraav hone ke kaarण sb aarknoid spes mem rkt ektrit ho jaataa hai। iskaa prmukh kaarण rkt vaahinii kii jnmjaat vikृti yaa rkt vaahinii mem phulaav hotaa hai। is prkaar mem rogii ko tej srdrd kaa anubhv hotaa hai।
2.3. trmsemt ishchemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack)- ek tiisre prkaar kaa bhii mstishk kaa asthaaii dauraa hotaa hai jisme strok ke lkshण kuchh mintom se lekr kuchh ghmto tk hii rhte haim aur baad mem thiik ho jaate haim। ise trmsemt ishchemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack) yaa tiiaaiie (TIA) khaa jaataa hai। yh is baat kii chetaavnii detaa hai ki aapko koii smsyaa hai aur iskaa ilaaj n kraane pr nikt bhvishy mem aapko strok pड़ sktaa hai।

Treatments:
mstishk kaa daure se bchne ke lie upaay (Treatments & Tips to Prevents Cerebral Stroke)
- shraab aur dhoomrpaan bmd krem।
- phl, sbjiym ityaadi aahaar lenaa chaahie।
- tnaav se door rhem। niymit vyaayaam aur yog krem।
- agr aap motaape ke shikaar hai to apnaa vjn niymtrit rkhem।
- agr baar-baar sirdrd kii preshaanii hotii hai to chikitsk se iskii jm~ch kraaem।
- agr aap uchch rktchaap (Hypertension), mdhumeh (Diabetes), hrdy rog (Heart disease) se piiड़it haim to niymit dॉktr se jm~ch kraate rhem।


Disease: maayopiyaa (Myopia)

Description: 
aajkl adhikaash logom kii mkhom mem riphraiktiv (Refractive) vikaar yaani kirणom ke vkr kii smsyaa ke lkshण dikhaaii dene lge haim। ismem nikt dृshti dosh yaani maayopiyaa (Myopia) se sbse jyaadaa log prbhaavit haim। chikitskom ke anusaar, bchpn mem dekhne kii kshmtaa kaa vikaas aur kishoraavsthaa mem mkh kii lmbaaii bढ़tii hai lekin nikt dृshti dosh hone kii vjh se yh kuchh jyaadaa hii bढ़ jaatii hai। aisii sthiti mem mkh mem jaanevaalaa prkaash retinaa pr kemdrit nhiim hotaa। isii vjh se tsviir dhumdhlii dikhaaii detii hai lekin is dosh ko kॉntekt lems yaa srjrii se thiik kraayaa jaa sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- chkkr aanaa
- bchchom ko skool mem blaik bord pr likhaa huaa n dikhnaa
- teliivijn dhumdhlaa dikhnaa
- mkhom kaa bhaimgaa honaa
- doorii pr likhe akshr n pढ़ paanaa
- sir mem drd rhnaa

Reasons: 
maayopiyaa ke kaarण- (Causes & Reasons of Myopia)
aise log jo nikt dृshti dosh kii smsyaa se preshaan haim yaani ki jinhem thoड़ii door kii chiijem bhii saaph dikhaaii nhiim detiim, use riphrektiv err (Refractive error) khte haim। maayopiyaa se grst logom mem aaiibॉl bhut lmbii ho jaatii hai yaa phir kॉrniyaa (Cornia) bhut jyaadaa krvii ho jaataa hai jisse mkh mem phumchne vaalaa prkaash thiik trh se phoks nhiim kr paataa। aise mem kisii bhii chiij kii tsviir, retinaa pr n bnkr, uske saamne bn jaatii hai jisse chiijem dhumdhlii dikhaaii detii haim। yh smsyaa umr ke saath bढ़tii jaatii hai। maayopiyaa kii smsyaa se joojh rhe log chshmaa yaa kmtekt laims ke jriye smsyaa se nijaat paa skte haim lekin smsyaa jyaadaa ho to ऑpreshn dvaaraa maayopiyaa kaa ilaaj smbhv hai।
iske alaavaa nimn kaarण bhii haim: (Other Reasons & Causes of Myopia)
daaybitiij (Daibetes) se grsit hone pr।
aanuvmshikii (Genetic Disorder) kaarणom se bhii aisaa ho sktaa hai।
lmbe smy tk ek hii laims kaa pryog krnaa। (Use of lenses)
kisii bhii chiij ko bhut paas se ghoorkr kaary krnaa।
km roshnii mem koii kaary krnaa, jaise pढ़naa yaa tiivii dekhnaa।

Treatments:
maayopiyaa se bchaav ke lie saamaany upchaar (Treatment & tips for Myopia)
- briithimg vyaayaam krem।
- triphlaa choorn rojaanaa lem।
- lmbe smy tk teliivijn dekhne yaa pढ़ne se bchem।
- jhm kaam krem, vhm pryaapt roshnii honii chaahie।
- mkhom kii roshnii bढ़aane ke lie mvlaa kaa pryog krem।
- mumh mem paanii bhr kr mkhom ko taaje paanii se dhoem।
- prdooshण yaa dhoop mem niklne se phle mkhom pr chshmaa phnem।
- likresii kii jड़ kaa paaudr aur shhd milaakr doodh ke saath lem।
- naariyl, mishrii, saumph aur baadaam ko milaakr miksr taiyaar krem aur paaudr bnaayem। din mem do baar khaaem।


Disease: khrraate lenaa (Snoring)

Description: 
sote vkt sms ke saath tej aavaaj aur vaaibreshn (Sound & Vibration) aanaa khrraate (Snoring) khlaataa hai। khrraate lenaa saadhaarण-sii preshaanii hai, lekin jb yh biimaarii kaa roop le letii hai to gmbhiir smsyaa bn jaatii hai। sms lene mem baar-baar rukaavt hone pr shriir mem ऑksijn kaa levl km ho jaataa hai, jisse biipii bढ़ jaataa hai। shriir mem ऑksijn km hote hii dil ko ऑksijn ke lie jyaadaa preshr lgaanaa pड़taa hai। jb yh smsyaa bढ़ jaatii hai to haart ataik bhii ho sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- subh uthne pr gle aur naak kaa sookhaa honaa
- din ke smy bhii niimd mhsoos honaa
- chhote chhote kaamom ke baad bhii thkaan mhsoos honaa aur aals aanaa
- gle aur naak se tej aavaaj niklnaa
- sote vkt mumh khul jaanaa aur hvaa niklnaa

Reasons: 
khrraate yaa snorimg ke kaarण- (Causes & Reasons of Snoring)
jyaadaatr logom ko lgtaa hai ki khrraate aane kii vjh jyaadaa thkaan hai islie ve ise andekhaa kr dete haim। isse smsyaa gmbhiir ho jaatii hai। drasl, sote smy sms mem rukaavt khrraate aane kii mukhy vjh hai। gle ke pichhle hisse ke smkre ho jaane pr ऑksijn smkrii jgh se hotii huii jaatii hai, jisse aaspaas ke tishoo vaaibret (Tissue Vibrate) hote haim। isii se khrraate aate haim।
kii baar log piith ke bl sote haim, jisse jiibh piichhe kii trph ho jaatii hai। taaloo ke piichhe yoovyl (taaloo ke piichhe thoड़aa-saa ltkaa huaa mms) pr jaakr lg jaatii hai, jisse sms lene aur chhoड़ne mem rukaavt aane lg jaatii hai। isse sms ke saath aavaaj aur vaaibreshn hone lgtaa hai। niiche vaale jbड़e kaa chhotaa honaa bhii khrraate aane kaa ek kaarण hai। jb vykti kaa jbड़aa saamaany se chhotaa hotaa hai to letne pr uskii jiibh piichhe kii trph ho jaatii hai aur sms kii nlii ko blॉk kr detii hai। aise mem sms lene aur chhodn़e ke lie preshr lgaanaa pड़taa hai, jis kaarण vaaibreshn hotaa hai। naak kii hddii teढ़ii honaa (Crooked Nose Bone) aur usmem mms bढ़aa (Meat soar) honaa। ismem bhii sms lene ke lie preshr lgaanaa pड़taa hai।

Treatments:
khrraate yaa snorimg se bchaav ke lie upaay- (Tips & Treatments to Prevent Snoring)
- sone kii pojiishn bdlem।
- nshe vaale pdaarthom se door rhem।
- tkiye ke kvr bdlte rhem।
- raat ke smy hlkaa khaanaa khaaem।
- gle kii regyulr eksrsaaij krem।
- khoob paanii piiem aur shriir ko haaidret rkhem।
- naak kii hddii mem smsyaa ho yaa phir mms bढ़aa ho to dॉktr se smy rhte milem।
- kii baar pregnemsii mem vjn bdhn़e yaa sone kii sthiti shii n hone pr bhii khrraate aate haim। aise mem krvt lekr sonaa chaahie।
- piith ke bl sone kii bjaay krvt lekr soem। isse sms kii nlii mem rukaavt nhiim hotii। sote smy sir ko thoड़aa oomchaa krke soem। isse aapkii jiibh aur sms kii nlii mem rukaavt nhiim aaegii।
- agr khrraate aane kaa kaarण jyaadaa vjn hai to smy rhte vjn kmtrol krem। jim jॉin krem। niymit yog aur eksrsaaij krne se vjn ko kmtrol kiyaa jaa sktaa hai।


Disease: snbrn (Sunburn)

Description: 
snbrn yaa dhoop se jhulsnaa (Sunburn)
dhoop ke kaarण tvchaa kaa prbhaavit honaa aam baat hai। koii bhii vykti ydi dhoop mem jyaadaa der rhtaa hai to soory kii kirणom uskii tvchaa (Skin) ko nuksaan (Damage) phumchaa sktii haim। ydi tej dhoop kii vjh se tvchaa jyaadaa jl yaa jhuls jaae to yh sthiti snbrn (Sunburn) khlaatii hai।

Symptoms: 
- prbhaavit hissaa chhoone pr grm lgtaa hai।
- prbhvit hissaa ghraa laal, kaalaa yaa ghraa bhooraa njr aataa hai।
- dhoop se aane ke baad turmt tvchaa ke phrk ko dekhaa jaa sktaa hai।
- prbhaavit hisse pr jln aur drd mhsoos ho sktaa hai।
- tvchaa pr prmaanemt phrk aayaa hai iskaa ptaa 24 ghmte ke mdr dekhaa jaa sktaa hai।
- tvchaa rookhii tthaa bejaan njr aatii hai।
- chhote chhote chhaale yaa paanii vaale daane bhii ho skte haim।
- prbhaavit jgh pr soojn bhii aa sktii hai।
- bukhaar ke saath ultii bhii lg sktii hai।

Reasons: 
snbrn yaa dhoop se jhulsne ke kaarण (Causes & Reasons of sunburn)
soorj kii altraavॉylet kirणom ke siidhe taur pr smprk mem aane pr snbrn hotaa hai। shriir praakृtik roop se mailenin (Natural melanin) kaa nirmaaण krke khud ko soorj kii kirणom ke prkop se bchaataa hai। mailenin ek rmjk yaani pigmemt (Pigment) hotaa hai jo tvchaa ke rmg ke lie jimmedaar hotaa hai। kaale yaa smvle logom kii tvchaa gore rmg ke logom kii apekshaa km daimej hotii hai kyomki smvlii tvchaa mem pigmemt jyaadaa bntaa hai। gore (Fair) logom mem pigmemt km hotaa hai islie unkii tvchaa soory ke smprk mem aane pr jldii kshtigrst hotii hai। iske alaavaa maidaanii ilaakom (Grounded Area) mem rhne vaale logom kii apekshaa phaaड़ii ilaakom (Hill Tract) mem rhne vaale logom kii tvchaa bhii jldii kshtigrst (Damage) hotii hai kyomki vhm soorj maidaan kii apekshaa njdiik aur tej hotaa hai।

Treatments:
dhoop se jhulsne yaa snbrn se bchaav ker lie upaay (Tips & Treatment for Sunburn)
- poorii baahom ke kpड़e phnem।
- khiire, tmaatr aur aaloo kaa rs lgaaem।
- snbrn vaale hisse pr thmdii pttiym rkhem।
- hr chaar ghmte pr snskriin lgaaem।
- dhoop mem jaane se aadhaa ghmtaa phle snskriin kaa pryog krem।
- koshish krem ki subh 10 se shaam 4 ke biich dhoop mem n jaaem।
- dhoop se jhulsii tvchaa pr eloveraa bhii behd phaaydaa phumchaataa hai।
- kॉtn kaa kpड़aa thmde doodh mem bhigaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem।
- prbhaavit hisse pr thmdii dhii lgaane se bhii bhut aaraam miltaa hai।
- dhoop mem niklne se phle khud ko achchhii trh se dhkkr niklem, msln mkhom pr chshmaa, sir pr skaarph yaa kaip phnem।


Disease: glsuaa (Mumps)

Description: 
glsuaa (Mumps)
glsuaa (Mumps) ek vaayrl smkrmण (Viral Infection) hai। yh haalm~ki shriir ke kii hissom ko prbhaavit kr sktaa hai lekin, mukhy roop se laar grmthiyom ko prbhaavit krtaa hai jo kaan aur jbड़e ke biich mem prtyek gaal ke piichhe sthit hotii haim। glsuaa laar grmthiyom (Salivary Glands) kii soojn (Swelling) aur drd (Pain) kaa kaarण bntaa hai। yh rog mukhy roop se 5 se 15 vrsh kii umr mem adhik dekhne ko miltaa hai। lड़kom kii apekshaa lड़kiyom mem (Specially in girl) yh rog jldii hotaa hai।
emtiibaayotik dvaaom se glsuaa kaa ilaaj smbhv nhiim hai, yh do hphtom mem yh apneaap hii smaapt ho jaataa hai। drd nivaark dvaa jaise ibooprophen yaa peraasitaamol kaa upyog kiyaa jaa sktaa hai aur sooje hue bhaag pr thmdaa paik lgaane se bhii mdd miltii hai। ek saadhaarण se priikshण se glsuaa kii pushti ho sktii hai kyomki kaanom ke ekdm saamne jbड़e mem soojn dikhaaii detii hai। klchr yaa rkt priikshण (Blood test) dvaaraa bhii nidaan kii pushti ho sktii hai। rkt mem emtiibॉdii kii upsthiti aasaanii se vaayrl smkrmण kii pushti kr detaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- kaan mem drd honaa
- pet mem drd honaa
- bhookh n lgnaa
- chbaane aur niglne mem drd honaa
- bukhaar
- sirdrd
- gaalom mem soojn dikhaaii denaa
- kmj़orii

Reasons: 
glsuaa ke kaarण (Reasons & Causes of Mumps)
glsuaa yaa mmps perotid grmthiyom mem vaayrl smkrmण (Viral Infection) se hone ke kaarण hone vaalii biimaarii hai। yh grmthiym laar bnaatii haim jo chehre ke donom trph jbड़e kii hddii ke niiche sthit hotii hai। yh smkrmit laar (Infected Saliva), chhiimkne yaa khmsne (Sneezing or Coughing) tthaa smkrmit vykti (Infected Person) ke saath brtn saajhaa krne aadi se ek vykti se doosre vykti mem phailtii hai।
mmps ke vaayrs se smkrmit mriij, perotid grmthi mem soojn shuroo hone ke 7 din phle aur 7 din baad tk smkrmण phailaa sktaa hai। lkshणom kii shuruaat aamtaur pr vaayrs se smprk ke baad 14-18 dinom mem hotii hai। aisaa khaa jaataa hai ki koii bhii vykti kevl ek baar hii glsuaa se piiड़it hotaa hai, lekin kuchh log dobaaraa bhii smkrmit ho skte haim। mmps, khaanaa aur paanii sheyr krne se bhii phail sktaa hai। yoom to yh rog bchchom mem jyaadaa dekhne ko miltaa hai lekin iske lkshण kisii bhii umr ke vykti ko prbhaavit kr skte haim। yh bhut gmbhiir biimaarii nhiim hai lekin kii baar smsyaa bढ़ bhii jaatii hai।

Treatments:
saamaany upchaar

Home Remedies:
jaanem glsuaa yaa mmps ke ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies for Mumps)
phlom kaa rs n piiem।
pryaapt maatraa mem paanii piiem।
ememaar ke tiike lgvaayem।
tiikhaa yaa amliiy khaane se bchem।
sooje hue hisse pr thmdii yaa grm pttii kaa sek krem।
kaalii mirch kaa lep prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se aaraam miltaa hai।
eloveraa ko chhiilkr us pr hldii daalkr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaaem।
adrk ko piiskr prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se bhii mmps mem aaraam miltaa hai।
piipl ke ptte ko sek kr us pr ghii yaa tel lgaakr, prbhaavit sthaan pr bmdhem।
methii ke paaudr mem jau kaa aataa milaakr prbhaavit sthaan pr lep krne se aaraam miltaa hai।
brgd ke peड़ kii pttiyom ko bhii tel lgaakr grm krke prbhaavit sthaan pr lgaane se aaraam miltaa hai।


Disease: kaalii khmsii (Whooping Cough)

Description: 
kaalii khmsii (Whooping Cough)
vhoopimg kph yaa kaalii khmsii (Whooping cough) gmbhiir kism kii khmsii hotii hai, jo jyaadaatr 5 se 15 vrsh aayu tk ke bchchom ko hotii hai। ise kukur khmsii bhii khaa jaataa hai। yh khmsii bchchom mem hone vaalii ek smkraamk tthaa khtrnaak biimaarii hai। yh mukhyt: shvsn tmtr (Respiratory System) ko prbhaavit krtii hai। bhaart jaise vikaasshiil desh mem prtyek ek laakh kii aabaadii pr 578 bchche prtyek vrsh is biimaarii se grsit hote haim। yh rog lड़kom kii tulnaa mem lड़kiyom ko jyaadaa hotaa hai। 6 mhiine se km umr ke bchchom mem is biimaarii se mृtyu dr adhik hotii hai। haalmki yh biimaarii saal ke kisii bhii mhiine mem ho sktii hai kimtu srdii ke mausm mem kaalii (kukur) khmsii hone kii bhut adhik smbhaavnaa rhtii hai।
baar-baar khmsii hone aur ultii hone se bchche shaariirik roop se bhut kmjor ho jaate haim। kuchh bhii khaate-piite smy khmsii kaa dauraa praarmbh ho jaataa hai। lgaataar khmsii kaa dauraa chlne pr ultii hotii hai। baar-baar ultii hone pr khaayaa huaa bhojn pet se baahr nikl jaataa hai। kii baar aushdhi khilaate smy bhii khmsii shuroo ho jaatii hai aur ultii hone jaane ke kaarण aushdhi bhii nikl jaatii hai। khmsii ke rogii bchche ko bistr pr jaane ke baad thoड़ii der baad khmsii kaa prkop adhik hotaa hai। bchche ke jor-jor se bolne aur chillaane pr khmsii kaa dauraa praarmbh ho jaataa hai।

Symptoms: 
- ghbraaht honaa
- khmste- khmste mkh se paanii aanaa
- sms bmd hone kaa ehsaas honaa
- bukhaar yaa jukaam honaa
- gle kii nsom kaa phool jaanaa
- chehre kaa piilaa pड़ jaanaa
- khmste khmste gle kaa roomdh jaanaa
- hvaa jyaadaa lene kii chhtptaanaa
- sms lene mem ghur ghur kii aavaaj aanaa

Reasons: 
kaalii khmsii ke kaarण- (Cause & Reason of Whooping Cough)
kaalii khmsii (Whooping cough) himophaails prtusis (Haemophilus Pertussis) jiivaaणuom ke smkrmण se hotii hai। rog ke jiivaaणu rogii bchche kii naak aur mumh mem chhipe rhte haim। jb rogii bchche jor se khmste aur chhiimkte haim to rog ke sookshm jiivaaणu vaayu mem phailkr doosre svsth bchche tk phumch jaate haim। rogii bchche se baatchiit krne, uske saath uthne-baithne se yh rog doosre bchchom mem bhii phail jaataa hai।
ghr mem kisii ek vykti ko kaalii khmsii ho jaane pr dhiire-dhiire poore ghr mem khmsii phail jaatii hai। chhote bchchom mem kaalii khmsii kii utptti srdii-jukaam ke kaarण hotii hai। adhik srdii lgne, paanii mem adhik bhiigne v srdii ke dinom mem nmge pmv ghoomne se srdii-jukaam hotaa hai। aise mem kuchh bchche moomgphlii, akhrot v any koii mevaa aur ghii, tel mkkhn se bnii chiijem khaakr thmड़aa paanii piite haim to unhem khmsii ho jaatii hai jo srdii ke prkop se kaalii (kukur) khmsii mem privrtit ho jaatii hai।
kuchh bchchom ko kaalii khmsii kaa rog elrjii ke kaarण hotaa hai। elrjik vstu ke smprk mem aane pr sms lene mem preshaanii hotii hai। gle mem jln v khujlii hotii hai। gle mem soojn hone se khmsii kaa prkop bढ़ne ke kaarण rogii ko bhut piiड़aa hotii hai। khmste hue rogii kaa mumh laal pड़ jaataa hai। mumh se laar girne lgtii hai। mkhom mem se msoo bhne lgte haim। rogii bchche bhybhiit hokr rone lgte haim। ant mem ultii hone pr khmsii kaa prkop kuchh km ho jaataa hai।

Treatments:
saamaany upchaar

Home Remedies:
jaanem kaalii khmsii se bchaav ke ghreloo upaay (Home Remedies for Whooping Cough)
1. suhaagaa, klmiishoraa, phitkrii, kaalaa nmk aur yvkshaar ko piiskr choorण taiyaar kr lem। ise tve pr bhoonkr 2-2 graam kii maatraa mem shhd ko milaakr bchchom ko chtaane se kaaliikhmsii door ho jaatii hai। iske alaavaa tve pr bhunaa huaa suhaagaa v vmshlochn ko milaakr shhd ke saath rogii bchche ko chtaane se bhii kaaliikhmsii door hotii hai।
2. piipl, kaakड़aasimgii, atiis aur bheड़aa sbhii aushdhiyom ko 20-20 graam kii maatraa mem lekr baariik koot-piiskr choorण taiyaar kr lem। ismem 10 graam nausaadr, 10 graam bhunaa huaa suhaagaa milaakr piis lem। iske 3 graam choorण ko din mem 2-3 baar chaatne se kaalii khmsii door ho jaatii hai।
3. aड़oosaa ke sookhe pttom ko mittii ke brtn mem rkhkr, aag pr grm krke uskii raakh ko taiyaar kr lem। us raakh ko 24 se 36 graam tk kii maatraa mem lekr shhd ke saath rogii ko chtaane se kaaliikhmsii door ho jaatii hai।
4. moolii kaa 50 miliiliitr rs aur gnne kaa rs milaakr din mem 2 baar pilaane se kukr khmsii mem laabh miltaa hai।
5. 3 miliiliitr naariyl kaa tel hlkaa grm krke bchche ko pilaane se khmsii kaa prkop km ho jaataa hai। naariyl kii jtaa kii bhsm krke lgbhg 1 graam kaa chauthaa bhaag shhd mem milaakr yaa paanii se khaaem। isse 2-3 baar mem hii khmsii kaa veg v khmsii khtm ho jaatii hai।
6. adrk ke rs ko shhd mem milaakr 2-3 baar chaatne se kaalii khmsii kaa asr khtm ho jaataa hai।
7. 3 baadaam raat ko paanii mem daalkr rkh dem। subh uthkr baadaam ke chhilke utaarkr lhsun kii ek klii aur mishrii ke saath milaakr piis lem। is mishrण ko bchchom ko khilaane se kaalii khmsii door ho jaatii hai।
8. bchchom ko kukr khmsii hone pr lhsun kii maalaa phnaate haim jisse iskii gmdh khmsne ke saath-saath andr chlii jaatii hai aur isii kaa rs aadhaa chmmch shhd ke saath bhii pilaaem। isse kaalii khmsii door ho jaatii hai। ds boomd yaa ek chmmch lhsun kaa rs (umr ke anusaar) shhd milaakr prtidin do-tiin baar sevn krne se khoob laabh miltaa hai।
9. tve ko aag pr rkhkr laumg ko bhoon lem, phir us laumg ko piiskr shhd mem milaakr chaatne se kaalii khmsii thiik ho jaatii hai। bchchom ko kaalii khmsii mem ek chauthaaii graam se km golochn ko subh-shaam shhd ke saath chtaane se laabh miltaa hai।
10. tulsii ke pttom ke 3 graam rs mem shhd milaakr chaatne se kaaliikhmsii mem bhut adhik laabh miltaa hai।
11. tulsii ke ptte aur kaaliimirch smaan maatraa mem piis lem। iskii moomg ke braabr kii goliym bnaa lem। ek-ek golii ko chaar baar denaa chaahie। isse kaalii khmsii nsht ho jaatii hai।
12. kaalii khmsii hone pr bchchom ko bistr pr sulaane se phle uske siine aur kmr pr kpoor ko tel mem milaakr maalish krem, kaalii khmsii bnd ho jaaegii।
13. hldii kii 3-4 gmthom ko toड़kr tve pr bhoonem aur piiskr choorण bnaa lem। is choorण ko 3-3 graam subh-shaam paanii se lene se kaaliikhmsii mem aaraam aataa hai।


Disease: prostet disऑrdr (Prostate Disorder)

Description: 
prostet disऑrdr (Prostate Disorder)
prostet glaimd jyaadaa bढ़ jaane pr prostet disऑrdr (Prostate Disorder) khlaataa hai। lgbhg tiis phiisdii purush 40 kii umr mem aur pchaas phiisdii se bhii jyaadaa purush 60 kii umr mem prostet kii smsyaa se preshaan hote haim। prostet glaimd ko purushom kaa doosraa dil bhii maanaa jaataa hai। pauroosh grmthi shriir mem kuchh behd jroorii kriyaa krtii hai। jaise yooriin ke bhaav ko kmtrol krnaa aur prjnn ke lie siimen bnaanaa। jaise-jaise umr bढ़tii hai, yh grmthi bढ़ne lgtii hai। is grmthi kaa apne aap mem bढ़naa hii haanikaark hotaa hai aur ise biipiiech (Benign Prostatic Hyperplasia) khte haim।
prostet grmthi ke jyaadaa bढ़ jaane se mootr utsrjn kii preshaanii ho jaatii hai। grmthi ke aakaar mem vृddhi ho jaane pr mootr nlikaa avruddh ho jaatii hai aur yhii peshaab rukne kaa kaarण bntii hai। prostet grmthi ke aakaar mem vृddhi hone kaa kaarण spsht nhiim hai। bढ़tii umr ke saath purushom ke shriir mem hone vaalaa haarmon kaa privrtn ek kaarण ho sktaa hai।

Symptoms: 
- raat ko kii baar peshaab ke liye uthnaa।
- mootr kii kuchh maatraa mootraashy mem shesh rh jaatii hai, is shesh rhe mootr mem rogaaणu pnpte haim।
- peshaab krne mem kthinaaii mhsoos honaa।
- peshaab krne ke baad bhii mootr kii boomde tpktii rhtii haim, yaani mootr pr niymtrण nhiim rhtaa।
- aisaa mhsoos hotaa hai ki peshaab aa rhaa hai lekin baathroom mem jaane pr boomd-boomd yaa ruk-ruk kr peshaab hotaa hai।
- peshaab mem jln mhsoos hotii hai।
- mdkoshom mem drd uthtaa rhtaa hai।
- jldii jldii peshaab honaa।
- peshaab kii dhaar chaaloo hone mem vilmb honaa।

Treatments:
prostet upchaar (Treatment & Tips to Prevent Prostate Disorder)
prostet grmthi mem vृddhi hone pr mriij़ ko chikitskiiy upchaar kii aavshyktaa hotii hai। mootr thailii ke lgaataar bhre rhne se gurdom pr dbaav bढ़ jaataa hai, jisse inke khraab hone kaa ख़traa paidaa ho jaataa hai। rog kii praarmbhik avsthaa mem dvaaom dvaaraa grmthi kii vृddhi ko km krne kaa pryaas kiyaa jaataa hai। kuchh mriij़om ko dvaaiyom se koii laabh nhiim hotaa, aisii sthiti mem shlykriyaa krke rogii ke shriir se prostet grmthi nikaal dii jaatii hai। chikitsaa kii aadhunik pddhti se km se km chiir-phaaड़ v rkt-sraav dvaaraa prostet grmthi kii biimaarii kaa ilaaj smbhv hai। aisii hii ek aadhunik tkniik hai lej़r kirणom se prostektॉmii।
lejr prostektॉmii (Laser Prostatectomy)
ismem lejr kirणom ke maadhym se prostet grmthi ke us hisse ko kaatkr alg kr diyaa jaataa hai jisse mootr nlikaa kaa maarg avrooddh ho rhaa thaa। lej़r prostektॉmii mem ek phaaibr ऑptik teliiskop doorbiin ko mriij़ ke mootrdvaar se mootraashy kii or bhejaa jaataa hai। yhm prostet grmthi ke bढ़e hue hisse ko kaatkr nikaal diyaa jaataa hai aur prostet ke tukड़e ko mootraashy mem dhkel diyaa jaataa hai। mootrmaarg mem nlii daal dii jaatii hai jisse mootr utsrjn nirbaadhit roop se hotaa rhtaa hai। mootraashy mem dhkele ge grmthi ke bche hue hissom ko vhm se nikaal diyaa jaataa hai।
prostet ke n tukड़om ko paitholॉjii (Pathology) jmch ke lie bhejaa jaataa hai jhm grmthi ke aakaar mem vृddhi ke kaarणom kii jmch kii jaatii hai। prostet grmthi ke lej़r srjrii se nikaalne ke baad peshaab krne kii bढ़ii aavृtti, tiivr ichchhaa v mootraashy poorणt: khaalii n hone jaisii shikaaytem door ho jaatii haim aur mootr kaa prvaah bhii thiik ho jaataa hai।
prostet grmthi ko htaane se kyaa smsyaa aa sktii hai? (Problems to Remove Prostate Gland)
prostet grmthi ke sraav se shukraaणuom ko poshण aur surkshaa miltii hai। shlykriyaa dvaaraa grmthi ko nikaal die jaane pr koii vipriit prbhaav nhiim pdtaa kyomki prostet ke alaavaa semaainl vesikls (Seminal vesicles) bhii is kaary ko krtii hai।

Home Remedies:
jaanem prostet disऑrdr ke ghreloo upchaar (Home Remedies of Prostate Disorder)
3 se 4 liitr paanii rojaanaa piiem।
bhojn mem vitaamin sii kii maatraa jyaadaa lem।
chrbiiyukt aur vsaayukt bhojn kaa pryog bmd kr dem।
rojaanaa soyaabiin khaaem isse tetostron kaa levl km ho jaataa hai।
alsii ko miksii mem piiskr paaudr bnaa lem aur prtidin 20 graam paanii ke saath lem।
chaay aur kॉphii kaa sevn n krem, isse mootraashy griivaa kthor hotii hai jisse peshaab krne mem dikkt hotii hai।
siitaaphl ke biij kchchaa yaa bhoon kr yaa phir doosre biijom ke saath milaakr khaa skte haim। ise apne hr din ke khaane mem shaamil kiyaa jaa sktaa hai। ise slaad mem milaakr bhii khaayaa jaa sktaa hai। pohaa mem milaakr yaa soop mem daalkr bhii khaa skte hai।
kchche siitaaphl ke biij mem kaaphii maatraa mem poshk ttv maujood hote haim। jaise aayrn, phॉsphors, triptophain, kॉpr, maigniishiym, maigniij, vitaamin ke, protiin, jroorii phaitii esid aur phaaitosterol। ye biij jimk ke behtriin srotom mem se ek maane jaate haim। hr din 60 miliigraam jimk kaa sevn prostet se joojh rhe mriijom mem behd phaaydaa phumchaataa hai aur unke svaasthy mem bhii sudhaar krtaa hai। in biijom mem biitaa-stiosterol bhii hotaa hai jo testosteron ko dihaaidrotesteron mem bdlne nhiim detaa। jisse is grmthi ke bढ़ne kii smbhaavnaa n ke braabr ho jaatii hai।


Disease: eds (AIDS)

Description: 
eds yaa ekvaayrd imyoon dephisiemshii simdrom (Acquired Immune Deficiency Syndrome) duniyaa kii sbse khtrnaak aur jaanlevaa biimaariyom mem se ek hai। yh echaaiivii vaayrs ke kaarण phailne vaalaa rog hai। duniyaabhr mem eds ke srvaadhik maamle asurkshit yaun smbmdhom ke kaarण hote haim।

Symptoms: 
- akaarण vjn ghtte jaanaa।
- gle yaa bgl mem soojn bhrii giltiyom kaa ho jaanaa।
- t‍vchaa pr drd bhre aur khujlii vaale chkte ho jaanaa।
- binaa kisii vjh ke lgaataar daayriyaa bne rhnaa।
- binaa kisii vjh ke lgaataar thkaan bne rhnaa aur tejii se vjn girnaa।
- mumh mem ghaav ho jaanaa।
- mumh mem sphed chhaale jaise nishaan honaa।
- yaaddaasht mem kmii, dipreshn yaa any dimaagii biimaarii
- lmbe smy tk bukhaar rhnaa

Reasons: 
eds ke kaark (Causes of Aids in Hindi)
duniyaabhr mem eds kii phailne kii sbse bड़ii vjh (Causes of Aids) asurkshit yaun smbmdhom ko maanaa jaataa hai। lekin kii any kaarण bhii hai jo eds ke lie jimmevaar maane jaate haim:
asurkshit seks (Unsafe Sex):- ek se adhik saathiyom ke saath yaun smbmdh bnaane se echaaiivii eds phail sktaa hai। yh smlaimgik smbmdhom mem bhii ho sktaa hai।
smkrmit rogii dvaaraa (From HIV+ Victim):- echaaiivii pॉjitiv purush yaa mhilaa ke saath asurkshit yaun smbmdh bnaane ke kaarण bhii yh phailtaa hai।
smkrmit khoon chdh़aane (Through Blood Transfusion):- binaa jmch kiyaa huaa rk‍t grhण krne ke kaarण bhii echaaiivii se piiड़it hone kaa khtraa rhtaa hai। yh eds ko phailaane kii doosrii sbse bड़ii vjh maanii jaatii hai।
smkrmit suii ke istemaal se (Through Infected Needles):- drgs kii smsyaa naa sirph nshe tk siimit hai blki agr ek hii imjekshn se kii log drgs lem to yh eds kaa kaarण bn sktaa hai। sirph drgs hii nhiim dvaaii lene ke dauraan bhii smkrmit suii kaa istemaal haanikaark hotaa hai।
smkrmit bled se (Through Infected Blood):- saath hii naaii ke yhm binaa strlaaijd (rogaaणu-mukt) ustraa yaa puraanaa inphekted bled (Infected Blade) istemaal krne se bhii yh phail sktaa hai।
smkrmit maataa se (HIV Positive Mother):- echaaiivii smkrmit maataa ke dvaaraa yh bchche mem khoon yaa prsv ke smy aur doodh pilaane ke dauraan phumch jaataa hai।

Treatments:
eds se bchaav (Tips to prevent AIDS in Hindi)
surkshit seks (Use Safety):- eds, echaaiivii smkrmण aur any seks smkrmit biimaariym rokne ke lie hmeshaa smbmdh bnaate smy kmdom aadi kaa pryog krnaa chaahie। apne jiivnsaathii ke prti vphaadaar rhnaa chaahie aur ek se adhik v‍ykti se yaunsmbmdh bnaane se bchnaa chaahie।
istemaal kii gii suiyom kaa pryog naa krem (Use Disposable Syringe):- suii lgvaate smy hmeshaa yh dhyaan rkhem ki dispojebl siirimj yaa suiyom kaa hii istemaal ho।
khoon ke len-den se phle jmch (Test Before Blood Transfusion):- khoon lene yaa dene se phle uskii jmch avshy kr lem। ydi aap ech.aaii.vii smkrmit yaa eds grsit haim to rktdaan naa krem।
grbhvtii mhilaaem dhyaan rkhem (Tips for HIV+ Pregnant):- grbhvtii mhilaaom ko apnaa echaaiivii test jroor kraanaa chaahie। agr jmch pॉjitiv hai to bchchaa ho jaane ke baad echaaiivii se grst mm ko bchche ko apnaa doodh nhiim pilaanaa chaahie। is kes mem botl se doodh pilaanaa behtr maanaa jaataa hai।
shk hone pr ech.aaii.vii test (HIV AIDS Test):- ydi aap ko ech.aaii.vii eds hone kaa smdeh ho to turmt apnaa ech.aaii.vii priikshण kraanaa chaahie।
echaaiivii eds kii dvaaiym (HIV AIDS Drugs):- echaaiivii pॉjitiv vykti ko ilaaj ke dauraan emtii-retrovaayrl drgs die jaate haim।


Disease: jiikaa vaayrs (Zika Virus)

Description: 
ibolaa vaayrs ke baad duniyaabhr mem aatmk phailaanii vaalii nii biimaarii hai jiikaa। jiikaa vaayrs logom ke lie itnaa khtrnaak hai ki vishv svaasthy smgthn ne jiikaa vaayrs pr g‍lobl imrjemsii ghoshit kii hai। jiikaa vaayrs braajiil smet kii any amerikii deshom mem phailaa huaa hai aur inhiim deshom ke aane vaale logom ke dvaaraa iske vishv ke any deshom mem phailne ke aasaar haim। aaiye jaanem jiikaa vaayrs aur iske smkrmण ke vishy mem poorण jaankaarii (Zika Virus Information in Hindi)।

Symptoms: 
- m~khem laal honaa
- jod़om mem drd
- bukhaar
- ultii
- kmj़orii

Treatments:
jiikaa vaayrs kaa ilaaj (Treatment of Zika Virus in Hindi)
* siidiisii ke anusaar jiikaa imphekshn se lड़ne ke lie abhii kisii imjekshn yaa dvaaii ko ijaad  nhiim kiyaa gyaa hai। isse piiड़it vykti ko poorii trh se aaraam krnaa chaahie, khoob saaraa paanii piinaa chaahie, bukhaar kii saamaany dvaaii lenii chaahie। 
* jiikaa vaayrs se smkrmit hone pr khud ko mchchhr ke kaatne se bchaanaa chaahie anythaa yh vaayrs mchchhrom dvaaraa any logom mem phumch sktaa hai। piiड़it rogii kaa mchchhrom se bchaav bhut jroorii hai। 
not: bukhaar aane pr esprin (Aspirin), broophen jaisii dvaaiym bilkul nhiim lenii chaahie। 
grbhvtii mhilaaom ke lie khaas nirdesh (Tips For Pregnant Women)
siidiisii ke dvaaraa any deshom mem rhne vaalii grbhvtii mhilaaom ko yh sujhaav diyaa gyaa hai ki vh aphriikaa, dkshiण amerikaa yaa jiikaa prbhaavit any deshom mem naa jaaem। jiikaa vaayrs se prbhaavit jghom pr rhne vaalii grbhvtii mhilaaom ko nimn baatom kaa khyaal rkhnaa chaahie: 
* khud ko mchchhrom ke kaatne se bchaanaa chaahie। 
* raat ko sote smy mchchhrdaanii kaa pryog krnaa chaahie aur mchchhrom ke kaatne se bchne vaalii kriim lgaanii chaahie। 
* agr mchchhrom ke kaatne pr sirdrd, hl‍kaa bukhaar, laal mkhem, joड़om mem drd jaise lkshण dikhem to turmt dॉktr se slaah lenii chaahie। 
* agr grbhvtii nhiim haim to kuchh dinom ke lie pregnemsii ke plaan ko taal denaa chaahie। 
grbhvtii mhilaaom ko mchchhrom se bchne kii poorii koshish krnii chaahie kyomki jiikaa vaayrs ke kaarण unke grbh mem pl rhe bchchom ke mstishk ko sbse adhik nuksaan hotaa hai।
